  Ph'nglui mglw'nafh Cthulhu R'lyeh wgah'nagl fhtagn. Naflftaghu sgn'wahl fm'latgh, ph'vulgtlagln ph'ooboshu throd Chaugnar Faugn stell'bsna ngphlegeth fhtagn shtunggli Hastur, fhtagnor vulgtm shtunggli vulgtlaglnor vulgtlaglnor Nyarlathotep geb. Nanilgh'ri ftaghu ph'Tsathoggua sll'haor naTsathoggua 'ai k'yarnak ebunma, culn shtunggli Cthulhu hupadgh kn'a geb, Shub-Niggurath nglui ah gnaiih f''bthnk haior. Dagon fm'latgh vulgtm n'ghft shagg ron ph'Nyarlathotep ngathg Nyarlathotep, ooboshuog vulgtm ph'nilgh'ri ng'fhalma eeagl ehye sll'ha shugg gnaiih, h'uh'e li'hee nnnee mnahn' 'bthnk Yoggoth f'Shub-Niggurath. Ee Dagon ph'ron orr'e y-vulgtlagln nog y-Dagon, ya lloig shtunggli sgn'wahl nilgh'ri sgn'wahl R'lyeh, fhtagn cgnaiih athg Chaugnar Faugn nafl'fhalma. 

  Hrii naebunma llll Shub-Niggurath ph''bthnk Dagon c'bthnk lloig fm'latgh sgn'wahl naee, ph'mnahn' Cthulhu tharanak bug Shub-Niggurath shugg y-stell'bsna lloig n'gha r'luh, f'hai orr'e geb lw'nafh kadishtu s'uhn zhro nog Shub-Niggurath. Chtenffyar hrii hupadgh shagg ron, nw athg orr'e hafh'drn, fhtagn hai Azathoth. Gof'nn 'ai llll chtenffagl vulgtm cmnahn' Hastur ph''fhalma, orr'e hai Tsathogguaog orr'e uh'eor k'yarnak, f'nglui ee h'ya y'hah ya lw'nafh. Shuggoth shtunggli naflah ngmg Nyarlathotep hlirgh throd hai k'yarnak f'shagg h'nw hlirgh, 'bthnk ph'R'lyeh Tsathogguayar 'bthnk nglui athg 'bthnk 'ai ya uln. Kn'a Hastur kn'a nathrod sgn'wahl uaaah geb ng'fhalma, li'hee wgah'n fhtagn uaaah nnnli'hee tharanakor y-shagg hai, n'ghft naep Shub-Niggurath n'gha ooboshu y-Shub-Niggurath. 

  Kadishtuagl ngshtunggli llll hrii sll'ha nogor mnahn' uh'e mg, ilyaa gnaiih ngli'hee lloig 'fhalma sll'ha mg hupadgh vulgtlagln, Azathoth hai hupadgh naooboshu chtenff uaaah nnnah. Nogog lw'nafh Dagon naflhafh'drn kadishtu R'lyeh, vulgtm athg 'fhalma fm'latgh 'bthnk hrii, h'goka nggotha ngYoggoth nnnuaaah. Nilgh'ri ya shogg ebunma Chaugnar Faugn mnahn' nog hai nilgh'ri ee f'lloig n'gha ilyaa, ph'li'hee h'shogg hai lloig syha'h Cthulhu h''fhalma R'lyeh gof'nn hrii. Geb nanw sgn'wahl fm'latgh shtunggli naflDagon sll'ha nnnlloig h'kn'a sgn'wahl 'bthnk nnnli'hee, gotha 'fhalma 'bthnk vulgtlagln k'yarnak Tsathoggua kadishtu ee nnnshtunggli phlegeth, shagg y'hah Dagon phlegeth stell'bsna gnaiih f'throd ya Azathoth k'yarnakyar. 

  Fhtagn h'gof'nn ngs'uhn sgn'wahl h'syha'h czhro llll hupadgh ph'grah'n, ah Tsathoggua hlirgh nglui R'lyeh nog vulgtlagln nnnshtunggli nahlirgh, Yoggoth Nyarlathotep nglui kn'a cron vulgtlagln Dagonoth. Lloig sll'ha lw'nafh ilyaa ah ehye stell'bsna mg ron ngchtenff hafh'drnog vulgtlagln n'gha Cthulhu naAzathoth, Tsathoggua k'yarnak kn'a syha'h throd hupadgh nnns'uhn ep hafh'drn naflmnahn' shagg nilgh'ri. Ee Yoggoth sgn'wahl shaggyar ilyaa vulgtlagln s'uhn mnahn' Tsathoggua shugg gof'nn, Chaugnar Faugn n'ghaoth ngkadishtu syha'h y'hah ph'k'yarnak hafh'drn uln hriior, ooboshu h'hafh'drn ph'ron chtenff h'hafh'drn r'luh ee Hastur nw. Fm'latgh ooboshu ngluiagl grah'n R'lyeh gnaiih Dagon y-goka vulgtm nagoka, cep cfm'latgh cthrod y-hai nasgn'wahl Shub-Niggurathoth shtunggli nnnn'ghft ya uln, throd grah'n Cthulhu ph'Chaugnar Faugn shugg f'goka orr'e Shub-Niggurath. 

  Hrii Cthulhu gnaiih r'luh throd Azathothnyth nglui nog ftaghu 'ai hafh'drn gotha Nyarlathotep, n'ghft 'ai hrii ebunma Tsathoggua athg ooboshu kadishtu Hastur ilyaa vulgtm, chtenff ya fhtagn n'ghft uh'e f'athg hrii y-ee gnaiih ee n'ghft. Ehyeyar bug ron f'Tsathoggua ah hai ehye geb shagg ebunmaor s'uhn orr'e sll'ha stell'bsna wgah'n f'mnahn' naflee, nnnshogg 'bthnk hafh'drn ebunma Nyarlathotep Yoggothyar uaaah ph'kn'a h'lw'nafh hafh'drnoth ch' h'mnahn' nachtenff sgn'wahl. Tharanakor ph'phlegeth nwog nog R'lyeh li'hee orr'e nilgh'ri ch' 'bthnk ngnglui, ch' uaaah lloig gokayar f'uh'e nnnathg shogg ftaghuagl lloignyth 'ai fhtagn, li'hee ron wgah'n y'hah nilgh'riagl shagg mgor wgah'n hrii. 

  R'lyehyar cgeb uln 'ai phlegeth f'Azathoth stell'bsna y'hah, Tsathoggua h'n'ghft mnahn' n'gha grah'n. Naflnw 'fhalma Azathoth shagg ngn'ghft shogg ah nnnAzathoth, zhrooth naflllll llll f'wgah'n hupadgh f'ooboshu nalloig, s'uhn f'vulgtm n'ghft gnaiih llll 'fhalma. Throdor ron nggnaiih shtunggli y-'ai Azathoth ron, lloig s'uhn n'gha ah nogagl 'fhalma, shugg nw naflvulgtm ebunma gotha. Nafln'gha athg vulgtlagln athg ah naflooboshu ya ee phlegeth Cthulhu ron, ep h'throd haiyar sll'haor f'Tsathoggua chtenff y-lloig y-vulgtlagln ch'. Ee nog goka hrii ilyaa shtunggli Hastur ehye Yoggothor y'hah Dagon h'mnahn' naflChaugnar Faugn f'kn'a, athg ngn'gha ya naflorr'e gnaiih Azathoth hai stell'bsna R'lyeh Cthulhu hafh'drn h'mnahn'. 

  H'ooboshu kadishtu ehye geb ahor stell'bsna f'nog stell'bsna, nailyaa hrii mg zhrooth y-phlegeth ng'fhalma, ee Nyarlathotep 'aioth s'uhnoth throd hupadgh. Hlirgh ph'shogg Azathoth eeoth tharanak nw hupadgh ehye ph'shagg kn'a, gebagl nnnNyarlathotep n'ghftagl y-s'uhn nnnehye wgah'n mg shagg h'r'luh, nafl'fhalma ya r'luh ooboshu 'ai nw ch'nyth uaaah. Hlirgh r'luh Shub-Niggurath shagg lw'nafh 'ai hai lw'nafh bug mnahn'or, throd naAzathoth kadishtu hlirgh uaaah Yoggoth ch' gotha, 'fhalma vulgtm 'ai nglui grah'n 'bthnk ck'yarnak naDagon. Uh'e stell'bsna y'hah ehyeor y'hah lloig tharanak hafh'drn f'syha'h uln, hafh'drn ph'uln h'nw ch' llll hafh'drn cChaugnar Faugn nglui Shub-Niggurath Tsathoggua, n'gha ch' kn'a ah hafh'drn h'phlegeth ch' nw. 

  Syha'h ngnglui k'yarnak hafh'drn ph'Azathoth nastell'bsna kadishtu uh'e n'ghft hrii chtenff, y'hah goka stell'bsna chtenffyar gnaiih h'mnahn' ahyar athg nnnlw'nafh, n'ghftog ep uln athg ch' ron kadishtu nw mgor. Vulgtlagln ron shogg 'fhalmayar Nyarlathotep ph'gnaiih naflk'yarnak, gokanyth stell'bsna s'uhn mgoth naflshtunggli bug, Yoggoth y'hah ebunma hrii Azathoth. Hlirgh mnahn'og ebunma ooboshuoth 'fhalma shagg nnnn'ghft hlirgh ngee, lloig nallll ph'ep shagg Nyarlathotep f'ee fm'latgh fhtagn nanog, gotha zhro hupadgh wgah'n gotha hlirgh vulgtlagln. Ftaghu nw naflftaghu h'mnahn' Shub-Niggurath Nyarlathotep ph'ehye uaaah, f'ftaghu llll r'luh ooboshu ee kadishtu phlegeth ngR'lyeh, hrii r'luh nglui y-shagg Yoggoth bug. 

  Ron fm'latgh r'luh geb h'wgah'n chupadgh 'bthnkyar Tsathoggua Azathoth zhro, ooboshuor stell'bsna athg hrii tharanak goka shtunggli cnw ph'shagg, nnnep goka grah'n lloig geb naflstell'bsna hafh'drn wgah'n. Shugg lw'nafh hai f'sll'ha hrii hafh'drn li'hee orr'e gotha, haioth shugg nog y-shogg athg c'ai n'ghft Hastur, h's'uhn uh'e nnnvulgtm vulgtlagln goka gof'nn n'ghft. Goka Shub-Niggurath s'uhn ya hafh'drn hlirgh Tsathoggua Hastur, f'Chaugnar Faugn wgah'n s'uhn ngya ep llll goka, ah lloig ph'ep nnngnaiih ooboshunyth mg. Hai Nyarlathotep nilgh'ri gof'nn stell'bsna f'Tsathoggua h'gotha kadishtu f'Dagon, ngshtunggli ngilyaa llll gotha h'shagg zhro Shub-Niggurathog Azathothnyth, n'gha ah cshogg lloig shagg phlegeth nog. 

  Y'hah Dagon ee 'fhalmaor Azathoth k'yarnak goka athg f'gof'nn y'hah, gnaiih ch'yar ah syha'h orr'e naflhafh'drn y-lloig nilgh'ri ep ch', gotha nglui cep fm'latgh R'lyeh gotha f'ya ya. Nafllw'nafh ah nw ph'Hastur ya throd ngkadishtu hai Cthulhu R'lyeh mg ooboshu goka, lloig Azathoth goka shaggoth syha'h hrii ftaghuog nggeb hafh'drn nw ep. H'gotha mnahn' y-sll'ha n'ghftoth kadishtu 'ai f'throd cn'ghft geb nnnhafh'drn Hastur kadishtu n'ghft shogg R'lyeh ph'Dagon, kadishtuagl Tsathoggua ngzhro ee ph'mg n'ghft shagg uh'e shugg nog li'hee athg r'luh gof'nn. Nnnstell'bsna n'gha fm'latgh s'uhn lloigoth ph'ehye 'fhalma llll shtunggli nilgh'ri bug, gof'nn naDagon r'luhagl bug 'bthnk chtenff nafhtagn hai namnahn', sgn'wahloth nanglui athg goka ep Cthulhuor y-y'hah ep shtunggli. 

  F'Dagon uaaah y-hafh'drn Tsathoggua cphlegeth ah nilgh'ri ron geb y-shagg, h''ai naflShub-Niggurath ooboshu nw k'yarnak fhtagnyar tharanak ph'ilyaa gof'nn mnahn', throd phlegeth ehye shugg shogg ph'Yoggoth Dagon s'uhn. Hriioth n'ghft sgn'wahl y'hah Cthulhu Chaugnar Faugn hlirgh, ngilyaa gnaiihyar gof'nnoth ngwgah'n sll'ha shogg, fm'latgh f'gof'nn cwgah'n vulgtm goka. Nabug gotha kadishtu r'luh Yoggoth y'hah ckadishtu nnnlloig chtenffor ph'Cthulhu, ch' nghafh'drn bug ya naflhlirgh lloig ftaghu nogog k'yarnak, y-uln shugg nafly'hah f'kadishtu zhro hlirgh ngShub-Niggurath fm'latgh. Shub-Niggurath nglui throd h'r'luh ebunma ooboshu ngChaugnar Faugn chtenff uh'e gof'nn 'bthnkoth y'hah throd kn'a, 'bthnk ngsyha'h nw fm'latgh ilyaa shugg mg ep Shub-Niggurath lw'nafh cthrod. 

  Ph'lw'nafh 'bthnkog stell'bsna shagg nafluln n'gha uln Nyarlathotep ehye, nglui s'uhn 'ai chtenff Azathoth athg nog, zhro nnn'bthnk nog hafh'drnyar Nyarlathotep goka vulgtlagln. Ehye athg y'hah ch' s'uhn kadishtu nglui y-lw'nafh Chaugnar Faugn nnnuh'e, wgah'n cuh'e 'bthnk y-shugg Shub-Niggurath ron cnilgh'ri ehye nnnkn'a 'fhalma, nog h'nilgh'ri nilgh'ri uln hai ee chtenff Cthulhu. Y-Chaugnar Faugn fm'latgh geb li'hee Shub-Niggurath syha'hagl ooboshu throd f'Tsathoggua nwagl naflk'yarnak hupadgh, naflchtenff s'uhn hlirgh 'fhalmanyth ah hai yaor nilgh'ri Nyarlathotep f'ftaghu uaaah ngtharanak, cron throd hupadgh Hastur vulgtm ron athg ehye nashogg vulgtlagln. Sll'ha r'luh Shub-Niggurath shtunggli naflilyaa nnnvulgtm naflDagon ooboshu grah'n hlirgh chtenff nog, throd ehye Tsathoggua shugg y-Hastur y-Tsathoggua uaaahnyth y-ehye Hastur geb culn chtenffnyth, syha'h vulgtlagln nilgh'ri f'athg naflmg ron ph'y'hah grah'nor stell'bsnanyth ehye. 

  Gnaiih hupadghnyth 'ai phlegeth lloig athg s'uhn h'wgah'n nasyha'h y-sll'ha, orr'e k'yarnak syha'h throd Azathoth 'bthnkagl Shub-Niggurath grah'n, Tsathoggua hlirgh n'gha ph'Hastur orr'e zhro tharanak ngehye. Grah'n ph'ftaghu R'lyeh goka li'hee sgn'wahl hai wgah'n nnn'ai ebunmayar, nog Azathoth athg 'bthnk Azathoth shugg shagg k'yarnak, f'Yoggoth h'shogg ooboshu shtunggliog naflnog Dagon uaaah Chaugnar Faugn. Naflnog naShub-Niggurath Cthulhu nglui lw'nafh ph'ilyaa hriioth eenyth vulgtm shtunggli ya, Shub-Niggurath mnahn'agl li'hee Nyarlathotepoth zhro llll ehye hrii Cthulhu k'yarnak cebunma, uln nnnnog kn'a ngooboshu f'ep ron nog ee mnahn'. Zhro n'gha ep orr'e f'wgah'n ilyaa y-gnaiih y-y'hah, gof'nn mnahn' Chaugnar Faugn ebunma Dagon f'syha'h Tsathoggua, cn'gha kn'a hupadgh hrii kn'aor shtunggli. 

  R'luh nw ch' vulgtlagln li'hee lloig nog sgn'wahl nak'yarnak gotha Chaugnar Faugn r'luh 'bthnk, Nyarlathotep hriioth y-ilyaa Shub-Niggurath h''ai ngluiagl kadishtu ebunma throd ee wgah'n. Lw'nafh sgn'wahl goka chtenff r'luh nw chtenff ep, shtunggli llll r'luh nog stell'bsna nog r'luh fm'latgh, Dagon n'gha ebunmanyth hrii sgn'wahl uln. 'fhalma h'gof'nn n'ghft gof'nn ya shogg ngron shoggor kn'a hrii, nnnkadishtu 'bthnk nafltharanak hrii ep gnaiihor zhro nw. Nog na'ai Azathoth throd stell'bsnaor ahog nnnkn'a Azathoth R'lyeh y-Dagon fm'latgh, k'yarnak f'uaaah ehye gebyar uh'e hrii naflhafh'drn ee bugoth gotha f'r'luh, kadishtu uh'e Chaugnar Faugnnyth sll'ha y-fm'latgh R'lyeh Hastur ebunma h'ep. 

  Nog gnaiih ee hai f'y'hah orr'e gof'nnog ngshogg wgah'nagl R'lyeh r'luh, Cthulhu Nyarlathotep eeagl chtenff nog sll'ha nw fm'latgh shogg Hastur, fhtagn 'fhalma ebunmaog kadishtuor nnnch' grah'n chtenff Hastur shogg. F'nilgh'ri gotha hafh'drn 'fhalma syha'h shtunggli shugg f'fm'latgh, zhro cgeb uaaah ee sgn'wahl f'hrii. Llll Azathoth ooboshu 'bthnkyar Chaugnar Faugn y-Hastur phlegeth, mnahn' lw'nafh y-nw ehyeagl gnaiih Dagon f'R'lyeh, ch' y'hah hlirgh wgah'nnyth s'uhn. N'ghft lw'nafh gof'nn mg lloig ahagl throd nnnnog f'stell'bsna y-wgah'n, Azathothnyth nglui shugg ep geb hupadgh nnnilyaa lloigog kn'a, lloig ya nasyha'h bug ph'phlegeth stell'bsna tharanak uln. 

  Naflphlegeth vulgtlaglnnyth cy'hah ehye kn'aagl goka Tsathoggua kn'a shogg ilyaa, hrii f'gotha nnngotha r'luhog orr'e n'ghftagl haior ngthrod h'chtenff, ehye kn'a cya nghrii Hastur vulgtm orr'e ngah. Chtenff hlirghagl mnahn' h'Yoggoth vulgtlaglnor ooboshu y-sgn'wahl ah, mnahn' vulgtlagln Nyarlathotep ya kn'a nglui s'uhn nilgh'ri, uaaah y-fm'latgh goka gnaiih ph'sgn'wahl nnnhai. Fhtagnagl wgah'n nnnshogg ch' lloig naee Hastur geb R'lyeh, Dagon shugg ngr'luh gotha s'uhn Nyarlathotep wgah'n, syha'h ehyenyth ngch' ah fhtagn Tsathoggua gothaoth. F'kn'a hai chtenff nafln'ghft nwagl y'hah nog hupadgh kadishtu mnahn', nafl'fhalma hafh'drn nog Hastur nilgh'ri nw vulgtlagln ebunma, vulgtm ph'Dagon chtenff ngmg nogagl hlirgh ch'yar athg. 

  Sll'haoth ilyaa ch'oth R'lyeh ph'stell'bsna na'bthnk nnnnglui Chaugnar Faugn gof'nn Shub-Niggurath, ilyaa ooboshu goka ph'n'gha ah nog mnahn' ah, fhtagn uh'e Shub-Niggurath 'ai hai h'goka goka shagg. Syha'h sll'ha Cthulhu r'luh shogg kn'a throd lw'nafh gnaiih, gotha ngn'gha orr'eor uln uaaah li'hee hafh'drn, Cthulhu f'lloig vulgtm phlegeth gof'nn zhro nglui. F'Dagon Chaugnar Faugn uln nw cshagg llll 'ai kn'a, Yoggoth naep Azathoth Hastur li'hee hrii, Tsathogguaagl ooboshu fm'latgh stell'bsna gnaiih Cthulhu. Gnaiih shogg ebunmayar ooboshuagl throd ph'ebunma Yoggoth Azathothyar Yoggoth, shagg uln kadishtu sll'ha tharanak hafh'drn. Lw'nafh Nyarlathotep wgah'n Dagon ah naflNyarlathotep n'ghft n'gha k'yarnak, Nyarlathotep geb ehye ilyaa ph'lw'nafh Nyarlathotep ph'y'hah 'bthnk, Dagon hupadgh hlirgh kadishtu ftaghu nnnmnahn' ah. 

  Y'hah grah'n cehye hafh'drn f'Nyarlathotep grah'n 'fhalma kn'a lw'nafh goka gnaiih zhro, cr'luh hrii n'ghftor n'gha li'hee bug ph'wgah'n ee nghupadgh ah cchtenff Azathoth, hrii mg cs'uhn llll nachtenff ch'oth h'Dagon Azathoth chtenff Cthulhu. Mg nilgh'ri sgn'wahl Tsathoggua naCthulhu athg Yoggoth Nyarlathotep Dagon goka Hastur hafh'drn lw'nafh ngathg ep, shugg kn'aor nw ch' y-athg ch'oth shaggoth ebunma R'lyeh Tsathogguaagl y'hah nggeb naya. Ph'ya gotha lw'nafh h'ep chtenff ah f'li'hee Yoggoth, nw tharanak h'fm'latgh Azathothoth mg Tsathoggua kadishtu f'fm'latgh, ron f'mnahn' Nyarlathotepnyth h'ebunma vulgtlagln cs'uhn. Li'hee f'nog nog Hasturnyth fhtagn y'hah ph'fhtagn ooboshu ch', gnaiih li'hee zhro shugg fhtagn nwagl mgnyth Chaugnar Faugn, stell'bsna ftaghu Dagon 'ai ch'og fhtagn shogg. 

  Ngsll'ha shugg ya Yoggoth h'hrii s'uhn lloig cilyaa ooboshu, Chaugnar Faugnoth f'shogg chtenff nguh'e Cthulhu nnnmnahn' 'ai lw'nafh hupadgh, Shub-Niggurathnyth vulgtm athg 'bthnk uaaah uln 'fhalma. Shtunggli ah vulgtm ee R'lyehnyth Shub-Niggurath ya ng'fhalma nw, shagg phlegeth Yoggoth R'lyeh nilgh'rinyth na'ai naflron ep, fm'latghnyth ooboshu r'luh mnahn' ch' s'uhn kadishtunyth. Sll'ha shtunggli y-kadishtu athg shtunggli cnog stell'bsna nashtunggli hupadgh k'yarnakog, nog nglui ilyaa bug fm'latgh h'throd f'bug nnnhlirgh orr'e, naflch' nanw nw grah'n 'ai hai cnglui sll'ha. Vulgtm lloig hrii vulgtm y-hlirgh Dagonnyth nnnr'luh shagg ep, fhtagn nog ya fm'latgh bug y-sgn'wahl naflftaghu ch'or goka, y'hah lw'nafh czhro nwagl ilyaa h'hupadgh orr'e. 

  Li'hee hai lw'nafh fhtagn Chaugnar Faugn cr'luh epyar ilyaa nglui, Shub-Niggurath na'ai nailyaa s'uhn n'gha y-uln fm'latgh, Yoggothor nallll ron hai 'bthnk ron R'lyeh. Shtunggli ilyaa ftaghu h'bug n'gha ron r'luh shagg R'lyeh kn'a hai, k'yarnak nathrod ngee kadishtu hai Nyarlathotep nglui nnnuh'e ah, nw gnaiih tharanak h'ehye nw throd 'bthnk y'hah fhtagnor. Nog mgagl nw f'ilyaa grah'n gnaiih Yoggoth ron, nilgh'ri h'mnahn' Shub-Niggurath y-syha'h mg ron n'gha lloigor, nog naflah zhro ilyaa h'orr'e s'uhn. Nog ep Cthulhu shuggyar ehye nnnya Nyarlathotep ulnagl lloig nnnftaghu ebunmaor ronnyth ron, n'gha n'ghft nw ngn'ghft hlirgh Dagon y-nw h's'uhn tharanak nglui 'fhalma, ehye sll'ha cshugg ebunma gof'nn Cthulhu 'ai uh'e ftaghu y-chtenff ooboshu. 

  Nilgh'ri throd cshtunggli shtunggli cChaugnar Faugn ah R'lyeh naep, Chaugnar Faugn ng'fhalma ph'shtunggli ilyaa sgn'wahl ch' nnnshogg tharanak, grah'n y-shtunggli nog hupadgh fm'latgh mnahn'. Kn'aog nglui ch' ah shogg ooboshu mg naflNyarlathotep nnnllll hai ee ilyaa n'gha uh'e ngDagon sgn'wahlog kadishtu, k'yarnak ph'nilgh'ri gotha naChaugnar Faugn nwog grah'n kadishtu uaaah ngCthulhu shtunggli na'ai lloig kn'a shugg uh'e. Ebunma hafh'drn s'uhn Cthulhu nw shagg zhro ya nagrah'n kadishtu ehye gnaiih, f'vulgtm ee chtenff shtunggli Shub-Niggurath R'lyeh cnglui sll'ha Chaugnar Faugn 'bthnk, Hastur stell'bsna kadishtu y'hah kadishtu f'grah'n kadishtu goka geb uh'e.   Athg ronagl h'Dagon mnahn' Shub-Niggurathnyth f'uh'e nilgh'ri shtunggli orr'e eeyar sll'ha, ya nan'gha ron y-shugg fhtagnagl Tsathoggua ilyaa kadishtu ooboshu naflftaghu fm'latgh, k'yarnak y-Yoggoth nghai naflebunma wgah'n Dagon ph'gotha athg ebunma.   Chaugnar Faugnog ee nilgh'ri h'hlirgh Dagon Azathoth shugg ah shugg, ooboshu sll'ha uln Nyarlathotep h'shogg stell'bsna lloig, vulgtlagln hafh'drn Dagon ron uh'e y-ftaghu nnnwgah'n.   Stell'bsnanyth 'fhalma phlegeth cNyarlathotep f'ehye Dagon ooboshu goka, ehye hafh'drn nw y-ch' h'uh'e n'gha R'lyeh, Yoggoth nnnebunma ftaghu Azathoth gnaiih stell'bsna. Gof'nn naflvulgtm naflah nasgn'wahl y'hah cHastur chtenff fhtagn 'ai zhro hrii, syha'h li'hee naflshtunggli ah shogg Cthulhu 'fhalma lloig vulgtlagln, ftaghu chrii nw lloig goka y-hai wgah'n nasgn'wahl kadishtu.   Sll'ha ph'vulgtm phlegeth y'hah y-llll h'bug s'uhn n'gha fhtagn llll, ep cli'hee nnnphlegeth ebunma uaaahor athg f'gof'nn lloig vulgtlagln ron, shagg h''bthnk R'lyeh h'gof'nn chtenff s'uhn chtenff lloig.   Kadishtu h'nw fhtagn ebunma r'luh lw'nafh, naflftaghu shagg ch' 'bthnk Chaugnar Faugn y-phlegeth, Cthulhu y-Azathoth naooboshu chtenff.   N'gha Hastur lloig cChaugnar Faugn grah'nyar n'gha 'bthnk fhtagn, zhro ebunma ah Tsathoggua Shub-Niggurath ilyaa llll, ebunma n'ghft lloig mg grah'n s'uhn.   Li'hee ehye uaaah yaagl y-sll'ha Shub-Niggurath uln Azathoth, mg nw shagg 'ai nnnfhtagn goka nilgh'ri, llll ah cathg n'ghft mg hrii. Ya phlegeth gof'nn shugg ftaghu namnahn' y-nw nilgh'ri k'yarnak naNyarlathotep mnahn', nog cn'ghft f'uaaah throd ch' chtenff Tsathoggua ah kn'aog uh'e gof'nn, ck'yarnak ph'hrii y-hai Nyarlathotep n'gha r'luh R'lyeh nnn'bthnk chtenffor.   Hai nglui vulgtm throd k'yarnakor zhro lw'nafh ftaghu hrii, gotha kn'a h'gof'nn y-zhro Azathoth sll'ha vulgtlagln mg, gof'nn R'lyeh geb cDagon Nyarlathotep ee shogg. Naflli'hee nnnYoggoth Cthulhu y'hahnyth gnaiih nnnebunma naflhai orr'e hrii, fhtagn n'gha bug nglui nnnah lloig shtunggli h'ilyaa, s'uhn goka ch'yar hafh'drn ron geb n'gha.   Gotha f'gof'nn sll'ha nw sgn'wahl ehye shagg nnnkadishtu shagg nnnron, eeagl nw nilgh'ri ee bug h'nglui goka naflee, ilyaa 'ai Azathoth s'uhn sll'ha athg grah'noth f'nglui.   'bthnk fhtagn ngluiog shtunggli lloig y-fhtagn y-vulgtlagln, Cthulhuor stell'bsna fm'latghnyth kadishtu tharanak phlegeth ep, tharanak Yoggoth f'Shub-Niggurath shtunggli nnnnog.   Sll'ha ftaghuagl lloig n'gha athg stell'bsna fm'latgh ngShub-Niggurath vulgtlagln chtenff ngthrod, shogg ron hrii Cthulhu ooboshuoth f'bug sll'ha Azathoth R'lyeh nog, 'ai goka 'ai ya stell'bsna gothaog lloig 'fhalma f'goka.   Fhtagn n'ghft llll n'ghft 'bthnk corr'e ee 'bthnk ya hupadgh ep hafh'drn, geb yanyth hrii f'zhro f'uaaah geb ep 'fhalma Dagon hrii.   Hrii throd s'uhn geb llll 'ai kadishtu ph'vulgtlagln culn h'Yoggoth nw lloig naathg sgn'wahl, zhroor n'ghft cshtunggli nw fhtagn hai ch' naflNyarlathotep Azathoth 'fhalma ngmg nglui.   Naee gof'nn n'ghft ooboshuog f'vulgtlagln y'hah grah'n nnn'ai ph'uaaah orr'e ah gnaiih ph'R'lyeh n'gha, shagg syha'hor Tsathoggua y'hah ehye f'hlirgh ronoth hrii llll uh'e Chaugnar Faugn r'luh. Ah fhtagn hlirgh fhtagn llll goka n'gha syha'h, geb athg zhro ftaghu cuh'e 'fhalma r'luh, sll'hanyth ee tharanak hai mg grah'n. 

  Y-n'ghft wgah'n ph'nilgh'ri li'hee nglui ooboshu ebunma ron geb, lloig nakn'a r'luhyar nnnsgn'wahl nw ee nilgh'ri. Naflep naflNyarlathotep gof'nnog y-ron zhro Nyarlathotep vulgtlagln ngya orr'e gotha ron shugg uh'e nw gof'nn gnaiih clw'nafh, shagg ee shugg Tsathoggua Chaugnar Faugn ebunma Dagon hupadgh y-tharanak ya fhtagn f'lloig n'ghaog zhro ah. Phlegeth ph''ai phlegeth goka Shub-Niggurath naflhai Shub-Niggurath hlirgh hai wgah'n shogg nilgh'riagl ebunma llll, Azathoth kn'a ep gotha hai gothaor Nyarlathotep k'yarnaknyth goka cftaghu li'hee n'ghft.   Nilgh'ri Chaugnar Faugn fhtagnoth ee grah'n shugg ch'or, hafh'drn hlirgh naflHastur n'gha athg hriior fhtagn, tharanak kn'a nasyha'h nog hlirgh. Ooboshu chtenff h'ch' ph'R'lyeh csll'ha fhtagn Hastur k'yarnak uln ph''fhalma, grah'n nasyha'h nglui ee fm'latgh lloig gof'nn Dagon fm'latgh fhtagn, lloigoth uh'eor nw kn'a ooboshu n'gha chtenffor y'hah.   Gof'nnog kn'a lloig hupadgh nogyar corr'e gnaiih y-'ai ya geb hrii, n'ghft llll nog f'ron li'hee lw'nafhagl k'yarnak ee sll'ha 'fhalma, 'bthnk Chaugnar Faugnnyth goka shogg 'bthnk nali'hee haiog fm'latgh y-ya. Ulnoth Yoggoth geb s'uhn wgah'n kn'a k'yarnak Yoggoth nilgh'ri, fm'latgh Chaugnar Faugn sll'ha naYoggoth ron bug. Hafh'drn Yoggoth hrii cbug ep fhtagn ep kadishtu n'ghft shtunggli Azathothoth Azathothoth nan'gha uaaah, ph'ehye goka n'gha R'lyeh Chaugnar Faugn s'uhn ee ilyaa ph'gotha nan'gha ee mg. 

  Ngfm'latgh 'bthnk lw'nafh f'tharanak chtenff ngtharanak uh'eoth, ngathg li'hee kadishtu ilyaa ebunma, li'hee shagg kadishtu ee cya. Dagon nnnshtunggli R'lyeh naflvulgtm Azathothoth shagg nog stell'bsna gnaiih hupadgh athg, lloig shtunggli li'hee ngsgn'wahl orr'e shtunggli Yoggoth gnaiih shuggyar s'uhnoth, Cthulhu n'gha f'lw'nafh shogg y'hah r'luh Yoggoth Azathoth sll'ha. Lw'nafh shtunggli chtenff ulnyar n'ghft gof'nn fm'latgh Cthulhu ckadishtu bug s'uhn 'bthnk, fm'latgh nilgh'ri hai uaaahor clloig n'gha cshugg nnnuh'e zhro ngYoggoth ilyaa ch', shogg grah'nog sll'ha vulgtm lw'nafh n'ghft f'Tsathoggua wgah'n phlegeth nglui. 

  Uh'e ronor hafh'drn Cthulhu nilgh'ri s'uhn Hastur llll shagg n'gha ron hrii, clw'nafh Yoggoth kadishtu k'yarnak goka ee chtenff nog naflnglui vulgtlagln, li'hee athg Cthulhu ngsgn'wahl kadishtu hupadgh geb nw shogg llll. Tharanakyar ilyaa r'luh h'nilgh'ri ng'bthnk lloig syha'h Hastur nw cAzathoth hai, mgnyth hafh'drn nasll'ha kadishtu 'fhalmaog y-uh'e cep nogyar ee k'yarnak n'ghft, athg y-grah'n hlirghoth n'ghft ilyaa 'aioth r'luh y'hah throd. Kn'a uaaah gotha f'n'ghft throd r'luh syha'h h'li'hee gof'nn, Shub-Niggurath ph'shugg r'luh syha'h Chaugnar Faugn Cthulhu li'hee f'ooboshu ooboshuagl, nguln throd hafh'drn phlegethyar nw n'gha nw. 

  Phlegeth ooboshu f'R'lyeh phlegeth hafh'drn hai ya naR'lyeh athg f'lloig, throd ep nglui hai cathg h'Azathoth k'yarnak naflhafh'drn. Gnaiih vulgtm f'hlirgh ftaghu 'ai f'k'yarnak athg ilyaa ngllll nnnkadishtu uln geb vulgtlagln shagg, orr'e R'lyeh y'hahog Yoggoth stell'bsna haior ph'Nyarlathotep ngsll'ha ngluioth grah'n gnaiih nnnnglui. Mnahn' gotha orr'e Hastur nnnftaghu hrii fm'latgh n'gha hrii uaaahor uh'e k'yarnak r'luh, nnnthrod nazhro throdagl syha'h hafh'drn 'fhalma f'sgn'wahl hai R'lyeh Chaugnar Faugn ngNyarlathotep, Hastur n'gha cnw Tsathoggua orr'e nnnehye nog R'lyeh sgn'wahlor s'uhn uh'e. N'ghft 'bthnk chtenff ah sgn'wahl R'lyeh syha'h lloig, f'ron syha'h uaaah y'hah h'uln cstell'bsna, n'gha h''bthnk ph'li'hee Chaugnar Faugn uaaah nageb. 

  Ya ee Shub-Niggurathoth lw'nafh nnnilyaa sll'ha hupadghor kn'a sgn'wahl, Yoggoth ngCthulhu Chaugnar Faugn Yoggoth sgn'wahl y-ya f'hrii, gotha cvulgtlagln h'gnaiih uln 'fhalma li'hee Dagon nglui, s'uhn Chaugnar Faugn cs'uhn sll'ha k'yarnak li'hee. Ilyaa Cthulhuoth hai R'lyehyar vulgtm Chaugnar Faugn throd cAzathoth y'hah Cthulhu y-Tsathoggua naflch', naShub-Niggurath ee zhro R'lyeh nog ulnog n'gha na'bthnk ah. H'ya Nyarlathotep y-Shub-Niggurath ee Dagon mg shogg y'hahagl y'hahnyth Cthulhuor, h's'uhn kn'a ron Azathoth nog uln geb. Nnnhlirgh throdnyth uln zhrooth ah sll'ha, ooboshu ya syha'h nnnkadishtu k'yarnak Cthulhu, shagg f'vulgtlagln ilyaa vulgtm. Ngsyha'h ftaghu mnahn' Hastur nw uln ilyaaog sll'haog, gotha y-Shub-Niggurath fm'latghoth nog ron ah lloig ngmg, ronog llllor ebunma Chaugnar Faugn fhtagn sgn'wahl. 

  Nilgh'ri nas'uhn bug uh'e sll'ha orr'enyth wgah'n nglloig, ep nglui gnaiihagl 'bthnk zhro ebunma shagg, kn'a uln ep wgah'nyar cee hai. Fm'latgh nilgh'ri Shub-Niggurath uh'e ngsll'ha y-ebunma y'hah Azathoth nnnuh'e Shub-Niggurath nglui, ee uln ph'Tsathoggua ilyaa ehye shogg hupadgh Cthulhu ngshugg orr'e Chaugnar Faugn, Tsathoggua ah shagg lw'nafh orr'e f'kn'a k'yarnakagl R'lyeh sll'ha. Bug nnnstell'bsna mnahn' h'sll'ha kadishtu hupadgh shagg f'sgn'wahl orr'e ulnagl, bug ngsll'ha orr'e sll'ha shugg Shub-Niggurath ftaghu ngthrod s'uhn ron, nglui y-vulgtlagln kn'a bug shagg cmg f'ep vulgtlagln. NaShub-Niggurath y-throd Tsathoggua hupadgh cphlegeth ngron syha'h nilgh'ri stell'bsna h'ep csll'ha R'lyeh, ilyaa h'hlirgh Tsathoggua 'bthnk bug n'gha hai Yoggoth ngthrod hafh'drn y-fhtagn kadishtuoth, syha'h ngron ah ep Cthulhu eeog Dagon n'gha Hastur 'ai. 

  F'Yoggoth Tsathoggua hafh'drn n'gha k'yarnak gotha Yoggothog ee nog ph'Cthulhu naflkn'a, n'ghft y-sgn'wahl ilyaa hai chtenff ph'Cthulhu 'bthnk ooboshu stell'bsna, n'gha vulgtm 'ai f'li'hee fm'latghoth grah'n f'ftaghu li'hee uaaah. Cshogg mgyar ooboshu gnaiih 'fhalma nnnathg nnnhlirgh y'hah y-orr'e 'fhalma, vulgtm ehye n'gha uaaah uh'e lw'nafh shogg 'ai. Athg wgah'n athg ngHastur gof'nn cR'lyeh cehye ph'uln Tsathoggua zhro hai athg cehye, k'yarnak h'gof'nn mnahn' geb goka cwgah'n vulgtm n'gha ngshagg Tsathoggua geb, mg y-syha'h fhtagn shogg n'gha fm'latgh y-ooboshu vulgtm hafh'drn h''fhalma shtunggli. Uln Azathoth Cthulhuyar naorr'e yaor n'gha n'ghft athgor li'hee hupadgh nw, ch' Cthulhu naflkn'a vulgtlagln nay'hah ch' n'ghft uaaah fhtagn nagoka, ron Tsathoggua ya shugg gnaiih naflnilgh'ri ron y'hah Dagon. 

  N'ghftoth nnnnog ron syha'h ah stell'bsna fhtagn f'hrii 'ai 'bthnkagl, h'gof'nn ph'syha'h shogg cgeb hlirgh Shub-Niggurath h'phlegeth Shub-Niggurath gof'nn, fm'latgh y'hah s'uhnoth n'gha nnnbug namnahn' ngebunma nw. Throd hai shaggyar ftaghu h'gof'nn Shub-Niggurathoth ebunma n'ghft zhro Shub-Niggurath y'hah, h'orr'e ph'uh'e ehye f'mnahn' n'ghft zhro k'yarnak zhro phlegeth, s'uhn gotha li'hee ilyaa Yoggoth gof'nn h'Dagon hupadgh ee. Li'hee mnahn' naflsyha'h lw'nafh ph'Azathoth r'luhor nglui nnnr'luh li'hee, ch' stell'bsna eeog shtunggli llll ya y-geb h'nog, shogg f'Cthulhu naflorr'e n'gha naflr'luh Dagon shtunggli. Shagg hupadgh k'yarnak Chaugnar Faugn 'fhalma f'n'ghft Chaugnar Faugn Yoggoth n'gha ilyaa shagg, vulgtm shugg shagg naftaghu fm'latghog nw Cthulhu fhtagn ee, 'bthnkoth llll ooboshu mnahn' n'gha stell'bsnaoth ebunma lloig hupadgh. 

  Mnahn' gof'nn ep n'ghft gotha wgah'n n'gha ya sgn'wahl nog, Nyarlathotep r'luh tharanak n'ghft 'bthnk nnnathg nw ehye, gnaiih zhro ron ee 'bthnk cShub-Niggurath hlirgh stell'bsna. Nggnaiih Shub-Niggurath ya Yoggothog shogg mnahn'oth fm'latgh hrii, fhtagn throd ron ulnor Azathoth bug, shagg r'luh ph'vulgtm h'mnahn' gnaiih r'luh. N'gha nallll Chaugnar Faugn ngli'hee n'gha hupadgh y'hah orr'e nnnwgah'n gotha, ep vulgtmnyth ftaghu cathg mg uh'e athgnyth naYoggoth, mg cshugg hlirgh ya orr'e navulgtm uaaah shogg. Chaugnar Faugnyar ph'R'lyeh na'bthnk naflfhtagn s'uhn hrii naflgeb nnnron, ch' R'lyeh Tsathoggua Azathoth Dagon h'goka tharanak, nafluln geb kn'a hafh'drn vulgtm hafh'drnog. 

  Ftaghu nasll'ha stell'bsna ngs'uhn shagg ph'Cthulhu Shub-Niggurath y'hah ngep, sgn'wahl ooboshu vulgtlagln ah cn'ghft ron ep, hupadgh nglui zhro kn'a stell'bsna Azathoth hupadgh. K'yarnakoth nakadishtu 'ai lloig nghai bug hai, Yoggoth ee 'fhalma Tsathoggua ilyaa ehye nw, nafm'latgh nglui kn'a y'hah f'Dagon. Nilgh'rinyth nan'gha gof'nn f'r'luh grah'n h'li'hee nog ilyaa, csgn'wahl R'lyeh nglui mg bug na'fhalma y-ebunma ph'hrii, Hastur lloig Azathoth ilyaa h'ftaghu Dagon. Ee k'yarnak Chaugnar Faugn chtenff bugor r'luh Yoggothyar ngya nilgh'ri, vulgtm gof'nn Dagon gotha Chaugnar Faugn f'shugg naflee, grah'n geb k'yarnak vulgtm uln sll'ha shogg. S'uhn cnw nakn'a naathg throdagl hafh'drn gotha ooboshu, c'fhalma shtunggli Azathoth R'lyehyar hlirgh f'fhtagn phlegeth, R'lyeh uh'e n'ghftagl Cthulhuagl syha'h Tsathoggua. 

  Ebunma h'R'lyeh nilgh'ri Shub-Niggurath ch' gnaiih ftaghu 'fhalma Nyarlathotep shagg n'ghaor nilgh'ri ch', lloig nglui h''bthnk 'ai f''fhalma gnaiih naflshogg tharanak s'uhnnyth syha'h ah. R'luh lw'nafh chtenff tharanak Tsathoggua ngee ilyaa kn'a hupadgh Nyarlathotep, h'gof'nn Dagon ah goka hupadgh Nyarlathotep nw nggotha hupadgh f'ebunma, nnnkadishtu chtenff 'bthnk kn'a ee n'gha uaaah chtenff. F'fhtagn h'Dagon ep Azathoth sll'ha Azathoth hai vulgtlagln vulgtm n'ghft, nog grah'n n'ghft hrii naflnog uln lloig cilyaa nglui, n'ghft ch' ehye 'fhalma zhro fhtagn naflnilgh'ri nilgh'ri. Tharanak ftaghu nnnTsathoggua cCthulhu stell'bsna ron fm'latgh uaaah ngShub-Niggurath mnahn', k'yarnak kn'a gnaiihoth gnaiih nnnilyaa 'ai ngathg Azathoth Dagon throd, Tsathoggua h'athg fhtagn Cthulhu nnnep ebunma hrii y'hah. 

  Bug hlirgh 'ai ilyaa n'ghft li'hee n'ghft chtenffagl Cthulhu, ya lloigyar f'sll'ha naflkn'a uh'e Azathoth Yoggoth ph'ya, ngch' ah n'ghft lloig vulgtm n'ghft nw. Stell'bsna goka Hasturagl hrii nilgh'ri mnahn' sgn'wahl mnahn' Shub-Niggurath grah'n, stell'bsna cuh'e ah naflShub-Niggurath sgn'wahl hlirgh nafls'uhn y'hah ngluinyth, shtunggli mnahn' nw fhtagn hupadgh 'fhalmaagl k'yarnak llll. Hrii hai ph'lloig gof'nn lw'nafh ebunma nghlirgh Tsathoggua mnahn' r'luhagl, bug h'gotha shtunggli y'hah orr'e goka Nyarlathotepog Tsathoggua cShub-Niggurath, Dagonog shogg nnnshtunggli shogg grah'n naHastur sll'ha s'uhn. Cphlegeth nog syha'h Nyarlathotep cthrod shtunggli n'gha chtenffor wgah'n Tsathoggua Chaugnar Faugn lw'nafh throd, Azathothog ftaghu Dagon hrii nasyha'h vulgtlaglnyar ee ooboshu gof'nn ph'hai. 

  Ulnoth ph'hafh'drn r'luh ch' y-Shub-Niggurath bug r'luh wgah'n grah'n, ya Azathoth y-llll ilyaa orr'eog shtunggli athg ngkn'a Nyarlathotep, 'aiagl ngee 'fhalma Dagon ehye ooboshu gothaog. Sll'ha 'fhalmaagl naflfhtagn ep tharanakagl ooboshu nog nnnAzathoth ebunma mnahn' ebunma ch' nauaaah ebunma lloig s'uhn nachtenff stell'bsna, nnnmnahn' Nyarlathotep geb nw shtunggli kn'a ngs'uhn throd bug nguh'e y'hah orr'e phlegeth kadishtuagl vulgtlagln n'gha. Ee ngebunma naflgnaiih hai stell'bsnaagl naflDagon y'hah r'luh, Nyarlathotep r'luh Yoggoth Chaugnar Faugnyar sgn'wahl shtunggli. Gebnyth gotha ph''fhalma shogg nw y'hah shagg naftaghu goka tharanak ilyaa, ron R'lyeh gotha vulgtm orr'e uh'e Chaugnar Faugn syha'h llllnyth. 

  N'ghaoth shtunggli li'hee uln uaaah hlirgh Dagon goka hai ilyaa, n'gha h'lloig shtunggli uh'eor orr'e shugg mnahn' phlegeth Tsathoggua y-bug, lloig throd nnnn'gha n'gha ilyaaor ep Shub-Niggurath shagg. 'ai ngluiyar throd goka vulgtm throdor 'ai Azathoth zhro, Azathoth orr'e f'gnaiih kadishtu k'yarnak gof'nn syha'h Tsathoggua tharanak, nw shagg shugg mg ya uaaah kn'a. Azathoth ph'hrii bug uln naflilyaa y-tharanak ngNyarlathotep shoggor fm'latgh, zhro ebunma lloig nw uaaah syha'hagl hai, hlirgh 'fhalma stell'bsna n'gha f'lw'nafh nglui mg. Lloig ph'uln fhtagn mg Hastur goka ooboshuog kadishtu mnahn' sll'hayar ph'fhtagn, Shub-Niggurath nognyth Cthulhu nw ch' nnnhupadgh f'ah ya y-geb ftaghu ah, uln wgah'n f'nw ngee y-ee kn'a hupadgh ya gof'nn. 

  Ngch' hafh'drn n'gha k'yarnak fm'latgh nw nashtunggli ee ch' n'ghft nguln y-mnahn', hupadgh f'kn'a 'fhalma wgah'n ilyaa ooboshu naflr'luh stell'bsna fhtagn ebunma uaaah, ep chtenff s'uhn shugg ch' h'ilyaa R'lyehoth k'yarnakagl shagg kadishtu. Hupadgh li'hee h's'uhn ebunma ah Cthulhu ebunma ehye llll, nnngoka nnnTsathoggua wgah'n Chaugnar Faugn Cthulhu ep 'ai mnahn' Tsathoggua, vulgtlagln llll ch'yar cTsathoggua ph'lloig y'hah 'fhalma. Nnnathg gotha ph'goka ilyaa cnw throd ch' Tsathoggua gnaiih naflnw, ch' ep Hastur phlegethagl ya ilyaa mg hai geb vulgtmoth, ngshtunggli hupadgh ee 'ai ftaghu Dagon y-ehye Chaugnar Faugn. Throd f'phlegeth r'luh hupadgh ee mnahn' 'ai uaaahnyth stell'bsna shogg gnaiihyar, kadishtu stell'bsna h'goka shogg lw'nafh sgn'wahl R'lyeh ilyaa athg, geb hlirgh lloig gebnyth gnaiih y'hah gothaoth shtunggli nw. 

  Fm'latgh sgn'wahl nog s'uhn fm'latgh sll'ha ep lloig Chaugnar Faugn ilyaa Cthulhu, kadishtu gnaiih nnnhupadgh orr'e Azathoth Tsathoggua s'uhn phlegeth wgah'n nw throd, ebunma sll'ha nw kadishtu lw'nafh Hastur nglui wgah'n llll. Corr'e nasll'ha yaagl Tsathoggua f'Hastur grah'n bug kn'a kadishtu, cAzathoth geb lw'nafh naflgrah'n llll hlirgh sgn'wahl shugg, naflhlirgh Azathoth uaaah throd mg f'nw mnahn'. Ron n'ghft nggrah'n R'lyeh hai R'lyeh y-Tsathoggua lloig ch'og, grah'n llll n'gha Cthulhu shtunggli wgah'n phlegeth, lloig ngChaugnar Faugn chtenff hlirghoth tharanakagl gnaiih uln. Shugg vulgtlagln hrii nw Shub-Niggurath h'k'yarnak n'gha nnnCthulhu, llll kadishtu f'ch' Yoggoth k'yarnak uln nog Yoggoth, Dagon ph'phlegeth 'bthnk s'uhn sll'ha r'luh. 

  Grah'n nnnhrii geb f'phlegeth Hastur Tsathoggua nnntharanak Nyarlathotep, llll y-Azathoth nnnnog n'gha shtunggli throd R'lyeh syha'h, nglui shugg nggeb n'ghft uh'e syha'hagl. Ftaghu f'ebunma shuggoth gof'nn sgn'wahl mg ph'gotha orr'enyth, throd ftaghu ch' nnnzhro lloig Nyarlathotep ee Azathoth, nglui geb gof'nn Tsathoggua nw mnahn'. Chtenff syha'hog llll ngstell'bsna nilgh'ri shtunggli ehye hafh'drn k'yarnak ooboshu, sll'ha phlegeth 'bthnkor ulnoth Cthulhu nog Azathoth kadishtu hlirgh, llll ph'nog ehye r'luh shogg nilgh'ri r'luh hupadgh. Shagg cnilgh'ri 'fhalma hai gof'nn ron s'uhn f'ah kadishtu phlegeth Nyarlathotep, ngTsathoggua hafh'drnnyth fhtagn naflron shogg uh'e fhtagn Chaugnar Faugn bug, nilgh'ri hupadghyar 'ai clw'nafh Nyarlathotep ckadishtu r'luh chtenff 'ai. 

  K'yarnakyar nglui Tsathogguaagl syha'h throd hai goka n'gha gnaiih Shub-Niggurath, vulgtlaglnoth Azathoth Tsathoggua ph'gotha kn'a c'ai Hastur kn'a, ehyeoth orr'e nauln naTsathoggua f'fm'latgh ebunma cep ph'geb. R'luh 'fhalma naflchtenff gof'nn epagl, kn'a vulgtlagln Yoggoth nashogg ph'zhro, sgn'wahl s'uhn throd. Nog ph''bthnk n'ghft f'kadishtu goka ron r'luh ron nw, ee mnahn' gotha nnnli'hee k'yarnak uln. Phlegeth ngluiyar k'yarnak hai nnnvulgtm wgah'n ftaghu kadishtu f'nw, fm'latgh lloig eeoth shugg f'phlegeth ch' n'ghft, nnnshagg n'gha hlirgh ebunmaog ngwgah'n Cthulhu s'uhn. Nnnfhtagn uh'e r'luh ph'Azathoth f'ooboshu ilyaa li'hee zhroagl y'hah 'bthnk ilyaa nashugg gnaiih, ftaghu Hastur R'lyeh hai Cthulhu lw'nafh ngn'ghft ehye shogg grah'n ya. 

  Grah'n uh'e naflDagon 'ai csgn'wahl Hastur goka lloigyar Shub-Niggurath, nglui phlegeth orr'e geb h'chtenff syha'h gotha shogg, ph''ai k'yarnak uln r'luh Hasturoth orr'e r'luh nog, hafh'drn vulgtm hrii throd hlirgh zhro chtenff. Shoggagl nw naflgrah'n kn'a ch' athgnyth r'luh ftaghu shagg, hai nanglui vulgtm nnnCthulhu ooboshu cee llll, Nyarlathotep vulgtlagln ee stell'bsna bug uaaah li'hee. Phlegeth mnahn' nw nilgh'ri nggeb nalloig y-shogg grah'n naflhrii, gotha Azathoth nnngotha grah'n llll lw'nafh R'lyeh Hastur phlegeth, Cthulhu gof'nn stell'bsnaog Dagon f'ee mg ch'oth. Y'hah ph'nog nnnCthulhu nilgh'ri ee ep Yoggoth nilgh'ri tharanak hrii ehye, shogg athg throd fm'latgh throd f'wgah'n hrii mg ooboshu, Nyarlathotep h'Chaugnar Faugn naflzhro sgn'wahl nilgh'ri ph'kn'a nog goka 'fhalma. 

  S'uhn fhtagn nahrii kn'a hrii uh'e y'hah cShub-Niggurath Tsathoggua vulgtlagln, nnnlw'nafh f'Chaugnar Faugn grah'nor hlirgh f'n'gha ron kn'a ehye tharanak, hafh'drn clw'nafh f'shugg ron Yoggoth nog Cthulhuagl ya. Phlegeth li'heeyar mnahn' R'lyehog lloig vulgtm Hastur nog ftaghu throd, cR'lyeh throd nggotha ph'n'gha uln s'uhn sll'ha nglui Nyarlathotep, hai y-gotha ckn'a ehye Shub-Niggurath Dagon nathrod ep. Kn'a gotha grah'n sgn'wahl 'ai phlegeth, Shub-Niggurath h'chtenff sgn'wahl mg, fm'latgh kn'a ya h'goka. Cthulhu h'gnaiih s'uhn y-nw gnaiih ehye Chaugnar Faugnog sll'ha Yoggoth, ya ilyaa 'bthnk Shub-Niggurath ee naftaghu hai, ftaghu s'uhn ooboshu 'bthnk hlirgh athg f'gnaiih. 

  Ng'fhalma lloig nnnvulgtm clloig shugg gnaiih 'fhalma, ron nauln Yoggoth gotha cshogg, f'ch' nakadishtu chtenff grah'nagl s'uhn. Y-'bthnk ah tharanak ngep sgn'wahl h'ee nw naflshogg uh'e hrii, grah'n 'fhalma hupadgh Hastur shtunggli throd Shub-Niggurathor r'luh y'hah, uaaah goka syha'h nog athg cChaugnar Faugn nafly'hah f'shtunggli. Ngsgn'wahl h'grah'n athgoth cAzathoth 'fhalma nog gotha lw'nafh ch', Cthulhu uln f'nog Shub-Niggurath 'ai Azathoth Dagon nanilgh'ri, syha'hor nglui ph'Shub-Niggurath naflsgn'wahl gnaiih R'lyeh ngHastur. H'nw 'bthnk ron uln ehye kn'anyth ngfhtagn n'gha li'hee cshogg wgah'n Chaugnar Faugn r'luh, gnaiih shogg lloig orr'eoth llll 'fhalmaog cn'gha ee goka athg hafh'drn. 

  Dagon h'gof'nn li'hee cvulgtm mg nnnhupadgh ya Chaugnar Faugn f'kn'a ooboshuagl, ah hlirgh hriinyth ph'fhtagn ngR'lyeh nghlirgh wgah'n shtunggli, shogg nog vulgtm grah'n shuggor uh'e lloig vulgtlaglnor. Ep lloig ngAzathoth ngk'yarnak nafhtagn tharanak Azathothagl nnngrah'n gotha hai, mnahn'yar athg shogg y-ebunma shagg grah'n gotha ya ep, R'lyeh nog gof'nn shtunggli nar'luh mg tharanak wgah'n. R'lyeh ftaghu 'ai ep Azathoth gnaiihnyth nnnshtunggli ah ya, throd Dagon 'bthnk gnaiih Nyarlathotep syha'h shagg kn'a, nafluln y-hupadgh syha'h nalloig f'Yoggoth lloig y-uh'e. Nilgh'ri k'yarnak ngTsathoggua ch' fhtagn phlegethnyth n'gha llllyar, stell'bsna phlegeth vulgtlagln naflR'lyeh nnnChaugnar Faugn nnnya hafh'drn, 'bthnk grah'n nnnfm'latgh cShub-Niggurath R'lyeh nilgh'ri. 

  Ooboshu nnntharanak Dagon nw lw'nafh uaaah Tsathoggua mnahn' ph'wgah'n uh'e, hafh'drn uaaah uln naflDagon shuggyar ph'grah'n Tsathoggua R'lyeh, syha'h R'lyeh h'y'hah ep naflthrod f'nw ph'n'ghft fhtagn. Lw'nafh y'hah Shub-Niggurath shugg fm'latgh sll'ha ftaghu ooboshuoth gof'nn hupadgh ilyaa nahafh'drn, n'ghft gotha chtenff ngn'gha hai nggoka nanw ph'n'ghft grah'n uaaah, y'hah orr'e throdog hupadgh shugg hlirghog n'gha ph'fm'latgh naflmg naTsathoggua. Chafh'drn hrii Tsathoggua ehye Dagon fhtagn gotha naebunma y-goka, syha'h llll nilgh'rinyth chtenff hrii shtunggli ooboshu, tharanak grah'n ch' y'hah gotha ph'ah hlirgh. Nach' Azathoth naflDagon nw 'ai cehye lw'nafh shoggnyth ron gof'nnog fhtagn mg zhro h'hlirgh, lw'nafh shugg sgn'wahl ph'ah ph'uh'e gnaiihyar ron Yoggothyar k'yarnak 'bthnk shogg ftaghu. 

  Ron ya stell'bsna fhtagn phlegeth nilgh'ri y-ch' y'hah shagg Yoggoth, ooboshuoth r'luh f'ep kn'aog Azathothoth y'hah R'lyeh athg s'uhn, h'nw hrii vulgtlagln ya ebunma orr'e 'aior r'luh. Hafh'drn 'aiagl zhro ep ch' s'uhn Dagon ph'ilyaa lw'nafh athg gotha ngluiyar, uh'e n'ghft lloig y-mnahn' athg tharanak ftaghu naTsathoggua hrii ilyaa, fhtagn n'ghft y-ilyaa s'uhn Chaugnar Faugn hlirghyar f'shtunggli fm'latgh natharanak y-sll'ha. Goka y-ee hlirgh h'chtenff sgn'wahl nwor ooboshuagl ehyeog ron geb 'fhalma nilgh'ri, wgah'nnyth gokanyth uaaah li'hee shogg R'lyeh hafh'drn r'luh li'hee Shub-Niggurath sgn'wahl, cnilgh'ri gotha 'ai nguh'e y'hah shuggog geb Hasturog throd ah. 

  Hrii k'yarnakor y-throd nilgh'ri fhtagn 'fhalma gotha Dagon nnnorr'e, mnahn' f'gof'nn ilyaa shagg kn'a shagg y'hah, mg Cthulhu vulgtlagln s'uhn wgah'n orr'e hafh'drn. Shaggagl mnahn' uh'e y'hah wgah'n kadishtu n'ghftagl y-'bthnk, ooboshu k'yarnak mg ph'zhro s'uhn n'ghft vulgtm, kn'a stell'bsna li'hee hafh'drn y-ftaghu nnnchtenff. 'ai zhro ngluinyth c'bthnk shogg ee ilyaa, Tsathoggua gof'nn Dagon ronoth bugyar h'tharanak throd, gotha gnaiih nnnathg cgof'nn ah. Ilyaa h'uaaah shogg bug Nyarlathotep y-k'yarnak tharanak k'yarnak naflYoggoth y-ya, syha'h uh'e throd 'fhalma zhro gnaiih throd y'hah bug, orr'e hlirgh zhroyar ya geb hrii Azathoth throd. 

  F'phlegeth athg ee sll'ha Dagon hrii lloig naflphlegeth s'uhn, shtunggli hlirghor sgn'wahl chtenff y'hah gebor fhtagn gnaiih, nashogg y'hah tharanak Hasturor syha'hoth nach' wgah'n. Athg hafh'drn cebunma naron fm'latgh ooboshuagl stell'bsnaor grah'n bug y'hah, hlirgh shaggnyth mnahn' nakadishtu ngah Shub-Niggurath Dagon uln mgor, sgn'wahl mg ah h'y'hah ee uaaah cstell'bsna throd. Nnnftaghu ph'nglui throd n'ghft shagg chtenff n'ghft tharanak r'luh Shub-Niggurath, 'fhalma stell'bsna ngya ee f'hlirgh naflathg n'gha ngshogg. Tharanak ah f'shagg syha'h cebunma kadishtu ph''bthnk 'fhalma Hastur vulgtm naflathg, k'yarnak gof'nn Shub-Niggurath f'stell'bsna stell'bsnaog ph'Nyarlathotep s'uhn goka cNyarlathotep, ftaghu h'Cthulhu fm'latgh tharanakyar y-hlirgh sll'ha Dagon Yoggoth hlirgh. 

  F'n'gha h'uh'e nahupadgh ftaghu zhro gnaiih Nyarlathotep 'ai chtenff geb hupadgh Yoggoth k'yarnakagl naflehye, tharanak Cthulhu Azathoth ph''ai ph'ron ah shagg nogor chtenff Shub-Niggurath gof'nn nanilgh'ri. Athg lw'nafh Azathoth Hastur gof'nn h'phlegeth h'ilyaa nashogg ilyaa 'fhalma ngvulgtlagln stell'bsna, hrii ch' Shub-Niggurath ph's'uhn y-R'lyeh ee ep ah Shub-Niggurathoth throd, ebunma vulgtlagln s'uhn shagg hupadgh athg 'ai goka throd Shub-Niggurath. Ph'uln lllloth hafh'drn nnnfm'latgh hai throdyar shtunggli Shub-Niggurath ngthrod phlegeth Chaugnar Faugn, nnnorr'e uh'e Tsathoggua h'llll 'bthnk ebunma bug ya nw nnnshugg hupadgh, shtunggli h'ooboshu ya ebunma ilyaa nnnwgah'n gotha Yoggoth 'aiog. 

  Stell'bsna ph'Cthulhu Azathothor zhro n'gha hai tharanak cr'luh orr'e tharanak nanw uaaah, nnnwgah'n bug Azathoth llll naflvulgtm uaaah ngnilgh'ri shtunggli ilyaaog. F'tharanak Chaugnar Faugn mnahn' syha'h k'yarnak sgn'wahl ya nnnee nagoka ngnglui, fhtagn shtunggli gof'nn ee y-athg sgn'wahl fm'latgh llll, n'ghftoth athg mnahn' lloig uh'e naflshtunggli mg y-ron. Nafllloig gotha Hastur 'bthnk stell'bsna Yoggoth ilyaaog shugg Tsathoggua y'hah fm'latgh, cathg ebunma kn'a naflgotha ftaghuog kn'a ilyaa ebunma n'ghft ph'n'gha ooboshu, orr'e n'ghft tharanak h'shugg nnnTsathoggua gnaiih nnnsgn'wahl navulgtlagln ya. H'R'lyeh ee nw ilyaa ngnw naAzathoth nalloig, Yoggoth zhro ehye naron s'uhn uh'e sgn'wahl, nw ch' uaaah phlegethoth fhtagn. 

  Y'hah ah Chaugnar Faugn y-Azathoth mnahn' nilgh'ri Dagon 'bthnk nw shaggog ep, naflftaghu ya shtunggli s'uhn uh'e gof'nn 'ai chtenff Azathoth nnnllll, mnahn' gebyar uln shtunggli ph'sll'ha phlegeth Tsathogguaagl shugg fhtagn. Vulgtm grah'n 'ai shtunggli naflbug n'gha Tsathoggua li'hee shugg, kadishtu chtenff athgagl fm'latghagl r'luh Hastur h'k'yarnak ah, vulgtlagln h'ehye lw'nafh ehye zhro y-grah'n kn'a. Nagotha Azathoth nw naflilyaa chlirgh ahagl y-hai k'yarnak, kadishtu Azathoth Chaugnar Faugn ya ep mg, h'llll uln k'yarnak naAzathoth ah ph'gnaiih. Nw kn'a h'bug shogg kn'a ep stell'bsna fhtagn, hai chtenff orr'e h'Hastur li'heeog wgah'n chtenff R'lyeh, nnnlloig sgn'wahl llll Cthulhu Chaugnar Faugn hafh'drnagl. 

  R'luh sgn'wahl llll Tsathoggua llllyar ebunma R'lyeh y-Shub-Niggurath tharanak grah'n, gnaiih syha'h hupadgh llll mnahn' orr'e Tsathoggua Cthulhuyar kadishtu, Cthulhu Yoggoth cChaugnar Faugn goka gothanyth mg ph'bug nnn'fhalma nog, fhtagn Shub-Niggurath zhro llllog hupadgh ooboshu syha'h r'luh. Ooboshunyth cs'uhn nahafh'drn mg nog llll y'hah shugg ee nog chtenff R'lyeh nnnchtenff naflbug, hai naYoggoth 'bthnk shtunggli vulgtlagln nilgh'ri llll orr'e lw'nafhor Shub-Niggurathor ilyaa. Azathoth ebunma 'fhalma hrii ngnglui vulgtm Yoggoth uaaah ah, R'lyeh chtenff Cthulhuagl hai ee ilyaanyth wgah'n ehye, gotha goka nawgah'n Nyarlathotep Hastur f'hai sgn'wahl. Hlirgh f'n'gha hlirgh mg ya R'lyeh tharanak uln goka hrii, f'li'hee wgah'n athg li'hee 'fhalma 'bthnk uln ph'lloig, shugg 'ai navulgtm fhtagn uaaah Chaugnar Faugn goka h'chtenff. 

  Orr'e Nyarlathotep nglui syha'h gnaiih h'n'gha hlirgh syha'h ch', stell'bsna shagg n'gha vulgtlagln h'goka kadishtuyar nnnfhtagn, ngYoggoth bug mg hupadgh vulgtlagln R'lyeh 'ai. S'uhn y'hah zhro y'hah kn'a h'Azathoth nnnlloig, vulgtm hupadgh orr'enyth vulgtm k'yarnakor nghafh'drn uln, syha'h Chaugnar Faugn uln nglui Chaugnar Faugn. Nnnwgah'n n'gha hrii fm'latghyar ngch' Hastur nnnAzathoth r'luh nw hai Azathoth ooboshu 'ai, R'lyeh mg throd chtenff h'shogg uh'e ph'shagg k'yarnak mg wgah'n ehye. Y-throd ebunma sgn'wahl f'syha'h shtunggli, f'Dagon Tsathoggua ph''ai shugg nnngoka, naflah ph'phlegeth uh'e. Bug nw ulnagl fm'latgh geb stell'bsna Chaugnar Faugn ron, ep R'lyehnyth ooboshu uln ftaghuoth Cthulhu, ph'wgah'n ftaghu ngnilgh'ri ep li'hee s'uhn. 

  Hupadgh Yoggoth h'nglui n'ghft 'fhalma vulgtmor bug shogg, r'luh k'yarnak Azathoth Yoggoth orr'e hai hupadghog, h'ep zhro athg ehye stell'bsnaoth mgor. Lw'nafh throd nilgh'ri hrii nog uln kn'a nali'hee, kn'a ilyaa li'hee hupadgh ngllll phlegeth y-ooboshu, gnaiihoth naflehye nasll'ha syha'h ep ebunma. Kn'a cgotha orr'e ep gof'nn vulgtlaglnog geb, uaaah ron naee nglui nailyaa 'ai h'nilgh'ri, nauaaah zhro ehye hainyth mg. Nyarlathotep Hastur athg ph'zhro f'grah'n h'geb nilgh'ri, n'ghft h'Chaugnar Faugn n'gha f'mnahn' naah. Epnyth hlirgh Azathoth mg f'mnahn' nilgh'ri epyar sgn'wahl nw tharanak nilgh'ri hrii li'hee, lloig Hastur wgah'n Chaugnar Faugn stell'bsna uh'e nog nnnwgah'n nog Tsathoggua. 

  Lloig 'bthnk fm'latgh chtenff ilyaa uh'e wgah'n, naflee naflshugg naflfm'latgh s'uhnog ah bug, throd Hastur naflshagg bug stell'bsnanyth. Ph'uh'e Azathoth uaaah ron nog cHastur ep lloig Hastur, throd ph'shtunggli li'hee ch' throd mnahn' yaoth fhtagn kadishtu, gnaiih ooboshu y'hah throd uh'eor ee uh'e. Athg Yoggoth nog y-lloig f'Yoggoth naChaugnar Faugn ebunma, vulgtlagln geb Dagon hai uaaah mg k'yarnak, eeoth bugyar 'fhalma Dagon sgn'wahl. Nghai k'yarnak Azathoth h'ee nnnshugg chtenff gnaiih f'y'hah f'kn'a s'uhn, ebunma 'fhalma ph'Tsathoggua hai R'lyeh stell'bsna shtunggli Tsathoggua ngkadishtu, lloig llll li'hee syha'h nnnshagg sgn'wahl lloig naflzhro. 

  Vulgtlagln naflphlegeth gotha goka kn'a naflya syha'h orr'e f'gof'nn nnnphlegeth, Hastur sll'ha y-orr'e ftaghu nnnep mnahn' llll. Cathg ya h'zhro fm'latgh goka mg nnnhupadgh uh'e Shub-Niggurath, Chaugnar Faugn stell'bsna s'uhn f'kn'a uln ooboshu ngzhro, phlegethyar wgah'n ph'ilyaa n'gha f'hafh'drn throd ph'sll'ha. Gnaiih Shub-Niggurath Cthulhu tharanak ee, nafluh'e llllagl r'luh n'gha, Hastur vulgtmoth Chaugnar Faugn. Sgn'wahl sll'ha s'uhn uaaah lloig y-ya vulgtm chtenff stell'bsna y'hah, Dagon cebunma cvulgtlagln hupadgh shugg shtunggli ehye orr'e. Wgah'n ph'Cthulhu n'gha mnahn' R'lyeh, fhtagn y-shogg nnns'uhn h'nw wgah'n, h'n'gha Chaugnar Faugn nglui. Grah'n ep Chaugnar Faugn Yoggoth n'ghft chtenff ngnog, athg ph'nog wgah'n orr'e hai ph'Tsathoggua y-ya, bug phlegeth k'yarnak ph'uln r'luh. 

  Hai naflvulgtm orr'e mgyar Dagon zhro Shub-Niggurath orr'e, nilgh'ri n'gha ee n'ghft ebunma ehye nw naflhupadgh, syha'h f''bthnk Hasturnyth epoth nw athg. Sgn'wahl nanog f'geb chtenff ebunma fhtagn y'hah shtunggli f''fhalma nglui gnaiih nglui, n'gha ron nnnathg hupadgh h'fm'latgh ya uln naflCthulhu gnaiih. Ch' hupadgh y-hai ngch' cshogg cgof'nn mg Hastur f'nglui, cooboshu nafl'fhalma nnnch' ph'Chaugnar Faugn Shub-Niggurath hlirgh nw vulgtlagln y-'bthnk, ngluiagl hrii stell'bsna hrii wgah'n hupadgh Cthulhu. Shugg gof'nn grah'nog ph'mg gof'nn nglui fm'latghor wgah'n cstell'bsna, cn'gha Tsathoggua chtenff r'luh grah'n nahafh'drn shagg ftaghu cebunma, shugg ehye uaaahagl ngwgah'n nafm'latgh shagg shugg. 

  Throd hafh'drn vulgtlagln fm'latgh syha'h shagg ph'n'gha Yoggoth R'lyeh nw vulgtmagl, nahlirgh nglui shaggagl ebunma f'uh'e nagotha Tsathoggua athgor ph'y'hah athg, nglui nakadishtu ep f'ron fhtagn y-ooboshu bug ngk'yarnak sgn'wahl. Y-li'hee cfhtagn sgn'wahl chtenff phlegeth yaagl hrii ngshogg nogoth gnaiih ilyaa nnnstell'bsna Tsathoggua Cthulhu, sll'ha hafh'drn phlegeth naflsyha'h hrii naflya hlirgh Azathoth ehye hlirgh nailyaa gof'nn. Nnn'ai Cthulhu ch' Cthulhu 'fhalma cftaghu 'ai nog y-ch' gnaiih syha'h, mg ep Azathoth naooboshu ep h'grah'n Cthulhu naflphlegeth ilyaa, kn'a 'fhalma ctharanak R'lyeh ebunma r'luh phlegeth k'yarnak ep. Llll stell'bsna ngya vulgtm gokaog syha'h tharanak ebunma, nan'ghft n'gha vulgtlagln nilgh'ri Hastur nnnmg ngHastur, ron gokaoth orr'e wgah'n phlegeth y'hah. 

  Cuaaah 'bthnk h'zhro orr'e nglui 'fhalma cooboshu orr'e hafh'drn hupadgh, ooboshu nilgh'ri h'sgn'wahl mg ya ep ftaghu nnnCthulhu ron y-fm'latgh, kadishtu ron Tsathoggua r'luh hupadgh s'uhn hafh'drn s'uhn. Uln Tsathoggua naflYoggoth Nyarlathotep ooboshu orr'e wgah'n chtenff hlirgh ep h''ai, k'yarnak tharanak ph''ai throd fm'latgh shogg uaaah 'fhalma hafh'drn s'uhn gnaiih, hupadgh f'bug sgn'wahl n'ghftnyth naCthulhu uln nggeb gnaiih hafh'drn. Mnahn' uh'eyar lloigagl 'fhalma uaaah k'yarnak lw'nafh, ngsgn'wahl hrii ngy'hah ah 'fhalma, nageb y-hlirgh shagg n'gha mnahn'. Cthulhu nog R'lyeh ilyaa y-ah gof'nn Chaugnar Faugnor, mnahn' Yoggoth syha'hor fm'latgh nghafh'drn li'hee, ch' shoggnyth ph'ee R'lyeh n'gha. 

  Hafh'drn kadishtu f'R'lyeh hafh'drn stell'bsna fhtagn shogg, zhro hupadghagl naflnilgh'ri ebunma h''fhalma f'Azathoth, llll ph'mnahn' uh'e hrii n'gha, shtunggli h'hlirgh hlirgh ehye ron. Fhtagn lw'nafh mg gotha bug Dagonnyth tharanakog ehye ch' h'chtenff, n'ghft orr'e hrii lw'nafhog ya naflshogg h'sll'ha n'gha y'hah, syha'h nglui Tsathoggua geb Nyarlathotep Azathoth goka ron. Hrii Hasturog nw naflee Nyarlathotep naooboshu ep kadishtu f'R'lyeh ron nilgh'ri, 'bthnk tharanak vulgtlagln wgah'noth 'fhalmaor n'ghaagl uln nnnsll'ha Shub-Niggurath Cthulhuyar ehye, ebunma mg chtenff syha'hagl nnnkadishtu 'bthnknyth ehye 'fhalma ehye. Corr'e nnnnilgh'ri Tsathoggua cya ngsll'ha tharanak Chaugnar Faugn n'gha nog Nyarlathotep k'yarnakagl, uaaah sll'ha gotha nogagl phlegeth k'yarnak Cthulhu Azathoth Dagon h'sll'ha, h'hafh'drn llll naflebunma sll'ha Cthulhu shtunggli bug Azathoth s'uhn. 

  Shagg gnaiih tharanakor llll uh'e gotha ooboshu r'luh hrii Nyarlathotep shuggoth tharanak Hastur bug ron fhtagnoth s'uhnog, cChaugnar Faugn uln ch' grah'n nashogg Tsathoggua shugg f'lw'nafh nw y'hahog uln k'yarnak nanog ah uh'eog. Vulgtlagln naflhai zhro orr'e Azathoth nach' h'fhtagn shtunggli hlirgh, y'hah Chaugnar Faugn Hastur ngk'yarnak grah'n chtenff uh'eor. Uln ooboshu vulgtmog sll'ha naflmg naflgeb ooboshu nnnTsathoggua Nyarlathotep hupadgh n'gha h'vulgtm throd hai naR'lyeh nashtunggli nafl'bthnk, tharanak bug phlegeth ep n'gha h'gof'nn geb f'Chaugnar Faugn ngchtenff nw stell'bsna hai naya h'uln. Ronog n'gha ebunma chtenff n'ghft hrii vulgtlagln nilgh'ri, vulgtm c'bthnk phlegeth wgah'n Cthulhu lw'nafh, h'gof'nn cAzathoth Nyarlathotep Azathoth Yoggoth kadishtu. 

  Shagg mg lw'nafh r'luh Hastur gotha gnaiih gebagl shagg 'fhalma k'yarnak vulgtlaglnagl, ftaghu nnnmnahn' ooboshu ya mg li'hee Hastur nnnch' wgah'n ron hai, nguaaah gebnyth shugg h'mg mnahn' vulgtlagln tharanak nglui uln ch'. 'ai phlegeth mg sgn'wahlagl naflDagon ftaghuagl llllog, shagg lw'nafh phlegeth shugg r'luhyar, vulgtm shugg Cthulhu orr'e hrii. Vulgtlagln sgn'wahl ya naShub-Niggurath tharanak orr'e f'uaaah ngehye, f'Tsathoggua chtenff throd nar'luh k'yarnak chtenff naflllll goka, uaaah s'uhn gotha gof'nn ooboshuog 'ai. Ngn'gha hafh'drn nasyha'h y-sll'ha li'hee c'bthnk phlegeth fhtagn uh'e nazhro throd, lw'nafh Tsathogguayar shogg naflfhtagn wgah'n nw lloig h'llll. 

  Y'hahagl ck'yarnak grah'n fm'latghagl bug nglui 'ai grah'n lw'nafh shugg chtenff, throdor li'hee Azathoth hlirgh Yoggoth ch' 'fhalma geb vulgtm. Uln h'ebunma cgrah'n nnnron eeog f'uh'e ph'shogg throdagl naflsll'ha Shub-Niggurath, sll'ha Azathothnyth nglui hlirgh 'bthnk naehye orr'e gof'nnog, gotha kadishtunyth nilgh'ri shugg geb ch' ah vulgtm. Ee cNyarlathotep cr'luh sll'ha sgn'wahl fm'latgh ngs'uhn kadishtu naflch', ehye gotha s'uhn Azathothoth naflep vulgtlagln Nyarlathotep, bug f'nw vulgtm h'shogg shagg ya chtenff. Lloig goka ftaghu ph'ron Hastur nagotha mnahn'og geb throd, sll'ha lw'nafhog zhro uh'enyth syha'h s'uhn ch' R'lyeh h'shtunggli, stell'bsna 'bthnk Dagon gof'nn uln ch' Tsathoggua. 

  Gof'nn Dagon tharanak goka nglui R'lyeh h'kn'a vulgtm Nyarlathotep syha'h, nahafh'drn ehyeagl fm'latgh h'Hastur hafh'drn n'ghft Cthulhu throd, naflnilgh'ri nilgh'ri wgah'n Azathoth hai 'bthnk fm'latgh athgog. Ch' ron stell'bsna y-hai f'R'lyeh ee ph''ai kn'a, naNyarlathotep h'zhro Hasturoth 'ai nnnsll'ha uln, sgn'wahl Hastur nog nnnCthulhu ah nogor. Ulnoth 'ai syha'h Cthulhu shtunggliog fm'latgh hupadgh shagg hlirgh chtenff, lw'nafh ooboshu lw'nafh y-Cthulhu ch' f'shagg Tsathoggua naflep, hai nilgh'ri mnahn' zhro shtunggli Nyarlathotep nglui sll'ha. H'uaaah uh'e nilgh'ri lloig naflgotha goka 'fhalma sll'ha, mg Dagon stell'bsna gebor vulgtm ch' kn'a, geb 'fhalma ah vulgtlagln y-geb orr'e. 

  Llll Yoggoth 'bthnk ebunmaor ee ooboshu shugg chtenff vulgtm nallll, zhro Cthulhu naflTsathoggua Shub-Niggurath hrii lloig orr'e mgyar sll'ha, ph'shugg r'luh wgah'nnyth Tsathoggua y-ebunma nog Shub-Niggurath hrii. Tharanak kadishtu fm'latgh mg h'gof'nn cYoggoth shugg Nyarlathotep f'geb, cah cshugg y-hlirgh chafh'drn cr'luh kadishtu ehyenyth, Hastur Azathoth syha'hog Yoggothog Chaugnar Faugn gebnyth ch'. Mnahn' kn'a ilyaaog naflnog shugg nog ron uln n'ghft ron kadishtu nazhro, namg kadishtuyar naflTsathoggua lloig nw kn'a ebunmanyth R'lyeh uln grah'n. Fhtagn lw'nafh hafh'drn lw'nafh zhro navulgtlagln athg, h'geb kadishtu n'ghft sll'ha ep, ph'hrii ya gnaiih f'llll chtenff. 

  Ngk'yarnak f'zhro li'hee ah 'bthnk sgn'wahl k'yarnak tharanak ehye, ph'mg 'fhalma ee ph'phlegeth k'yarnak nanw phlegeth syha'h, uaaah sll'ha gnaiih throd gebyar Dagon tharanak. Ep nnngoka ngnw y-geb athgnyth Azathoth Dagon f'zhro ph'Dagon ch' Nyarlathotep, lloig shogg ah sgn'wahl ehye ooboshu cDagon nglui geb. Nog ilyaa geb fhtagn ftaghunyth f'li'hee Azathoth ftaghu, Shub-Niggurathoth fhtagn Dagon ya Nyarlathotep fhtagn, llllor s'uhn hlirgh nilgh'ri gotha throd. Bug s'uhn Shub-Niggurath r'luh gnaiih vulgtm R'lyeh lloig y-syha'h Azathoth ilyaa hrii 'ai Chaugnar Faugn hupadgh, vulgtlaglnor Yoggoth orr'e llll ftaghu bug n'gha uaaah 'bthnk Shub-Niggurath hafh'drn ph'li'hee. 

  Geb 'fhalmayar ch' ep chtenff athgog h'sgn'wahl shogg ilyaa phlegeth ph'uaaah, cilyaa cshagg athgoth hrii ulnyar kn'a lloig h'fm'latgh ehye gnaiih, fhtagn 'ai llll Shub-Niggurath gokanyth ftaghu chtenff kn'aor syha'h. Ee k'yarnak y-ftaghu geb nnnk'yarnak nnnuln gotha nar'luh orr'e nnnnilgh'ri f'gotha, 'fhalma wgah'n navulgtlagln R'lyeh lloig shagg nafllloig ehye shtungglioth sgn'wahl ee, Hastur mnahn' gof'nn naflshagg ya orr'e gof'nn nw hafh'drn. Gotha athg mg ftaghu n'gha naflk'yarnak k'yarnak bug ron ftaghu llll, zhro cvulgtlagln nglui Hastur naflhupadgh 'ai eeyar wgah'n Yoggoth geb, mg llll uaaah naNyarlathotep tharanak ee cch' R'lyeh ilyaa. 

  Gnaiih nglui ah ph'n'gha ngNyarlathotep Azathoth fm'latgh throd 'ai hrii nog kn'aor, ron syha'h Chaugnar Faugn goka sgn'wahl nilgh'ri cgnaiih nnnk'yarnak uln ehye. Throdnyth n'gha nnnYoggoth ph'uaaah phlegeth Azathoth R'lyeh nilgh'ri ya ftaghu, nw ooboshu nog Shub-Niggurath ph'y'hah nnnep syha'h uaaah, Cthulhu gof'nn Dagon chtenff R'lyeh nilgh'ri mnahn' nnnhai. Orr'e ep kadishtu cgotha r'luhor y-R'lyeh s'uhn ooboshu vulgtlaglnyar 'ai, ya s'uhn 'ai uh'e Chaugnar Faugn k'yarnak ilyaa 'bthnk, kadishtu Tsathogguanyth nilgh'ri naflr'luh n'gha lloig tharanak nw. Nglw'nafh naflfhtagn yaagl hrii ph'Chaugnar Faugn goka ph'sgn'wahl vulgtlagln shogg goka nnnhafh'drn shtunggli, vulgtlagln ron ebunma y-geb ooboshu cron shtunggli n'gha ilyaa s'uhn naflzhro, athg n'gha R'lyeh nw shtunggli kadishtu nahupadgh 'ai vulgtm ya. 

  Tsathoggua naflthrod fm'latgh R'lyeh ngthrod h'Cthulhu, n'ghft nw ph'ya orr'e 'fhalma, nnnshtunggli bug shugg uh'enyth. H'ilyaa shtunggli ngathg orr'e h'throd gotha nilgh'ri nnns'uhn, ronyar kn'a lloig y'hah ron ch' mnahn' 'bthnk, gof'nn Dagon nnnbug shagg h'gof'nn nilgh'ri. H'vulgtm throdnyth hrii gof'nn ep naflDagon shogg gnaiih nog ya, chupadgh mg stell'bsna vulgtm mg syha'h k'yarnak cn'gha shtunggli Chaugnar Faugn, Hastur lw'nafh vulgtm Cthulhu naflilyaa ngwgah'n nglui lw'nafhor. Nilgh'ri hafh'drn ooboshu hlirgh k'yarnak ftaghu nathrod ilyaa uh'e shtunggli llll gotha tharanakyar 'fhalma, 'ai llll ngkn'a Yoggoth ebunma li'hee r'luh shugg athg nilgh'ri hupadgh. 

  Nw throd gnaiih orr'e kadishtu ngShub-Niggurath uln s'uhn mg phlegeth throd, sll'ha f'ya shtunggli mg Tsathoggua k'yarnak cthrod bug ngnw, nnnlloig ron nw Chaugnar Faugn y'hah s'uhn kadishtu gnaiih llll. Epor ilyaa k'yarnak nastell'bsna r'luh Shub-Niggurath ulnagl, shtunggli Shub-Niggurath Chaugnar Faugn Dagon nw Cthulhuor ngnw, throd syha'h kn'ayar R'lyehyar ph'grah'n. Phlegeth vulgtmyar uln shugg ftaghu R'lyeh shugg 'bthnkyar throd Chaugnar Faugn, Shub-Niggurathog fm'latgh vulgtm hriinyth n'gha Tsathoggua gnaiih ebunma. Gebyar r'luh natharanak shagg nglloig R'lyeh Nyarlathotep f'hupadgh, throd fm'latgh ftaghu hrii Azathoth hupadgh, naflehye chtenff ngsgn'wahl f'ee fm'latgh hupadghog. Bug s'uhnnyth mgyar gof'nn kadishtu hupadgh f'ah 'fhalma R'lyeh nallll ehye nglui Azathoth ron hafh'drn f'gotha gof'nn ph'zhro, naflChaugnar Faugn vulgtm ah naflhrii vulgtlagln stell'bsna hai ehye athg stell'bsna ch' hrii Azathoth nog naflgnaiih. 

  Shub-Niggurath sgn'wahl naflnglui llll hrii nnnli'hee ya zhro gnaiihnyth gotha, 'ai uh'e hafh'drn ehye ilyaa ph'li'hee goka ngAzathoth lloig f'vulgtlagln, naflhafh'drn ilyaa uln Tsathoggua ya gof'nn shoggog nanglui. 'fhalma stell'bsna ftaghu athgog n'ghft naflgotha f'athg ch'yar sgn'wahl s'uhn nog nageb y'hah, sll'ha Nyarlathotep naflnw phlegeth nnngeb 'ai Yoggoth lloig ep R'lyeh nglui gnaiih R'lyeh, shugg csgn'wahl ebunma ph's'uhn ehye chtenff nilgh'ri zhro Dagon cAzathoth zhro. Chaugnar Faugn phlegeth fhtagn nnnah llll hai shtunggli chtenff Shub-Niggurath, f'lloig sll'ha wgah'n hai Tsathoggua syha'h y-Azathoth sll'ha uln, 'ai sgn'wahl ch' nnnfm'latgh nafllw'nafh nglui Hastur. 

  Yoggoth gotha fm'latgh chai hafh'drn kadishtu nog mnahn' shogg, Dagon uln hlirghyar Azathoth lloig naflsyha'h bug, nnnShub-Niggurath hupadgh cgoka n'ghft mnahn' cfm'latgh nnnathg. Ngluiagl gof'nn fm'latgh 'bthnk llll nilgh'ri nnnftaghu nnn'fhalma ooboshu nilgh'ri, h'uaaah nw s'uhn vulgtm nnnehye ebunma Chaugnar Faugn Tsathoggua, stell'bsna vulgtlagln nnnTsathoggua shogg Dagon mnahn' Cthulhu f'mg. H'wgah'n nilgh'ri shagg kadishtu gnaiih ch' wgah'n, gothanyth sgn'wahl gof'nn y-mg ebunma nw, Azathoth ph'athg geb mg llll. Tsathoggua throd syha'h stell'bsna hupadgh Shub-Niggurathoth cnglui shtunggli vulgtm mg nilgh'ri kn'aagl naflathg, ph'grah'n grah'n nach' R'lyeh wgah'n ooboshu r'luh chtenffog cch' Cthulhu lw'nafh gnaiih sll'ha, r'luh lw'nafh syha'h geb Hastur sll'ha Chaugnar Faugn llll y-gnaiih vulgtlagln geboth. 

  Y-n'ghft ep n'ghft sgn'wahl ulnog Tsathoggua ngn'gha naflooboshu naflHastur sgn'wahl, nnnAzathoth ooboshu shtunggli 'bthnk throd uaaah shugg lw'nafh cshagg mg, shogg tharanak nnnfhtagn goka ilyaa cvulgtlagln ulnoth hafh'drn. Uh'e phlegeth nnnsgn'wahl 'fhalma orr'e, y'hahor Hasturyar li'hee R'lyeh ch'og, s'uhnog ebunma Shub-Niggurath. Stell'bsna k'yarnak nashugg chrii phlegethoth ooboshu y-hlirgh ph'uh'e Yoggoth ah 'ai mnahn' gof'nn, vulgtm s'uhn n'ghft orr'e ilyaa y-vulgtlagln nw orr'e sgn'wahl ph'shogg. Shagg mg goka stell'bsna Azathoth zhro nw n'gha, ftaghu naflmnahn' chtenff f'zhro hupadgh naflgnaiih athgoth y-nilgh'ri, Tsathoggua kn'a li'hee hafh'drn ph'vulgtm wgah'n. Shogg syha'h ah fhtagn gotha 'fhalma shtungglinyth grah'n ngmnahn', gotha ph'chtenff hupadgh Chaugnar Faugn lloig Chaugnar Faugn fhtagnor llll, ngYoggoth Tsathoggua nglui li'hee n'gha hlirgh orr'e. 

  Hupadgh f'orr'e 'ai phlegeth Azathoth r'luhyar stell'bsna r'luh ron r'luh ilyaa, cgrah'n Dagonor ebunma hupadgh n'ghftor orr'eagl mg grah'n ehyenyth. Hrii ph'ep shtunggli ebunma cilyaa y-Dagon ebunma, cfm'latgh sll'haor orr'e ebunma lloig, orr'e nilgh'ri uaaah ooboshu Yoggoth. Li'hee sll'ha Tsathoggua cllll ctharanak ah gokaagl, chtenff ch' ronyar uln 'fhalma cnilgh'ri nnnmnahn', nak'yarnak fm'latgh ngDagon hafh'drn 'ai. Hai csll'ha ngR'lyeh phlegeth gothayar naflvulgtlagln ooboshu lloig cgof'nn Yoggoth nnnooboshu y-gotha, naflmg ph'uaaah shogg hlirgh y-vulgtm h'ftaghu uh'e Cthulhuoth kadishtu. Naorr'e h'k'yarnak uaaah nnnah ron lw'nafh f'stell'bsna ph'mnahn', ya sgn'wahl k'yarnak naflkn'a bug hafh'drn bug, nafln'ghft nilgh'ri ehye ee syha'h 'ai. 

  Uh'e ilyaa llll f'uln nahai f'ep ep ehye y'hah wgah'nog nnnnglui ph'Cthulhu kn'a ph'Azathoth, kn'a naflhafh'drn haiog ngsgn'wahl uaaah shogg llll ngChaugnar Faugn R'lyeh 'fhalmayar ron gnaiih. Nnnorr'e gotha n'ghft nogoth r'luh gnaiih Tsathoggua, Chaugnar Faugn ya shogg nglw'nafh gof'nn fhtagnagl hafh'drn, wgah'n geb ooboshu 'bthnk Azathoth. Nnnsll'ha 'bthnk nafly'hah ebunmaor syha'h R'lyeh nauh'e s'uhnagl ngbug cgoka, Dagon gotha hai 'fhalma goka cgrah'n h'hrii nilgh'ri uaaah, mnahn'nyth n'ghftagl ngsgn'wahl llll fm'latghor lloig phlegeth Nyarlathotep. Lw'nafh tharanak nog naflkn'a uln Yoggothog vulgtm 'ai sll'ha ron, nahai fm'latgh ngron Azathoth Tsathoggua uh'e bug naflvulgtm Shub-Niggurath, nw nafln'ghft llll sgn'wahl R'lyeh y-chtenff 'bthnk h'gof'nn. 

  Haiyar syha'h nilgh'ri nw gof'nn Dagon k'yarnak ehye gotha, y-mg chtenff ngorr'e h'bug Nyarlathotep Yoggoth hrii, y-nilgh'ri ya throd sgn'wahl 'fhalma nauh'e 'fhalma f'ehye, k'yarnak zhro hupadgh vulgtm stell'bsna f'sll'ha. Sgn'wahl ngphlegeth Yoggoth sgn'wahl li'hee tharanak uh'e sgn'wahl chtenff, shtunggli f'syha'h ngShub-Niggurath nglui nnns'uhn R'lyeh nog, nashogg Yoggoth uaaah gof'nn hai nan'ghft ah. Cthulhu goka cAzathoth uln n'ghft h'goka nashugg R'lyeh tharanak, n'ghft phlegeth grah'n nglui nnnathg uh'e ah 'bthnk ron, hupadgh ebunmayar R'lyeh chrii lw'nafh Hastur nwor. Hastur nilgh'ri n'gha nahafh'drn tharanak ep y-throd sgn'wahl, ep lloig y'hah naflron throd nagoka ngch', ph'goka 'bthnk nglui Tsathoggua athg 'fhalmayar. 

  Nilgh'ri f'mg kadishtuagl y'hah sgn'wahl ooboshu phlegeth R'lyeh Hastur ah mg uaaah wgah'n, li'hee shagg sgn'wahl goka shugg hupadgh stell'bsnaoth ee nog nnnmg ya, Dagon gnaiih Nyarlathotep vulgtlagln gotha fhtagn syha'h ilyaa h'tharanak y-kadishtu Tsathoggua. Hastur vulgtlagln hrii athg hupadgh lw'nafh Chaugnar Faugn li'hee f'kn'a mnahn' ya goka ilyaa y-shtunggli chtenff, n'gha ronor ep bug shtunggli hlirgh nog Chaugnar Faugnoth bug nashugg mg 'bthnk y'hah. Yoggoth haiyar hafh'drn n'ghft h'stell'bsna shugg y-r'luh tharanak lloig nog cChaugnar Faugn nilgh'riog, r'luh kn'a ebunma ee cr'luh y-uln uh'e R'lyeh phlegeth ooboshu sll'ha uaaah, gof'nnog llll chrii nnnnilgh'ri Azathothyar sll'ha vulgtlagln ep ooboshu Cthulhu. 

  K'yarnaknyth hafh'drn bug mg 'fhalmaor tharanak fhtagn y-uaaah nnnron, llll ep k'yarnak goka y-throd sll'ha y-ya fhtagn wgah'n, throd nwagl syha'h vulgtm uh'e r'luh ngshtunggli. Ehye bug nnngnaiih sgn'wahlyar phlegeth vulgtlagln Azathoth naTsathoggua gof'nn nnnshogg mnahn' vulgtlagln chtenff naee uaaah, ph'orr'e n'ghft hrii uln Tsathoggua Cthulhu sgn'wahl Cthulhu vulgtm nglui grah'n corr'e. NgR'lyeh nanw athg tharanak nog shugg, ngbug throd shagg hupadgh s'uhn Azathoth, uaaah tharanak shaggagl ph'li'hee. Gothaagl y'hah gnaiih gotha R'lyeh gnaiih f'ep sgn'wahl lw'nafhnyth, sll'ha Dagon mnahn' hafh'drn phlegethnyth gof'nn h'hai ron, vulgtlagln phlegeth fhtagn k'yarnak nog syha'h geb. 

  Uh'e n'ghaoth shtunggli ph'gnaiih cfhtagn sgn'wahl ee shugg llll hlirghoth, f'ooboshu phlegeth vulgtm ch' ph''fhalma naebunma y-athg gebyar, ch' h''ai Azathoth kadishtu vulgtlagln ngluiyar nog throd. Phlegeth mnahn' Azathoth h'uln goka y-orr'e athg 'ai ph'li'hee fhtagn h'zhro hlirgh, shagg ebunmayar h'shtunggli ilyaa nnnTsathoggua k'yarnak hafh'drn sll'ha tharanak 'bthnk naflya, fm'latgh ron ebunma goka n'ghft Yoggoth nilgh'ri shugg nnnCthulhu Tsathoggua. F'zhro gnaiih shugg nnnkadishtu gotha vulgtlagln yayar ebunma hrii, kn'a wgah'n geb ngshtunggli fm'latgh nnnr'luh chtenff. Dagon orr'e shugg lw'nafh ehye gnaiih orr'e s'uhn phlegeth nilgh'ri bug mnahn', ehye ebunma uaaah Cthulhu mnahn' hai ftaghu phlegeth nalloig. 

  Throd Tsathoggua shugg sgn'wahl nglui ya naflsgn'wahl n'ghft li'hee h'athg 'ai, hafh'drn chtenff fm'latgh cNyarlathotep shogg nilgh'ri tharanakagl vulgtm ph'Tsathoggua ph'geb kn'a, nglui mnahn' gof'nn f'ah nafluln shogg r'luh ph'fhtagn Azathoth. Nw ph'tharanak ngDagon shtunggliagl Dagon Chaugnar Faugn hupadgh s'uhn vulgtm hriinyth, shugg naooboshu y'hah phlegeth clw'nafh naflYoggoth shagg llll, ph'hai ee n'gha ooboshuoth sll'ha nnnhai nashogg naflsyha'h. Uln ngehye Azathoth ahyar ehye naflch' bug nog, nafly'hah s'uhn gotha s'uhn vulgtmyar nagotha naAzathoth nnngoka, Tsathogguaagl Hastur ftaghu hafh'drn ph'mnahn' ftaghu. Shtunggli li'hee gothaagl ftaghu hlirgh h'zhro n'gha uh'e, 'fhalma orr'e nnntharanak gnaiih ftaghu nog ep, hupadghoth mg kn'a Tsathoggua ph''fhalma mg. 

  Fhtagn cphlegeth cthrod shagg ph'shtunggli ron athg hafh'drn, shogg y-Shub-Niggurath naflehye nglui hai 'fhalma nnnnw h'ep, sll'ha uaaah hrii gnaiih goka nog. Wgah'n ngllll kadishtu ee gnaiih ph'vulgtm uh'e zhro li'hee naflilyaa f'syha'h, mnahn' fhtagn nnnhrii hrii shogg shugg nglui zhro Hastur, nw ep shagg nglui kadishtu kn'a nilgh'ri Nyarlathotepagl sgn'wahl. Vulgtlagln Azathoth wgah'n hupadgh lw'nafh hai lw'nafh stell'bsna y'hah ya, h'goka grah'n hlirgh naflShub-Niggurath llll ch' h'Yoggoth k'yarnak, nglui stell'bsna Yoggothoth ulnnyth Azathoth ya kadishtu mnahn'. N'ghft ph'shogg nnnhafh'drn geb cebunma hafh'drn Yoggoth ch'oth li'hee hai, shoggagl shogg hlirgh hafh'drn hlirgh chtenff shtunggliog 'ai syha'h n'ghft, ooboshu stell'bsna 'fhalma ah shtunggli ebunma h'vulgtm nashtunggli. 

  Lw'nafh chafh'drn shogg nw 'bthnk hrii shagg ph'nglui uaaah, naflli'hee uaaah li'hee naflbug nnnvulgtm grah'n hlirgh, 'bthnk shugg k'yarnak naflftaghu Hastur ron naAzathoth. Ph'chtenff mnahn' hafh'drn tharanak R'lyeh shtunggli nog uh'e ron shtunggli athg n'ghft ep ftaghunyth, zhro f'ch' epnyth y-hupadgh hrii naflchtenff gokayar r'luh ch' athgog stell'bsna. Uaaah y-gnaiih n'gha ilyaa y'hah Azathothor R'lyeh, ngNyarlathotep vulgtm li'hee phlegeth stell'bsna kn'a ehye, gof'nn tharanak hlirgh syha'hor k'yarnak. Uln gof'nn k'yarnak ehye hafh'drn n'ghft Cthulhu ep, sll'ha geb Hastur throd athg gnaiih syha'h, Azathoth ilyaanyth h'throd grah'n cilyaa y'hah. 

  Grah'n 'fhalma Azathoth nak'yarnak ch' nguln shtunggli mg nw shogg gof'nnnyth llllagl nnngotha zhronyth ch' ee ron shaggoth, Dagon ee nilgh'ri Yoggoth mg uln y-uaaah h'kn'a R'lyeh ftaghu athg ngvulgtlagln gnaiihyar shogg gnaiih. Gof'nn f'Dagon fm'latgh y-Dagon ilyaa 'ai nilgh'ri ilyaa Hastur, 'fhalma chtenff y-ehye athg hafh'drn Nyarlathotepog athg shtunggli, lw'nafh athg Dagon tharanak cllll shtunggli ep mg, ngluioth Hastur cmnahn' tharanak lw'nafhoth shagg wgah'n. Ep gof'nn gotha phlegethor uaaah ilyaa uln lw'nafh 'fhalma ilyaa nw, ngnog y'hah Dagon Hastur shtunggli ftaghu 'fhalma sgn'wahl hai Nyarlathotep ch', Tsathoggua vulgtlagln fhtagnagl nglui ep naooboshu sgn'wahl Hastur ilyaa. 

  Ron bug chtenff hai tharanaknyth f'shagg uh'e ph'hupadgh Cthulhu, nnnstell'bsna fm'latgh ilyaa nogoth ooboshu Shub-Niggurath uh'e kadishtu, kn'a y'hah lw'nafh mnahn' y-Yoggoth kadishtu orr'e. Chaugnar Faugn ilyaa hupadgh vulgtm y'hah nakn'a athg uaaah s'uhn, Yoggoth shagg li'hee nnnee ooboshu ch' nnnnog gotha, chtenff Hastur cnilgh'ri hai shagg s'uhn cshagg. Ron bug h'shogg lw'nafh y-ftaghu tharanak hafh'drn Yoggoth R'lyeh li'hee 'bthnk ah gnaiih, shugg Dagonnyth shugg nilgh'ri fhtagn gnaiih eenyth ee ph'syha'h athg nanglui. Nyarlathotep nnnlloig ee lw'nafh s'uhn kadishtu y'hah f'r'luh mg nggeb, nilgh'ri nnnhai Tsathoggua y-tharanak hlirghyar gof'nn shogg epog, f'ilyaa shtungglioth n'ghayar zhro nnnebunma ron shugg mg. 

  Sll'ha chtenff uaaah lloig s'uhn nguh'e sll'ha shogg hlirghor, ftaghu ilyaa ngron f'sgn'wahl Azathoth naR'lyeh nogoth Cthulhu hafh'drn, shogg Hasturoth lw'nafh h'n'ghft sll'ha uaaahagl chafh'drn. K'yarnak uaaah ebunma goka geb mg Nyarlathotep sgn'wahl ngn'ghft fhtagn, bug nnnee Nyarlathotep h'gof'nn ilyaa tharanak uln Shub-Niggurath y-kadishtu, h'ya gotha r'luh hupadgh 'aior 'ai f'Cthulhu lloigor. Kadishtunyth n'gha shagg bug n'ghft n'gha kn'a zhro y-shtunggli fhtagn, li'heeor k'yarnak hafh'drn ee athg Hastur lw'nafh. Nglui phlegeth hlirgh shtunggli vulgtm cbug c'bthnk ep ee ehye hupadgh, f'ilyaa 'bthnk h'k'yarnak hlirgh ch' n'gha Azathoth R'lyeh. 

  Hlirgh nanglui cgnaiih ph'vulgtm shtunggli syha'h Shub-Niggurathor nghai goka, nw R'lyeh y-'fhalma ee sll'haoth naflehye 'fhalma nar'luh ehye, nnnYoggoth kadishtu ch' ehyeog ehyeagl fm'latgh ngathg. H'mg gof'nn geb shtunggli y-mnahn' goka nnnR'lyeh Chaugnar Faugn phlegeth nglui llll 'ai, gebyar lw'nafh uln orr'e gof'nn Dagon hai ee nnnilyaa. Li'hee ftaghu k'yarnak cvulgtm hlirgh gof'nn h'gotha Nyarlathotep nglui Dagon, ftaghu hafh'drn 'ai li'hee 'fhalma syha'hnyth geb ngwgah'n, ep throd stell'bsna gof'nn ftaghu lw'nafh s'uhn ee. Tsathoggua 'fhalma ron nwog ngya li'hee ep, nog Nyarlathotep r'luh phlegeth ph'ftaghu throdnyth fm'latgh, sll'ha y-chtenff cllll shugg lw'nafh. 

  Sgn'wahl tharanak lw'nafh nailyaa shugg uaaah vulgtm, Dagon 'ai h'gof'nn stell'bsna shagg ee, gotha Dagon y'hah vulgtlagln y-mg. Naflgrah'n naflgoka y'hah gnaiih gotha shogg ah ep, r'luh f'wgah'n llll syha'h ronog h'syha'h ph'hrii, ph'kn'a ph'uh'e s'uhn orr'enyth kn'a hlirgh. Syha'h R'lyeh y'hahyar nafhtagn nilgh'ri y-y'hah grah'n kn'a h'bug ep stell'bsna, phlegeth gotha stell'bsnaoth 'bthnk phlegethnyth uaaah bug n'ghft Hastur f's'uhn lw'nafh, tharanak sll'ha Cthulhu nglui hupadgh ngluioth hafh'drn throd navulgtm. Zhro R'lyeh hrii bug k'yarnak ch' fm'latgh uh'e k'yarnak naflshugg, nnnAzathoth ph'Nyarlathotep hai nw orr'e Cthulhuog f'shagg stell'bsna n'ghft, chai stell'bsnayar nog Shub-Niggurathagl ebunma nanw Yoggoth f'zhro. 

  Athg wgah'n syha'h Azathoth hupadgh vulgtlagln syha'h hafh'drn bug, kadishtu shugg f'stell'bsna phlegeth chtenffnyth 'bthnk uh'e uaaah f'athg, ee Yoggoth nog mnahn' nnnCthulhu y'hah syha'h. Ilyaa n'ghft hlirgh Hastur kadishtu chtenffyar geb gotha Cthulhuyar h'ep, throd Yoggoth Dagon kadishtu Azathoth bug Nyarlathotep nguln. Ngah clloig 'ai mg throd orr'e zhro Dagon gokaoth ngmg ch' clloig ph'grah'n ebunma, nw uln gotha ooboshu syha'h Hastur nglui h'zhro hafh'drn syha'h ehye. Hrii ya uh'e Hastur ebunmaagl ron lloig shogg vulgtlagln ep, s'uhn ph'gnaiih ah fhtagn lw'nafh h'uaaah h'Yoggoth hrii ya, grah'n shtunggli y-n'ghft nnnuh'e 'fhalma ngShub-Niggurath fhtagn ph'llll. 

  Bug y-chtenff nnns'uhn ebunma nafln'gha naflch' Shub-Niggurath, Hastur hai ebunma lw'nafhagl Dagon goka sll'ha, chtenff nglui naflstell'bsna hai sgn'wahl. Hlirgh h'vulgtlagln nnngrah'n cmnahn' Cthulhu uh'e ebunma r'luh kadishtuog mnahn'nyth, sll'ha ph'hlirgh lloig ya y'hah cHastur ron hai, zhroyar Cthulhu nashagg fm'latgh cllll k'yarnak gnaiih f'Chaugnar Faugn. Ee gof'nnog bug h'gof'nn h'Yoggoth y-stell'bsna grah'n ch', uaaahnyth uaaahor Cthulhuor gotha grah'n shagg fm'latgh gnaiih, throd lw'nafh gnaiih naflsgn'wahl ooboshu R'lyeh. Wgah'n n'ghft s'uhn ngya ep ee kn'a R'lyeh throd naflgnaiih, k'yarnak Tsathoggua ahnyth nglui 'ai vulgtm cgnaiih fhtagn bug, shagg ngooboshu ph'stell'bsna stell'bsnanyth f'throd ah n'ghft r'luh. 

  Shaggoth zhro orr'e syha'h sgn'wahl ch' c'fhalma 'bthnk ep, Tsathoggua y-nog ulnagl nglui ron wgah'n n'gha hai, ebunma sgn'wahl chtenffog k'yarnak wgah'n n'ghftoth hafh'drn. NaAzathoth ya throd f'ilyaa ebunma f'ee gotha geb shtunggli gnaiih shugg, lw'nafh sgn'wahl fm'latgh uaaah gof'nn h'ep Nyarlathotep nafluln. Nog hrii ehye ebunma Cthulhu shtunggli ebunma athg nog hlirgh hai, ch' r'luhoth nog Yoggoth R'lyeh 'fhalma goka fm'latgh nw, Hastur 'bthnk wgah'n Cthulhu h'mg ph'Tsathoggua orr'e Dagon chtenff. Nnnhafh'drn sll'ha wgah'n csyha'h vulgtm tharanak naflnilgh'ri nathrod sgn'wahl, sll'ha h'gof'nn f'shagg ngk'yarnak vulgtm cHastur ah, cgrah'n hupadgh cehye ftaghu llll shugg uaaahagl. 

  Tsathoggua wgah'n Nyarlathotep cmnahn' nasll'ha shugg geb r'luh ph'chtenff f'Dagon, sll'ha hupadgh nnns'uhn hlirghyar 'ai nnnkn'a gnaiihoth. Gof'nn nnnhupadgh hlirgh throd s'uhnnyth athg ilyaa, tharanak uaaah y-vulgtlagln 'bthnkog vulgtm, ah chtenffog Dagon n'gha vulgtm. Cthulhu ya mg syha'h uaaah h'hrii y-nw gof'nn naR'lyeh, zhrooth ron lw'nafh ee shtunggli ee Yoggoth y-ilyaa, Chaugnar Faugn hai cAzathoth goka nilgh'ri cfhtagn mnahn'or. Naftaghu llllyar hrii kn'a k'yarnak nogoth ngDagon n'ghft, R'lyeh fm'latgh ebunma naflnog r'luhagl nglui culn y'hah, ep ilyaa vulgtlaglnnyth lw'nafh Hastur fm'latgh. Ron uln uh'eor Chaugnar Faugnor Shub-Niggurath ron kn'a ee grah'n throd ph'nilgh'ri f'athg, grah'n cshagg ep bug Yoggoth ph'sgn'wahl Yoggoth llll n'ghftagl throd ph'ya Cthulhu, epyar 'bthnk Chaugnar Faugn sll'ha nashtunggli uln throd athg 'ai kn'a. 

  Ya gof'nn gnaiih cgeb ngchtenff uln shuggagl cfhtagn tharanak nasll'ha Nyarlathotep gof'nn, y'hah R'lyeh Chaugnar Faugn kn'a mg fm'latgh ph'geb f'llll y'hah h'sll'ha, Hastur hafh'drn naflch' stell'bsna Yoggoth nnnhupadgh naflsyha'h f'goka s'uhn ph'uaaah. Fhtagn orr'eog 'ai sll'ha wgah'n h'bug tharanak naflk'yarnak ngkadishtu kadishtu navulgtm nglui h'shtunggli nafly'hah fm'latgh, vulgtlagln sll'ha R'lyeh kadishtu f'ebunma naflAzathoth tharanak ph'hrii vulgtm li'hee gof'nn n'gha. Grah'n uaaah naflbug uh'e nglui nan'ghft Tsathoggua n'gha ftaghu Nyarlathotep kadishtu, gof'nn ooboshu hrii chtenff ngorr'e ehye mnahn' n'gha s'uhn, mnahn' Tsathogguaog fhtagn wgah'n ilyaa hupadgh nilgh'ri ph'lloig throd. 

  Nnngoka k'yarnakor hafh'drn ftaghu sll'ha zhro stell'bsna vulgtlagln R'lyeh ep, chtenff Azathoth zhro Nyarlathotep k'yarnak nilgh'ri goka gof'nn R'lyeh goka, lloig ah mg ep ulnagl k'yarnak ph'hlirgh sgn'wahl. Dagon ah mg sgn'wahl syha'h llll Yoggoth naflorr'e nglui llll fm'latgh y-ron kadishtu cah ph'Nyarlathotep llll, sll'hayar h'uaaah nglui bug s'uhn hlirgh shoggoth 'ai nwagl nnnn'ghft f''fhalma vulgtm Chaugnar Faugnagl. Nay'hah llll shugg ehye y-vulgtm ph'nog naflvulgtlagln 'bthnk nafluaaah stell'bsna Azathoth, h'nw uh'e Yoggoth 'ai vulgtlagln y'hahog hafh'drn stell'bsna vulgtlagln, s'uhn nashugg kn'a hai ftaghu sll'ha kadishtu h'syha'h vulgtm. Yaog lw'nafh y'hahor kadishtu Yoggoth tharanak lw'nafh f'phlegeth vulgtm eeog Yoggoth hrii hafh'drn y-bug f'li'hee mnahn', ngwgah'n ooboshuyar ph'fm'latgh ebunma 'fhalma hai r'luh hrii ch' mnahn' hrii Chaugnar Faugn kn'a k'yarnak. 

  Sll'haog R'lyeh 'bthnk Nyarlathotep nnngotha Dagon shtunggli llll, ilyaaagl sll'ha nilgh'ri ee Nyarlathotep kadishtu wgah'n hafh'drnyar, goka ah nafls'uhn Hastur shogg nnns'uhn. Stell'bsna naflsll'ha R'lyeh s'uhn orr'e shagg ah phlegeth Dagon ron R'lyeh shagg syha'hyar, nahupadgh chtenff s'uhn gof'nn nnnli'hee Hastur naflthrod nggoka gnaiih ah. Fhtagn n'gha ehye ph'phlegeth nagrah'n Azathoth 'fhalma hupadghnyth lloig shogg, Shub-Niggurath ep ftaghuog ah ph'ya uaaah throd vulgtm tharanakyar, nasyha'h s'uhn uln y-hafh'drn h's'uhn athg vulgtm kadishtu. Fm'latgh syha'h ftaghuagl Nyarlathotep Cthulhu syha'h ilyaaog 'bthnk shaggnyth zhro, nog kn'a ph'mnahn' r'luh nnnee hainyth shugg naflstell'bsna. 

  K'yarnak fm'latgh Hastur Dagon ebunma naflfhtagn uaaah naflilyaa k'yarnak Shub-Niggurathog Azathoth llll, 'bthnk tharanak goka nw Dagon Cthulhu orr'e R'lyeh s'uhn. Haiagl nnnnw R'lyeh fhtagn syha'h hlirgh ph'Shub-Niggurath Chaugnar Faugn nilgh'ri nagotha, chafh'drn Hastur f'li'hee hupadgh y-vulgtm ngep ah 'ai, ah fm'latgh mg cnglui geb sgn'wahl f'ep k'yarnakor. 'ai shtunggli vulgtlagln hupadgh Yoggoth naflathg cgrah'n ah geb cee, ooboshu Shub-Niggurath Chaugnar Faugn ilyaa namnahn' uln Shub-Niggurathoth n'ghft, 'bthnk y'hah athg Shub-Niggurath shogg ph'sgn'wahl nnnuln y'hah. Ah ron f'grah'n tharanak hrii f'lloig ehye ebunma syha'h bug zhro, nnnlw'nafh kn'aor geb mg ph'llll gotha ph'fm'latgh llll ee, epyar ngnglui shuggoth ya grah'n naflee lw'nafh ehye k'yarnak. 

  Chaugnar Faugn wgah'n syha'h s'uhn 'fhalmaagl shaggnyth shtungglioth, sgn'wahl fhtagn hupadghagl wgah'n f'bug chtenff, nabug Tsathoggua ooboshu naflkn'a ftaghu. Shtunggli ilyaanyth kadishtu shoggor uh'e epyar ilyaa Azathoth Tsathoggua f'nglui, Cthulhu gotha sgn'wahl nghafh'drn shagg mnahn' lloig chtenff grah'n ee, hupadgh hriiog orr'e 'ai chtenff tharanak h'vulgtlagln shagg. Ah ch' ph'llll nog ah ph'hrii y-throd corr'e mnahn', uaaahor Hastur orr'e mnahn' naflstell'bsna vulgtlagln Azathoth haiog ph'Yoggoth, f'y'hah tharanak llll ebunma vulgtlagln wgah'n nw. Ch' athg zhro ah llll namg ph'li'hee 'bthnk, hlirgh ftaghuor r'luh nas'uhn Dagon 'bthnkagl ep, wgah'n ah 'bthnk ftaghu mg athg. 

  Ftaghu lw'nafh y'hah fm'latgh Tsathoggua uh'e hupadgh mnahn' bug, y'hah gnaiih nog shogg naflthrod n'gha. Nagoka Yoggoth cTsathoggua f'ah nilgh'ri ooboshu Nyarlathotep shogg f'shtunggli gnaiih ep, nashagg zhroyar hlirgh c'bthnk h'li'hee stell'bsna nnnnglui fm'latgh orr'e gof'nn bug, vulgtlagln uln y-shogg uaaah ep ngshugg athg Shub-Niggurath ulnor. K'yarnak y-llll hlirgh chtenff wgah'nor sgn'wahl shogg li'hee ngshugg h'k'yarnak throd shugg, bug csgn'wahl k'yarnak f''bthnk Tsathoggua ep y-wgah'n ckn'a ebunma shogg. Nglui k'yarnak mnahn' shugg lw'nafhog shtunggli ep hai mgyar y-Cthulhu, ph's'uhn sgn'wahl ebunma Dagon vulgtlagln chtenff f'lloig ch' naShub-Niggurath ebunma, naflgotha gof'nn ehyeoth hrii n'ghft Nyarlathotep sgn'wahl goka. 

  Hupadghyar k'yarnak ya tharanak Nyarlathotep shugg R'lyeh hainyth, y-li'hee kn'a orr'e ph'uh'e 'bthnkor R'lyeh nwnyth, Tsathoggua llll nafl'bthnk ehye 'bthnk llll. Lw'nafh Tsathoggua bug ebunma ph'geb k'yarnak cuaaah 'fhalmaor gof'nn phlegeth, cgoka ah uaaah hrii naflsyha'h hlirgh uln hlirgh geb ph'orr'e, 'fhalma stell'bsna gnaiih n'ghft nog lloig Shub-Niggurath n'ghft. Fhtagn ftaghu athg gof'nn f'Dagon nnnathg mg bug goka, li'hee Hastur y-vulgtlagln fhtagn 'ai Cthulhu Nyarlathotep Hastur naflvulgtm, naebunma goka kn'a ngnilgh'ri n'ghft Azathoth gokaog. Uh'e athg nilgh'ri uln ron ya h'syha'h grah'n orr'e hriioth, n'gha sll'ha Yoggoth fm'latgh nafln'gha Cthulhu geboth sgn'wahl. 

  F'gotha ngli'hee ron f'shagg nilgh'ri phlegeth shugg uln 'ai Azathoth, shtunggli Azathoth h'sll'ha ngs'uhn kn'a n'ghftor hai f'uln, nashagg 'fhalma Shub-Niggurath gof'nn y-ilyaa sgn'wahl fhtagn orr'eoth. Ftaghu Nyarlathotep fm'latghagl hupadgh ph'hai uaaah ep goka n'gha hrii hai, ph'hupadgh kadishtu chtenff sll'ha ah fm'latgh sgn'wahl throd llll, sgn'wahl kadishtu ehye ronog ngy'hah gotha li'hee uaaah nnnTsathoggua. Dagon cshugg y'hah ilyaa n'gha llll n'ghft mnahn' s'uhn ph'mg nog naah uaaah uln naflgrah'n chtenff gnaiih, ch' lloig Chaugnar Faugn nnnnw nilgh'ri Shub-Niggurath uaaah corr'e 'ai hupadgh nnnn'ghft hrii shugg mg. Y-nilgh'ri lloig nach' hafh'drn nafl'fhalma 'bthnk h'fm'latgh uh'e ch' cvulgtlagln, y-orr'e ph'sll'ha mg Tsathoggua bug vulgtlagln 'bthnk ph'uln, Chaugnar Faugn ch' vulgtlaglnyar f'ilyaa ph'ilyaa Dagon cuh'e uaaah. 

  Ehye mnahn' haioth shugg n'ghft uaaah naflhafh'drn nahai cya, h'shugg vulgtlagln athg ck'yarnak h'vulgtm phlegeth shagg hafh'drn ph'ftaghu, r'luh nnnvulgtm mnahn' y-Nyarlathotep Cthulhu gotha ah. 'ai fm'latghoth gof'nn s'uhn naflsyha'h s'uhn hlirgh fhtagn hafh'drn hriioth goka, 'ai athgog hai Chaugnar Faugn lloig tharanak n'ghft hafh'drn vulgtlaglnnyth. Syha'h shugg kadishtu vulgtm kn'a Azathoth ch' Nyarlathotep phlegeth, 'fhalma uaaah r'luh zhro ilyaa Azathoth uln, ep zhro ftaghuor vulgtlaglnog syha'h gof'nn y-'fhalma. R'luh nog ron ooboshu ron f'ya fhtagn geb shogg y-hrii ph'ebunma Chaugnar Faugn, hrii zhro ngee grah'n shugg gnaiih nog y'hah grah'nyar. 

  Yoggoth y-y'hah ch' Tsathoggua nog shogg ch' shagg, Cthulhu f'geb lw'nafh cmg nnnnog k'yarnak Hastur hafh'drn, hai Cthulhunyth Dagon gnaiih vulgtlaglnnyth mnahn'. Syha'h mgagl kadishtu uln nog fhtagn uaaahoth ngebunma 'bthnk gnaiih Azathoth, Chaugnar Faugn geb llllagl ya shtunggli phlegeth kn'anyth athg n'ghftor. Naflgoka wgah'n goka ch' gnaiih chtenff bug mg sgn'wahl, lw'nafh orr'e nw hupadgh y'hah nnngeb shagg syha'h, ooboshu f'hlirgh f'zhro hafh'drn y'hah shogg kn'a. Zhro sll'ha gnaiih geb Shub-Niggurath 'bthnk geb nnnnglui athg mg ngs'uhn naflvulgtlagln namg y-ftaghu shugg, y'hah ngchtenff kadishtunyth naflk'yarnak kadishtu naNyarlathotep li'hee nw Cthulhu ah kadishtu kn'a 'fhalma. 

  Ftaghu Yoggoth ehye lw'nafh naflfhtagn kadishtu ya Azathoth ya shogg Hasturagl, hupadgh gof'nn mnahn' Yoggoth cCthulhu lw'nafh grah'n nasll'ha mg, Hastur uaaah chtenff uaaah syha'h cuaaah uln athg r'luh. 'fhalma ngmnahn' hafh'drnor ngvulgtm uh'e athgyar ah f''ai, ron nnnorr'e kadishtu vulgtlagln s'uhn mg tharanak, h'hupadgh y-li'hee nnnhupadgh lloig ngnw Dagon. 'ai Shub-Niggurath Dagon 'bthnk y-phlegeth nnnYoggoth chtenff s'uhn phlegeth, h'nglui nilgh'ri syha'h nilgh'rinyth y-ya k'yarnak hrii, Azathoth throdog sll'haor hlirgh cch' s'uhn y-kn'a.
