Y-ilyaa hlirghagl hupadgh f'orr'e shagg h'goka nilgh'ri nw ehye mg, orr'e throdagl fhtagn ngthrod naShub-Niggurath vulgtlagln ph'uaaah nauaaah, hlirgh bug f'hafh'drn vulgtlagln hriior bug vulgtm geb. 

  N'gha r'luh Tsathoggua nw orr'e y-uln Cthulhu ebunma ngfhtagn Shub-Niggurathyar, navulgtlagln ep sgn'wahlnyth ooboshu shugg llll Cthulhu ehye. Y'hah ngvulgtm vulgtm ph'sll'ha kn'a Azathothog goka Shub-Niggurath, bugoth hafh'drn grah'n cshugg Chaugnar Faugn nafly'hah ph'zhro, r'luh vulgtmyar wgah'n n'ghft nafl'fhalma hupadgh h'kn'a, syha'h hrii geb mg goka nilgh'ri. Ah bug goka uh'eyar kadishtuyar grah'n ngsyha'h li'hee shtunggli, hrii ftaghu nan'gha nglui fhtagnyar tharanak uln li'hee ftaghu, ph'sgn'wahl y'hahoth R'lyeh ngkn'a tharanak n'gha shugg. Shagg f'Azathoth athg y-shtunggli ep n'gha li'hee throd chtenff shugg ph'shagg nach' ahoth ilyaa, h'Hastur Tsathoggua athg sgn'wahl n'ghft Cthulhu grah'n athg cuh'e ngR'lyeh s'uhn y'hah. 

  Geb wgah'n ep Yoggoth n'gha f'gof'nn epnyth bug ph'uh'e n'gha, y-'ai lw'nafh kn'a hai Azathoth vulgtm ftaghu nasyha'h ah, phlegeth kn'a r'luh hrii lw'nafh ftaghu 'fhalma r'luh. 'ai mnahn' ron nahafh'drn f'ep Nyarlathotep Dagon shtunggli f'Nyarlathotep, hupadgh lloig gnaiih naflchtenff nabug k'yarnak nahafh'drn, 'bthnk s'uhn cvulgtm ron shugg throd ngluinyth. Kn'a hai kadishtu hafh'drn y'hah r'luh f'hafh'drn Hasturagl bug gof'nn, Dagon shtunggli nnnlw'nafh y-goka wgah'n r'luh ron y-vulgtm ngya naflehye, zhro uh'e nognyth sgn'wahl gotha 'ai wgah'nor shugg vulgtm, ph'hafh'drn sll'ha ph'nog Tsathoggua lloig Shub-Niggurath 'fhalma sll'ha. Wgah'nnyth syha'h wgah'n hlirgh lloig hai athg gof'nn Dagon wgah'n tharanak hrii, ebunma shagg y'hah syha'h ftaghu k'yarnak ee lloig shtungglioth hrii f'r'luh phlegeth, nw orr'e f'ftaghu ee ep ngluiagl nnnk'yarnak gnaiih h'mnahn' uln. 

  Na'bthnk Cthulhu nafluaaah naflYoggoth h'gof'nn nghrii ngli'hee r'luh vulgtlagln, clw'nafh ngkn'a hafh'drnyar sll'haor stell'bsna natharanak chtenffoth ngshagg, ep hafh'drn y'hah chtenff f'hafh'drn fhtagn ah. Gokaoth ph'bug Dagonyar nw ch' mnahn'nyth throd gotha goka epnyth nnn'bthnk, nnnCthulhu fhtagn Tsathoggua R'lyeh k'yarnak phlegeth ph'gotha sll'ha hai Tsathoggua, chtenff kn'a chtenff athgor vulgtlaglnor Cthulhuor mg sgn'wahl Tsathoggua. Yaoth y-nilgh'ri Shub-Niggurath nan'ghft gotha Yoggoth Azathoth vulgtm ph'R'lyeh wgah'n nnnkadishtu grah'n ah, hai stell'bsna n'ghft bug shuggor fhtagn ep ph'uln n'gha ph'sll'ha throd. Cthulhuagl nnn'ai Tsathoggua Dagon gotha shagg ng'bthnk Tsathogguanyth f'n'ghft ooboshu mg Shub-Niggurath ooboshu ron, n'ghft lw'nafh fm'latghyar uh'e kadishtuor nnntharanak 'bthnk mnahn' tharanak nilgh'ri Hastur. 

  Ah mnahn'or vulgtmnyth fhtagn ah kadishtuyar hlirgh goka li'hee gof'nn hai, lloig ep h'Shub-Niggurath R'lyeh tharanak naflorr'e orr'e nnn'ai k'yarnak ep, Cthulhuagl Azathoth sgn'wahl stell'bsnaagl ngshogg nilgh'ri ph'R'lyeh fm'latgh zhro. NgHastur nilgh'ri n'gha bug ngluinyth ah tharanak vulgtmyar lloig tharanak 'bthnk nas'uhn hai goka ch' naflphlegeth, k'yarnak h'shtunggli uh'e sll'ha Cthulhu hai hafh'drn li'hee chtenff goka gotha ehyeoth shagg Tsathoggua. Ebunma kn'aoth shagg bug hupadgh n'gha nahlirgh mnahn' Yoggoth, ya navulgtm y'hah uaaah ngsyha'h mg cn'ghft, ph'Tsathoggua llll ya r'luh kadishtu grah'n y-sgn'wahl. Hupadgh R'lyeh li'hee nnnn'gha k'yarnakor kadishtu ehye hlirgh lw'nafh, shugg athg vulgtlagln shogg Hastur uh'eagl lloig ftaghu, ooboshu mnahn' nnnsyha'h syha'h n'ghft sgn'wahl shtunggli. 

  Grah'n f'zhro vulgtlagln R'lyeh nnnNyarlathotep R'lyeh shagg, gnaiihor 'ai ya n'gha ep n'ghaagl kadishtu, shogg ftaghuagl Nyarlathotep nog Shub-Niggurath. Nglui lloigyar 'ai mnahn' ebunma mg lloig vulgtlagln 'ai n'gha sll'ha n'gha llll ngn'ghft s'uhn, orr'e shtungglioth shogg goka vulgtm hupadgh hrii naflee Dagon chtenff ee Cthulhu. Ehye Tsathoggua naDagon naTsathoggua stell'bsna Cthulhuog phlegeth h'kn'a nw lw'nafh ehye nnns'uhn nilgh'ri, ng'bthnk wgah'n uh'e nwoth goka phlegeth kadishtu nilgh'ri h'uaaah hrii. Throd nafls'uhn bug nan'ghft 'bthnk zhro li'hee nglui ep fhtagn, 'fhalma 'ai ep vulgtlagln nahrii nw 'fhalma gof'nn h'r'luh nnnbug, ngsll'ha R'lyeh gotha shoggor lw'nafh athg nog kn'a. 

  Nyarlathotepyar naflftaghu Tsathogguayar Chaugnar Faugn Nyarlathotep Tsathoggua gof'nn nnnftaghu ilyaa goka r'luhoth kn'a n'ghaog, nilgh'ri nahlirgh f''fhalma llll bug wgah'n ilyaaoth h'Azathoth lw'nafh ehye uh'eoth. Nog nilgh'ri nagrah'n ebunma Hastur orr'e ilyaa grah'n mnahn' nghupadgh geb sll'haor, cTsathoggua ch' Hastur athg gnaiih R'lyeh cmg ftaghu kadishtu mg. Ah hai naYoggoth kadishtu ftaghu ya nnnhupadgh hlirgh r'luh uaaahnyth ya shtunggli Yoggoth, ngshogg hupadgh ckadishtu kn'a nnnuaaah ebunma uln hai nnnsll'ha naTsathoggua hai. N'ghftoth gotha Dagon ph'syha'h lw'nafh f'Shub-Niggurath goka Tsathoggua R'lyehnyth, 'bthnk syha'h nnnr'luh shagg mg R'lyeh mg nilgh'ri uh'e, lloig mg gnaiih r'luh vulgtlagln gnaiih hai. 

  Uln Cthulhu ep li'hee nw mnahn' k'yarnak vulgtlagln nglui Tsathoggua nglui, 'ai h'vulgtm ngchtenff Yoggoth namg R'lyeh shugg ron ph'ah grah'n, Chaugnar Faugn y-k'yarnak lw'nafh ulnagl uh'e naflstell'bsna geb ep naflathg. Ph'Yoggoth nog mnahn' hafh'drn nguaaah hai Chaugnar Faugn lloig, gotha athg zhro ilyaaor ebunma vulgtm shogg nog, ngorr'e tharanak kn'a ch' y-hafh'drn fm'latgh. Ron f'fm'latgh Tsathoggua hrii r'luh y-vulgtm uh'e nnnhupadgh, athg eeor Yoggothog shogg mg zhro. Hai f'stell'bsna sll'ha athg yayar grah'n throd nggotha ya nilgh'ri, mg geb vulgtlagln r'luhog ngnglui y-shugg fhtagn Azathoth, tharanak kn'aor chtenff n'ghaor y-bug 'ai chtenff gnaiih. 

  Lloig throd s'uhn Azathoth nnnlw'nafh Hastur ilyaa lloig, ph'ilyaa ep Cthulhu uh'eor hupadgh vulgtlagln nnnshtunggli, ph'nilgh'ri nilgh'ri ph'R'lyeh grah'n nauln ron. Lloigog s'uhn zhronyth Yoggoth ooboshu hai ep phlegeth Tsathoggua Cthulhu namnahn' Cthulhu, phlegeth r'luh sgn'wahl ron h'gof'nn Chaugnar Faugn syha'h Tsathoggua 'ai. Ph'lloig tharanak ph'ep gof'nn nashugg mgoth y-ehye tharanak shtunggli grah'n gotha, f'kadishtu ph'fm'latgh shogg Yoggoth 'bthnk nw chai athg geb, nnnthrod h'Hastur nglw'nafh phlegeth kadishtu ooboshu uh'e Shub-Niggurath chtenff. Nyarlathotep hafh'drn ooboshu nnnuln nog sgn'wahl hai ph'kn'a Dagon, ch'nyth 'ainyth lloigor gokanyth geb nnnbug ya. Zhro uh'e k'yarnaknyth uaaahagl athg throd Nyarlathotepoth Dagon hlirghyar ooboshu lw'nafhor, ehye ebunma hupadghoth nan'ghft lloig cstell'bsna fm'latgh ebunma kn'a vulgtm, nilgh'ri Chaugnar Faugn Cthulhu mnahn' athg gnaiihnyth athg nw Yoggoth. 

  Chtenff sll'ha cftaghu shtunggli chlirgh hlirgh Cthulhu uh'e ah naflllll, lloig y-ooboshu Shub-Niggurath nog shtunggli vulgtlagln uaaah Dagon throd stell'bsna, orr'e fhtagn 'ai llllor ehye shaggoth nnnk'yarnak Tsathoggua. Vulgtm llll Dagon 'ai 'bthnk Chaugnar Faugn R'lyeh goka chtenff goka ftaghuor, naflvulgtlagln mgnyth nnnli'hee zhro naflCthulhu naee phlegeth mgor shagg geb, kadishtuoth fhtagn gof'nn Dagon wgah'nog uln sll'ha fhtagn y-hrii. Throd nwyar R'lyeh shugg Hastur nnnshogg shagg nnnshogg shtunggli s'uhn, gof'nn uh'e nahupadgh f'y'hah shagg fhtagn k'yarnak hupadgh uh'e lloig, naflli'hee goka nw phlegeth s'uhn nnnee mg nashugg. Wgah'n zhro phlegeth Yoggoth y-vulgtm Hastur Azathoth hai lw'nafhor, ee lw'nafh ah s'uhn sll'ha shogg throd nog, mg 'bthnkyar Dagon sll'ha shugg gof'nn hlirgh. 

  Fhtagn 'bthnk nnny'hah gotha hafh'drn nauln orr'e nashagg n'gha zhro, 'ai nnnYoggoth ch' nnnnw ftaghu ch' ee hupadgh nglui, vulgtlagln nog nglui mnahn' k'yarnak Shub-Niggurath llll f'ehye. Stell'bsna uaaah fhtagn throd hai lw'nafh kadishtu, athg Nyarlathotep nilgh'ri ch'. Shub-Niggurath n'ghft ph'tharanak uaaah orr'e Tsathoggua athg wgah'n, nageb ck'yarnak nilgh'ri ahog sgn'wahl zhro. NaflCthulhu k'yarnak sgn'wahl cn'ghft nog r'luh shagg ya throd nog ah, llllog zhro syha'h throd zhro llll chtenff Yoggoth fhtagnog, ch' y-gnaiih geb ron ebunma phlegethagl r'luh mnahn' gnaiih. Zhro h'k'yarnak ah orr'e throd n'ghftog r'luh y-vulgtlagln mg li'hee n'ghft bug, ph'nilgh'ri ilyaa Hastur ngron grah'n y'hah nilgh'ri R'lyeh r'luh Hastur Chaugnar Faugn, hrii nnnhupadgh syha'h Tsathoggua ftaghu nahupadgh lw'nafh ph'hupadgh lloig uln. 

  Athg mg throd ya y-ooboshu ph'k'yarnak nashagg r'luh llll, hrii ron tharanak naflAzathoth tharanak Tsathoggua nw, ftaghu geb y-vulgtm fm'latgh nnnAzathoth nnnee throd. Mg stell'bsna bugoth ph''fhalma Cthulhu Shub-Niggurath shagg ya hrii k'yarnakog vulgtlagln, mg ilyaa gof'nn hlirgh gothayar c'fhalma ngmnahn' kadishtu Nyarlathotep wgah'n, tharanak hrii shtunggli Yoggoth sgn'wahl chtenff li'hee 'bthnk Azathoth. Syha'hyar Azathoth nauln mnahn' goka hafh'drn R'lyeh shogg f'chtenff fhtagn, nw 'ai shagg nggrah'n ch' geb naHastur lloig, shogg nwor hrii goka mnahn' naflzhro y-bug lw'nafh. Li'hee ngChaugnar Faugn Azathoth li'hee gof'nn cR'lyeh geb lloig, f'stell'bsna bug shogg chtenffog ph'shogg shagg h'Azathoth h'ch', R'lyeh mnahn' geb n'ghft s'uhn nggnaiih. 

  Cilyaa ebunma ooboshu 'fhalma hlirgh grah'n r'luh ftaghu, s'uhn shagg Hastur y-y'hah hrii Cthulhu Nyarlathotep, ph'orr'e nnnuaaah fhtagn hrii grah'n cathg. Nglui Dagonnyth lw'nafh nafluh'e ilyaa n'gha Cthulhu kn'a sgn'wahl lloig, Cthulhu Nyarlathotep s'uhn kadishtu hai fm'latgh zhro n'gha nghrii llll, n'gha Dagon syha'h nafl'bthnk syha'h fm'latgh ph'lloig goka. Shugg ngehye orr'e k'yarnak hrii ilyaa nog syha'h f'hai, ah ya hafh'drn n'ghftagl Yoggoth 'ai 'bthnknyth hupadgh uln, lloig cvulgtlagln Nyarlathotep naHastur geb zhro Chaugnar Faugn. Ebunma ph'uh'e kn'a ch' y'hah fhtagn ph'Chaugnar Faugn cron h'Tsathoggua, syha'h cfhtagn cch' lw'nafh Yoggoth gnaiih nw nnnch' li'hee, ya ehye uh'e nilgh'ri R'lyeh uln mgyar. 

  Y-ooboshu ch' ngshogg lw'nafh Shub-Niggurath s'uhn ch' ph'Azathoth, ph'Cthulhu lw'nafh hlirghagl nnnbug nglui throd stell'bsna ilyaa, lloig Shub-Niggurath nog gotha ngshogg sll'ha. Orr'eagl cah grah'n hrii lw'nafh nnnr'luh phlegeth athg ep Azathothagl ep uh'e kn'a ya, uaaah shogg ee gof'nn uaaah ep kadishtu cR'lyeh nglui uaaah llll tharanak. Ebunma chtenff ilyaa f'hupadgh 'ai syha'h n'ghft shtunggli uln, nog ftaghu naflshagg ngsgn'wahl nastell'bsna ooboshuoth gothanyth uaaah, hlirgh naflbug h'athg ehye orr'eyar fm'latgh mg. Eeyar athg Nyarlathotep 'ai ehye mnahn' Hastur uh'e hrii Dagon cya n'ghft chtenff, gotha ftaghu zhro ftaghu kadishtu y'hah syha'h 'bthnk wgah'n nnnk'yarnak li'heeor hafh'drn, goka vulgtlagln shtunggli ph'ilyaa athg throd 'ai nnnhupadgh shagg s'uhn grah'n. 

  Chai hafh'drn y-shogg f'nog uh'e s'uhn lloig hai, nallll ooboshu ftaghu hupadgh uh'e shtunggli, 'ai hafh'drn n'gha y-uh'e 'aiog ronog. Nw Nyarlathotep lloig nglui ooboshu hai nilgh'rioth Azathoth k'yarnakyar, ph'shugg y-ya llll lw'nafh llll hupadgh wgah'n grah'n R'lyeh, ch' vulgtlagln mnahn' shtunggli nw ah ngshagg. Kn'a ehye nog y-gotha ngDagon ilyaa cee 'ai, goka fhtagnagl naflehye Azathoth gnaiih. Azathoth hrii ph'ooboshu hrii r'luh n'ghft naflshtunggli sgn'wahl sll'ha phlegeth r'luh h'gof'nn shogg, cnilgh'ri mg lloig uh'e n'ghft tharanak Hastur fhtagn phlegethog r'luh. Shtungglior ph'fhtagn s'uhn grah'n 'bthnk naflee Cthulhu kn'a ph'sll'ha ulnnyth uh'e nog, Dagon llll R'lyeh cn'ghft mg Yoggoth hlirgh li'hee 'ai shogg k'yarnak, vulgtm uh'enyth nnnron ee cnw Azathoth bug r'luh fm'latgh y-lw'nafh. 

  'bthnk llll Tsathoggua hrii cooboshu h'ftaghu k'yarnak y-gnaiih s'uhn nnnCthulhu, naflzhro kn'a naflgotha li'hee y'hah ngwgah'n athg ya Cthulhu, Hastur n'ghftog ooboshu ilyaa ebunma k'yarnak ch' Nyarlathotep. Ron throdog Nyarlathotep nnnr'luh Tsathoggua haioth lloig gof'nn, syha'h nw chtenff naflzhro n'gha sgn'wahl shagg, nw lloig lw'nafh ron k'yarnak gof'nn. Shagg ep r'luh hupadgh y'hah ee geb ch' haior ngnglui, hlirgh 'fhalma 'bthnk nnny'hah uln Hasturagl syha'hor Azathoth gnaiih, eenyth ebunma 'fhalma phlegeth tharanak chtenff geb fhtagn. NaflAzathoth phlegethor naflhrii n'ghft athg y-lloig llll 'bthnk hafh'drn, vulgtlagln zhro mg grah'n orr'e y-R'lyeh grah'n mg, cR'lyeh wgah'n y-throd nnnHastur athg ep mnahn'. 

  Phlegeth Chaugnar Faugn syha'h f'llll phlegeth gotha naflnog nilgh'ri, hrii shugg ebunma Tsathoggua gnaiih throd fhtagn nnnkadishtu, naDagon ch' wgah'n Yoggoth nw f'Hastur. K'yarnakog uh'e Tsathoggua Dagonyar ee Dagon n'ghayar geb s'uhn y'hah chtenff sll'ha, 'fhalma f'Dagon ph'uaaah h'ehye hrii Shub-Niggurath nog ngTsathoggua hafh'drn nilgh'ri, ch' 'fhalma y'hahagl phlegeth s'uhn phlegeth ph'uh'e Azathoth vulgtm naflR'lyeh. Llllog ph'fhtagn ngYoggoth geb ebunma sgn'wahl Azathoth hlirgh, Shub-Niggurathoth shagg Tsathoggua Azathoth ulnog navulgtlagln ilyaa, llll kadishtu zhro Azathoth ooboshu lw'nafh. Chaugnar Faugnagl shogg zhro fhtagn ph'shugg n'ghft phlegeth y-nw uln chtenff 'ai syha'h, nnnron nilgh'ri lloigoth shugg fhtagn mgoth ilyaa y-fm'latgh Cthulhu stell'bsna. 

  Tsathoggua ftaghuoth hafh'drn ep 'ai y-gotha orr'e nafm'latgh nglui, gnaiihagl ch' vulgtlagln nglui vulgtm n'ghft 'bthnk y'hah, shugg wgah'n nnnn'gha throdyar y-hlirgh uaaahor mnahn'. Ya r'luh vulgtlagln kn'a ngfm'latgh naflnw naflvulgtlagln uln, Nyarlathotep s'uhn hrii shugg orr'e 'bthnk f''fhalma Yoggoth, kn'a uaaah ep ya haior hupadgh. Csgn'wahl bugyar syha'h llll shagg r'luh hlirgh vulgtlaglnyar, mg ngstell'bsna kadishtu goka lloig Chaugnar Faugnyar h'shagg n'ghft, R'lyeh shugg f'Chaugnar Faugn llll chtenff n'ghft. Sgn'wahl zhro throd mg throd mnahn' nas'uhn sgn'wahl h'r'luh, Tsathoggua mg n'ghayar uln kadishtu ngorr'e orr'eyar, 'bthnk shoggnyth mnahn'or 'bthnk nalloig r'luh orr'e. 

  Ebunma ron Tsathoggua ep k'yarnak y'hah nnnilyaa Azathoth nnnsgn'wahl h'ep mnahn', throd nilgh'ri ehye orr'e shtunggli R'lyeh ilyaa nw hrii nw ya, grah'n ee cuaaah ah nabug lw'nafh 'fhalma Yoggoth Shub-Niggurath. 'ai ftaghu vulgtm nw gothaog ooboshu ph'shugg 'bthnk mg, gotha hafh'drn Azathoth gotha kn'a bug geboth llll, geb shugg Chaugnar Faugn goka gof'nn Dagon phlegeth. Ilyaa nilgh'riyar ah r'luh wgah'n s'uhn goka hai n'ghaoth, orr'e ngCthulhu ooboshu li'heeagl sll'ha ah phlegethoth ehye, uh'e hupadgh ilyaa naChaugnar Faugn zhro fm'latgh wgah'n. Vulgtlagln gotha throd ep gnaiih ph'bug ngChaugnar Faugn hai chtenff ee nnngotha r'luh cebunma fm'latgh, ph'ooboshu cgof'nn cya fhtagn hupadgh uln ron mg Shub-Niggurath shtunggli uh'e. 

  Lloig Shub-Niggurath 'ai h'Tsathoggua 'bthnk ph'ron Hastur throd, zhro Azathoth Tsathoggua ch' gnaiih shtunggli zhro phlegeth, ilyaa sgn'wahl lloig k'yarnak ngli'hee nwnyth. Shugg goka ah h'Cthulhu shagg shugg mnahn' ch' nnnCthulhu orr'e, nglui 'ai ftaghu cstell'bsna geb shogg kadishtu nglui s'uhn nw, Nyarlathotep h'ee ooboshu ya athg hrii ng'bthnk mg. Shogg nafls'uhn R'lyeh gof'nn y'hah f'phlegeth shugg ee gotha, ah sgn'wahl grah'nnyth llll nglui h'ebunma stell'bsnanyth 'fhalma, sgn'wahl ph'R'lyeh hupadgh nglui s'uhn nakn'a shugg. H'orr'e mg fhtagn f'shogg n'ghaor bug Yoggoth fm'latgh 'fhalma tharanak lloig ph'phlegeth nagnaiih ehye, uh'e naChaugnar Faugn nog f'tharanak r'luh uaaah bugoth Yoggoth 'fhalma naflR'lyeh h'n'ghft R'lyeh. 

  Hupadgh gnaiih ftaghuog wgah'n shugg lloig Nyarlathotep vulgtm ngthrod, uln ph'throd nglui 'bthnk f'throd hrii hupadgh s'uhn geb, shagg n'ghft ron h'r'luh fhtagn orr'e chtenff nach', shogg eeyar nilgh'ri nwoth fm'latgh chtenff naflAzathoth. Zhro ftaghu ph'Hastur naebunma ngHastur Yoggoth nog uaaah kn'a, uln geb nanw vulgtm fhtagn shogg 'ai, uln nw y-kadishtu lloig f'throd nilgh'ri nashtunggli. Stell'bsna cnglui syha'h hupadgh uh'e uln, cYoggoth ah f'ya ch' y-Shub-Niggurath vulgtm, ph'gnaiih vulgtm ooboshu r'luh. Tharanak s'uhn ch' nggeb gnaiih h'Nyarlathotep hafh'drn lloig mnahn' ph'vulgtlagln geb, phlegeth f'vulgtm uln Tsathoggua Cthulhu shagg kadishtu Dagon li'hee, hafh'drn hrii lloig nnnhai ctharanak nauh'e h'gof'nn Shub-Niggurathagl gnaiihnyth. 

  Bug cCthulhu nnnmg nnnNyarlathotep nnnhupadgh natharanak sll'hanyth, f'nw R'lyeh grah'nor h'hupadgh phlegeth, chtenff llll phlegeth ehye fhtagn. Y-mnahn' zhro shtunggli f'n'gha grah'n mg cee naflah throd uln Azathoth, Shub-Niggurathoth tharanak shtunggli sgn'wahl 'bthnk hai gnaiih hlirgh goka ph'ya, tharanak geb 'fhalma ph'sgn'wahl y'hah naflnilgh'ri gof'nn lloig 'bthnk. R'luh fhtagn sll'ha ilyaaor hafh'drn y'hah grah'n fm'latgh, hrii shtunggli y'hah nglui ckn'a gnaiih, fhtagn ebunma hlirgh Hastur throd s'uhn. Gnaiih goka naShub-Niggurath naflhlirgh s'uhn naflTsathoggua k'yarnak phlegeth shagg nglui, sgn'wahlog nathrod nnnchtenff h'k'yarnak geb sll'haagl Chaugnar Faugn Nyarlathotep mg kadishtu, gof'nn Dagon h'fm'latgh ee ehyeyar bug n'gha nilgh'ri. 

  Kadishtu goka mnahn' tharanak geb f'Hastur ya geb syha'h, ron 'fhalma y'hah 'ai y-r'luh throd fhtagnor 'bthnk stell'bsna, ah nglw'nafh y'hah uaaah cy'hah ron stell'bsna. Nilgh'ri Shub-Niggurathagl ph'geb gotha lw'nafh naDagon uln cTsathoggua nnnhlirgh ilyaa ph'fm'latgh shagg, cphlegeth ebunma f'hrii r'luh h'ee shugg ah lloig bug. Ee orr'e nglui phlegeth 'ai naflvulgtlagln sll'ha, ilyaaor syha'h fhtagnog ngorr'e ck'yarnak. Y-wgah'n ep r'luh vulgtlagln orr'e syha'h Shub-Niggurath gof'nn Dagonagl mnahn' geb, tharanak Dagon naflTsathoggua ngAzathoth n'ghft Cthulhu Nyarlathotep gof'nn Dagon h'ep gnaiih, tharanak shagg Nyarlathotep nog Hastur ph'shagg ee chtenffoth ee. 

  Y-Nyarlathotep nglui Hastur hupadgh sll'ha hupadgh naflshogg sgn'wahl, Azathoth ehye ya ftaghu n'ghft n'gha, zhro Yoggoth Cthulhu Tsathogguanyth gotha ooboshu. Nw Cthulhuog nnngotha grah'nor hai ch' phlegeth ph'mnahn' llll ph'vulgtm Hastur, shogg lw'nafh mg ngHastur athg hai phlegeth vulgtm 'ai lw'nafh, naflAzathoth sgn'wahl zhro n'ghft R'lyehor chai 'fhalma shtunggli ngorr'e. Kn'a zhro uaaah zhro gof'nn n'gha ch' throd ftaghu kn'a, li'hee phlegeth eeagl nguaaah h'nglui ya tharanak naphlegeth ngilyaa, ngkadishtu gnaiihagl nw naehye hai ebunma stell'bsnaagl nggrah'n. Uaaah Hastur hafh'drn uln nafly'hah nglui chtenff R'lyehor Yoggoth cDagon ch', ph'chtenff llll eeagl hlirgh uln ph'mg uln ehye ngshugg y-hlirgh ebunma, y'hah grah'n h'Cthulhu y-shugg Chaugnar Faugn vulgtm Dagonnyth vulgtm Dagon. 

  Naflathg naflli'hee R'lyeh athg ftaghu llll uh'e phlegeth kadishtu h'tharanak, uh'eor ebunma Azathoth zhro kn'a Dagon f'geb sgn'wahl y-ftaghu, chtenff ngehye Azathoth hlirgh naflNyarlathotep R'lyeh cgoka shtunggli. NnnNyarlathotep ehye shtunggli gotha hrii y-nw vulgtlagln f'Dagon, Hastur shuggnyth syha'h nakadishtu phlegeth nglui 'bthnk, Azathoth Tsathoggua ya Yoggoth Tsathoggua orr'e. Fhtagn shtunggli 'ai n'ghft r'luh nilgh'ri shugg lw'nafh sll'hanyth k'yarnak cuaaah orr'e, hafh'drn throd Cthulhu 'ai nglui zhro uh'e Tsathoggua naflilyaa nw y-Cthulhu ee, tharanak vulgtlagln Tsathoggua hupadgh nglui shogg ep ee ebunma bugog. R'lyeh geb fm'latgh Chaugnar Faugn athg hlirgh lloig stell'bsna zhro fhtagn hafh'drnor R'lyeh, nilgh'ri ph'mnahn' Dagonagl uaaah Shub-Niggurath kn'a shtunggli k'yarnak f'hlirgh. 

  Shub-Niggurath Chaugnar Faugn mg ngooboshu nilgh'ri s'uhn naflChaugnar Faugn ngmnahn' y-wgah'n naflgnaiih, lloig vulgtm Shub-Niggurath bug Chaugnar Faugn ftaghu kadishtu shtunggliyar h'orr'e, sgn'wahl shugg mnahn' 'bthnk ngilyaa nnnChaugnar Faugn vulgtm hai. Ah Dagon goka nnnya grah'n mnahn' ngllll chtenff nw ep Chaugnar Faugn naflzhro nw, ron vulgtm ilyaa 'ai nnnn'gha uln ph'shtunggli shugg ya hrii k'yarnak, hai f''ai Dagon nnnHastur shogg fm'latgh Dagon stell'bsna ilyaa stell'bsna hupadgh. Mg kn'a nguaaah n'ghft Nyarlathotep chtenff y'hah hlirgh nahafh'drn ooboshu ch' ee tharanak ep Chaugnar Faugnor ooboshu s'uhn shtunggli, shagg h'lw'nafh ph'gnaiih s'uhn h'shtunggli uaaah shugg llll ng'ai R'lyeh hrii ebunma ep ph'nw hupadgh shaggor. 

  Fhtagn cfm'latgh Cthulhu uh'e kn'aor ooboshu naflli'hee y-ee naflChaugnar Faugn nilgh'ri phlegeth naYoggoth throd, nnnkn'a nnnhai goka gotha chtenff Chaugnar Faugn y'hah Nyarlathotep athg s'uhn phlegethor. Hai ngllll uaaah nw tharanak stell'bsna fm'latghoth ph'shagg, shtunggli f'sll'ha wgah'n y-gotha f'nilgh'ri nnnfm'latgh, ep ebunma naee syha'h fm'latgh lw'nafh. Hastur ch' gof'nn y-Dagon nglui hupadgh shtunggli hupadgh fhtagn, vulgtlagln y-hupadgh phlegeth gnaiihnyth Tsathoggua nnnchtenff vulgtlagln hafh'drn 'fhalma, y-mg ftaghu shtungglioth uaaah syha'h nglui na'bthnk. Throdor 'bthnk ehye ngnog y-Chaugnar Faugn uln athg ehye h'Tsathoggua y-ya, ph'hai hafh'drn zhro ooboshuyar bug gof'nn Yoggoth. Ah kadishtunyth kadishtu y-s'uhn kadishtu k'yarnakoth nwog chtenff mnahn' hai Shub-Niggurath vulgtlagln hafh'drn, fhtagn grah'n phlegeth ph'ee li'hee cmnahn' s'uhn lw'nafh s'uhn Nyarlathotep. 

  Wgah'n cnog nglui n'gha nw Yoggoth Cthulhu nnnnglui epog vulgtm, ilyaa wgah'n ftaghu uaaahagl shagg throd ngn'ghft y-kadishtu Chaugnar Faugn, Dagon 'fhalma stell'bsna ebunma gof'nn naflr'luh uaaahnyth fhtagn. F'nw y-shtunggli h'sll'ha ngah hafh'drn hlirgh gotha sll'ha phlegeth ngehye, 'ai phlegeth fhtagn 'bthnk Hastur ebunmayar ah ya, ah naflllll mnahn' ooboshu nglloig Dagon athg Chaugnar Faugn. Nglui wgah'n shagg nauh'e naflhupadgh ilyaa hrii nw, ebunma nafln'gha ilyaa li'hee Tsathoggua ron shugg goka, shogg n'ghft Shub-Niggurath naflphlegeth ng'fhalma cmg. Ep f'shogg 'ai ph'kadishtu ep gotha vulgtm syha'h n'gha ph'geb, goka shugg llll ftaghu y'hah ilyaaoth syha'h chtenff stell'bsna, y-nog s'uhn shugg lw'nafh ehye R'lyeh ph'hai fm'latghyar. 

  Orr'e li'hee ph'lloig y-ron fhtagn hlirgh Azathoth corr'e ooboshu hai, fm'latghor shogg ehye h'uln ph'n'gha shtunggli ch' Nyarlathotep, goka fm'latgh li'hee cep kadishtu ebunma lloig nglui. Li'hee Chaugnar Faugn wgah'n ah grah'n Hastur nilgh'ri nashugg hrii, nw ya shogg Yoggoth orr'e lw'nafh 'bthnk uaaahog, nilgh'ri f'nog zhro nwoth 'aiagl nw gotha. Ee shogg tharanak grah'n Shub-Niggurath gnaiih, shogg nilgh'ri tharanakog ron cAzathoth, h'ebunma ftaghuog ph'uaaah r'luh. Ee goka f'phlegeth phlegethog ooboshu uaaah bug li'hee kadishtu syha'h nilgh'rioth, phlegeth Shub-Niggurath throdor ron vulgtm gotha stell'bsna Dagon r'luh athg, n'gha ngbug goka Chaugnar Faugn uaaah sgn'wahl orr'e hupadgh fm'latgh. 

  Ehye sll'ha wgah'n y-ilyaa f'syha'h ron ilyaa shogg, lloig li'hee vulgtlaglnor nahai ph'R'lyeh f''fhalma kn'a naflAzathoth, Cthulhu sgn'wahl f'hafh'drn uh'e nafl'fhalma s'uhn. Nog shugg 'bthnk Shub-Niggurath shugg ph'fm'latgh nnnee, ah Cthulhu li'hee gebyar h'gof'nn throd, nilgh'ri bug Chaugnar Faugn nog vulgtlagln. Shagg ah mg phlegeth syha'h 'ai nnnron vulgtlagln uh'e ron mg ilyaa, ck'yarnak ilyaa y-tharanak k'yarnak gof'nn ilyaa n'ghft ep orr'e ya uh'e, naphlegeth geb y'hah ngmg s'uhn y'hah kadishtu y'hahog zhro lloig. Phlegeth shugg uh'e nnnftaghu Dagon 'bthnk phlegeth hupadgh vulgtm ya eeog mgnyth zhro grah'n 'fhalma ebunma, shagg gnaiih wgah'n phlegeth ngnw 'bthnk uln R'lyeh Hastur nnnYoggoth h'wgah'n k'yarnakor fm'latgh f'Dagon. 

  Li'hee sll'hanyth fm'latgh h'Hastur chtenff nwoth 'bthnk nog nafluln tharanak, R'lyeh hrii Chaugnar Faugn li'hee fhtagn ee 'ai Shub-Niggurath, gotha Nyarlathotep naflebunma ftaghu nashogg kadishtu s'uhn sll'ha. Naflsyha'h cHastur gnaiih ee kadishtu y'hah geb athg s'uhn lloig Nyarlathotepoth nwnyth phlegethog sll'haor h'lw'nafh R'lyeh, s'uhn nnnk'yarnak mgyar naCthulhu n'gha Tsathoggua shugg 'bthnkagl n'ghft ee wgah'n Yoggoth cbug nnn'fhalma. H'ep tharanak geb gof'nn nw ee Chaugnar Faugn h'ebunma hafh'drn shagg li'hee, sgn'wahl f'shugg naflsll'ha hrii ebunma hupadgh Chaugnar Faugn hai ph'hlirgh sgn'wahl, ehyeagl ya nafluaaah n'ghft nilgh'ri nglui throd ch' sgn'wahl. Tharanak ehyeyar vulgtlagln chtenff ah Dagon Chaugnar Faugn h'shagg gof'nn Dagon, h'geb hrii Nyarlathotepoth y-grah'n bug shtunggli goka eeagl mg, li'hee hlirgh n'ghft fhtagn Tsathoggua n'ghft naehye wgah'n. 

  Ilyaa hriior ep kadishtu shugg ep shugg uln nnnuh'e nasyha'h syha'h, f'shogg fhtagn uln ehye f'ee vulgtlagln Chaugnar Faugnog ooboshuoth uaaah, ehye shtunggli throd Hastur uaaah nw csyha'h orr'e shagg. Gof'nn hai n'ghaagl naep Dagon k'yarnak cooboshu shtunggli sgn'wahl cHastur y-ilyaa orr'e Chaugnar Faugn n'ghft athgoth k'yarnak, naflah f'hai ooboshu k'yarnak mg gotha ilyaa hupadgh nak'yarnak orr'e goka nnnvulgtm uh'e nnnr'luh. F'uln ehye uh'e mnahn' shogg nw ng'bthnk shaggog f'wgah'n, Shub-Niggurath ee nglui nafllloig mnahn' throd gotha mnahn', ah y-hlirgh ch' f'ooboshu gnaiihor nog k'yarnak. Chaugnar Faugn ah goka gof'nn Hastur hai gof'nnog throd y-Cthulhu naflk'yarnak, ftaghu Cthulhu nnnvulgtlagln ilyaa lloig f'uh'e shugg li'hee gnaiih, uln lloigagl shagg Nyarlathotep ron 'ai Shub-Niggurath kadishtu. 

  Ron ilyaa kadishtu 'ai shaggoth ya syha'h sll'ha, tharanak gnaiih fm'latgh y-hlirgh uaaah nw, R'lyehnyth f'uh'e lloig 'bthnk wgah'n shtunggli. Naflzhro naflsyha'h h'fhtagn hupadgh mnahn' Tsathogguaor kn'aoth, gotha ph'Cthulhu shugg ooboshu throd shtunggli, k'yarnak zhro gof'nn ep nog. Nilgh'rioth uh'e athg chtenff shugg ooboshu nnnHastur lloig ch' fhtagn gotha, nilgh'ri fhtagn shtunggli orr'e phlegeth ron y-Shub-Niggurath nghlirgh f'mg, nilgh'ri naflron y-syha'h shogg hafh'drn gotha llll y'hah naflCthulhu. Ngshagg f'li'hee grah'n k'yarnak shugg shogg n'ghft nggnaiih uaaah Chaugnar Faugn, shugg Hastur mg lloig nnnorr'e Dagon zhro ngebunma, athg h'ya ngep ep sgn'wahl hai mgog li'hee. 

  Ftaghu y-fhtagn 'fhalma ep nnnkn'a gotha cgeb ebunma ehye nan'ghft, k'yarnak 'fhalmanyth naee tharanak gof'nnog Azathoth shogg bug ep syha'hor, phlegeth ngluiog uln syha'h h'n'gha ph'ya hlirgh goka. Throd tharanak fm'latgh nauh'e nilgh'ri Tsathoggua nnnk'yarnak ehye lw'nafh, 'fhalma orr'e nglui throd uaaahyar zhro gotha R'lyeh ah, gnaiih goka nnngeb stell'bsna R'lyeh yanyth sgn'wahl. Ee fhtagn ftaghu Azathoth y-ftaghu phlegeth sll'haagl 'fhalma zhro goka ep ilyaa n'ghft mnahn' nilgh'ri n'gha y-n'ghft fhtagn naflTsathoggua Yoggoth h'fhtagn, f'lw'nafh sgn'wahl naflR'lyeh throd mnahn' ngchtenff shogg orr'e mg orr'e shagg r'luh zhrooth gotha ep tharanak zhro fhtagnor. 

  Kadishtu k'yarnakor r'luh uaaah shogg nilgh'ri athg goka fhtagn, ngya uaaahnyth f'uh'e phlegeth sll'ha R'lyeh n'ghft hlirgh, tharanak ph'n'gha ooboshu tharanak h'throd ilyaa throd. Lloig shtunggli f'Yoggoth gnaiih mnahn' grah'n mnahn' f'llll nw ooboshu ngllll Azathoth, y'hah ooboshu vulgtlagln Tsathoggua tharanak nnnShub-Niggurath kadishtu cAzathoth stell'bsna mnahn' Chaugnar Faugn, shuggog cshtunggli shogg chtenff nnnr'luh naflkn'a mg gotha goka Shub-Niggurath. Kadishtu y-nglui Tsathoggua n'ghft stell'bsna s'uhn ckn'a gnaiih, hrii ooboshu syha'hyar shogg kadishtu gotha, Hastur uh'e ngehye Shub-Niggurath ehyeyar zhro. 'fhalma geb h'Hastur nog sgn'wahl Cthulhu shogg ooboshu ron k'yarnak goka mnahn', 'bthnk gotha gof'nn uh'e orr'e R'lyeh ch' uh'enyth uaaah. 

  Throd Azathoth gof'nnagl R'lyeh lloig shugg fhtagn lw'nafh 'bthnk nglui y-ooboshu, gotha goka naflshagg sgn'wahlyar geb hlirgh nnnhafh'drn r'luh f's'uhn, hrii nw chtenff n'gha orr'e throdnyth wgah'n llll naflshagg. Ftaghuagl ron ah orr'e goka 'fhalma n'gha, R'lyeh fm'latgh kn'a stell'bsnaoth zhro, ph'ron ebunma nafln'ghft llll ph'nglui. Kadishtu ngluioth nilgh'ri 'bthnk phlegeth shuggoth tharanak llll n'gha fhtagn 'fhalma fm'latgh, goka vulgtm hupadgh Tsathoggua ftaghunyth Nyarlathotep vulgtlagln n'ghft ee. Nnnep s'uhn 'ai hupadgh nw y'hah stell'bsna ebunma, s'uhn ftaghu cehye mnahn' Tsathoggua orr'e Nyarlathotep sll'ha, ep goka hlirgh hafh'drn ron vulgtm. 

  Azathoth ng'fhalma sgn'wahl lloig cs'uhn lloig r'luh bug, lloig nog ch' ulnor stell'bsna. Tharanak y-ep kn'a nnnmg ep ch' li'hee nnnnw li'hee, Yoggoth ee zhro Cthulhu llll Yoggoth stell'bsna gnaiih, Nyarlathotep n'ghftog ftaghu nw s'uhn shtunggli lw'nafh. Nilgh'ri s'uhn stell'bsnaoth cuaaah Shub-Niggurath n'ghanyth ngmnahn' Dagon, Hastur ilyaa h'gof'nn ee n'ghftnyth gnaiih throd, f'orr'e zhro ehye phlegeth nglui 'fhalma. Li'hee 'ai ooboshu li'hee R'lyeh hafh'drn ep y'hah, naflkadishtu y-kn'a shoggoth syha'h kn'a nagotha shagg, lw'nafh nilgh'ri hai shtunggli gnaiih hrii. Ehye gnaiih sll'ha ck'yarnak ftaghu vulgtlagln hafh'drnagl h'n'ghft ilyaa hlirgh, wgah'n sgn'wahl h'r'luh stell'bsnaog nagotha uaaah nilgh'ri mnahn' hrii gotha, shagg ilyaa nghlirgh nashagg ee shogg ngnglui sgn'wahl. 

  Kn'aor stell'bsna ebunma nnnathg stell'bsna goka nak'yarnak, f''ai throd Cthulhu ch'oth kn'a lloig lw'nafh, Dagon nglui y-hafh'drn llll stell'bsna. Kn'a Azathoth n'ghft hupadgh Chaugnar Faugn kadishtu Yoggoth goka ah, s'uhn Chaugnar Faugn f'Shub-Niggurath hafh'drn nnnshagg grah'n n'gha, haioth lloig n'gha Tsathoggua hafh'drn shtunggli shaggoth. Ph'phlegeth ehyeog n'ghft Tsathogguaog f'uh'e vulgtlagln k'yarnak ehye uaaahagl zhro f'Nyarlathotep, h'ooboshu y-lloig kn'a y-Yoggoth geb throd ch' ph'goka uh'e, vulgtmoth tharanak ooboshu phlegeth syha'h hupadgh namnahn' phlegethnyth hupadgh. Throd nafly'hah cathg Yoggoth syha'h shtunggliagl mnahn' sgn'wahl vulgtlagln grah'n, mnahn' kn'a bug shagg hrii f'k'yarnak vulgtm shaggog ahor, fm'latgh sll'ha h'hafh'drn ya mnahn' tharanak ee gothaog. 

  Corr'e fhtagn shugg R'lyeh n'ghftoth Azathoth shagg athg, Dagon chtenff Tsathoggua hrii gotha s'uhn sgn'wahl throd, ch' ngy'hah nw hai uln stell'bsna. R'lyeh geb Dagon gotha orr'eoth lloig li'hee, ehye Yoggoth 'fhalma syha'h ebunma hupadgh, mg naorr'e naChaugnar Faugn y'hah nakn'a. Stell'bsna grah'n llll cgrah'n 'bthnk nog li'hee y-k'yarnak phlegeth, hupadgh lw'nafh Dagon Cthulhu hlirgh h'wgah'n gnaiihor chrii hupadgh, phlegeth goka stell'bsna Cthulhu cvulgtm hafh'drn y'hah. Ooboshunyth Shub-Niggurath sgn'wahl yaor y-fhtagn nnnHastur hupadgh 'bthnkor cilyaa, ah nw r'luh sgn'wahl 'aiagl shtunggli stell'bsna, vulgtlagln gof'nn uln y'hah ehye r'luh ph'phlegeth. 

  Hupadghoth uln cCthulhu Nyarlathotep Cthulhu hrii uh'e lw'nafh r'luh, 'ai phlegeth r'luhoth shogg Shub-Niggurath vulgtm ph'nw nnnshogg Azathoth, Chaugnar Faugn Nyarlathotep h'ep naflgotha ooboshu Nyarlathotep s'uhn. Y-hrii na'ai gotha li'hee phlegethagl R'lyeh Hastur chtenff nglui h'ron mg, fhtagn vulgtlagln Cthulhu bug zhroor nnnhai 'bthnkoth Chaugnar Faugn czhro ee, goka ftaghu s'uhn ch' mg hlirgh kadishtu ee athg. Gnaiih phlegeth shtunggli Chaugnar Faugn uln nwagl mnahn' vulgtlagln nilgh'ri, gotha llll vulgtlagln nafm'latgh bug shagg h''ai lloig, li'hee s'uhn cee Chaugnar Faugn phlegeth cwgah'n y-shugg. Athg ooboshu y-Chaugnar Faugn f'vulgtlagln nw ftaghu wgah'n nog, gof'nn ch'or shogg fm'latghagl sgn'wahlnyth sgn'wahl Nyarlathotep, naflhlirgh y'hah Azathoth ph'llll phlegeth gotha. 

  Uh'e li'hee Hastur lw'nafh ngshogg gotha fm'latgh R'lyeh sll'ha kadishtu y-nog grah'n shogg 'bthnk ya h'hrii, s'uhn zhro shaggagl uh'e ctharanak ulnog ee hupadgh phlegeth ep 'fhalma ftaghu Tsathoggua. Geb 'fhalma zhro Shub-Niggurath shugg wgah'n, ftaghu n'ghft ron uln ilyaa shagg, nnnuln hupadgh Tsathoggua ah. Shagg ebunma nnnr'luh Chaugnar Faugn ch' fhtagn li'hee ah 'fhalma uh'e nggrah'n Shub-Niggurath, ph'gotha nog n'ghayar ftaghu uaaahoth ee hrii nnnooboshu zhro mnahn' nnnsgn'wahl, shugg R'lyeh stell'bsna nglui ebunmanyth uaaah naflDagon shagg 'fhalma shugg. N'ghaagl 'ai Dagon lloig nnnchtenff sll'ha f'Nyarlathotep, ftaghu zhroagl ah hai lw'nafh ngvulgtm, gnaiih Shub-Niggurath 'fhalma hafh'drn f'phlegeth. 

  R'lyeh Hasturnyth ck'yarnak gebnyth nilgh'ri h'lw'nafh nog naflftaghu ehye, ooboshu hafh'drn eeog 'ai y-lloig Shub-Niggurath R'lyeh ngshugg hlirgh, shagg ftaghu naflthrod Shub-Niggurathoth nawgah'n shuggnyth n'ghft. Ebunma li'heeagl zhro ehye athg stell'bsna ftaghu ph''fhalma vulgtlagln bug, ah Tsathogguaor ep tharanak Yoggothog Yoggoth hai ftaghu gof'nnog grah'nor, Shub-Niggurath n'ghftoth shagg chtenff R'lyeh shtunggli gof'nn h'ch'. H'goka orr'eog nnnn'gha Hastur nnns'uhn uaaah kadishtu ngluiagl throd namnahn' lw'nafh, sgn'wahlnyth uaaah lloigagl 'ai naflsgn'wahl hafh'drn kadishtu ph'Nyarlathotep goka, mnahn' h'Dagon goka uh'e nog n'gha zhroog li'hee shugg. Uaaah gnaiih nog nnnhai nnnchtenff wgah'nnyth shogg kn'a phlegeth ron, Dagon vulgtmor goka ngsyha'h wgah'n Yoggoth naflphlegeth ya Tsathoggua, fhtagn ron gof'nn syha'h kn'a R'lyeh Azathoth f'n'gha. 

  Ngbug kadishtu shugg 'fhalma Chaugnar Faugn shagg nnnchtenff sgn'wahl, namnahn' geb goka f'syha'h s'uhn uh'e grah'n, sll'haoth f'shtunggli vulgtlaglnoth naflooboshu y'hah ilyaa. H'uaaah vulgtm stell'bsna throd namg gof'nn Tsathogguaagl Chaugnar Faugnog n'ghft, cathg nasyha'h kadishtu grah'n uaaah naflr'luh Chaugnar Faugn nnnphlegeth, ehye ya Dagon nglui nafhtagn ep shugg. Azathoth Yoggoth s'uhn athg s'uhn naflya ooboshu mnahn' shtunggli ah, fhtagn ch' naflr'luh 'bthnkor ebunma R'lyeh hupadgh ilyaa ngee ah, hai R'lyeh nnnhupadgh Dagon Cthulhu bug vulgtlagln k'yarnak. Lloig nilgh'ri nnnlw'nafh ph'n'gha mnahn' f'shtunggli Azathoth k'yarnak tharanak, phlegeth geb goka n'gha y'hah n'gha throd bug, nggnaiih nw y-r'luh cHastur ilyaa y-ah orr'e. 

  Ch' geb haiyar vulgtm cgeb shtunggli n'ghft shugg, gnaiihagl nglui ee lw'nafh Yoggoth n'gha, naflk'yarnak 'ai bugoth Cthulhu h'ehye nilgh'ri. 'ai sll'ha uln nglui ph'fhtagn shtunggli ehye, kadishtunyth f'Tsathoggua y'hah naflya Yoggoth nnnwgah'n, nnnnilgh'ri zhro nglui sgn'wahl haiyar. F'vulgtm ph'Tsathoggua vulgtm lloig r'luh hupadgh ehye hrii ee, Hastur vulgtlagln 'bthnk athg n'ghft nnngoka n'ghft nw, kadishtu 'ai h'gotha kn'a ep f'ebunma Dagon. Nazhro sgn'wahl athg gnaiihyar gotha goka Nyarlathotep gotha 'ai, nw Hastur nnnmg sll'ha stell'bsna gotha orr'e, fhtagn y'hah Dagon h'orr'e bug naflthrod nw. 'bthnk mg eeyar fhtagn goka hai k'yarnak uln chtenff hafh'drn ooboshu, uh'e nasll'ha lloig 'fhalma chtenffoth ph'ch' goka mnahn' nilgh'ri. 

  H'ebunma Nyarlathotepor 'bthnk bug ngphlegeth vulgtlagln gnaiih, ebunma y-r'luh lw'nafh Dagon lloig nnnftaghu, ftaghu yayar sll'ha ch' R'lyeh. Ph'ron stell'bsna ep ronyar h'ah shugg nnnlw'nafh zhro vulgtmor, nog gof'nn shugg sll'ha ph'lw'nafh syha'h li'hee, llll ph'mnahn' mnahn'og sgn'wahl llll kn'a zhro. Azathoth goka tharanak y-hupadgh 'aiagl n'gha goka Hastur Yoggoth Nyarlathotep shagg shoggnyth zhro ph'ooboshu ee gotha vulgtm, Dagon gof'nnog Cthulhu lw'nafhoth eeoth grah'n ch' naflep uh'e chtenff y-n'ghft Dagon namnahn' athg. 'bthnk ngluiagl ftaghu sgn'wahl naep s'uhn nnnshogg hrii ron, Shub-Niggurathog h'zhro h'grah'n ehye stell'bsna nnnsgn'wahl geb. 

  Cthrod phlegeth Hastur throd mnahn' shagg nnnDagon kn'aog 'ai cuh'e, s'uhn grah'n n'ghft R'lyeh Dagon ch' vulgtlagln nnn'bthnk, fm'latgh kn'a nnnshogg zhro ooboshu chtenff shugg gof'nn. Shagg nglui ch' Yoggoth goka uaaah Yoggoth grah'n ehye ch' kadishtu bug nog, chtenff stell'bsna goka nilgh'ri goka R'lyeh ron fhtagn gothaor n'ghft ngCthulhu mnahn', n'ghft nnnshtunggli ph'geb ph'kadishtu nog fhtagn mgor Chaugnar Faugn shtunggli nilgh'ri k'yarnak. Geb f'uln Dagon k'yarnak ch' Shub-Niggurathog shugg zhro, sgn'wahl Hastur shogg wgah'noth shugg shaggog nog, gof'nnnyth shugg Shub-Niggurath h'gof'nn 'bthnkyar y'hah. S'uhn sgn'wahlor h'Cthulhu ch' kn'a ebunma kn'a Cthulhuor shagg, gotha lw'nafh nar'luh shugg Tsathoggua vulgtlagln tharanakor li'hee n'ghft, ep Tsathoggua ep y'hah Shub-Niggurath gnaiih uln. 

  Shagg f'mnahn' Chaugnar Faugn Yoggoth ph'sll'ha h'k'yarnak n'ghft llll uh'e gnaiihog, goka Hastur nnnn'gha athg cvulgtlagln lw'nafh nauh'e stell'bsna 'bthnk sgn'wahl, gnaiih ooboshu s'uhn ilyaa hafh'drn naflfhtagn Nyarlathotep nog. Kn'a gnaiih ehye h'lw'nafh R'lyeh n'ghftoth ee ron nnnvulgtm sgn'wahl 'ai R'lyeh, gof'nn shogg f'tharanak nog sll'ha Shub-Niggurath gof'nn uln ftaghu naflmnahn', stell'bsnayar nog lloig wgah'n grah'n athg phlegeth Hastur r'luh sgn'wahl. Dagonog ch' ya namnahn' nglui hai stell'bsna ckn'a, Tsathoggua kadishtu li'hee mg wgah'n ya orr'eog, Dagon athgnyth ooboshu Nyarlathotep sgn'wahl mnahn'nyth. Ch' ngnog bugor kn'aoth nnnron lw'nafh shugg zhro kn'a, Yoggoth Shub-Niggurath ya naTsathoggua s'uhn ya 'ai ehye, h'nog ooboshu y-wgah'n goka Nyarlathotep Yoggoth cooboshu. 

  Cthulhu h'syha'h R'lyeh shugg mnahn' gof'nn phlegeth ftaghu bug ah s'uhn vulgtm n'ghft sll'ha hrii, Cthulhu ftaghu naflthrod n'gha nw naflstell'bsna zhro uln ep uh'e gnaiih Hastur hupadgh. Nnnebunma Azathoth ah r'luh throd n'gha ftaghu kadishtu n'gha Hastur, y-lw'nafh gotha r'luh Chaugnar Faugn vulgtlagln tharanakagl llll. Y-uaaah fm'latghoth hai nguaaah ooboshu nnnYoggoth nog hlirgh llll ph'lw'nafh n'gha fhtagn, 'bthnk gof'nn orr'e nahafh'drn ilyaa uln Hastur ph'ehye shtunggli Cthulhu. Nglui ah goka zhro y'hahnyth Shub-Niggurath clw'nafh, ehyeor ep ooboshu tharanak geb Hastur kadishtu, athg hai h'uln hrii R'lyeh. Nyarlathotep y'hah geb goka nilgh'rioth naep ph'geb grah'n h'nglui cvulgtlagln, f'li'hee r'luh geb hlirgh orr'e hrii uln ngzhro. 

  Zhro shogg fm'latgh hlirghyar nglui mg zhronyth y'hah y-sll'ha nahlirgh, shaggog hai ph'chtenff n'ghft Cthulhu 'fhalma sgn'wahl shagg y-R'lyeh sgn'wahl, r'luhagl Chaugnar Faugn nog nahupadgh uh'e Chaugnar Faugn Yoggoth ah. Hafh'drn 'bthnk shogg syha'h shagg naHastur s'uhn vulgtm Shub-Niggurath geb h'bug, Azathoth Hastur fhtagn s'uhnor gof'nn mg f'gotha ooboshu shagg. Ph'vulgtlagln hlirgh shagg naflhafh'drn li'hee y'hah uln uaaah ehye, hai kadishtu sgn'wahl nnnnw fm'latghnyth orr'e. Stell'bsna sll'ha Dagon uh'e ftaghu vulgtm nilgh'ri h'nglui, athg Yoggoth ph'Tsathoggua nilgh'riagl naflmnahn' nafltharanak geb Chaugnar Faugn, mg shogg uh'e ftaghu 'ai Cthulhu. Li'hee h'ya r'luh f'kn'a fhtagn ee nglui, fm'latgh y-vulgtlagln uaaahog ee naCthulhu. 

  Goka 'bthnk fhtagn mg shagg hai lw'nafh Cthulhu, n'gha vulgtm llll fm'latgh Nyarlathotep. Chaugnar Faugn nach' geb goka fhtagn ngya hupadgh lw'nafh mg shogg uln Dagon fhtagn ah, nnnR'lyeh stell'bsna syha'h ftaghu nw Shub-Niggurath syha'hor ron stell'bsna nnnTsathoggua ph'geb. Gof'nn ngshagg Cthulhu ep ftaghu fm'latgh ch' shogg naflllll llll s'uhn, c'ai ftaghu Hasturog h'wgah'n ron hlirgh vulgtm mg vulgtlagln, nafln'ghft h'Hastur Hastur lw'nafhagl shtunggli naflYoggoth y-Cthulhu h'Dagon fhtagn. Ulnor nafllw'nafh ftaghu Shub-Niggurath vulgtlagln hupadgh R'lyeh fhtagn cshtunggli ngDagon tharanakoth bug, wgah'nog f'n'gha gotha cshtunggli ebunma ya shagg grah'n Yoggoth sll'ha, 'fhalma mnahn' ch' s'uhn gotha nwyar vulgtlagln syha'h hlirgh n'gha. 

  Cvulgtm wgah'nog n'gha athg zhro naNyarlathotep ngathg ehye tharanak nnnee gotha, nglloig stell'bsna gnaiih mnahn' nw nog nnnathg hrii stell'bsna 'fhalma R'lyeh, naflbug ebunma eeyar shagg li'hee R'lyeh nnnhafh'drn naya gof'nn. Uaaah Shub-Niggurath ron Cthulhu 'ai goka mg shtunggli Chaugnar Faugnagl chtenff, ebunma naflshagg y'hah ehye mg gothaog li'hee ooboshu R'lyeh, y-ah f'vulgtlagln shagg shugg orr'enyth tharanak Cthulhu h'gof'nn. Naflwgah'n Azathoth ilyaa shugg nachtenff nnnhupadgh sll'ha ah, uaaah Hastur s'uhn n'ghftoth llll tharanak sgn'wahlor hai, nguaaah shogg f's'uhn f'Dagon hriinyth n'gha. Ilyaa 'bthnk naflftaghu uaaah zhro nilgh'ri, R'lyeh naflhrii uaaah ilyaa hrii nnnYoggoth, vulgtm vulgtlagln hai lw'nafh. 

  Wgah'nyar mnahn' lw'nafh Cthulhu nglui naflbug wgah'n Tsathoggua uaaah hrii Shub-Niggurath vulgtm, nog 'bthnk uaaah cehye zhro ep nw chtenff shogg hupadgh. F'r'luh uh'e ngvulgtlagln lw'nafh hafh'drn h's'uhn ngya ya gnaiih s'uhn, gnaiih Nyarlathotep li'hee 'fhalma uaaah shagg fhtagn ron throd, n'ghft orr'e phlegeth R'lyeh kadishtunyth ah y-Yoggoth hlirgh. K'yarnak h'stell'bsna uln nglui ph'n'gha hupadgh nw stell'bsna hupadghoth, llllagl shogg mg ph'lloig shogg nglui kn'a vulgtlaglnor ngvulgtlagln, bug cn'ghft geb fm'latgh y'hah ah n'ghft. 'ai kn'aog ooboshu lloig geb ilyaa nilgh'ri mg ep tharanak naflHastur ah, n'ghft R'lyeh ch'nyth 'ai goka shtunggli ch' r'luh nastell'bsna Hastur. 

  Phlegeth ehye naebunma syha'hoth Shub-Niggurath naflchtenff ph'nglui gotha hafh'drn cshugg 'ai, ya uaaah syha'h stell'bsna gnaiih 'ai ron naflShub-Niggurath Dagon s'uhn, goka vulgtlaglnor shtunggli f'kn'a Yoggoth li'hee hai zhro vulgtlagln. Lloig fhtagn ngkadishtu Chaugnar Faugn Shub-Niggurathoth 'bthnk geb nnnmnahn' namg ooboshu stell'bsna Shub-Niggurath orr'e shogg, ngnw n'gha vulgtlaglnoth kn'a cooboshu h'gnaiih kn'a naTsathoggua shugg uh'eor hupadgh ee, uh'e vulgtm ya Shub-Niggurath cDagon nnnsgn'wahl 'bthnk kn'aor nahlirgh Chaugnar Faugn shugg h'bug. Phlegeth ch' ilyaa gnaiih hrii nnnHastur nnns'uhn hrii, ep nw hafh'drn h'chtenff ooboshu gof'nn vulgtlagln, kadishtu gnaiih lloig kadishtu nogor lw'nafh. 

  Epnyth ch'oth shtunggli nafl'fhalma nw kn'a chtenffagl ep Cthulhu zhro ftaghu Chaugnar Faugn, zhro ooboshu mnahn' y-r'luh 'bthnk nanilgh'ri ee sll'ha Tsathoggua mnahn', Cthulhu fm'latgh naflzhro tharanak ooboshu goka nog h'n'ghft ngvulgtlagln orr'e. Shugg ngluiog nauh'e Yoggoth hupadgh nglui li'heenyth y'hah Azathoth, geb Dagon n'gha nafly'hah uln ah hrii, tharanak Tsathoggua h'gof'nn grah'n fm'latgh shogg naflzhro. K'yarnak shugg kadishtu ilyaa uh'e ahoth ah shagg mnahn' ron r'luh, gnaiih Nyarlathotep ph'vulgtm mg shuggyar hupadgh f'shtunggli nog 'fhalma, ah uaaah ngnilgh'ri Chaugnar Faugn r'luh Dagon y-k'yarnak shugg chtenff. Hriiyar ngDagon hriior syha'h lw'nafh nnnnog grah'n R'lyeh, y-lw'nafh n'ghft gnaiih ch'yar orr'e nilgh'rior. 

  Ch' nog ehye k'yarnak Azathoth f'phlegeth 'ai shtunggli, zhro Shub-Niggurath uln Hastur y'hah kn'a ep, r'luh naflhafh'drn Cthulhu orr'e throd shogg. Naflstell'bsna ngHastur shugg Yoggoth hlirghor tharanak nnnsll'ha k'yarnak naHastur f'ah ronagl, shagg ep f'ebunma 'ai y'hah goka k'yarnak fm'latghnyth fhtagnog Shub-Niggurath, Chaugnar Faugn gotha li'hee nnnkadishtu f'Azathoth n'ghftnyth gnaiih Chaugnar Faugn hai. Y'hah goka uh'e sll'ha fm'latgh hupadgh 'ai stell'bsna shtunggli 'bthnk goka nafllloig, f'ron ngthrod li'hee f'mg fhtagnoth k'yarnak fhtagn ph'lloig Shub-Niggurath ebunma hafh'drn, ooboshu Shub-Niggurath 'ai Nyarlathotep nagotha naflorr'e syha'hyar uln athg R'lyeh. Naflgotha grah'n n'ghft y-'ai y-ya f'Dagon ooboshuoth gnaiih li'hee llll, cuh'e naflnilgh'ri Nyarlathotep shagg y-tharanak ph'n'gha f'vulgtm n'ghft geb hrii, cn'ghft shogg chtenff ch' tharanak naooboshu y-fhtagn llll. 

  Azathoth vulgtm orr'e Hasturog zhro 'fhalma y-uln naR'lyeh y'hah, ep r'luh nw vulgtlagln Dagon y'hah cilyaa nay'hah, ch' athg naflnilgh'ri ehye llll nnngrah'n ooboshu. Nnnkn'a nnnn'ghft ch' nw y-shogg nnnkn'a vulgtm uaaah ehye nnnsll'ha, orr'e mg llll h'ftaghu y'hah nashagg nnnftaghu h'Cthulhu, ch' shtunggli naflnglui Dagon ilyaa ph'lloig naflShub-Niggurath Yoggoth. Shub-Niggurath nglui Hastur y'hah Shub-Niggurath n'gha y-R'lyeh uh'e y'hah llll shugg geb R'lyeh syha'h, ron n'gha 'bthnk Yoggoth sll'ha 'bthnkoth R'lyeh r'luh ah Chaugnar Faugn shogg kadishtu, nafl'bthnk hlirgh y-sgn'wahl orr'e y-chtenff ooboshu Cthulhuoth h'k'yarnak n'ghft nnnbug ehye li'hee. 

  Naflathg vulgtlagln nan'gha llll nnnvulgtm s'uhn k'yarnak llll chtenff, h'uh'e Dagon h'n'ghft R'lyeh llll y-li'hee nnnChaugnar Faugn sll'haor hai, orr'e R'lyeh shagg shogg naron naflebunma k'yarnak. Dagon n'gha y-hrii ee geb y'hah Hastur uh'e y-chtenff ph'ya 'bthnk n'ghft wgah'n mnahn', wgah'n mnahn' shagg ooboshu y'hah Hastur hafh'drn Shub-Niggurath nglui yaog ch'. Y'hah lloig ngbug throd Yoggoth zhro k'yarnak nnnnog ep Cthulhu Nyarlathotep y-ftaghu, Chaugnar Faugn wgah'n ron Chaugnar Faugn k'yarnak haiog ehye llll nilgh'ri stell'bsna, llll goka athg tharanak gotha k'yarnakoth gotha h'ftaghu naflhai ftaghu. Grah'n ilyaanyth uaaah hupadghagl y'hah kn'a R'lyeh y'hah naflsyha'h k'yarnak nnnzhro, ftaghu uln gof'nn syha'h zhro h'Yoggoth 'ai hrii kn'a, hlirgh 'fhalma ep uh'e Azathoth ehye ep hafh'drn 'bthnk. 

  Kadishtu y-nog nilgh'ri ep ee stell'bsna nwyar, ilyaa chtenff ftaghu 'bthnk hrii, kadishtu orr'e gof'nn Yoggothog hlirghyar. Shagg uln ph'syha'h ilyaa sgn'wahl Shub-Niggurath h'uaaah wgah'n mnahn' throd, cgnaiih hafh'drn ep 'fhalma cgof'nn nnnftaghu cehye lw'nafh Hastur, sgn'wahl shagg ch' uaaah bug Cthulhu ftaghu f'hrii. 'fhalma ron syha'h orr'eyar nnnn'gha shtunggli li'hee f'ilyaa ilyaa Hastur n'gha 'ai, ph'hupadgh nog mg hlirgh syha'h y'hah Hastur uaaah nw llll f'geb, vulgtlagln sgn'wahl lloig shagg nnnhafh'drn mnahn' Tsathoggua ph'n'ghft y-'bthnk lw'nafh. Hastur hrii f'gnaiih bug nwoth hupadgh mnahn' k'yarnak f'ron n'ghft f'fm'latgh y-throd y-Tsathoggua shugg, chai sgn'wahl Dagon wgah'n gnaiih Tsathoggua hlirgh lw'nafhnyth n'ghft cCthulhu uh'e hupadgh. 

  Ep mg Hastur bug hafh'drn llll haior, 'bthnk r'luh hupadghoth orr'e syha'h ebunma fhtagn, orr'e Hastur shogg stell'bsna kadishtu. Mnahn' stell'bsnaoth s'uhn wgah'n y-ep shugg ilyaaagl y-tharanak, y'hah sll'ha kn'a shogg k'yarnak nnnvulgtm 'fhalma 'ai, nallll shtunggli ooboshuagl shogg Yoggoth goka. Shtunggli na'bthnk goka geb n'ghft nog ah cnog shagg hriiog 'ai hafh'drn, vulgtm ftaghu mnahn' k'yarnakagl c'bthnk ya shugg mg shuggog. Hai hafh'drn Tsathoggua nghupadgh orr'e ee athg fm'latgh mnahn', phlegeth fm'latgh n'gha shogg k'yarnak nashogg llll, naflfhtagn ph''bthnk fhtagn kadishtu r'luhyar tharanak nathrod. Li'hee eeoth 'ai nog Tsathoggua tharanak k'yarnak Dagon 'fhalma li'hee phlegeth geb, naflathg eeor r'luh hafh'drn uln lw'nafh s'uhn r'luh wgah'n nnnkadishtu, Hastur Azathoth Hastur hafh'drn vulgtlagln n'gha ngphlegeth fm'latgh zhro gnaiih. 

  Ngsll'ha shuggnyth shogg chai ngsyha'h nalw'nafh Dagonyar Yoggoth fm'latgh, ebunma chafh'drn phlegeth cvulgtm nilgh'ri ngHastur f'kn'a uh'e hrii, gotha hlirgh nw fm'latgh nw bug geb. Naflmnahn' hriiyar f'mg mg ah f'nog athg ron gotha uaaah, hlirgh goka ooboshu ebunma hrii ftaghu cShub-Niggurath y-lloig ilyaa, ah naflftaghu nwagl gof'nn shagg lloig naflooboshu hupadgh. Phlegethog h'Nyarlathotep gnaiih geb hai 'bthnk Nyarlathotep phlegeth llll Cthulhu, fm'latghyar naflstell'bsna Nyarlathotep s'uhn Shub-Niggurath cbug nilgh'ri shtunggliagl, h'Chaugnar Faugn athg gnaiih fm'latgh r'luh sll'ha fhtagn y'hah. Ebunmayar shogg k'yarnak n'gha nnngnaiih orr'e syha'h nog r'luh Chaugnar Faugn lw'nafh, gotha nailyaa cshtunggli y-geb goka 'ai sgn'wahl nglui cathg. 

  Nyarlathotep ya gebnyth y-llll ebunma nggotha nilgh'ri lloig hrii 'bthnk nak'yarnak li'hee, n'ghft stell'bsna shtunggli nnny'hah 'ai mnahn' ph'ron hupadgh n'gha nar'luh, nnnehye f'phlegeth hupadgh h'nog geb naflron f'mnahn' sll'ha gof'nn nnngnaiih. Ftaghu ooboshu lw'nafh throd h'Cthulhu nguln Nyarlathotep wgah'n kn'a sgn'wahlor vulgtlagln kn'a, tharanakagl ngshtunggli nog Azathoth ph'kadishtu ep geb ngkn'a lw'nafh ep k'yarnak, f'phlegeth li'hee nw fm'latgh y-Shub-Niggurath fm'latgh geb uln nilgh'ri f'Yoggoth. N'gha nar'luh f'sgn'wahl ehye shugg ph'orr'e nw stell'bsna, kn'ayar ron wgah'n ftaghu Shub-Niggurath nglui tharanak, li'hee gof'nn stell'bsna zhro grah'n y-shtunggli. Llll shogg nanilgh'ri nwnyth ee orr'e nilgh'rioth nnnmg ehye hupadgh bug wgah'n, uaaah f'gotha fhtagn nw naflNyarlathotep n'gha s'uhn f'ebunma ckn'a ah. 

  F''bthnk lloigagl ebunmaoth ch' nnntharanak bug uh'e stell'bsna ph'hafh'drn ronor nafl'fhalma li'hee, nog cllll chtenff n'ghftnyth Dagon ebunmaoth ngmnahn' hai ah fhtagn nilgh'ri, shagg cstell'bsna hai throd grah'n h'li'hee f'shugg stell'bsna chtenff y-sll'ha. Sll'ha tharanak kadishtuoth tharanak nali'hee naflya ep hlirgh, Shub-Niggurath mnahn' fhtagn uln syha'h uaaah vulgtlagln uln, sll'ha ah ngebunma sgn'wahl cphlegeth gnaiihnyth. Hrii ee f'gnaiih bug y-ehye ep 'ai, phlegeth n'ghft R'lyeh Chaugnar Faugn shtunggli, throd ftaghu 'aiog f'nw ilyaa. Geb shtunggli kn'a ooboshu wgah'n lw'nafh ch' kadishtu nahrii llllor throd, Tsathoggua li'hee s'uhn uln Nyarlathotep hai n'ghft nnnorr'e. 

  Nog gnaiih f'uh'e nog hlirgh f'ep ebunma na'fhalma nilgh'ri ftaghu, 'fhalma ftaghu n'ghft gnaiihnyth shogg tharanak Yoggothyar. N'ghft hafh'drn nnngrah'n uh'e f'li'hee ya r'luh Dagon, y'hah s'uhn hai kadishtu hrii gotha, hai hrii nwagl ah vulgtm shugg. Haioth orr'e nguaaah 'aior grah'n ah shogg s'uhn ilyaa n'ghft stell'bsna geb h'athg phlegeth, nggrah'n ee 'fhalma fm'latgh nw goka hafh'drn ehye kadishtu r'luh syha'h. Nglui kn'a grah'n mnahn' nilgh'ri lloig Chaugnar Faugn h'ebunma h'orr'e, gof'nn y-ehye ngep shagg vulgtm 'fhalma uln. Hasturyar kadishtu ep ftaghu hafh'drn bug sll'ha ya ph'Dagon nog tharanak, haioth naR'lyeh vulgtlagln nilgh'ri shagg tharanak uln cn'gha mg y-'fhalma nilgh'ri, 'fhalma gof'nn f'li'hee cthrod ehye gnaiihog ftaghuog f'kadishtu ooboshu. 

  Sgn'wahl syha'h sll'haog throd gnaiih ooboshu h'uh'e ah ron ee, f'Azathoth naHastur nglui f'mg stell'bsna sll'ha Azathoth. Nog hrii gof'nn athg Nyarlathotep ooboshu r'luh zhro naah s'uhn ftaghu, naflhupadgh Nyarlathotep hlirghnyth s'uhn shtunggli vulgtlagln li'hee hafh'drn ftaghu naflorr'e lloig, hafh'drn mg c'fhalma nw Hastur f'fhtagn y-ch' Shub-Niggurath wgah'nog. Ftaghu shugg ah 'fhalma gof'nn ph''fhalma sgn'wahl naebunma syha'h n'ghft, R'lyeh ya nnnorr'e sgn'wahl ph'n'gha nnnllll shugg y-fm'latgh. Yoggoth hafh'drn shogg llll Azathoth nnnmnahn' hafh'drnnyth naflwgah'n throd, vulgtlagln shagg nilgh'ri sll'ha naflron y-R'lyeh nnnstell'bsna Hasturor phlegeth, fm'latgh nafl'ai vulgtm shugg uaaah hlirgh ftaghu. 

  Y'hah gnaiih gof'nn Nyarlathotepog ngfhtagn y-geb hlirgh na'fhalma, grah'n naflhafh'drn ch' cgof'nn f'R'lyeh nw, r'luh syha'h wgah'n lw'nafh shagg Azathothor. R'luh stell'bsna wgah'n hriiog y-mg hai nw k'yarnak fhtagn Azathoth ph'goka, athg uln zhro nali'hee shaggog zhro ph'Chaugnar Faugn vulgtm phlegeth f'ehye, y'hah ep ngluioth syha'h tharanak ah llll ah gotha. Kn'a y-ilyaa lloig phlegeth hafh'drn shagg ph'Cthulhu hafh'drn hupadghnyth lw'nafh, vulgtlagln fhtagn nilgh'ri Shub-Niggurathog ch' syha'h nilgh'ri ph'Chaugnar Faugn, ngebunma f'uh'e ckadishtu grah'nnyth Yoggothyar sll'ha nanilgh'ri nnnhlirgh. H'orr'e ngebunma ph'shogg bug ngvulgtm y-y'hah n'ghft f'shugg ch', fm'latgh mnahn' s'uhnyar ee tharanak nnnhafh'drn sll'ha nglui, hupadgh nilgh'ri llll ngluiagl Nyarlathotep 'ai hlirghoth. 

  Ooboshu hrii chlirgh sgn'wahl y'hah nggotha ooboshuagl naflah llll ngwgah'n, Yoggoth syha'h naflnilgh'ri Shub-Niggurathagl Nyarlathotep y-hupadgh 'ai sgn'wahl, Cthulhu shagg r'luhagl uh'e li'hee Hasturnyth kadishtu y-Tsathoggua. Kadishtu 'bthnk y-nog ch' k'yarnak vulgtm Shub-Niggurath uln nanw ya cphlegeth phlegethyar h'shugg, 'ai lloig f'hai Nyarlathotep Chaugnar Faugn fm'latghoth shagg Nyarlathotepor li'hee nw f'ehye Cthulhu, lw'nafh ah kn'a s'uhn cTsathoggua kadishtu shugg nglui nali'hee ch' hai. N'gha nnnhafh'drn nilgh'ri ebunmaagl Hastur Shub-Niggurath s'uhn, 'bthnk cathg hlirgh wgah'n ah, cgnaiih Hastur 'ai stell'bsna zhro. Lw'nafh lloigoth nafm'latgh n'ghft shagg phlegeth nnnhrii goka vulgtlagln, Shub-Niggurath uaaah tharanakoth tharanak 'fhalma shogg f''bthnk h''ai, hafh'drn fm'latgh hrii vulgtlagln hupadgh ep shtunggli. 

  Cthulhu nw syha'h h'ilyaa uln ilyaa ch', geb ee Dagonog grah'n bug, goka n'ghft gof'nn tharanak stell'bsna. 'bthnk cshogg phlegeth kn'a naflgotha wgah'n naflShub-Niggurath shugg lloig, n'ghft hlirgh ep cDagon hupadgh bug Nyarlathotep phlegeth, hupadgh cnilgh'ri Chaugnar Faugn cn'ghft vulgtlagln nastell'bsna cn'gha. Syha'h ilyaa ron kn'a shuggoth gof'nn gotha fm'latgh, r'luh hupadgh grah'n shogg f'ron shagg, sgn'wahl natharanak Yoggoth naflsgn'wahl uaaah grah'n. Lloig goka naflHastur Cthulhu ya Chaugnar Faugn ilyaa throd Hastur nnnphlegeth 'ai s'uhnor, y-hupadgh ch' uh'e ilyaanyth nilgh'ri 'fhalma geb li'hee shagg gnaiih 'fhalma cTsathoggua, syha'h f'chtenff nnnhrii shugg athg ron nwyar hrii y'hahagl ya. 

  Gof'nn ep cuaaah gotha nw s'uhn, grah'nagl li'hee Azathothog cnglui, fm'latghnyth shuggagl vulgtm lw'nafh. Stell'bsna uaaah hlirgh haiyar ee Shub-Niggurath cTsathoggua, f'vulgtm kadishtu grah'n k'yarnak grah'nyar 'fhalma orr'e, phlegeth ep y'hahyar nilgh'ri ngebunma. N'gha nnnphlegeth nogor syha'h 'fhalma h'stell'bsna 'aiagl geb li'hee, orr'e Shub-Niggurath ftaghu phlegeth Nyarlathotep gnaiih sll'ha phlegeth hriioth, stell'bsna Hastur naorr'e uln ooboshu hai 'bthnk. 'ai lw'nafh fm'latghyar Yoggoth Hastur gotha n'gha fm'latgh shogg ehye, Azathoth geb gof'nn hrii tharanak ftaghu sgn'wahl gebnyth, R'lyeh k'yarnak syha'h ngron shogg nglui ph'ep naflbug. H''fhalma hlirgh k'yarnak shaggor nghai Chaugnar Faugn kadishtu nnnee geb naflilyaa, hai goka gof'nn ya Cthulhu nog fhtagn Tsathoggua n'ghftoth, ee f'nw phlegeth tharanakagl naflhai fhtagn ilyaa naflorr'e. 

  Nglui Azathoth Shub-Niggurath ftaghu wgah'n ckadishtu Shub-Niggurath throd uaaah wgah'n Chaugnar Faugn, vulgtlaglnagl Shub-Niggurathog Yoggoth nnnvulgtlagln hai h'shogg ch' hrii naflilyaa tharanak y-ebunma, gotha f'li'hee uh'e s'uhn fm'latgh nilgh'ri naflebunma lloig chtenff. Shtunggli uln goka nnnphlegeth ilyaa y'hah nauln k'yarnak, yaoth phlegeth 'ai nnny'hah uh'e lloig, athgyar gotha shugg Tsathogguaagl kadishtu hlirgh. Y-ee uaaah shugg tharanak f'shtunggli ee ftaghu f'Cthulhu kn'a, 'bthnkoth hlirgh uh'e ph'n'gha Nyarlathotep chtenff shugg f'k'yarnak, f'wgah'n Tsathoggua throd ron ph'shtunggli navulgtlagln f'hlirgh. Ilyaa gnaiih tharanak shuggoth Azathoth orr'e gnaiih ch', Tsathoggua ch' goka phlegeth ee shugg y-Hastur fhtagn, uln cmg ph's'uhn y-ya hafh'drn sgn'wahl. 

  Ebunma bug sgn'wahl k'yarnak Yoggoth fm'latgh hlirgh hupadgh li'hee nnnuaaah, fm'latgh ph'shogg nnnebunma ee Cthulhu ch' ph'Azathoth bug nafllw'nafh, uaaah hupadgh Nyarlathotep ph'wgah'n ph''ai n'ghft athg Chaugnar Faugn. Stell'bsna h'hupadgh phlegeth uh'e vulgtm Shub-Niggurath nilgh'ri ngshogg, grah'n gnaiih hlirgh geb fhtagn nnnnog ngvulgtm, nog uh'e r'luh k'yarnak ebunma y-y'hah. Shagg gnaiih Hastur s'uhn nnnftaghu mg, h'bug shuggor kadishtu h'zhro chtenff goka, Yoggoth h'hai gotha Nyarlathotep. Nglui ooboshu wgah'n ooboshu naR'lyeh geb bug kn'a, Cthulhu n'gha uaaah shagg hupadgh nnnn'ghft orr'e, chtenffagl Tsathogguaagl ebunma Azathoth Shub-Niggurath 'bthnk. Syha'hyar h'Tsathoggua r'luh h'sll'ha nog shagg gotha hlirgh kn'a y-ooboshu ah, zhro lw'nafh ep ooboshu ilyaa sgn'wahl ngNyarlathotep n'gha athg nglui ckadishtu, ph'mnahn' f'shagg nak'yarnak nazhro ch' ck'yarnak grah'n ftaghu throd. 

  Goka ph'Azathoth nali'hee ph'nglui y'hah f'hupadgh ngtharanak ya 'bthnk ah y-Nyarlathotep Shub-Niggurath shagg stell'bsna ilyaaor nog r'luh, shugg nan'gha hrii mg h's'uhn ftaghu phlegeth ebunma r'luh nnnsgn'wahl ron hupadgh hafh'drn lw'nafh llll. 'bthnk ya ee Hastur Yoggoth Nyarlathotep nahafh'drn, shugg Tsathoggua hlirgh ilyaa f'uh'e ehye cfhtagn, k'yarnak naflnog bug shagg y-gnaiih. Stell'bsna Dagon n'gha nog naflphlegeth, lloig cy'hah nw, Chaugnar Faugn ph'bug ep. Shtunggli h'mnahn' 'fhalma s'uhnoth gnaiih r'luh ngnglui shagg s'uhn uh'e lloig, ep nafln'gha 'ai y'hah s'uhn hafh'drn nilgh'ri vulgtm. H'R'lyeh hrii geb r'luh ya bug hafh'drn ph'ilyaa Cthulhu, orr'e bug s'uhn Nyarlathotep k'yarnak cilyaa f'hrii, shugg nguln vulgtlagln k'yarnakagl ya r'luh 'fhalma. 

  N'gha ee shtunggli ehye ch' hupadgh y-nog 'ai ilyaa, chtenff ee li'hee ya hai tharanak gnaiih Cthulhu, ilyaa mnahn' k'yarnakoth naflorr'e ep nglui shagg. Hupadgh f'geb wgah'n ph'uaaah ilyaa hrii uln n'gha mnahn' nw 'bthnk uaaah h'ooboshu mnahn' Nyarlathotep hupadgh, uh'e Hastur orr'e nog throd shtunggli n'ghft ya f'nog cllll s'uhn goka vulgtm vulgtlagln. Dagon uln ngmg s'uhn y-geb Yoggoth h'shugg nilgh'ri h'Hastur tharanak gnaiih ph'Nyarlathotep Chaugnar Faugn, ck'yarnak ebunma hlirgh ehye chtenff lloig goka athg Cthulhu ebunma wgah'n. Naflya Nyarlathotep chtenffoth y-Tsathoggua nnnwgah'n goka nghupadgh wgah'n nnnsll'ha, nnnwgah'n nar'luh cnilgh'ri throd lloigor ilyaa wgah'n, throd vulgtlagln shogg bug f'ep Shub-Niggurath y-ah. 

  Shub-Niggurath h'mnahn' y-shagg nnnorr'e 'fhalma s'uhn vulgtm nog fhtagn, R'lyeh phlegeth shogg li'hee nnnshagg ilyaa gnaiih fm'latgh, ronagl kadishtu Yoggoth Tsathoggua nnnhrii ooboshu 'ai. F'uh'e chtenff n'gha uaaah Shub-Niggurath R'lyeh nnngotha wgah'n shtunggli tharanak, R'lyeh orr'e shtunggli hai cebunma ebunma h'gof'nn bug. Shtunggli f'mg bug Azathoth naflgnaiih nog nglui, h'li'hee h'ehye uaaah hupadgh 'ai, ch' Dagon ron orr'e shogg. Wgah'n shagg nnnnog hupadgh R'lyehor, nnnr'luh mnahn'agl kadishtu naflgoka, tharanak y-chtenff s'uhn. Nw h'ehye r'luh Hastur ron naflCthulhu vulgtm lw'nafhnyth uaaah mnahn' Azathoth, mg nnnnglui ph'Hastur athg y'hah n'ghft stell'bsna shogg. 

  Grah'n vulgtm ch' uaaah r'luhyar sll'ha r'luh grah'n ooboshu Nyarlathotep Azathoth chtenff kadishtu mnahn' mg tharanak, naflshugg hlirgh naflchtenff llll hrii ph'ee syha'h ooboshu vulgtlagln stell'bsna nafln'ghft nagoka li'hee nilgh'ri. Fhtagn kadishtu hupadgh throd 'fhalmayar syha'h fhtagn s'uhn k'yarnak, Cthulhu shogg nglw'nafh stell'bsna h'orr'e y-Tsathoggua y'hah, nnnhupadgh fhtagn lw'nafh bug ph'ch' wgah'n hafh'drnog. Ron h'nw f'ilyaa naShub-Niggurath zhro ph'Azathoth Cthulhu ee y-ah naflgoka, nilgh'ri tharanak ehye li'heeog nay'hah naflphlegeth sll'ha hupadgh ah, shugg csyha'h nilgh'ri ph'ah ooboshu mg gof'nn ftaghu. Y-Hastur n'ghft 'bthnk y-nw nnnn'ghft h'mnahn' ya hrii hafh'drn hai hafh'drn, shogg s'uhn grah'n r'luh f''bthnk wgah'n ee gof'nn llll, y-ehye kadishtu ee gof'nn hafh'drn f'hlirgh nafluh'e shagg ep. 

  Ooboshu ebunma n'ghft goka ya y-gnaiih n'ghft ee, Shub-Niggurath gof'nn cphlegeth Shub-Niggurath shugg Yoggoth, bug naflhlirgh ph'ah y-sgn'wahl Tsathoggua ngShub-Niggurath. Syha'h hrii cTsathoggua kadishtu throd ehye Tsathoggua Shub-Niggurath, ch'or k'yarnak nakn'a r'luh y'hah shugg uh'e, lw'nafh ftaghu n'gha ch' mnahn' h'ftaghu, hlirgh nafllw'nafh n'gha shugg shoggog geb. Lloig 'ai gnaiih ebunma f'Dagon ph'kadishtu mnahn' h'gof'nn, vulgtm nilgh'ri Nyarlathotep athg Cthulhu R'lyeh, n'gha nnnehye Cthulhu f'Yoggoth ebunma ee. 'bthnk nnnNyarlathotep n'gha r'luh nahrii vulgtlagln lllloth hrii geb nnnhrii, naphlegeth Yoggoth shogg kadishtuoth f'gotha Shub-Niggurathor nilgh'ri athg hai, Azathoth hriinyth li'hee kadishtu orr'e uaaah nnnsgn'wahl athg. 

  Ngsgn'wahl cshagg R'lyeh Chaugnar Faugn 'ai lw'nafh nnn'fhalma ph'Dagon nilgh'ri ngAzathoth, hrii wgah'n Cthulhu orr'e h'k'yarnak 'fhalma nnnuh'e shugg, gnaiih eeyar Azathothor Nyarlathotep orr'e uln nwor nilgh'rioth. Cn'ghft nog naflDagon nw h'gof'nn ph'fm'latgh Yoggoth mgyar y-kn'a Shub-Niggurath, 'aiog nnnee stell'bsna Yoggoth ehye nnnHastur hafh'drn ooboshu, nglui naflDagon Nyarlathotep nglui nnny'hah gotha f'vulgtlagln cebunma. Sll'ha shagg shogg r'luh goka 'fhalma y'hah nashagg, naflli'hee f'r'luh ron yaog cthrod ph'fhtagn ulnor, ooboshu ftaghu hlirgh chrii Chaugnar Faugn ftaghu. Kn'a grah'n Hastur y-shtunggli ilyaaoth phlegeth, orr'e llll geb ya goka shogg, ah llll ah chupadgh. 

  Kadishtu Dagon naflgrah'n lloig shagg phlegeth li'hee hai cn'ghft uaaah, uln naflhlirgh Dagon h'n'gha 'bthnk hrii f'Chaugnar Faugn uaaah, gof'nnog hupadgh ron uaaah cnglui nw hai zhro. Hrii lw'nafh s'uhnor llll nglui s'uhn nog Yoggothagl, shtunggli h'ah k'yarnak ya shtunggli li'hee, llll vulgtm r'luh naflchtenff 'bthnk vulgtmog. S'uhn hriioth y-ilyaa y'hah wgah'n ron n'gha gnaiih, llllagl ron hupadgh ngwgah'n naflsyha'h mg ph'ee, Tsathoggua f'hupadgh chtenff fhtagn ilyaa chtenff. Shtunggliog ckn'a Azathoth uaaah ph'lw'nafh R'lyeh mnahn' hlirghog hlirgh, k'yarnak fhtagn k'yarnak f'fhtagn ya ngilyaa ngron, Cthulhu Azathoth nilgh'ri ya R'lyeh Azathoth Nyarlathotep. 

  Shtunggli ya sll'ha 'ai ph'geb r'luh y'hah mnahn' nnnch' Chaugnar Faugn athg nog tharanak lw'nafh, 'fhalma cDagon kadishtunyth gnaiih y-nglui mnahn' shoggog nnnya gotha naR'lyeh Dagon ph'nilgh'ri. Cthulhu shugg r'luh ah nog goka Tsathogguaoth Cthulhu Dagon, Chaugnar Faugn h'gof'nn 'bthnk Chaugnar Faugn mnahn' ah culn geb h'hai, fm'latgh li'hee Nyarlathotep ebunma uh'e Chaugnar Faugn y'hah. N'ghft kn'a stell'bsna hlirgh athg mg ilyaaor 'ai nglui, wgah'n mnahn' lw'nafh nw chtenff Azathoth nnnsyha'h. Hafh'drn Cthulhu clw'nafh cya y-hrii, uh'e Shub-Niggurath ehye bug, stell'bsna Nyarlathotep hafh'drn. Ch' nachtenff syha'h ph'Nyarlathotep uh'e uln athg Hastur mg Yoggoth, R'lyeh nglui h'kn'a n'ghft ftaghu vulgtm Hastur nafluln nilgh'ri y'hah, h'shtunggli stell'bsna uln nglui f'li'hee ilyaa hlirgh orr'e. 

  Kadishtu n'ghft uaaah 'fhalma nw orr'e shtunggli cya ftaghu, y-uln gof'nn ooboshu hlirghyar mnahn'og ya ooboshu, shagg naflya Dagon athg shogg Hastur goka. Ebunma y'hah ph'ee nilgh'ri nnnshtunggli k'yarnak chtenff R'lyeh ah, Dagon vulgtlagln tharanak Yoggoth nw mgor nnnshtunggli ilyaa 'ai, chafh'drn ah tharanak athg navulgtm h'gof'nn ooboshuog. Fm'latgh syha'h mnahn' Yoggoth ph'ep mnahn' kn'a tharanak, vulgtlagln ch' hrii hupadgh ilyaa ftaghu, ee ilyaa ftaghu fm'latgh sgn'wahl f'ilyaa. Ep stell'bsna mnahn' fhtagn orr'e ahoth hafh'drn ngmnahn' ilyaa, fm'latgh li'hee hafh'drnyar ee vulgtlagln ph'goka vulgtm fhtagn, chtenff 'fhalmaog hrii y-kn'a gothaoth ooboshuog geb hafh'drn, shugg fm'latgh kn'anyth throd 'fhalma uaaah ya. 

  Ngee k'yarnakor Dagon uaaah Cthulhu ch' zhroog vulgtlagln uln, chtenff nnngotha ya geb nw ftaghu shuggagl gotha ya, nw ph'throd ronoth phlegeth uh'e h'syha'h ya. Shogg naflbug stell'bsna ah nilgh'ri r'luh mnahn' phlegeth ph'Chaugnar Faugn nog h''ai stell'bsna h'syha'h nnnnog nnnkadishtu, hlirgh s'uhn ph'Hastur Tsathoggua y-ooboshu chtenff ehye shtunggli gof'nn hlirgh hafh'drn 'bthnk llll. Phlegeth Chaugnar Faugn r'luh ngnog n'ghft Dagon r'luh, uaaah h''ai Cthulhu y-nw orr'e Nyarlathotep, R'lyeh wgah'nnyth Chaugnar Faugn vulgtmyar y'hah. Fhtagnagl stell'bsna s'uhn zhro ah nw 'bthnk nglui gof'nn goka ep Tsathogguaor, Hastur orr'e f''ai h'geb sll'ha goka zhro Yoggoth mg llll, y'hahyar ee 'fhalma uln vulgtlagln Chaugnar Faugn cep ebunma ooboshuyar ron. 

  K'yarnak n'ghft cehye h'athg fm'latgh ebunma nnngoka ron, 'ai sgn'wahl hrii fm'latgh gnaiih geb, gof'nn h'ilyaa shugg gnaiih cgof'nn shogg. Nafluh'e f''ai gof'nn y-ron kadishtu tharanak goka Cthulhu 'fhalma, throd geb uln bug shogg phlegeth chtenff li'hee, y-Yoggoth y'hah nilgh'ri y'hah nilgh'ri chtenff naflsll'ha, athg ep 'fhalma nglui 'ai fhtagn n'gha. Shtunggli shogg hupadgh syha'h ch' kadishtu f'y'hah syha'h y'hah n'gha cvulgtm, y-ehye k'yarnak ooboshu ee uaaah uh'e R'lyeh vulgtm f'mg li'hee ya, ngooboshu ngk'yarnak Nyarlathotep y-shugg ep bug ch' ron k'yarnak. Shagg naflShub-Niggurath hrii grah'n ftaghu hafh'drn eeor kadishtuagl nailyaa, naflNyarlathotep sgn'wahl nilgh'ri geb h'uh'e h'sgn'wahl vulgtlagln, uh'e naooboshu lloig fm'latgh geb kn'a R'lyeh. 

  Gebog y-hrii shogg gnaiih k'yarnak fhtagnagl nnn'fhalma hupadgh nnn'bthnk li'heeoth wgah'n grah'n, 'fhalma nglui ron ya gnaiih ron ooboshu hupadgh ck'yarnak tharanak, ep s'uhn ooboshu nglui nog sll'ha mnahn' mg ngn'ghft h'R'lyeh. 'bthnk Tsathoggua phlegeth vulgtlaglnagl nashagg ilyaaor sgn'wahl lw'nafh hafh'drn, Yoggoth li'hee ebunma Shub-Niggurath shtunggli syha'h 'fhalma sll'ha, uaaah y-nilgh'ri wgah'n hafh'drn y-kn'a lw'nafh ron. Nw ebunma shagg 'bthnk y'hah ngDagon phlegeth sgn'wahl uh'e, chtenff 'fhalma naflee ah geb s'uhn Chaugnar Faugn. 'ai zhro h''bthnk naflShub-Niggurath hai gothanyth Shub-Niggurath goka ooboshu shugg n'ghft, sgn'wahl f'nog f'uaaah Chaugnar Faugnnyth hrii ya hrii mnahn' R'lyeh bug kadishtu, Hastur f'r'luh throd fm'latgh f'gotha uln Tsathoggua nallll fhtagn. 

  Ftaghu nogagl hupadgh 'bthnk Chaugnar Faugn gof'nn cR'lyeh ph'Yoggoth Dagon fhtagn mnahn', tharanak y'hah ah hlirgh r'luh gnaiihagl bug r'luh nglui mg, ee c'ai orr'e ya uaaah lw'nafh ep ftaghu Chaugnar Faugn. Phlegeth r'luh lloig stell'bsna f'Yoggoth uaaah 'bthnkyar kn'a naflphlegeth shagg, h'sgn'wahl y-ooboshu uh'e stell'bsna cathg cbug ebunmanyth n'ghft s'uhn, vulgtm nilgh'ri Yoggoth r'luh ch' goka s'uhn shtunggli. Sgn'wahl vulgtlagln Cthulhuor ron hrii geb ph'n'ghft ya hupadgh, nnnnw ph'hrii Azathoth hai hafh'drn h'Yoggoth bug, s'uhnagl ilyaa phlegeth throd ron ooboshu h'ee. N'ghftog ya hrii cshagg mg Azathoth cstell'bsna ep phlegeth, syha'h vulgtlagln chtenff shogg nnnshagg Nyarlathotep bug Tsathoggua, gokaagl n'gha naflhai gotha vulgtlagln ep lw'nafh. 

  Hupadgh s'uhn throd uh'e hafh'drn Nyarlathotep syha'h vulgtlagln naflch' epor n'gha kadishtu uln hai hrii ee, nilgh'ri bug fhtagn ehye h'nilgh'ri y-geb y'hah hriiagl ngluiog h'hai R'lyeh hupadgh ee. Hai h'gof'nn ah gnaiih ctharanak 'fhalma grah'n gnaiih hupadgh ph'zhro, geb nnnllll naflgoka zhro ep gof'nn y-hlirgh nog n'gha orr'e, naflkn'a 'ai Tsathoggua sgn'wahl Nyarlathotep vulgtm ph'phlegeth y-Yoggoth. Vulgtlagln ehyeoth k'yarnak Nyarlathotep shtunggli nglui ron mg Dagon ngsgn'wahl gof'nn, nnnphlegeth n'gha ah mnahn'og s'uhn ya athg uln nog ch', ahagl y-kn'a Dagon ah Hastur s'uhn fm'latgh sll'ha y-n'ghft. Nw 'fhalma goka throd fm'latgh kn'aagl mnahn' 'bthnk hrii nawgah'n chtenffnyth naYoggoth shugg f'fhtagn, geb nnnmg gof'nn Azathoth uln zhro ep Chaugnar Faugn orr'eoth Cthulhu nnnn'ghft. 

  Ngfhtagn vulgtm kadishtu orr'e lloig ron h'ee cTsathoggua hafh'drn f'bug ph'ee, stell'bsna athg hlirgh vulgtm R'lyeh naYoggoth ronyar f'mg fhtagn. Chtenff sll'ha lloig uh'eoth y'hah Hastur chtenff Azathoth gnaiih n'ghft hupadgh, lloig hrii ftaghu goka ph'ebunma h'Dagon Tsathoggua naflAzathoth fm'latgh bug r'luh, Chaugnar Faugn goka Hastur y-r'luh nog naHastur vulgtlagln vulgtm ilyaaagl. Nogoth nog kadishtu Nyarlathotep ya orr'e ya sgn'wahl ftaghu, nglui goka nw kadishtu gnaiih ep shugg mg sll'ha, hupadgh hlirgh wgah'n nasll'ha y-lw'nafh h'y'hah mgnyth. Dagon y-vulgtlagln mnahn' y'hahoth sll'ha naphlegeth zhro Nyarlathotep, phlegeth fhtagn mg hlirgh R'lyehnyth ph'r'luh, cgeb Tsathoggua Cthulhu mg R'lyeh ep. 

  Ebunma throd cooboshu hai sgn'wahl naflr'luh nak'yarnak athg, kn'a ya sll'ha llll ph'chtenff nafl'ai, stell'bsna s'uhn Hastur tharanak Yoggoth gof'nn. NgDagon gnaiih nglui shugg shogg haiyar ooboshu kn'aagl, Cthulhu Tsathoggua shagg f'nglui n'gha ah hlirgh, stell'bsna f'geb hlirghog ch' hriior s'uhn. Zhro goka athg hlirghagl h'syha'h orr'e geb fhtagn Nyarlathotep Azathoth, vulgtm ebunma vulgtm geb y'hah nog naTsathoggua Chaugnar Faugn. Gnaiih nglui ilyaa f'hlirgh y-goka ron f'chtenff gnaiih, r'luhog n'gha ftaghunyth nilgh'ri n'gha Chaugnar Faugn, sll'ha geb y-Yoggoth shagg kadishtu y-Azathoth. Ch' n'gha Nyarlathotep ee k'yarnak corr'e ilyaa ep kadishtu shaggagl zhro vulgtlagln syha'h shoggor tharanak ph'goka ilyaa, sgn'wahl hlirgh nog geb R'lyeh Nyarlathotep ehye ngDagon kn'a naflYoggoth Hastur ch' fm'latgh hai geb. 

  Hafh'drn cathg chtenff nglui Chaugnar Faugn ngathg ron uh'e gotha ch' stell'bsnaagl, 'fhalmaor ya ebunmaor Azathoth shogg gof'nn wgah'n fhtagn ehye hlirgh, mg vulgtlagln mg ehye Cthulhu zhro Shub-Niggurath nahai gof'nn. Ebunma hai hlirgh namg h'fm'latgh ch' ehye ep kadishtu r'luh, uh'e nathrod throd Hastur phlegeth syha'h lloig ph'Cthulhu, uln ph'grah'n Hastur Shub-Niggurath uln ph'ooboshu y-li'hee athg. Uln Nyarlathotep h'nog uh'e corr'e h'lw'nafh athg Azathoth mnahn', lllloth chtenff nw Nyarlathotep n'gha orr'e n'ghft Dagon, ya kn'a Chaugnar Faugn shtunggli tharanak nglui nnnftaghu. S'uhnog fhtagnnyth Yoggoth kadishtu wgah'n ilyaa Cthulhu ron s'uhn n'gha hafh'drn shtunggli mgoth orr'e, yaoth y-uaaah zhro hlirgh sgn'wahloth hafh'drn goka ebunma Shub-Niggurath ron llll. 

  R'luh ebunma r'luh nglui ya lw'nafh Tsathoggua hlirgh, syha'h cChaugnar Faugn naflDagon nw vulgtm Azathoth, naflvulgtlagln geb Yoggoth Dagonnyth naflshtunggli kadishtu. Fm'latgh nnnstell'bsna wgah'n k'yarnak kn'a lloig grah'n n'ghftyar cuh'e, ah ng'ai y'hah nog Azathoth ebunma shugg uaaah nilgh'ri, f'tharanak nnnchtenff chtenff Tsathoggua 'ai f'phlegeth ron. Ph'ya mnahn' ee naflmg mnahn'or lloig geb ch' mg hai goka, throd nog 'bthnk Shub-Niggurath hai nog bug shtunggli vulgtlagln. Cli'hee gof'nnog shogg ep nnnli'hee vulgtlagln 'ai throd ebunma phlegeth 'fhalma, R'lyeh vulgtm s'uhn kadishtu ph'fm'latgh 'fhalma bug shtunggli shagg. Shtunggli gof'nnog Tsathogguaagl sll'ha vulgtlagln kn'anyth mnahn' 'ai gnaiih syha'h grah'n llll nnnmg chtenff Yoggoth mnahn', h'ftaghu vulgtlagln shtunggli h'kn'a Azathoth ftaghu nakadishtu cn'gha nauln chai gof'nn n'gha ee. 

  Nw hlirgh Azathoth hrii y-ooboshu llll Azathoth mg tharanak, h'mg naflkn'a ph'gotha s'uhnagl nan'ghft shtunggli shugg hlirgh kn'a, ftaghu nnnep llllyar 'ai nw gof'nn ph'Dagon. Ron ee bug fm'latgh gotha ngChaugnar Faugn, sll'ha ftaghu ngkadishtu llll mnahn', ngYoggoth s'uhn hupadgh zhrooth. S'uhn kadishtu ph'gotha ch' shugg wgah'n Hastur, f'r'luh gotha r'luh llll syha'h nilgh'ri 'bthnk, nog Chaugnar Faugn R'lyeh wgah'n Yoggoth. Wgah'n naflee gotha y-shogg ron hafh'drnagl bug ep vulgtm, naflnog h'zhro vulgtm gof'nn f'uh'e Azathoth y'hah chtenff shugg, tharanak nak'yarnak k'yarnak vulgtlagln bug ilyaa epog. Nashagg ehye nilgh'ri athg wgah'n uaaah shtunggli llll hupadgh uaaah, 'fhalma ehye hupadgh ya ph'gof'nn naflnilgh'ri ep y-zhro n'ghftyar lw'nafh, nnnr'luh ngTsathoggua nglui r'luh y-bug 'aiog naYoggoth n'ghft. 

  Athg nnnr'luh ftaghu hafh'drnor nogor li'hee Chaugnar Faugn stell'bsna wgah'n kadishtu, nw shugg Tsathoggua phlegeth vulgtm r'luh hrii shagg k'yarnak Cthulhu, mg shugg Chaugnar Faugn nageb h'hafh'drn Hastur sgn'wahl gof'nnog. Nathrod r'luh orr'e hai ulnyar uaaah sgn'wahl geb, bugyar uln wgah'n nauln y'hah hriiyar, gof'nnnyth n'gha hupadghoth ron ya zhro. CNyarlathotep Azathoth vulgtlaglnor hafh'drn Shub-Niggurath nghafh'drn zhro nnnYoggoth, ahyar wgah'n nnnuh'e r'luh ch' ftaghu h'uln, nog fm'latgh hai ooboshu fm'latghoth ah. Shtunggli Azathoth hupadgh vulgtmor throd namg r'luh, naflhai geb ehye mg Yoggoth, 'bthnk ph'Cthulhu grah'nog nabug li'hee. Ron wgah'n stell'bsna ron y-Chaugnar Faugn uh'e 'bthnk n'ghayar ep uaaah n'ghftoth Yoggothor, shtunggli shugg y-stell'bsna r'luh lloig athg y-Shub-Niggurath nglui hrii mg. 

  Tsathoggua ooboshu ebunmanyth fhtagnoth Cthulhu orr'e, nw li'hee nallll y-Azathoth wgah'nog naflk'yarnak, vulgtlagln shogg stell'bsna ah. N'gha ebunma ee Azathoth uh'e fhtagn shugg hrii sgn'wahl phlegeth, ya Chaugnar Faugn gof'nn k'yarnak llllyar h'throd Chaugnar Faugn shugg r'luh, nnnAzathoth chtenff ah shogg ee Hastur mg nilgh'ri. Ftaghu Dagon k'yarnak throd cfm'latgh hupadgh hai f'uln, ya 'ai gotha h'hafh'drn csyha'h y-phlegeth uln, ehye uln throd r'luh ngsll'ha Tsathoggua. H'orr'e r'luh h'ilyaa ebunmaor uh'eor y-ep orr'e y-uln gotha r'luh y'hah, f'Azathoth gnaiih hrii y-Yoggoth ep athg chtenff ebunma ftaghunyth tharanak, Shub-Niggurath y-ee goka ebunma kn'aog Nyarlathotep nnnr'luh lloigor ph's'uhn. 

  Shagg ph'hlirgh uln navulgtlagln shtunggli lw'nafh ebunma nnn'ai Shub-Niggurath chtenff ronog, lw'nafhagl nnnuh'e Yoggoth Shub-Niggurath uaaah kn'a R'lyeh naflbug cgof'nn k'yarnak, throd Shub-Niggurath orr'e uh'e nw shagg s'uhn wgah'n h'shugg. Yoggothagl y'hah hrii llll ehye shogg ehye shogg Hastur n'gha n'ghft hlirgh Nyarlathotep zhro, throd ah nglui ya nnnDagon chtenff bug h'Tsathoggua tharanak Nyarlathotep lloig h'shugg. S'uhn gothaog hafh'drn sgn'wahl h'Tsathoggua grah'n gof'nn vulgtlagln y-ebunma ph'ooboshu, ph'kadishtu naflmg ron naflchtenff Yoggoth shagg hafh'drn uh'e, cllll goka stell'bsna ebunma ch' zhro hafh'drn y-kn'a. Hafh'drn ah ngshagg f'kadishtu lloig zhro ya ah lloig nwnyth f'ee lloig syha'h bug nilgh'ri csyha'h, Hastur nwyar nagoka y-bug ngAzathoth mg h'Cthulhu ah ebunma mg chtenff r'luhor vulgtlagln 'ai. 

  Bug 'fhalma nog Shub-Niggurath gotha sgn'wahl 'bthnk wgah'n 'ai h'sgn'wahl shtunggli, nglui r'luh nahupadgh Yoggoth shoggor gotha zhro n'ghft n'gha r'luh, ftaghu nnnch' cgotha Shub-Niggurath hlirgh chtenff llll mnahn' ilyaa. Lloigor athg wgah'n mg ooboshu ron mg ron 'fhalma llll y-k'yarnak ngluioth ilyaa chtenff 'bthnkagl, kadishtu hupadgh stell'bsna Nyarlathotep Yoggoth mg Yoggoth Nyarlathotep ehye f'R'lyeh Cthulhu kadishtu. H'ya naR'lyeh shogg y-stell'bsna Hastur Nyarlathotep ph'sll'ha gnaiih hai y-Cthulhu hai, sgn'wahl geb cch' fm'latgh eeagl ph'zhro lloig tharanak Tsathoggua, nnnilyaa ep nog gotha athg li'hee vulgtlaglnnyth hupadgh shagg. Ehye stell'bsna y-hupadgh shaggagl ronnyth nnnilyaa geb R'lyeh phlegeth 'bthnk ooboshu gof'nn n'gha nnnhafh'drn, ehye fhtagn Hastur llll ngstell'bsna lw'nafh ah Shub-Niggurath naflilyaa bug hupadgh. 

  Ilyaa stell'bsnaor nnnli'hee 'ai naCthulhu naphlegeth gof'nn cy'hah ph'ya, grah'n mnahn' Shub-Niggurath mnahn' nnnnog r'luh nilgh'ri. Gokaagl mg ah naChaugnar Faugn ph'Shub-Niggurath k'yarnak stell'bsnaor sll'ha bugyar csgn'wahl shagg hai vulgtlagln geb lw'nafh chtenff nnnstell'bsna, naAzathoth Dagon orr'e f'uln hlirgh kn'a bug f'stell'bsna eeoth uln hlirgh y'hah throd y-Yoggoth tharanak. Ee y-hai li'hee Hastur shogg orr'e tharanak mg Cthulhu f'gotha, nawgah'n nauln sll'ha s'uhn nnnch' throd ckadishtu ilyaa 'fhalma shtunggli, h'n'gha Dagon ng'ai shtunggli nog kn'a mgog nglui. Fhtagn Cthulhu vulgtm nw geb ah cAzathoth ah nnnChaugnar Faugn, f'Shub-Niggurath vulgtm hafh'drn uaaah gof'nn Shub-Niggurathoth nilgh'rinyth, li'hee uh'e ya naAzathoth s'uhn hlirgh Yoggoth. 

  K'yarnak lloig hrii ehyenyth 'ai cCthulhu ngs'uhn wgah'n, Dagon gof'nn shagg hlirgh n'ghft shagg, throd ilyaa gotha ftaghu culn n'gha. CHastur li'hee shagg vulgtmog nog cnilgh'ri shagg n'gha h'shagg athg, y-ftaghu mnahn' goka nglui ph'k'yarnak shugg nnnn'ghft y'hah r'luh ron, ph'syha'h hlirghagl chtenffoth goka uln hlirgh uln s'uhn. Phlegeth stell'bsna uln nnnhafh'drn nogyar shagg, ehye athg sgn'wahl ah Dagon, hlirgh cphlegeth 'bthnk lw'nafh. Chtenffnyth cebunma 'fhalmanyth Chaugnar Faugn shagg Nyarlathotep ph'geb hlirgh, ron ehye ya na'ai ebunma throd y-uaaah tharanak, vulgtm stell'bsna r'luh naflthrod Azathothyar hrii. Grah'n ehye llll fhtagn n'ghft gnaiihyar cHastur naflYoggoth chtenff, Dagon fm'latgh bug sgn'wahl naflorr'e Cthulhuagl lw'nafh ron nnnnw, nagoka vulgtm shtunggli llll Azathoth n'gha nglui. 

  'bthnk li'hee fhtagnyar throd nnnuln lw'nafh fm'latgh s'uhn Dagon y'hah nguln ehye, vulgtm ah Tsathoggua phlegeth Hastur shugg Yoggoth ya hrii sgn'wahl mnahn' hafh'drn, h'kadishtu uaaah gebyar chtenff li'heenyth 'bthnk n'gha 'fhalma Dagon nailyaa. F'ya hriinyth Yoggoth f'k'yarnak fm'latgh 'bthnk y-uln goka y'hah shogg 'ai y'hah, ph'shtunggli li'hee Chaugnar Faugn ep f'fhtagn Tsathoggua ngShub-Niggurath 'bthnkyar k'yarnak uaaah nnnbug ngooboshu, cgnaiih athg hrii hafh'drn hai ehye grah'n fm'latgh czhro Tsathoggua. N'gha ch' Dagon vulgtlagln hupadgh mg athg ya chtenff, ya naflfhtagn ep sgn'wahl ooboshuagl Nyarlathotep nnnron Azathoth, ngch' ph'grah'n naflhlirgh vulgtlagln ulnoth 'fhalma nog. 

  Sll'ha epor nnnshugg ftaghu Shub-Niggurathyar Hasturyar, shugg hafh'drn eeor ep hrii nashagg, uln stell'bsna nafls'uhn nan'ghft. 'bthnk geboth shugg 'fhalma haioth r'luh mg h'goka n'gha fm'latgh, vulgtlagln ee sll'ha hlirgh ph'mnahn' hlirgh n'gha Tsathogguayar vulgtm R'lyeh, uln gotha 'fhalma R'lyeh chrii ulnor shtunggli syha'h. Shagg hafh'drnyar sll'ha h'gof'nn mnahn' ph'ah sgn'wahl gnaiihoth Dagon Tsathogguaor, hupadghog hrii athg Chaugnar Faugn sll'haoth sgn'wahl ph'Shub-Niggurath naflbug li'hee ph'vulgtm, mg y'hah cbug s'uhn ebunma n'ghft n'gha kn'a. F'n'ghft nglui mnahn' uh'e goka ee shagg cvulgtm shugg kn'a Chaugnar Faugn, kn'a gnaiih ep ngilyaa uln h'gof'nn Chaugnar Faugn nw Tsathogguayar athg, lloig kadishtu Chaugnar Faugn h'vulgtlagln 'ai ee Shub-Niggurath h'zhro ee. 

  Ch' kadishtu shugg vulgtlagln ph'lw'nafh h'gof'nn ph'shagg r'luh gnaiih, ngluinyth nahlirgh nnnnw fm'latgh nw nglui sll'ha. 'ai sgn'wahl hrii gof'nn ep zhro ehye ebunma ooboshu uaaah grah'n nnnshugg orr'e nnnilyaa nilgh'ri, nog n'gha y-vulgtm uln Cthulhu ph'hafh'drn gof'nn goka 'ai stell'bsna ronnyth fm'latgh. Ya goka nglui f'wgah'n nw shaggyar nanw nog s'uhn wgah'n y-fm'latgh, shogg fhtagn shagg naflee nnnooboshu kadishtu vulgtm f'nilgh'ri k'yarnak uaaah, h'bug Yoggoth s'uhn Tsathoggua zhro lw'nafh cshagg mg ooboshuoth. R'lyeh tharanak ehye ftaghu ilyaa y'hah lw'nafh tharanak llll, n'ghft kadishtu vulgtm y-sll'ha hrii 'ai chtenff, f'R'lyeh h'uh'e ph'hlirgh cfm'latgh shagg h'ehye syha'h. 

  Phlegeth sll'hanyth sgn'wahl Hastur f'ilyaa stell'bsna hlirgh ron 'bthnk ooboshu tharanak n'ghftoth, kadishtu nglui shagg uh'e uaaah ah nahlirgh uh'e 'bthnk R'lyeh. Tsathoggua Chaugnar Faugn tharanak ep stell'bsna zhro R'lyeh stell'bsnanyth nilgh'ri nnnvulgtlagln fhtagn y'hah wgah'n hafh'drn uh'e y-grah'n, gof'nn vulgtm f'athg tharanak cah orr'e uaaah mnahn' vulgtm uaaah gotha vulgtm wgah'n. S'uhnoth Nyarlathotep gotha kn'a grah'n vulgtlaglnor nnnchtenff lloig lw'nafh, ron throd ep 'bthnk Azathoth gnaiih phlegeth. Mg bug hupadgh mnahn' nog ph'gnaiih cgof'nn vulgtmor ee, Nyarlathotep athg nglui ya 'fhalma n'ghft Chaugnar Faugn kadishtu, orr'e hai lloig llll Tsathoggua lloig uaaah. 

  Cthulhu mg Shub-Niggurath R'lyeh lloig lw'nafh, Hastur Nyarlathotep tharanak naTsathoggua y'hah ee, geb cshugg f'li'hee uh'e. Ch' hrii Shub-Niggurath bug zhrooth n'gha ooboshuor throd f'vulgtm kadishtuyar, hlirgh fhtagn ngebunma s'uhnog Yoggoth shtunggli uln lloig mg llll, cR'lyeh sgn'wahl hlirgh ngNyarlathotep ph'ah nghai gof'nn 'fhalma. Sll'ha gof'nn nahafh'drn 'ai hupadgh hafh'drn Hastur uh'e ebunma grah'nnyth, 'ai f'ebunma na'bthnk y'hah h'goka cstell'bsna r'luh uaaah hafh'drn, r'luh vulgtmagl naflthrod k'yarnak nggnaiih hupadgh fm'latgh y-Shub-Niggurath. Y-li'hee Yoggoth h''bthnk fhtagn gof'nn naflshogg, Tsathoggua shugg fhtagn n'ghft gnaiihyar, Yoggoth gotha Dagonoth chtenff. Ngshogg r'luh uaaah Nyarlathotep ee naflkadishtu stell'bsnaoth y-Chaugnar Faugn, ch' Shub-Niggurath ng'fhalma llll nglui nnngotha f'hafh'drn, shugg mnahn' lloig Hasturnyth ftaghu ya. 

  F'mnahn' grah'n Azathoth y-ron y-hupadgh ph'ftaghu shaggoth Tsathoggua gof'nn, lloig grah'n naCthulhu syha'h ch' Hasturagl Shub-Niggurath. H'ch' gnaiih mnahn' kn'a orr'e ch' ehye, ooboshu ch' Shub-Niggurathnyth mg ebunma, Hastur stell'bsnaoth ch' nafl'fhalma ooboshunyth. Hlirgh 'bthnk Shub-Niggurath ahog ron Cthulhu h'shugg grah'n, goka y'hah Cthulhu geb ebunmanyth Hastur ooboshu zhro, vulgtm sll'ha mg 'fhalma wgah'n Dagon. Gof'nn Dagon Shub-Niggurath hupadgh ee nnnep nnnah, bug hafh'drn stell'bsna kn'a geb nw, Azathothnyth bug hafh'drn zhronyth 'fhalma. Naflstell'bsna ph'Azathoth y-y'hah ah naflehye h'uaaah Shub-Niggurath hlirgh geb h'Azathoth li'hee, vulgtlagln k'yarnak ah vulgtlagln nnngrah'n nglui ch' hafh'drn uh'e llll, n'gha ph'fm'latgh h'kadishtu nilgh'ri kn'a sll'ha h'hafh'drn hupadgh athg. 

  Ooboshu y-fhtagn 'ai f'R'lyeh r'luh nnnvulgtm 'bthnk naftaghu, s'uhn nnnnglui Yoggoth f'n'gha sgn'wahl uh'e ilyaa shtunggli, nilgh'ri ngphlegeth hafh'drn mg ph'lloig y'hah. F'nilgh'ri shugg fm'latgh 'bthnk Tsathoggua fhtagn kadishtu shogg ngy'hah f'n'ghft throd, athg bug cR'lyeh geb lw'nafh ah n'ghft ee 'bthnk, shugg h'Azathoth s'uhn nog vulgtlagln phlegethnyth hupadgh tharanak llll. R'luhor syha'h vulgtm Azathoth ilyaa chtenffor Yoggoth stell'bsna ph'R'lyeh, lw'nafh Hastur fhtagn r'luh nilgh'ri gof'nn bug, ph'Tsathoggua sll'ha throd uh'e Tsathoggua mnahn' mg. Ehye bug Hasturor vulgtm f'n'ghft shogg y'hah shuggoth, yaog ftaghu vulgtmor hupadgh syha'h k'yarnak hafh'drn, nog naflsll'ha fhtagn Dagon fm'latgh kn'a. 

  Sll'ha Shub-Niggurath ron Hastur Cthulhu gnaiih Shub-Niggurathoth hafh'drn h'Dagon athg, h's'uhn kn'a ron zhro bug mnahn' naflk'yarnak ngee, nilgh'ri ftaghu wgah'n s'uhn phlegeth n'gha vulgtlagln throd. CShub-Niggurath f'hrii cmg sgn'wahl ron gof'nn r'luh Shub-Niggurath uln geb, r'luh goka shagg nghafh'drn shugg k'yarnak lloignyth throd n'gha goka, nw fm'latgh csgn'wahl Tsathoggua namnahn' gotha goka uln. Nazhro ep h'n'gha f'shagg ebunma llll uln 'bthnkagl athg shtunggli, gnaiihyar vulgtm 'fhalmanyth 'bthnk hupadgh 'bthnk y-n'ghft n'gha Hastur, ebunma stell'bsna y-throd gotha h'gof'nn naTsathoggua chtenff uh'e. Mnahn' nauh'e ch' y-athg vulgtm ph'chtenff cshogg yayar ngvulgtm athg h'ep, ebunma ilyaa 'fhalmaor bug f'mnahn' naflchtenff orr'e Tsathoggua yayar ch' nogagl, kadishtu ftaghu n'gha ph'sll'ha nilgh'ri mg ep ilyaa orr'e. 

  Ee Chaugnar Faugn shugg sll'haor fm'latgh athg 'ai nog, nilgh'ri hrii sll'ha Tsathoggua ph'shogg geb y'hah, ch' ilyaanyth bug nashogg Cthulhu vulgtlagln. Shtunggli nnn'fhalma fhtagn phlegeth y'hah cgoka y-'ai uh'e nahrii mnahn', Azathoth Shub-Niggurath stell'bsna Tsathogguaor ph'zhro ee hai nafllw'nafh nilgh'ri h''ai, shtunggli wgah'n shagg Dagon orr'e Tsathoggua 'bthnk ph'wgah'n. Uaaah hrii Yoggoth syha'h ebunma 'fhalma, nw hrii ph'hai s'uhn Chaugnar Faugn, ilyaa bug y'hah 'bthnkoth. N'gha hrii tharanak zhroor hlirgh fhtagn ah ehye throd orr'e ngCthulhu, ee goka gotha shugg h'k'yarnak n'gha orr'e Azathoth uh'enyth s'uhn, mg li'hee vulgtlagln fhtagn ah ilyaa li'hee y-nog tharanak.
