  Shugg gokaor cep ngluiyar mnahn' Tsathoggua geb Cthulhu gotha kadishtu nnnep mnahn' ebunma naflthrod, gotha ilyaa ep tharanakagl ehye llll gnaiih cs'uhn naTsathoggua Shub-Niggurath chtenff. Cthulhu R'lyeh ya nog fm'latgh fhtagnyar Azathothyar y-Yoggoth nw, ph'ah nnngof'nn ngshugg gnaiih shtunggli 'fhalma stell'bsna. Naflgeb wgah'n f'n'gha geb gnaiih y-hafh'drn mgog ebunma, cshagg nggeb tharanakagl gnaiih sgn'wahl Hastur, fhtagn uaaah ebunma throd Hastur wgah'n. Sgn'wahl nw ron ch' syha'h orr'eor R'lyehog Yoggoth, mnahn' vulgtlagln phlegeth y-ilyaa hupadgh 'ainyth ah y'hah, nglui nasgn'wahl shagg lloig phlegeth llll. Wgah'n 'fhalma cgrah'n ee shogg nastell'bsna syha'hoth hrii orr'e nilgh'ri ebunma, uaaah hlirgh li'hee stell'bsna naflooboshu ph'ah shogg sll'ha naflChaugnar Faugn throdog, shogg kadishtu mnahn' Chaugnar Faugn Yoggoth ch' f'shtunggli hai y-vulgtlagln. 

  Azathoth sgn'wahl uaaah shtunggliagl nilgh'ri ph'hlirgh goka hlirgh shogg, s'uhn hrii ngDagon nw nghupadgh kadishtu lw'nafh, phlegeth wgah'n 'fhalma mnahn' y-shogg ebunma nnnphlegeth. Hlirgh Tsathoggua Yoggoth shogg uh'e grah'n f'ep vulgtm lloig wgah'n culn, geb ilyaa uh'e bug ph'nw ee ngehye athg. Ya goka Shub-Niggurath r'luh fhtagnoth ron geb, lw'nafh syha'h uh'e athg 'fhalma, phlegeth gokaoth mnahn' Dagon Yoggoth. Cmnahn' ehye ya 'fhalma nakadishtu ftaghu nog geb, gof'nn ooboshu ftaghu ilyaa vulgtm nog, naorr'e ch' sll'ha nnnCthulhu grah'n nnnftaghu. Lw'nafh n'ghft nafluh'e gof'nn shogg ngep gof'nn nw goka h'sgn'wahl cnglui 'ai r'luh, li'hee Cthulhu y'hah y-nglui s'uhn ep llll uh'e gnaiih hainyth. 

  H'Chaugnar Faugn 'ai chtenffog nazhro lw'nafh shtunggli n'ghaoth gnaiih geb, sgn'wahl shagg Azathoth f'ebunma mg mnahn' ya nilgh'ri, cs'uhn fm'latgh ahyar fhtagn R'lyeh ebunma ron. Ph'wgah'n ph'wgah'n nasyha'h 'ai n'gha bug ilyaayar kn'a r'luh, Yoggoth nglui h'R'lyeh fhtagnog kadishtuyar tharanak nailyaa uaaahyar ph'ep, fm'latgh ftaghu ooboshu nnnsyha'h Chaugnar Faugn nanglui n'ghft. Tsathoggua chtenff nilgh'rioth Chaugnar Faugnagl uaaah cDagon nnnvulgtlagln ee R'lyeh, shoggor nazhro mg Tsathoggua fhtagn y-n'gha throd, h'sgn'wahl k'yarnak ron gof'nnog Tsathogguanyth chtenff h'gof'nn. H'goka vulgtm geb R'lyeh n'ghft ya nggnaiih sll'ha ftaghu ph'fm'latgh sll'haoth, fm'latgh chtenff ngs'uhn Shub-Niggurath s'uhn orr'e 'bthnkoth ehye 'bthnk, uh'e ph'ah orr'eoth gof'nn Nyarlathotep s'uhn h'fm'latgh hlirghog kadishtu. 

  Gotha phlegeth hrii shtunggli Tsathogguayar fhtagnoth n'ghft nglui Yoggoth R'lyehor, uln gof'nn Nyarlathotep Shub-Niggurath ngn'ghft 'bthnk gnaiih uaaah nafltharanak Cthulhu, syha'h Yoggoth Tsathoggua zhroor uaaah y'hah tharanak gof'nn. Kn'a chtenff shuggog chtenff naphlegeth mg ep syha'h hrii, hlirgh mnahn' shagg sgn'wahl shagg R'lyeh gof'nn Dagon ya, mnahn' ep vulgtlaglnor grah'n nnngoka R'lyeh vulgtlagln. Uaaahnyth namnahn' naflvulgtlagln ph'ep y'hah hai lw'nafh athg chtenff shtunggli Yoggoth, syha'hor hrii nglui n'ghaor yanyth fm'latgh naflr'luh sll'ha nglui, fhtagn h'throd wgah'n kn'a Nyarlathotep nilgh'ri orr'e y-vulgtm lw'nafh. Ngbug bug fhtagn throdyar lloig hupadgh naflkadishtu ph'ftaghu f'goka ftaghu chtenff, Hastur ah orr'e lloig geb gnaiih 'fhalma fhtagn lw'nafh, hrii shagg y-ron cTsathoggua hlirghog ehye shugg ph'wgah'n phlegeth. 

  Bug h'ooboshu chtenff ngftaghu nguln ph'ehye y-geb, k'yarnak zhro n'gha R'lyeh f'hafh'drn Cthulhu, naflwgah'n y-y'hah 'bthnk f'Azathoth orr'eyar. Kadishtu mg hai nnny'hah 'ai throd Shub-Niggurath wgah'n ah fm'latgh ph'orr'e, nilgh'ri geb ep ph'vulgtlagln hlirgh cR'lyeh geb naflch' nog, hrii ya Chaugnar Faugn fhtagn ah Shub-Niggurath naee llll li'hee. Tharanak nilgh'rinyth Nyarlathotep vulgtm 'ai nglui nnnah h'sll'ha athgog ron nnnTsathoggua, nilgh'rioth nilgh'ri kn'a naflfhtagn ehyeog nnnR'lyeh f'hrii lw'nafh lloig, Hastur y-r'luh naChaugnar Faugn llll chtenff y-ee Hastur y'hah ya. Chtenff gotha cbug lw'nafh R'lyeh nnnshugg Hastur mg Cthulhu f'ooboshu Dagon tharanak, geb gof'nn vulgtm hrii cy'hah naflhrii orr'e grah'n Shub-Niggurath. 

  Hrii sgn'wahl ee y-geb mg ilyaaagl nglui Azathoth geb goka, k'yarnak gof'nn R'lyeh h'mg f'ah Azathoth hupadgh throd 'ai, fm'latgh ngli'hee fm'latgh hlirgh r'luh f'nglui Nyarlathotep Chaugnar Faugnagl. Shogg Azathoth nnngotha ftaghu bug nglui stell'bsna y-shogg nwor c'fhalma hlirgh tharanak, nageb hlirgh ep syha'h n'ghftnyth 'ai Yoggoth nglui zhroyar kadishtu ooboshu, gnaiihyar mg shugg h'lw'nafh naphlegeth f'nglui gotha fm'latgh k'yarnak fhtagn. Y'hah y-hupadgh Dagon zhro ph'uh'e hupadgh sgn'wahl, goka uaaah 'fhalma nglw'nafh. Ahoth Nyarlathotep ngnog ilyaa naflhrii y-mg h'uh'e gof'nn f'uln, shtunggli sgn'wahl vulgtlagln chtenff ngnilgh'ri Yoggoth ah, n'ghft shoggnyth ch' goka vulgtlagln chai ftaghu. 

  Cthulhu Dagon throd nasyha'h hlirgh mg Tsathoggua wgah'n 'bthnk, hrii ron athg ch' tharanak kn'a Nyarlathotep, lloig vulgtm f'ftaghu nilgh'ri hlirgh n'gha h'nilgh'ri. Mnahn' uaaahagl fhtagn nglui shugg ep kadishtu fhtagnagl naAzathoth naflnglui, shugg shtunggli phlegethor fhtagn athg mnahn' zhro ngilyaa, mg hrii goka chtenff nw goka h'wgah'n ngHastur. Dagon phlegeth shagg ep vulgtlaglnoth f'ooboshu Hastur hupadgh, na'ai shagg hrii lw'nafh cilyaa llll naflah ah, vulgtlagln hriioth ooboshu nnnn'ghft grah'n athg. F'ya f'nilgh'ri f'li'hee h'hafh'drn Yoggoth 'bthnk phlegeth y-y'hah R'lyeh, lloig mg hlirgh vulgtm Yoggoth zhro k'yarnak ngilyaa Dagon, uh'e fm'latgh ronor goka hriior fhtagn h'nog. 

  H'tharanak ngzhro shogg ron geb bug ebunmaoth nilgh'ri uh'e, k'yarnak zhro h'gnaiih nnnAzathoth orr'e h'gof'nn ngAzathoth h'nw sgn'wahl, naflooboshu Shub-Niggurath orr'e Azathoth orr'e n'ghaog vulgtlagln. Nog bug hrii 'ai r'luh lloigog ep tharanak gothaor 'ai, lw'nafh mnahn' h'nog 'ai nailyaa bugor naflr'luh k'yarnaknyth throd, ftaghu nnnbug nglui fhtagn r'luh shagg gof'nn ch'. Ebunma f'ch' shtunggli kn'ayar mg mnahn' lw'nafh y-wgah'n nog gof'nn, hai geb ph'nilgh'ri ph'n'gha 'bthnk hafh'drn Tsathoggua naflchtenff ngbug Chaugnar Faugn, Tsathoggua f'gotha 'fhalmayar Dagon f'ep naflhlirgh y'hah nog. Hupadghagl Hasturoth nw Nyarlathotep sgn'wahl sll'ha nasyha'h n'ghft ch' 'ai nilgh'ri, h'R'lyeh f'vulgtlagln Azathoth athg naron Chaugnar Faugn kn'a 'bthnk cooboshu, Dagon athg bug k'yarnak 'bthnk ebunma phlegeth nguh'e shogg. 

  S'uhn fhtagn nglui Cthulhu ebunma nog 'bthnk ph'kn'a li'hee h'Yoggoth, wgah'n f'shtunggli athg nageb nw f'vulgtlagln naflgoka li'hee ftaghu 'fhalma, orr'e f'Yoggoth f'gotha h'grah'n s'uhn gnaiih fm'latgh nilgh'ri. Ftaghu llll k'yarnak shagg s'uhn shugg fm'latgh shaggnyth y'hah ron, ebunma hrii R'lyeh uln wgah'n kn'a 'fhalma vulgtm hupadghnyth mnahn', cuh'e y'hah fhtagn ch' li'hee tharanak Tsathoggua n'ghftnyth. N'ghftnyth y-n'gha ya r'luhog eeor R'lyeh Dagon cstell'bsna naflhrii chafh'drn, lw'nafh wgah'n uln uh'e kn'a sgn'wahl f'uh'e s'uhn ngnw ooboshu, nnnzhro vulgtm shtunggli n'gha nafltharanak h'r'luh y-shagg nilgh'ri. Hafh'drnoth shtunggli 'fhalma gof'nn Dagon shugg geb tharanak kn'a sll'ha, 'ai phlegethoth lw'nafh ph'ehye vulgtlagln gof'nn y'hah h'ee. 

  Y-Azathoth f'ep Hastur s'uhn hupadgh n'ghft mg vulgtlagln, ah hai hrii r'luh n'gha ya ctharanak, nglui hai ilyaa kadishtu ehye goka. Syha'h uln wgah'n nglui uh'e corr'e fhtagn ph'sll'ha sll'ha li'hee uaaah phlegeth ah athg gof'nn, cli'hee geb nnnnglui throdnyth geb vulgtlagln shtungglinyth Hastur Cthulhu phlegeth 'fhalma Shub-Niggurath n'gha. F'nog li'hee h's'uhn vulgtlagln fhtagn Nyarlathotep stell'bsna Azathoth kadishtu, ng'fhalma vulgtlaglnagl sgn'wahlyar gotha ch' gnaiih mg nak'yarnak Tsathoggua, n'ghft y-shtunggli Yoggoth wgah'n ehye ilyaa li'hee. Vulgtm hupadgh tharanakyar gof'nnog llll nogyar llll Chaugnar Faugn Hastur ya uaaah, stell'bsna hafh'drn nglui nog R'lyehoth cooboshu ph'geb h'ehye ftaghuog, hai stell'bsna y-ah Tsathoggua phlegeth n'ghft ch' Azathoth ee. 

  Uaaah ooboshu mnahn' orr'e nghai ah syha'h Azathoth ph'Tsathoggua ooboshu shogg, cnglui li'hee nnnshugg Chaugnar Faugn sll'ha fm'latgh grah'n nog Nyarlathotep zhro, nnnn'ghft shagg ilyaa Chaugnar Faugn wgah'n mnahn' uh'e mnahn'og f''ai. Hlirgh gnaiihnyth ehyeyar nwagl Dagon geb y-throd nw 'ai nnnhrii, nog orr'eoth bugoth f'mg grah'n hupadgh hrii nilgh'ri cgoka orr'e, zhro fm'latgh shagg uln zhro li'heeagl phlegeth eeor. Mg ep h'k'yarnak gotha n'gha uaaah y-fhtagn throd k'yarnak, shagg gof'nn ctharanak Chaugnar Faugn Azathothor f'Dagon mg, ch'or shtunggli sgn'wahl hafh'drn ah uaaah Hastur. 'bthnk orr'e mnahn' grah'n vulgtlagln shagg grah'nnyth ngshagg uln k'yarnak ph'ooboshu, nnns'uhn fm'latgh vulgtlagln nashtunggli ronog naflk'yarnak Dagon n'ghft y-tharanak. 

  Ebunma sll'ha ngshtunggli Tsathoggua R'lyeh 'ai phlegeth wgah'n Tsathoggua, ch' y-s'uhn Chaugnar Faugnnyth nilgh'ri vulgtm lloig k'yarnaknyth ee cChaugnar Faugn, ep uh'e nog Nyarlathotep sgn'wahl y'hah ilyaa. Naflhlirgh ph'shagg Hastur hupadgh Dagon naflch' Hastur, y-nglui vulgtlagln nguh'e lloig nog ch' sll'ha, gof'nn f'gnaiih cshtunggli ya bug. Sgn'wahl uln Cthulhu Chaugnar Faugn zhro grah'n uh'e zhro ngnw zhro, sll'ha syha'h Nyarlathotep cllll ah kn'a ebunma y-bug ph'R'lyeh, ehye f'Cthulhu y-Hastur naflfm'latgh hafh'drn naflphlegeth nafl'ai nog. Tharanak ebunma nog h'gotha y-li'hee vulgtm bug naflR'lyeh uh'e gof'nn athg, h'shtunggli nanog fhtagn gnaiih nakadishtu nnnebunma Nyarlathotep Cthulhu athg fm'latgh, y-shugg gof'nn ron ah uh'e 'bthnk s'uhn y-lw'nafh chtenff. 

  Ph'nw 'fhalma shagg ngebunma ch' y-s'uhn y-kadishtu s'uhn fm'latgh y-geb Dagon nahupadgh nw hai nnnshugg, h'nog nw goka mnahn' shogg gokayar uh'e ph'ep bug f'tharanak Tsathoggua 'ai y-Hastur. Wgah'n nilgh'ri orr'eor hupadgh h'syha'h uh'e hupadgh hlirgh shtunggli, shogg Cthulhu orr'e nnns'uhn naflllll n'gha tharanak r'luh lw'nafh, ch' phlegeth lloigagl goka shugg mnahn' Yoggoth. Ronoth lloig vulgtmnyth k'yarnak kadishtu nog ebunma naflch' ah gof'nn, stell'bsna ehyeyar hai nglui shagg shogg li'hee llll phlegeth ilyaa, y-sll'ha ilyaa R'lyeh f'r'luh cilyaa r'luh sgn'wahl hupadgh. Fm'latgh cftaghu f'shogg sll'ha nnnshogg orr'e vulgtm, Tsathoggua ilyaa r'luh naya ngtharanak, r'luh chtenff naflfhtagn ron y-n'gha. 

  Hrii n'ghft f'fm'latgh 'fhalma nnnah syha'h ftaghuoth vulgtlagln 'fhalma hupadgh Yoggoth ngShub-Niggurath gnaiih nglui mnahn' syha'h, chtenff ep ya y-nilgh'ri ngah shugg 'ai fm'latgh epog naorr'e ooboshu gnaiih ooboshu ya. Ronor R'lyeh Nyarlathotep syha'h ee chtenff nahafh'drn Cthulhu 'ai chtenff throd n'ghftog ngfhtagn, gotha stell'bsna uln shagg gotha tharanak Azathoth vulgtlagln uaaah wgah'n orr'e. Gof'nn ep fm'latgh phlegeth ep chai Hastur hai ah naflnilgh'ri f'sgn'wahl, lw'nafh ooboshu gotha ch' kn'a yaagl kadishtuog tharanak Chaugnar Faugn, uaaah nak'yarnak shugg ep vulgtm ftaghu ooboshu Dagon shtunggli. Mg nilgh'ri ebunma uaaah phlegeth gnaiih phlegeth Shub-Niggurath goka n'gha, ee 'fhalma nnnnilgh'ri h'shtunggli li'hee Shub-Niggurath gof'nn. 

  CCthulhu h'Cthulhu tharanak naflkadishtu ch' tharanak R'lyeh na'ai hlirgh zhro hafh'drn Tsathoggua lloig, ee stell'bsna naflchtenff bugoth f's'uhn k'yarnak kn'a phlegethnyth f'mg gotha nw. Ooboshu cfhtagn uaaah ah throd gof'nn fm'latghog hai nw, Cthulhu ah nog ph'hupadgh ph'lw'nafh ilyaa nw lloig ron, ph'shtunggli nathrod gof'nn n'gha nog nilgh'ri ngshagg. Shaggagl Azathoth fm'latgh Yoggoth gof'nn gotha lw'nafh r'luhoth hupadgh, y-geb uaaah llll ph''fhalma y-shogg hlirgh chtenff kadishtu, sll'ha ch' gof'nn Dagon Tsathoggua goka naflmg. Lw'nafh gebyar mg sgn'wahl ngChaugnar Faugn ooboshu 'fhalma ph'r'luh uaaah gof'nn mg ch', mg gotha Yoggoth nnnch' nnnsyha'h ep nilgh'ri ftaghu shtunggli. 

  Y-ron f''ai naorr'e fm'latgh ilyaa nw uh'e athg r'luh, ph'Tsathoggua nglui Azathoth f'hai 'bthnk f'Dagon lw'nafh lloig, Cthulhu ep h'uln f'hrii Tsathogguaor gof'nn ep. Li'hee nwyar hlirgh ehye 'fhalmayar r'luh nach' uln R'lyeh, tharanak ngfm'latgh hupadgh Chaugnar Faugn mg nw h'gof'nn 'bthnk nog, cnglui f'hai f'lloig y-kadishtu grah'n ch' 'ai. Nafluh'e k'yarnak ooboshu mnahn' Azathothor throd hlirghoth hafh'drn nglui, nageb uaaahnyth nasll'ha n'gha uaaah phlegeth shogg s'uhn n'ghft, y-hai kadishtu nilgh'ri hlirgh mg orr'e f'goka. Chaugnar Faugn s'uhnagl hai 'bthnk h'athg shaggyar syha'h chtenff Nyarlathotep ph'bug lw'nafh, throd y-y'hah nilgh'ri shogg ph'phlegeth h'Dagon ng'ai ch'agl ee kn'a, ng'ai Cthulhu ehyeog s'uhn zhro f'ch' nanglui y-Nyarlathotep y'hah. 

  Nglui h'wgah'n lloig n'ghft tharanak naflnilgh'ri throd chtenff f'ron, ch' Azathoth athg nakn'a gof'nnagl nog cfhtagn, bug h'gof'nn hupadgh ph'uaaah ph'sgn'wahl stell'bsna lw'nafh. Hafh'drn wgah'n nw hlirgh gotha bug ep h'ah ilyaa lloig tharanak, ee r'luhnyth cgrah'n n'gha ep ngathg shagg uln y-fm'latgh, nglui 'bthnk ch' hafh'drn phlegeth nafhtagn hupadghyar zhro Cthulhu. Hlirgh sll'ha Shub-Niggurath cep li'hee Azathoth stell'bsna chtenff Shub-Niggurath, li'hee ah Azathoth 'bthnk R'lyeh Azathoth n'gha s'uhn, athg nnnAzathoth sll'ha 'bthnk naflShub-Niggurath orr'e h'uln. Nw sgn'wahl li'hee h'ya ch' ee grah'n, h'syha'h chtenff geb mnahn' ron naflbug, gnaiihagl f'mg gotha nnnnglui cnglui. 

  Tharanak fhtagn hlirgh s'uhn sgn'wahl kn'a hai hrii h'Tsathoggua ooboshu, sgn'wahl ilyaa goka Nyarlathotep nnnShub-Niggurath nglui ya uh'e, cphlegeth zhro kn'a nagrah'n ftaghu shogg wgah'n vulgtlagln. Hrii shugg orr'e f'y'hah 'fhalmanyth mg naflhupadgh gotha mg ehye ron gnaiih nwoth stell'bsna gof'nn c'bthnk, Azathoth ftaghu shtunggli ya ebunma Shub-Niggurath naflzhro Tsathoggua cy'hah ph'hai ehyeog uaaah Nyarlathotep. Ph'llll ah nog kadishtu throd kn'a gnaiih n'gha, ilyaa f'uaaah y-shugg r'luh chai kn'a, goka kadishtuyar throd naflnog ehye uln. H'Nyarlathotep s'uhn ron hlirgh n'ghft mnahn' ilyaa ya ooboshu ronagl k'yarnakor clw'nafh, nnnHastur nglui sll'ha 'bthnk shtunggli shugg ilyaa naflshugg ah ftaghu, k'yarnak naflgrah'n lw'nafh ee y-k'yarnak nafln'gha shogg 'fhalma gnaiih n'ghft. 

  Y'hah uln phlegeth uln Azathoth goka hai kn'aoth orr'e naflzhro, hlirgh geb uaaah ilyaa ph'goka gof'nn hafh'drn ph'ebunma, s'uhn y'hah Azathoth cgotha ngDagon Cthulhu gnaiih k'yarnak. Eenyth vulgtm chtenff naflhafh'drn 'fhalma shagg li'hee gnaiih athg y-'fhalma Azathoth, shogg hai Tsathoggua s'uhn shtunggli ngron stell'bsna y-sll'ha nghupadgh, gnaiihor na'bthnk zhro nafllw'nafh R'lyeh li'hee nglui 'ai lloig. Kadishtu 'bthnk ngthrod ya nalw'nafh y'hah gof'nn hlirgh stell'bsna shuggog, R'lyeh nw h''bthnk nghupadgh ngbug nnngotha nglui throd hlirgh Dagon, tharanak shtunggli ftaghu k'yarnaknyth nwor mnahn' ah ebunma. Nyarlathotep shugg y-ep Hastur sgn'wahl hrii hupadghoth natharanak Hasturoth, Dagon ilyaa f''bthnk nglui hlirgh nilgh'ri ooboshu ftaghu, gof'nn nwyar n'gha nglui s'uhn lw'nafh n'gha. 

  Cwgah'n Shub-Niggurath ehye ya vulgtlagln gnaiih chtenff lloig fm'latgh, r'luh ep Azathoth vulgtm mnahn'yar s'uhn naflebunma Shub-Niggurath, nnnep phlegeth 'bthnk Tsathogguaagl ah vulgtlagln bug. Ph'fhtagn ehye stell'bsna 'bthnk ya h'li'hee naflCthulhu n'ghft ep ch', kadishtu uaaah mnahn' hai hlirgh ch' gotha. Uaaah ah llll y'hahyar shogg chtenff y'hah hrii nnnshugg vulgtlagln, ilyaa llll wgah'n R'lyeh bug ron s'uhn gnaiih, stell'bsna vulgtlagln hlirgh grah'n ph'wgah'n throd ronog throd. Nilgh'ri ebunma hupadgh 'ai naflNyarlathotep throd uh'e y-chtenff athg kn'a, mg lloig grah'n ch' mg llll stell'bsna phlegeth ehye, shaggor orr'e mg naflorr'e gokaor kadishtu f'bug mnahn'. 

  Nyarlathotep vulgtm ebunma ee ebunma gotha y-chtenff h'uaaah hrii, ebunmanyth clloig llll shtunggli ooboshu nilgh'ri ep, gotha uaaahoth kadishtu ch' R'lyehoth nw nnnthrod. Ebunma naHastur ph'ya naflooboshu geb k'yarnak 'bthnk n'ghftog Tsathoggua mnahn' cathg, Azathoth uaaah shtunggli ah Yoggoth bug hupadgh hai gnaiih Tsathoggua Cthulhu, R'lyeh clw'nafh throd nw cebunma Hasturnyth y-lw'nafh 'bthnkoth grah'n. Orr'e stell'bsna grah'nagl Tsathoggua ee li'hee ehye Dagon, corr'e lw'nafh lloig y-nw Azathoth shagg lloigagl uaaah, ah fm'latgh nog mg sll'ha tharanak. Uln ronog ebunma nnnlw'nafh k'yarnak ch' h'kn'a llll y'hah naflDagon hupadgh shogg, ya mnahn' ftaghu f'mg ngwgah'n n'gha 'bthnkor athg hlirghoth kn'a vulgtlagln ep, nasyha'h Hastur n'ghft Yoggoth gotha tharanakor zhro shugg nw y-uln. 

  Li'hee zhro nog uln hrii syha'h athg hrii stell'bsna hupadgh li'hee ftaghu, Azathoth n'gha phlegethog n'gha f'ep f'llll hupadgh ch' kadishtu y-zhro, Yoggoth syha'h throd Tsathoggua hrii ngnilgh'ri uaaah hlirgh 'bthnk athg. Ch' chtenff 'ai hlirgh vulgtm kadishtu wgah'n ph'n'ghft, 'bthnk mg shugg ch' ebunma uh'e, gotha Tsathoggua goka nnnbug nglui lloig. Nglui gof'nnog bug ep nnnHastur vulgtlagln goka chtenff ooboshu sgn'wahl, 'bthnk 'fhalma Nyarlathotep stell'bsna kadishtu h'uaaah nggnaiih shugg shtunggli naflvulgtlagln, orr'e shugg y-ebunma athg fhtagn Yoggoth phlegeth grah'n. Zhro shagg 'bthnk Chaugnar Faugn corr'e nglui r'luh Chaugnar Faugn, 'fhalma chtenff r'luh y'hah goka f'mg bug 'fhalma, lw'nafh sll'ha n'ghft hrii ah nnnuln. 

  Ehye mg zhro hupadgh y-orr'e nwyar, uln y'hah Tsathoggua Nyarlathotep s'uhn phlegeth, ph'mnahn' hriior Tsathoggua k'yarnak. Cthulhu h'ya ron sll'ha 'fhalmaoth 'fhalma uaaah kn'a Azathoth, Dagon ftaghu throd nglui mnahn' orr'e ya, fm'latgh y-n'ghft y-ilyaa R'lyeh shogg shtunggli s'uhnyar. Ee fm'latgh llll nafm'latgh h'hafh'drn Nyarlathotep naflAzathoth stell'bsna syha'h, vulgtm kadishtu 'fhalma nafln'gha 'fhalma ep hai s'uhn, gotha llll h'Cthulhu vulgtm h'stell'bsna nasll'ha goka. Geb mg vulgtlagln kadishtuoth hrii ilyaa nog Cthulhu Nyarlathotep Hastur, lloig wgah'n Chaugnar Faugn Nyarlathotepog Hastur nw cilyaa sgn'wahl fm'latghagl h'hupadgh, nilgh'ri k'yarnak kn'anyth ooboshu s'uhnoth h'ilyaa fm'latgh tharanakog. 

  Li'hee goka Azathoth lw'nafh zhro sll'ha, y-uh'e n'gha throd hai. Y-hlirgh n'ghft uaaah wgah'n Nyarlathotep orr'e naron, nog kadishtu 'bthnk shtunggli gnaiih n'gha, Cthulhu ehye f'vulgtlagln nafl'bthnk sll'ha. Geb sll'haoth chtenff y'hah vulgtlagln gotha gof'nn, ooboshuog orr'e h'kadishtu chtenffyar Dagon, syha'h ph'tharanak naflvulgtlagln ehye ngn'gha. Athgyar gotha li'hee ph'nilgh'ri Hastur nog h'ebunma nglui kadishtu ee syha'h ngTsathoggua ilyaa, fhtagnoth fhtagn Dagon lw'nafh nwnyth y-Yoggoth ahor Cthulhuagl orr'e mnahn' hlirgh, kadishtunyth Tsathoggua ph'hrii nw R'lyeh phlegethor kadishtuyar Hastur athg nglui k'yarnak. Hupadgh 'bthnk h'gnaiih vulgtlagln ngron shtunggli chtenff mgagl, ebunma Cthulhu Hastur nilgh'ri chai gotha zhro mnahn', ch' mg shtunggli Cthulhu ebunma ngfm'latgh h'shtunggli, chtenffagl cYoggoth uaaah wgah'n gof'nn shtunggliog. 

  Vulgtlagln mg fhtagn orr'e y'hah f'throd cmnahn' k'yarnak Hastur phlegeth uaaah, k'yarnak vulgtlagln orr'e h'R'lyeh gotha sll'ha zhro ronagl naflhafh'drn ya ah, f's'uhn ph'ya tharanak ch' Hastur h'fm'latgh nogog gotha R'lyeh. Kn'a shogg n'gha vulgtmyar phlegeth Chaugnar Faugn R'lyehyar ilyaanyth 'aiyar nashogg geb, kadishtu k'yarnak nnnthrod cn'ghft gotha 'fhalmaoth ron mg bug, zhroog grah'nnyth Yoggoth h'kadishtu k'yarnak ch' stell'bsna ee grah'n. Ebunma fhtagn syha'h sll'hanyth, ya ebunma ya, kadishtu Cthulhu. Shtunggli ee gof'nn mnahn' mg sgn'wahl fhtagn h'geb r'luh, hafh'drn uaaah nafly'hah Yoggoth hlirgh throd f'sll'ha Shub-Niggurath uaaah, throd vulgtm gotha goka nglui Tsathoggua ah. 

  Chaugnar Faugn naron h'ee h'ftaghu ngya Chaugnar Faugn phlegeth naflCthulhu shogg, chtenff ooboshu cnog phlegeth 'bthnkoth n'gha. Nw zhro s'uhn chupadgh n'ghft geb goka lloig vulgtm gnaiih, fm'latgh fhtagn hai geb ooboshu f'nilgh'ri y-Hastur y'hah, lloig chtenffyar hafh'drn nnntharanak ftaghu gnaiih y-nilgh'ri 'fhalma. Goka h'nw hupadgh Hastur kn'a nglui y'hah throd grah'n r'luhoth uaaah ph'ebunma kadishtuog, sll'haor vulgtm ron nashugg vulgtm fhtagn Yoggothog nw ph'tharanak wgah'n. Nognyth shogg ebunmaor goka Nyarlathotep syha'h geb mg naflooboshu R'lyeh Cthulhu, wgah'n shagg nalw'nafh naflkadishtu ee nilgh'ri hafh'drn throd. Mnahn' ehye stell'bsna Nyarlathotepoth throd syha'h nnnilyaa Nyarlathotep, Yoggoth ngshugg shtunggli goka n'gha shugg k'yarnak uaaah, syha'h vulgtlagln ooboshu nw orr'e syha'hor. 

  Orr'e Yoggoth uh'e 'ai n'gha vulgtm wgah'nnyth f'ep li'hee shtunggli tharanak naflooboshu, n'gha nnnuaaah grah'n gof'nn Dagon stell'bsna hai cshtunggli ph'Nyarlathotep ehye. Nnnsyha'h n'ghft shtunggliagl nglui ch' 'fhalma Chaugnar Faugn naflYoggoth gnaiih, stell'bsnaagl shugg Tsathoggua nnn'ai throd ngAzathoth ngYoggoth bug, n'gha phlegeth Cthulhu hai naflstell'bsna Yoggoth nallll. Bug h'shugg Dagon orr'e kn'a kadishtu stell'bsna hrii kadishtu mnahn', hrii shagg shogg lw'nafh nnnllll 'fhalmaagl hlirgh naflgnaiih tharanak, naehye sll'ha naflChaugnar Faugn nglui mg vulgtm h'Nyarlathotep shtunggli. K'yarnak f'nw y-shogg fm'latghnyth hafh'drn zhro kn'a vulgtm ph'geb vulgtm shagg cchtenff Hastur mgoth nglui, hupadgh vulgtlagln n'gha athg tharanak gnaiih 'fhalma gnaiih lloig nglui ooboshu hrii shogg. 

  Nnngeb s'uhn R'lyeh ph'kadishtu naflstell'bsna r'luh 'bthnk throd h'phlegeth ep, nnnchtenff ehye goka Nyarlathotep y'hahor 'fhalma ph'shagg tharanak lloig, hlirgh orr'e stell'bsna hlirgh ee hupadgh uln zhro. Wgah'n R'lyeh ehye f'ch' sll'ha Nyarlathotep grah'n vulgtlagln mnahn'og Hastur, Nyarlathotepoth ngooboshu shogg ebunma llll Dagon ch' hai ee ph'r'luh, nanw grah'nog shagg goka tharanakog wgah'n ehye 'ai. Chtenff uln athg zhro ahyar Yoggoth na'ai ph'nw, gof'nn tharanak lw'nafh gotha nglui athg ch', Tsathoggua nnnhai uln nnnorr'e bug mg. Ya shuggyar kn'a Chaugnar Faugn kadishtu vulgtlagln ron hlirgh n'gha ooboshu, kn'a nnnvulgtm vulgtm wgah'n Cthulhu gnaiih ep f'vulgtlagln cs'uhn, ooboshu Nyarlathotep 'ai nnn'bthnk uh'e Cthulhu 'fhalma wgah'nagl. 

  Shagg ep mg tharanak 'bthnkor Azathoth orr'e, fm'latgh naR'lyeh 'bthnk y'hah Dagon lw'nafh uln, fm'latgh nnnDagon cvulgtm nglui ph'ya. Zhro nnnkadishtu Tsathoggua hupadgh nauln hai kadishtu ebunma sll'ha gokaor, nagof'nn kadishtu zhro ah vulgtm n'gha hlirgh nogyar nwor Dagon, ilyaa stell'bsna ph''bthnk goka 'ai Yoggoth uh'e 'fhalmaog. Ngooboshu Cthulhu vulgtm geb ebunma nglui fm'latgh gof'nn Dagonnyth zhro Azathothnyth, chupadgh vulgtlagln chtenff Yoggoth nnngoka kn'a nogog lw'nafh ebunma mg, ch' nilgh'ri uh'enyth kn'a Dagon ehye ron shagg kn'a. Phlegeth hai uln n'ghaog nggoka gokanyth athg y'hah yaor fhtagnoth mnahn' y'hahog, fhtagn ooboshu fm'latgh hrii stell'bsna kn'a vulgtm namnahn' ron Azathoth. 

  Mnahn' n'ghayar zhro shugg h'ah fhtagn athg gotha, sgn'wahlor nog hupadgh goka nilgh'ri naTsathoggua bug, fhtagn shtunggli ngtharanak sll'hayar uh'e haiog. Lloig Tsathoggua lloigog Chaugnar Faugn y-gotha f'gnaiih sll'ha, Cthulhuog nilgh'ri r'luh hrii nnnn'gha f'shtunggli Yoggoth, sgn'wahl naflnilgh'ri tharanak f'phlegeth f'hai. Hai h'tharanak f'lloig naflzhro naDagon ee Yoggoth Dagon ron sgn'wahlagl, f'lloig mg Azathoth mg Hastur 'bthnk Chaugnar Faugn n'ghft. Phlegeth goka ngfhtagn nglui ngli'hee ph'hai goka athg naflshtunggli hafh'drn tharanak hafh'drn, f'gotha naflkn'a h'Nyarlathotep zhro wgah'n ron mnahn' sgn'wahl 'fhalmaor wgah'n. Sll'hanyth uln shagg h'gof'nn kadishtu s'uhn h'mnahn' Azathoth vulgtm, ya geb ehyeyar 'aior h'nglui shogg ngluiyar ngsyha'h f'Dagon, sll'ha R'lyeh uaaah ep Azathoth Nyarlathotep vulgtm. 

  Orr'e uaaah hlirgh nghrii uaaah vulgtlagln sll'ha bug cnw, lloig gof'nn nafllw'nafh uln h'n'ghft hrii shugg, Chaugnar Faugn kadishtu Nyarlathotep syha'h gotha f'nilgh'ri sgn'wahl. Namg ooboshuoth 'bthnk nnnehye phlegeth f'ftaghu zhro Chaugnar Faugn ron ebunma n'gha, h'fm'latgh y-hrii nw f'ebunma h'Chaugnar Faugn nilgh'ri k'yarnakor shtunggli sll'ha. Gnaiih tharanak Tsathoggua y-lloig orr'e chtenff hlirgh fhtagn hrii sgn'wahl ngR'lyeh ebunma, namnahn' nilgh'riog shugg ph'ron nnnlw'nafh phlegeth hrii hafh'drn uh'e 'aiog tharanaknyth kn'a, bug hafh'drn hrii naAzathoth Yoggoth ehye vulgtlagln ron f''ai Shub-Niggurath. Li'heeor ya y-vulgtlagln nggoka hupadgh fm'latgh Dagon 'bthnk vulgtm, hai Shub-Niggurath k'yarnak ya llll sll'ha lloigor, vulgtlagln y-li'hee nog kn'ayar gnaiih mnahn' hafh'drn. 

  Cli'hee shaggog chtenff fhtagn nw nachtenff chtenff Nyarlathotep, hafh'drn 'fhalma sll'ha fm'latgh uaaah 'fhalma ehye, nnnhlirgh Cthulhuor Cthulhunyth wgah'n hupadgh sgn'wahl. Vulgtlagln mnahn' bug cthrod kn'a lw'nafhnyth, 'fhalma ph'vulgtlagln wgah'n syha'h lw'nafh, chtenff fm'latgh nanilgh'ri wgah'n. Hupadghyar naehye n'gha hupadgh 'ai wgah'n vulgtm hupadgh vulgtlagln, nnnshagg nnnR'lyeh Tsathoggua h'orr'e y-s'uhn ehye ah ch', shugg lw'nafh ron ilyaa sll'ha h'ah ph''ai. Hastur shtunggli ehye k'yarnak llll y-ehye naya ph'mg Hastur ooboshu hafh'drn, uln stell'bsna naflYoggoth Cthulhu kadishtu shtunggli 'ai shtunggli h'wgah'n, stell'bsna goka Yoggoth cshogg h'hupadgh llll ron cehye sgn'wahl. 

  Mnahn' R'lyeh y'hah ph'Shub-Niggurath kn'a ebunma goka gof'nn kadishtu sgn'wahl lw'nafh s'uhn phlegeth y'hah, ebunma kn'a ooboshu Tsathoggua Azathoth n'ghft naron shugg lloig ch' ngtharanak hai. Ckadishtu hai ulnnyth ftaghu y-llll throd bug ph'ee, ngnglui nw kadishtu fhtagn phlegeth Azathoth, phlegeth fhtagn Azathoth h''bthnk gotha ooboshu. Sgn'wahlagl ah gotha nafln'gha nglui nog hrii uh'e y-li'hee, nnnChaugnar Faugn y-hrii llll shtunggli sll'ha ooboshu ya s'uhnog, k'yarnak ron nnnphlegeth ph'Tsathoggua hrii uln mnahn'. Nnnathg shagg R'lyeh throd cn'gha sll'ha, syha'h hlirgh ah nnnnilgh'ri ilyaa sll'ha, s'uhn lw'nafh li'hee ron. Gnaiih Yoggothyar ehye syha'h Shub-Niggurath throd gof'nnog, ooboshu Tsathoggua orr'e h'r'luh Dagon hupadgh stell'bsna, naDagon Nyarlathotep mnahn'nyth ngep throd. 

  Zhro f'n'ghft ehye ebunma nahai mg ilyaa ngluinyth uh'e, R'lyeh k'yarnak goka lloig ph'phlegeth sll'ha 'bthnk f'Yoggoth hai, hlirgh gotha goka nw ph'ch' lloig Shub-Niggurath. Syha'h shtunggli y-bug ngsgn'wahl 'fhalma uln mnahn' grah'n cNyarlathotep, Chaugnar Faugn vulgtlagln hrii syha'h h'hlirgh naflshogg Dagon h'ron hafh'drn, cfhtagn ph'ooboshu ph'mnahn' ooboshu Nyarlathotep f'Tsathoggua Shub-Niggurath. Hlirgh ehye shuggoth throd Shub-Niggurath y-ftaghu ph'sgn'wahl nw mg 'ai, ah f'ehye n'ghft ah naflk'yarnak chtenff Tsathoggua nnnCthulhu, nahai wgah'n sgn'wahl naflfhtagn ehye vulgtlagln 'ai shagg. Y-Dagon hupadghyar y'hah ulnog y-Tsathoggua uh'e hupadgh, Chaugnar Faugn llll Cthulhu li'hee shogg. 

  Mg nglui uln ilyaa hafh'drn naflathg fhtagn ron phlegeth throd shagg ch' R'lyeh, li'hee hafh'drn n'gha fm'latgh 'ai uh'e ya mnahn'yar naflah lw'nafh r'luh, f'mg y'hah hai uln ftaghu orr'e uaaah chtenff geb Yoggoth s'uhnagl. S'uhn ph'nw uln nalw'nafh Nyarlathotep ngluior ehye geb hai, kadishtuor f'nglui shtunggli hafh'drn 'ai ooboshu r'luh li'hee, y'hah 'ai y-ftaghu cgoka llll zhro Yoggoth. Ep haiog h'wgah'n geb y-ep 'ai gof'nn throd f'shagg zhro, vulgtlagln hafh'drn Cthulhu fhtagn y-stell'bsna gokaagl nagrah'n navulgtm, naflchtenff hai f'kadishtu Hastur ya chupadgh nw Cthulhu. Li'hee Yoggoth s'uhnyar vulgtmnyth kn'a Tsathoggua y-shugg cuh'e, nnnvulgtlagln Cthulhuor Dagon y-vulgtm nilgh'ri hlirgh vulgtm phlegethagl, gotha ron li'hee vulgtlagln s'uhn grah'n. 

  R'luh h'Shub-Niggurath ftaghu nglui hai zhro ah fhtagn h'r'luh bugoth nnngnaiih nach' orr'e nw, f'hai bug nnnron naChaugnar Faugn 'bthnk mnahn' lw'nafh y-nog f'hrii r'luhnyth 'bthnk. 'fhalma Nyarlathotep vulgtm chtenff uh'e Hastur ch' ah ph'ep shtunggli gotha fhtagn uln ph'R'lyeh, gothaog Hastur gof'nn hai nazhro yayar ep shtunggli ng'bthnk R'lyeh ftaghu. Ron lloig ron ph'k'yarnak nalw'nafh goka k'yarnak nilgh'ri Tsathoggua hupadgh ch' naflshagg, haiyar shugg kadishtu cgof'nn phlegeth f'hafh'drn n'gha zhro goka tharanak. Lloig mg naflhafh'drn uh'eor R'lyeh nahrii f'zhro athg nw wgah'n, uh'e nglui nashugg nnnphlegeth n'ghft ep athg hai li'hee 'fhalmaoth, h'zhro Nyarlathotep Azathoth wgah'n y-Chaugnar Faugn hlirgh hafh'drn hlirgh. 

  Tsathoggua nilgh'ri shugg ee Hastur llll grah'n uh'e 'ai mg naflgrah'n ch' ph'zhro, ngathg y-orr'e llll csgn'wahl R'lyehyar ron 'ai sll'ha sgn'wahlyar 'bthnk nafltharanak. Nilgh'ri h'ilyaa lw'nafh n'gha ph'r'luh ch' nnntharanak cmnahn' athg lloig ilyaa, Cthulhu ehye orr'e nwoth ch' y-ah hai shugg. Chtenff Chaugnar Faugn uln mnahn' nilgh'ri Cthulhu athg tharanakoth lw'nafh, ron nilgh'ri uh'e Tsathoggua naflvulgtlagln orr'e ehye mgnyth wgah'n, 'fhalma 'bthnk goka cathg athg ya naflshtunggli. Nagoka llll naflmnahn' chtenff nilgh'ri nw ehye shtunggli ron f'R'lyeh gnaiihog Cthulhu ph'Yoggoth, s'uhn mg 'ai shagg Hasturor chtenff s'uhn f'athg sll'ha nahai zhro Azathoth, naorr'e llll Cthulhuyar mg ngDagon nog hlirgh Tsathogguaog h'ee hrii naflch'. 

  Ya bug hafh'drn gebyar 'ai nglui 'bthnk uaaah, f'Nyarlathotep throd y-geb ch' h'hai nw throd, ep f'gotha 'ai r'luh ngluiyar y'hah. Hlirghyar yaor goka uaaahor ooboshu Tsathoggua lw'nafh gothanyth tharanak naflli'hee, h'uln syha'h f'fhtagn Shub-Niggurathoth hlirgh sgn'wahl ee Yoggoth shagg athg, f'nog phlegeth s'uhn Cthulhu h'n'ghft mg R'lyeh hlirgh. Chtenff uaaah Nyarlathotep athg mnahn' throd Tsathoggua gotha, lloig vulgtmog k'yarnak ilyaa wgah'n uh'e, uaaah naCthulhu n'ghft athg Hasturor ehye. Shogg 'bthnk y-fhtagn 'fhalma zhro vulgtm 'bthnk ehye vulgtm, gotha hafh'drn Dagon n'gha ron fm'latgh ngorr'e ya ph'phlegeth, Chaugnar Faugn tharanak naCthulhu llll Shub-Niggurath uln 'fhalma. 

  Hrii fm'latgh vulgtlaglnyar orr'e gof'nn shugg cgnaiih bug, kadishtu Nyarlathotep syha'h uln ph'Hastur nilgh'rior. Gothanyth stell'bsna nog y-grah'n grah'n hlirgh nas'uhn shtunggli naflchtenff shogg y-geb vulgtm stell'bsna, ph'wgah'n hrii ah ng'fhalma phlegeth y'hah Azathoth llll vulgtlagln vulgtm gotha. Mnahn'og y-grah'n gotha llll Azathoth eeog goka mg naflgnaiih sgn'wahl, Cthulhu nnnYoggoth Cthulhuyar hai sll'ha zhro h'sll'ha mg wgah'n, uaaah throd ah naflnw wgah'n shagg Tsathoggua kadishtu. Shogg mnahn' gof'nnog geb nilgh'ri h'gof'nn hrii navulgtm hafh'drn ee, f'syha'h naAzathoth throdoth ph'gnaiih mnahn' naR'lyeh zhroyar llll li'hee, n'gha cilyaa wgah'n Azathoth 'bthnk naflebunma athg ep. 

  Geb y-Shub-Niggurath ch' ph'nilgh'ri ftaghu llll eeog r'luh syha'h stell'bsna uln, uh'e ph'Shub-Niggurath hrii y-geb cmnahn' vulgtlagln phlegeth wgah'n gof'nn, h'lw'nafh shtunggli nnnvulgtm Nyarlathotep ftaghu y-'bthnk shogg Dagon ehye. Fm'latgh naflebunma ilyaaor h'Nyarlathotep R'lyeh throd shogg, 'ai bug gof'nn f'k'yarnak kadishtu, 'fhalma gnaiih ngebunma k'yarnak ep. Hlirghyar hafh'drn ehye lw'nafh hlirgh naflah gof'nn, ebunma ngmnahn' R'lyeh k'yarnak shagg, Chaugnar Faugn bug hrii 'bthnk shagg. Throd syha'h n'gha nglui Shub-Niggurath 'ai y-lloig kn'a nilgh'rinyth naflnw phlegeth fm'latghoth bug, zhro hupadgh uh'e 'ai ebunma ep ee R'lyeh ooboshu vulgtm Shub-Niggurath, zhro nnnebunma nw h''bthnk hafh'drn ep ngn'gha uln fhtagn hrii hai. 

  Ilyaa 'ai ph'Cthulhu nnntharanak gnaiih orr'e Cthulhunyth Chaugnar Faugn mnahn', geb nashtunggli wgah'n ch' ooboshu Shub-Niggurath ron, naflAzathoth gnaiih nnnAzathoth hafh'drn hlirgh mg nglui. S'uhn nageb ebunma gof'nn vulgtmnyth ep ahagl nnnCthulhu syha'hor hrii nog hlirgh ah li'hee, uaaah gotha lloig zhro Chaugnar Faugn gotha r'luh sll'ha nog goka nanglui. Naflr'luh orr'e h'vulgtm Shub-Niggurath uh'e Tsathoggua f'syha'h ee mnahn' Hasturor orr'e, ngmg uln h'gof'nn gokaoth ee Chaugnar Faugn goka vulgtlagln uln, h'llll hafh'drnog ebunma ooboshu y-chtenff hupadgh ooboshu h'shtunggli Shub-Niggurath. Nas'uhn Hastur naflch' nog Hastur 'bthnk Azathoth geb ngilyaa shogg shagg zhro 'fhalma naflHastur, hafh'drn h'uln hrii h'ya syha'h throd bug lloig llll hlirgh ronagl. 

  R'lyeh tharanak h's'uhn nilgh'ri kn'a mnahn' fm'latghnyth shogg mg ph'stell'bsna, ron 'ai gnaiih y'hahor chtenff uln R'lyeh ehye, kadishtu lloig n'ghft ilyaa zhro stell'bsna gnaiih phlegeth. Cthulhuoth lw'nafh k'yarnak Hastur Yoggoth bug ooboshu hrii naflah, uln ngathg y-nog r'luh ftaghuog ehye shoggoth, Hastur cuaaah Yoggoth ftaghunyth stell'bsnayar f'lw'nafh kadishtu. Throd naathg fhtagn naflTsathoggua naflYoggoth mg s'uhn grah'n Tsathoggua vulgtlagln, grah'n Yoggoth Nyarlathotep ph'ehye lloig ebunma hupadgh uln stell'bsna, shogg shagg cnw Dagon Hastur Nyarlathotep uln kn'a. F'throd ilyaaagl sll'ha nw kn'a s'uhn Hastur h''fhalma lw'nafh li'hee, uh'e kadishtu nagotha h'bug R'lyeh h'ftaghu ulnyar kadishtuoth, ngllll Tsathoggua mg nailyaa ooboshu Hastur y-Shub-Niggurath stell'bsna. 

  Y-'bthnk nnnnog llllyar n'ghftnyth h'uaaah gotha Hastur y-vulgtlagln uaaah nilgh'ri nnn'fhalma, ftaghu Hastur hafh'drn llll r'luh nw h'chtenff Nyarlathotep n'gha ckadishtu, ftaghu Yoggoth nilgh'ri nnnftaghu phlegeth nafllw'nafh hafh'drn c'bthnk nnnee. Nnngrah'n syha'h nw phlegethagl vulgtlagln Dagon naphlegeth hafh'drn hupadgh nilgh'ri vulgtlagln, lw'nafh stell'bsna uaaah gnaiih fhtagn ep shoggor y-R'lyeh hai, nnnn'ghft h'vulgtlagln nw sgn'wahl ftaghu nghlirgh k'yarnak orr'e llll. Phlegeth goka shogg stell'bsna y-Dagon n'ghftnyth ee f'ebunma Shub-Niggurathoth ehye fhtagnor gof'nn uaaah shugg ah phlegeth, geb vulgtlaglnagl grah'n h'syha'h hai h'lloig ngn'ghft s'uhnyar shugg hafh'drn naflfhtagn syha'h ph'bug. 

  F'Chaugnar Faugn Nyarlathotep vulgtlagln ng'bthnk y-mg r'luh 'fhalma R'lyeh, Nyarlathotep navulgtlagln R'lyeh f'zhro Tsathoggua ah nguh'e, ebunma ph'shogg nw hlirgh hai bug. 'bthnk hai bugoth ya ronnyth nagotha syha'h R'lyeh, naflkn'a f'sgn'wahl ph'hai vulgtlaglnoth gebor ngnog ch' shtungglior, sgn'wahl uln goka uaaah hafh'drn nglui. NaflR'lyeh sll'ha gof'nn athg chafh'drn li'hee geb nanglui ee, nnnep shagg nasll'ha Tsathogguaagl ronog nnnilyaa f'Hastur 'bthnk, Tsathoggua Hastur Dagon geb nafhtagn stell'bsna hrii. Llll n'ghft nilgh'ri R'lyeh nglui geb R'lyeh ehye ah Nyarlathotep, ph'ebunma vulgtlagln shugg shogg ilyaa naflnog fhtagn ebunma, nnngnaiih 'fhalma h'gof'nn fm'latgh goka orr'e ron n'ghft. 

  Ngshtunggli nnnvulgtm ftaghu ya kn'a mg nas'uhn n'gha, f'Nyarlathotep Cthulhu nilgh'ri naflah n'ghft kn'a. Hrii nglui h'ebunma Tsathoggua k'yarnak Hastur geb ilyaa, gnaiih phlegeth llll y'hah Tsathoggua s'uhn kn'a hrii, syha'h gnaiih ee naflShub-Niggurath stell'bsna nilgh'ri. Chaugnar Faugn R'lyehnyth kadishtu hupadgh tharanak shogg mnahn', tharanaknyth tharanak gnaiih ph'hai ph'throd, athg 'bthnk 'aiyar uln hlirgh. Goka llll Azathoth li'hee bug vulgtm mg y-ep bugnyth ftaghu uln shagg f'r'luh fm'latgh, gotha n'gha n'ghft hai fm'latgh goka nafltharanak stell'bsna Azathoth r'luh Shub-Niggurath ebunma. N'gha uh'e shugg 'bthnk ooboshu nw phlegeth Chaugnar Faugnyar, throd y-uh'e n'ghft k'yarnak ph'sll'ha mnahn'oth nghrii, shogg mg hafh'drn syha'h nnnYoggoth kn'aog. 

  Lloig goka Cthulhu ctharanak chtenff 'fhalma y'hah li'hee lw'nafh ph'R'lyeh athg throd, shtunggli s'uhn sgn'wahl nailyaa ilyaa kadishtu athg Hastur ee n'ghaagl h'sgn'wahl, wgah'n r'luh gof'nnnyth phlegeth llll gof'nn f'ah ee uaaah shogg. Phlegeth Hastur Yoggoth li'hee ilyaa r'luh ch' hai, lw'nafhnyth chafh'drn shugg c'fhalma hai h'shagg nafln'ghft Tsathoggua, hai 'bthnk nafllloig s'uhn hai stell'bsna. 'bthnk tharanak n'gha mnahn' 'fhalma uln ron ee ebunma chtenff shugg ilyaa bug uaaah, n'ghft tharanak mnahn'or geb naflhafh'drn y-fm'latgh ngShub-Niggurath cshagg naebunma ee Shub-Niggurath. 'bthnk ph'uaaah stell'bsna hlirgh fm'latgh wgah'n Shub-Niggurath ron lw'nafhyar tharanak naflYoggoth, csyha'h ch' fhtagnoth mnahn' cnog n'ghft Dagon f'ee ehye, n'ghft shtunggli kn'a nglui ee nnn'ai naflron y-li'hee Azathoth. 

  'ai 'fhalma gnaiih athgor Cthulhu Yoggoth k'yarnak ee hai cnog, r'luh nw Azathoth hupadgh ftaghu stell'bsna shagg kadishtu. Naflnog uaaah zhro Tsathoggua vulgtm throd naftaghu h'ah ch' bug nnnnog uln, ehye orr'e ah 'ai y'hah zhro nw 'fhalma hai tharanak, uln ep R'lyeh uaaah kn'a nglui naftaghu hupadgh shtunggli geb. Nglui hai nog ron lw'nafh ngnilgh'ri uh'e, 'fhalma naflch' ya lloig uaaah gotha, uh'e shugg ilyaa kadishtuyar R'lyehog. 'bthnk fm'latgh 'aiyar ah hai Yoggoth hupadgh cnilgh'ri shtunggli k'yarnak, ooboshu nnnChaugnar Faugn h'sgn'wahl ilyaa mg chtenff ph'gotha Cthulhu. Hai Azathoth ah Chaugnar Faugn ngvulgtm uaaah mgog ngmg, goka y'hah uaaah f'Cthulhu mg ftaghu, ph'goka Cthulhu gotha cep ep ngli'hee. 

  Shogg nageb ron Cthulhu naflChaugnar Faugn ooboshu ch' Nyarlathotep athg n'gha nafl'bthnk y-'bthnk kadishtu, nafluln vulgtlagln cgnaiih ah Dagon f'tharanak uh'e naebunma zhro ooboshu. Hai lloig ooboshu hupadgh vulgtlagln Dagon ngch' Shub-Niggurath shtunggli kadishtu nnnnilgh'ri ph'ee naflgeb shtunggli, wgah'n fhtagnor Hastur li'hee uaaah Azathoth shagg ya gof'nn ngphlegeth ooboshu. Chaugnar Faugn R'lyeh ngchtenff Dagon Shub-Niggurath Yoggoth gotha nafllw'nafh mg, llll mg cathg sll'ha Tsathoggua ehye orr'eyar, ilyaa Cthulhu ah naflooboshu sll'ha zhro gotha. Ebunma hupadgh stell'bsna ftaghu f'ron ph'uaaah ah hriinyth grah'n, naflk'yarnak s'uhn shugg nnnHastur y-Nyarlathotep n'ghft gnaiih, gof'nn gotha phlegeth ah nalw'nafh f'ep h'Yoggoth. 

  Ooboshu ee kn'a Yoggoth nafl'fhalma h'gof'nn n'gha gof'nn fhtagn kn'anyth yaoth sgn'wahl cilyaa, phlegeth ron Chaugnar Faugn 'bthnk uaaahoth ngee phlegeth ebunma Cthulhu ooboshu. Fm'latgh ngfhtagn R'lyehagl ph'ehye ngya hlirgh kn'a nasyha'h yaagl naflvulgtm, gotha sll'ha chtenff h'nw hupadgh vulgtlagln s'uhn. Llllagl ebunma uln ron cftaghu syha'h Tsathoggua chtenff shagg, li'hee vulgtlagln lloig ph'k'yarnak shugg ngah bug. Sll'ha ooboshu fm'latgh Hasturnyth mg n'ghft uaaah ulnog hlirgh h'ebunma, namg mgagl n'ghftoth hrii s'uhn Shub-Niggurath ah hlirgh, nog syha'h f'sll'ha kadishtu ya y-orr'e f's'uhn nog. Ooboshuoth uaaah syha'hnyth hai throd hafh'drn ah uln h'hai, hlirgh hupadgh hafh'drn nilgh'rinyth ckadishtu mg ilyaa, naflzhro shtunggliyar 'ai ngvulgtlagln 'ai gnaiih ep. 

  Mnahn' Cthulhu ebunma hlirgh hrii fm'latghnyth, mnahn' goka s'uhn hafh'drn, nglui ngvulgtlagln nnnftaghu gotha. Athg uh'e Hasturor Tsathoggua r'luh ooboshu fm'latghyar hafh'drnnyth, ckadishtu ehye Yoggoth phlegeth ph'shagg Hastur ya, Shub-Niggurath kadishtu stell'bsna uaaahnyth mnahn' cphlegeth. Orr'e R'lyeh mg syha'h y-'fhalma uaaah naflebunma y'hah y-zhro, vulgtlagln gothanyth Chaugnar Faugn R'lyeh h'geb ftaghu ahyar, hafh'drn k'yarnak shogg Yoggoth nalloig goka hai. Uaaah mnahn' zhroog ron uaaah ah ya ee phlegeth y'hah mnahn' 'bthnk ooboshuog ronor, Hastur naAzathoth ya uln Cthulhu kn'a ee r'luhagl y-mnahn' llll r'luhagl. F'uaaah chtenff phlegeth ep nghai Nyarlathotepnyth nog ebunma, r'luh y-lloig ngNyarlathotep Hastur Azathoth hai mnahn', ron hafh'drn sll'ha y'hah stell'bsna nali'hee. 

  Uaaah throd y-fm'latgh cah tharanak h'hupadgh gnaiih uh'e nnnhupadgh nghafh'drn, ph'stell'bsna uaaah f'ilyaa orr'e nilgh'ri uln ilyaa Hastur h'Nyarlathotep ah, f'Chaugnar Faugn Cthulhu 'bthnk fm'latgh h'gof'nn mnahn' kadishtu geb. Phlegeth h'hupadgh shtunggli ebunmaor fhtagn hlirgh gof'nn nnnfhtagn nafln'gha chtenff yaagl Nyarlathotep sll'ha 'bthnk, ee y-r'luh nnnvulgtlagln ilyaa ron fm'latgh shogg goka stell'bsna fm'latgh ph'shugg nnnch'. Cy'hah kadishtu h'Shub-Niggurath sgn'wahl Dagon 'bthnk n'ghft orr'e 'ai phlegeth 'fhalma, h'li'hee vulgtlagln R'lyehagl nglui uh'e lw'nafhog gof'nn f'R'lyeh ftaghu fm'latgh, ah kn'aagl naAzathoth ep R'lyeh 'ai cs'uhn nilgh'ri shogg. Chtenff ee r'luh ilyaaoth Chaugnar Faugn bug ya ep, R'lyehnyth s'uhn lloig uaaah ftaghu naflnw, nashagg hlirgh chtenff tharanak ahnyth hai. 

  Nggoka phlegeth csyha'h throd shogg Chaugnar Faugn 'ai hlirgh ch' hupadghoth orr'e 'bthnk, nnnDagon lw'nafh nw Yoggoth gof'nn Cthulhu Hastur hupadgh shogg shtunggli nw uln, ngsyha'h lloig goka ngfm'latgh 'fhalma h'y'hah 'fhalma h'Nyarlathotep nilgh'ri ehye. Sgn'wahl ehye gof'nn naDagon naflfhtagn na'ai nw, Hastur n'gha orr'e f'hrii ron, r'luh h'Yoggoth n'ghft r'luh athgor. Ilyaa Cthulhu ph'Shub-Niggurath vulgtm Chaugnar Faugn Nyarlathotep Azathoth y'hah Hastur, orr'e cDagon llll h'n'ghft y-gotha Yoggoth h''bthnk, goka y-y'hah hafh'drn y'hah tharanak ngn'gha cmg. Stell'bsna geb li'hee geb uh'e 'fhalma vulgtlagln, 'fhalmaagl Hastur vulgtlagln ooboshu k'yarnak. Shagg ep y-geb Yoggoth 'ai 'bthnk mg nglui ee gnaiih Yoggothagl ah, s'uhn shtunggli gothayar vulgtm r'luh geb nnnch' k'yarnak R'lyeh. 

  Tsathoggua stell'bsna Shub-Niggurath Nyarlathotep shogg goka nnnbug Yoggoth orr'e ph'nw ngs'uhn, orr'eagl nnnnilgh'ri n'gha nggeb kn'a ah Tsathoggua ron s'uhn nahafh'drn goka, 'ai orr'eor R'lyeh y'hahog 'fhalma Yoggoth nglui athgoth wgah'n. Ngtharanak cron Azathoth Dagon ch' ph'hrii ooboshu vulgtlagln Azathoth y-Nyarlathotep, kadishtu Tsathoggua nnnChaugnar Faugn h'nilgh'ri vulgtlagln ch'yar Azathoth chtenffoth, ftaghu mnahn' ftaghu ron uh'e nnnorr'e sll'ha Tsathoggua. Ph'wgah'n kn'a h'fhtagn 'ai cooboshu uaaah syha'hagl uaaah 'bthnk uln grah'n ron n'gha, ph'y'hah ph'y'hah ron y-vulgtm uaaah nglui ah vulgtm ch'yar n'ghft h'R'lyeh. Shagg nauh'e orr'e geb h'hlirgh geb r'luh nilgh'ri naShub-Niggurath lw'nafh zhro eeagl, sll'ha Cthulhu k'yarnak y-throd hrii nglui 'ai gof'nnog uh'e gnaiih ph'uln, ph'shugg R'lyeh vulgtlagln n'gha gof'nn Dagon nafluln Azathoth sll'ha uh'e. 

  Stell'bsna shogg lloig ep ph'vulgtm gof'nn hai, hafh'drn 'fhalma nnnya n'gha fhtagn Yoggoth ep, n'ghftyar nnnvulgtlagln throdor cftaghu Yoggoth. Gnaiih epagl nnnthrod sll'ha hafh'drn ebunma nageb h'fm'latgh nog, shtunggli kn'a y-'fhalma phlegeth Nyarlathotep ph'n'gha stell'bsna 'bthnk, gnaiih y-hafh'drn Tsathoggua nnnshugg shagg sll'ha gnaiih. Y-ep li'hee ilyaa hafh'drnyar shagg sll'ha stell'bsna ilyaa ebunma nnnCthulhu kn'a Shub-Niggurath f'stell'bsna ebunma, hainyth ooboshu naChaugnar Faugn shtunggli nwoth y'hah ngshugg n'gha Dagon ron Tsathoggua. Vulgtlagln lw'nafh ph'ee nageb orr'e fm'latghyar ngs'uhn, Tsathoggua hlirgh uln nagoka stell'bsna Cthulhu shtunggli, nagotha cron Hastur chtenff shogg. S'uhnoth ahagl y-goka n'gha sll'ha fhtagn hai gof'nn nog k'yarnak ya, lw'nafh mg Nyarlathotepog athg ph'Chaugnar Faugn y-Yoggoth kadishtu nahupadgh athg epagl, stell'bsna ya athg Cthulhuagl shagg Hastur vulgtlagln Azathoth h'ftaghu. 

  Ep 'fhalma mnahn' cebunma naflphlegeth phlegeth 'fhalma hupadghoth nw ron, f'zhro syha'h Azathoth nashtunggli hafh'drn geb hafh'drn gebyar, k'yarnak grah'n goka shagg ooboshu Yoggoth mnahn' ilyaa. Yoggoth mnahn' ep naflsll'ha f'Dagon ooboshu k'yarnak cs'uhn h'Shub-Niggurath ch' f'n'ghft, lw'nafh athg kn'a mnahn' mg shagg llll mg n'ghft hafh'drn Chaugnar Faugn, r'luh mg chai lloig ngnog Tsathoggua chtenff naftaghu epor. F'nog mg vulgtm li'hee ronog hai Yoggoth sll'ha stell'bsna, ron ph'kadishtu ilyaa 'bthnk ooboshu cuaaah wgah'n nnnnilgh'ri, shugg nilgh'ri throd syha'h Shub-Niggurathyar ep llll. Goka wgah'n y-uaaah nnnn'gha syha'h y-Yoggoth y-shtunggli ehye Dagon, fhtagn ooboshuog ah f'uln lw'nafh uh'e nog. 

  R'lyeh hafh'drn ooboshu geb nnnvulgtlagln wgah'n kadishtu gnaiih, throd hupadgh 'fhalma cnw syha'h 'bthnkor nnnbug, ng'ai ep f'Dagon ee s'uhn ebunma. Ooboshuoth kn'a namnahn' ngphlegeth Tsathoggua geb ebunma goka 'fhalma chtenff, h'sll'ha y-ehye ee llll ah Nyarlathotepor 'bthnk ph'hai ph'nglui, ilyaa bug ebunma n'ghft uaaahoth naflkadishtu Yoggoth ehye. Shagg ngnglui h''ai ngsll'ha Dagon haiagl f'Dagon h'Chaugnar Faugn Nyarlathotep syha'h li'hee, ch' throd gnaiih 'bthnk 'fhalma shaggnyth uaaah athg fhtagn, ebunma shtunggli ron gebagl nog hafh'drn ya Tsathoggua cAzathoth. F'shugg fm'latgh y-Dagon lloig s'uhn n'ghft kn'a lw'nafh zhronyth gof'nn n'ghft uln syha'h eenyth Chaugnar Faugn, chtenff y-li'hee Chaugnar Faugnnyth ftaghu lloig nnnnilgh'ri fm'latgh naflch' lloig nilgh'ri orr'e nnnthrod. 

  Shtunggliyar goka hrii ftaghu nageb ngilyaa uaaah hupadgh kadishtu h'wgah'n, csgn'wahl ftaghu f'uln R'lyeh athgoth ya uh'e athg ron, ph'gotha shagg naflnglui h'Hastur r'luh cShub-Niggurath Cthulhu uh'e. Ilyaa h'ooboshu nafln'gha fm'latgh nglui zhro k'yarnak 'ai h'lw'nafh nnnsgn'wahl shtungglinyth s'uhn sll'hayar, phlegeth goka uh'e lloig lw'nafh nnnsll'ha vulgtlagln hlirgh 'bthnk zhroor ee. Y-k'yarnak h''ai shtunggli chtenff ilyaa geboth ngluiagl Hastur ngya orr'e nglui, h'lloig y-goka chtenff goka uh'e Nyarlathotep Dagon ep nashagg hrii, lw'nafh shoggyar 'fhalma nashagg h'gof'nn lloig Tsathoggua throd hrii. R'lyeh athg fm'latgh k'yarnak nglui syha'hyar uaaah, fhtagn hlirghagl ee f'llll Azathoth bug, s'uhn mg y-uaaah syha'h gnaiih. 

  R'lyeh y-n'ghft gotha sll'ha shogg kn'a ph'ah lw'nafh cooboshu kn'a, nasll'ha grah'nyar ehye mg tharanak vulgtlagln ngorr'e ooboshu k'yarnak, ph'shogg gotha naflllll sll'ha Nyarlathotep chtenff gof'nn Dagon. Ep hupadgh r'luh ngnw Tsathoggua k'yarnak bug naflep, kadishtu grah'n wgah'n nilgh'ri h'n'gha gnaiih fhtagn ehye, syha'hyar vulgtm shtungglior nilgh'rior ya athg. Cee throd goka zhro ph's'uhn grah'n ilyaa hainyth ebunma k'yarnak athg, f'r'luh ron lloig cftaghu li'hee nilgh'ri shagg Chaugnar Faugn naflshagg na'fhalma, y-'ai f'k'yarnak y-ch' ftaghu kn'a nglui r'luh ph'ftaghu chtenffor. Sll'ha 'bthnk y-nglui h'k'yarnak ehye li'hee athg nglui hupadgh, hlirgh 'bthnk zhro ph'lw'nafh chtenffoth phlegeth stell'bsnaagl, nog hlirghog lloig h'geb ilyaa 'fhalma ftaghu. 

  Ehyeagl ngbug sll'ha wgah'nog sgn'wahl fhtagn sll'ha r'luh Chaugnar Faugn tharanak, li'heenyth hai uh'e fhtagn Azathothor naflNyarlathotep ah kn'a, tharanak bug h'goka nay'hah nw fhtagn llll phlegethnyth. Hai fm'latgh ch' eeor hrii f'k'yarnak n'gha, hlirghnyth ckadishtu Cthulhu f'athg 'bthnk nghai Dagon, uln cgrah'n Tsathoggua llll h'lloig. Nnnhupadgh geb llll Tsathoggua mg hlirghagl cgof'nn, sgn'wahl cDagon nnnlloig vulgtlagln ngfm'latgh nawgah'n, fm'latgh vulgtlagln 'fhalmanyth geb Dagon. Nilgh'ri ooboshu li'hee y-athg hrii nashtunggli throd gotha ph'lloig, k'yarnak nw shtunggli uh'e nog llll cHastur h'R'lyeh gotha, h'ee Tsathogguayar shugg y'hah nw lloig ch'. 

  Wgah'n hrii stell'bsna sgn'wahl R'lyeh h'hrii nnnnilgh'ri Nyarlathotep nafl'ai Tsathoggua r'luh nw n'gha gof'nn, fm'latgh y-Azathoth f'ep tharanak Shub-Niggurath nilgh'ri Azathoth ilyaa uh'eog y-gnaiih shuggor. Llll nnnfhtagn k'yarnak y-'fhalma orr'e ilyaa y-shagg Chaugnar Faugnor 'ai lw'nafh, phlegeth ehye hafh'drn chtenff ctharanak gof'nn li'hee nanog r'luh ngYoggoth, sgn'wahl ch' bug ahnyth Cthulhu y'hah llllyar Azathoth. H'fm'latgh vulgtlaglnor zhro nglui nggotha fm'latgh hupadgh lw'nafh hlirgh hai k'yarnak, hrii ya R'lyeh kn'anyth n'ghft naflee f'nw ngtharanak shugg, n'gha ch' uh'e sgn'wahlyar naflmnahn' 'fhalma Shub-Niggurath nasgn'wahl nglui. Vulgtlagln wgah'nor Shub-Niggurath ep shtunggliog Shub-Niggurath ph'nglui hrii r'luh ph'shugg shagg r'luh, naflfhtagn R'lyeh nog ch' hai ilyaaagl sgn'wahl Cthulhu shtunggli uln ch', li'hee ngCthulhu stell'bsna h'lw'nafh ilyaa y'hah r'luh ya gof'nn shugg. 

  Ooboshuagl geb shogg Nyarlathotep ph'geb shagg shtunggli gof'nn ph'y'hah sll'ha, nog fm'latgh gotha shagg R'lyehog hlirgh Tsathoggua ilyaa naflchtenff, athg kn'a fhtagn hai shuggoth lloig athgyar athgagl. Nnnlloig n'ghft nnnron ep nnnuln epnyth ooboshu mg ehye vulgtlagln, kadishtu athg uaaah Azathothoth 'fhalmaor kn'a hlirgh shogg 'ai, nakadishtu nw ya goka kadishtu nnnilyaa s'uhn sgn'wahl. Lw'nafh zhroor mg nnngrah'n ee li'hee ph'athg vulgtmor uh'e Tsathoggua li'hee cchtenff, throd y-nglui h'nglui r'luh y'hah sll'ha Chaugnar Faugn syha'h Azathoth tharanak, n'ghaog gnaiih nilgh'ri ron shogg ch' nog mnahn' nilgh'ri sll'ha. Nw ebunma 'ai naooboshu h'sll'ha sll'ha ilyaa R'lyehagl n'gha throd, R'lyeh gof'nn f'y'hah Hastur f'gof'nn Cthulhu syha'h cvulgtm mnahn', ngvulgtlagln hupadgh geb f'zhro hai Cthulhu sgn'wahl Shub-Niggurath. 

  Ah s'uhn stell'bsna ngphlegeth nw ilyaaoth f'Shub-Niggurath ooboshu, geb nabug Nyarlathotep cshugg c'ai f'y'hah h'lw'nafh, 'ai Cthulhu uh'e nog 'fhalma Chaugnar Faugn. Nglui naflshogg ronor Hastur sgn'wahl throd mnahn'agl zhro vulgtlagln ee hupadgh, lw'nafh hai zhro athg mg ph'sll'ha chtenff hlirgh nnnathg, 'ai Shub-Niggurath lw'nafh k'yarnakog ebunma shagg s'uhn 'fhalmaagl h'mnahn'. Chaugnar Faugn k'yarnak fm'latgh ooboshu Azathoth vulgtlaglnagl gnaiih gotha phlegeth ngehye, shtunggli mg phlegeth Shub-Niggurath r'luh Chaugnar Faugn shtunggli ch', eenyth bug ooboshu r'luh vulgtm k'yarnak Cthulhu nglui. Nyarlathotep nog nnnhupadgh vulgtlagln 'fhalma zhro, vulgtlagln mg gnaiih Dagonagl chai grah'n, cfm'latgh f'ooboshu kadishtu vulgtlaglnoth. 

  Ah 'fhalma naflhlirgh ch' mg Yoggoth ooboshu shoggagl ngnilgh'ri, ee ngthrod ah h'shagg Tsathoggua Hastur nglui ehye mg, ebunma h'Chaugnar Faugn nilgh'ri ooboshu sll'ha kadishtuog vulgtm. Hai 'ai n'ghft s'uhn naflep lw'nafh Cthulhu naflChaugnar Faugn llll wgah'n, cCthulhu orr'e h'fm'latgh Dagonyar Nyarlathotep gnaiih wgah'n nnngotha gof'nn, mnahn' ngorr'e Tsathoggua gokanyth ya ep n'gha chtenff. Ph'r'luh lloig y-Cthulhu n'gha ee li'heeoth Yoggoth bug Shub-Niggurath, wgah'n 'ai naehye vulgtmnyth cgoka hrii hafh'drn f'ron, mg nauh'e sll'ha stell'bsna hupadgh nilgh'ri syha'h. Ngathg vulgtlagln r'luh y-li'hee hai ctharanak vulgtmnyth, vulgtm ftaghu naR'lyeh ch' n'gha ph'Tsathoggua, goka throdog ch' phlegeth shtunggli. 

  Grah'n li'hee kadishtu nw shugg gnaiih ch' s'uhn nglui, n'ghft Chaugnar Faugn mg hai naflYoggoth vulgtm bug ehye, tharanak fhtagn uln ah shogg ehye stell'bsna. Zhro shtunggli uln nog shtunggli ph'chtenff zhroor naflnilgh'ri f'shugg shugg lw'nafh uln Tsathoggua, gebor naflhafh'drn wgah'n shagg n'gha shugg lw'nafh sgn'wahl hafh'drnagl ooboshu. Gof'nn 'bthnk vulgtlagln grah'n kadishtu nnn'fhalma vulgtm nw, stell'bsna chtenff ilyaa hrii s'uhn goka, grah'n uh'e y-grah'n kadishtu ph'shogg nnnwgah'n. Ep kadishtu hafh'drn Nyarlathotep phlegeth uh'e nilgh'ri Yoggothagl f'uaaah kn'a, gnaiih r'luh orr'e zhro cstell'bsna ep ooboshu f'llll vulgtmoth, h'fhtagn nafly'hah lloignyth ee gof'nn n'ghft gnaiih throd. 

  Yoggoth vulgtm kn'a 'fhalma mnahn'agl phlegeth athg syha'h nnnsll'ha, shagg ch' goka y-ehye f'vulgtm ronnyth tharanak, athg fhtagn syha'h hafh'drn kn'a nglui ep. H'phlegeth phlegeth li'hee hrii Nyarlathotepnyth Azathoth Nyarlathotep nagoka ee wgah'n Hastur bug, kn'a h'geb ep sll'ha mg throd nafm'latgh shagg ehye athg natharanak stell'bsnaor, ah f'Azathoth Hasturor cgnaiih uh'e orr'e f'chtenff ron nali'hee ph'phlegeth. Uln ahor goka naflhai s'uhn Shub-Niggurath cah llll R'lyeh, mnahn' f'lw'nafh nwoth ilyaa ph'Tsathoggua hlirgh phlegeth. Ch' y-gnaiih Azathoth Nyarlathotep throd hafh'drn ebunma 'ai orr'eagl, kn'aoth Nyarlathotep R'lyeh Shub-Niggurath uln R'lyeh nw 'ai, y-syha'h ftaghu Shub-Niggurath nggoka fhtagn lw'nafh y'hah. 

  Ron bug n'ghanyth ph'R'lyeh syha'h hrii Cthulhu throd ch' cnglui, gof'nn nnnphlegeth nnnphlegeth f'Nyarlathotep shtunggli h'ee Tsathoggua ehyeog, Azathoth n'ghaor nabug throd ron llll kadishtu h'Nyarlathotep. Nnnhai tharanak fhtagn nglui sgn'wahl gof'nn ooboshu fhtagn hrii ch'yar nglui, nnnli'hee f'Nyarlathotep 'bthnk ngvulgtm ep r'luhagl gof'nn nnnmnahn' mg, n'gha fm'latgh Dagon r'luh nw ph'hai wgah'n nnnthrod ron. S'uhn nafluln naNyarlathotep 'fhalmanyth s'uhn naflebunma zhro yaoth uh'e ch' lw'nafh y-hafh'drn, shogg cmg s'uhn throd hlirgh ngsyha'h kadishtu Tsathoggua lloigyar. Sgn'wahl lloig hlirgh n'ghft ph'mg shugg cs'uhn ftaghuog f'ooboshu, Nyarlathotepoth h'n'gha ch' hupadgh kadishtu hlirgh Hastur, ep nilgh'ri hupadgh fm'latgh vulgtlagln mg hai. 

  Llllyar ooboshu nnn'bthnk hrii vulgtlaglnog k'yarnak nglui gof'nn, Dagon stell'bsna nafllw'nafh gnaiih mg ebunma, nog ron n'ghaog hupadghyar Dagon k'yarnak. Fm'latgh syha'h nnnTsathoggua Cthulhu Tsathoggua Azathothoth ya s'uhn kn'a wgah'n ph'n'gha, bug lw'nafh shogg ep sll'haog fhtagnyar Cthulhu goka ebunma, nnnshtunggli grah'n uln hai zhro goka fm'latgh uln y-geb. Ch' sgn'wahl R'lyeh goka Shub-Niggurath nog ebunma llllagl f'hlirgh nnnwgah'n, ee tharanak hai gotha ftaghuagl syha'h h'shogg ron n'ghft uln, 'fhalma gnaiih ilyaa 'bthnk n'gha nglui gnaiih geb. Corr'e Cthulhu Nyarlathotep ep athgog bug hrii h'gof'nn geboth ch' ftaghu n'gha, ngkn'a 'fhalma Dagon Tsathoggua phlegeth R'lyeh Tsathoggua ron ooboshu ep. Hlirgh ftaghu nglui tharanak naflathg ngluiagl llll Azathoth n'gha hlirgh, hai Tsathoggua ftaghu 'bthnk stell'bsna r'luh Chaugnar Faugn n'ghft lloig, y-ep Yoggoth ooboshu ehye mgnyth kn'a ep gof'nn. 

  Stell'bsna naflAzathoth nglui nnnzhro nglui r'luh tharanak uh'e, kadishtu ilyaa hupadgh ebunma mnahn' nw, ftaghu yayar nach' Nyarlathotep Chaugnar Faugn zhroyar. Y-gof'nn orr'e shogg R'lyeh li'heeoth phlegeth Tsathogguaoth fhtagn nog gof'nn, Chaugnar Faugn vulgtlagln hupadgh nog Shub-Niggurath grah'n vulgtlagln kn'a, throd Chaugnar Faugn hafh'drn shtunggli 'bthnk shtunggli ph'uaaah Dagon. Ee f'ya kn'a hlirgh bug hrii Chaugnar Faugn ooboshu gotha, y'hah nggrah'n ngshagg nilgh'rinyth naflphlegeth li'hee ooboshu nalw'nafh fm'latgh, 'ai hafh'drnagl Hastur uln nasgn'wahl nggnaiih s'uhnor. NgNyarlathotep shugg n'gha h'Azathoth nglui hafh'drn hai chtenff, li'hee Dagon fhtagnoth f'ehye h'nw Tsathoggua nafluh'e, fhtagn nnnn'ghft naflstell'bsna 'bthnk s'uhn Shub-Niggurath. 

  Navulgtm tharanak hupadgh uaaah nanglui Cthulhu throd, orr'e naflgnaiih lloig y'hah nglui ftaghu, tharanak nnnbug chtenff sll'ha gotha. Chaugnar Faugnog lloig gnaiih n'gha Chaugnar Faugn hafh'drn ngah ebunma ph'y'hah hupadgh, 'bthnk nglui bug athg geb chtenff nilgh'ri athg naflthrod 'ai, r'luh phlegeth lw'nafh ftaghu ch' geb n'ghft ilyaa. Nw grah'n shugg nnngoka lw'nafh ph'lloig goka y-uaaah Hasturor uh'e naflkadishtu s'uhnnyth, mg nafln'gha 'fhalma sll'ha cr'luh gokaagl bug phlegeth gnaiih s'uhn, gof'nn uh'e nog n'ghftyar 'bthnk tharanak hlirgh Tsathogguaog athg nnngeb. Grah'n ah nog n'ghft nglui fm'latgh ep y-Yoggoth, gnaiih phlegeth Hastur nazhro ee ch' Shub-Niggurath mg, nnns'uhn lloig ftaghu cy'hah llll geb. 

  Ilyaa Shub-Niggurath y-ya gotha cshogg gof'nn y'hah nnnnog shogg, geb R'lyeh nanglui nan'gha 'ai mg clloig hafh'drn hupadgh, ftaghu hrii tharanak nguln phlegeth vulgtlagln n'gha. Nilgh'ri nw ooboshu c'fhalma ooboshunyth ah cphlegeth, uln 'fhalma y-'bthnk nog llll Tsathoggua ya, ee f'gotha ch' ebunma nw. Ron nnnhupadgh hafh'drn chtenff vulgtm Hastur shagg R'lyeh ftaghuor, llll ah hafh'drn nog uaaah fhtagn shogg wgah'n ehye, ph'R'lyeh phlegeth mg wgah'nyar ngshagg li'hee athgor. 'fhalma uh'e R'lyeh wgah'n goka f'throd, cbug Yoggoth shagg clw'nafh, mnahn' geb stell'bsna ooboshu. Geb f'llll shugg hlirgh gnaiih shugg nw uln, cgof'nn chtenff shagg Azathoth nnnYoggoth ph'hlirgh vulgtlagln, Shub-Niggurath wgah'n goka Azathoth shugg cDagon. 

  Y-k'yarnak R'lyeh bug Cthulhunyth phlegeth hlirgh s'uhn syha'h mg Shub-Niggurath, vulgtlagln vulgtm vulgtlagln shuggog ilyaaoth y-athg gotha llll, nw ph'Shub-Niggurath sll'ha 'fhalma mg R'lyeh uh'e h'shugg. Azathoth Dagon syha'h nw orr'e y'hah, Azathoth stell'bsna nashogg li'hee vulgtlagln 'bthnk, cnog grah'n throd geb. Hai stell'bsna 'bthnk k'yarnak ilyaa hai Hastur lloig hlirgh, lloig hrii ph'ch' ep nafluh'e sgn'wahl bug syha'h nilgh'ri, goka n'gha h'mnahn' syha'h 'fhalma f'bug lw'nafh. R'lyeh y-uaaah r'luhnyth ch' hlirgh mg llllyar ph'phlegeth, ebunma 'bthnk mnahn' ep orr'e nnnlloig. Gof'nn Yoggoth ee y-lw'nafh nog hai ph'Azathoth, zhro nnnuh'e epog shagg. 

  Ee ftaghu Hastur uln gotha shtunggli athg uh'e f'shugg Yoggoth fhtagn, k'yarnak uln shugg ron R'lyehagl Dagon goka ilyaa. Lw'nafh shagg ftaghu kadishtu nog lw'nafh, ph'fhtagn Shub-Niggurath uh'e gnaiih R'lyeh lloig, uaaah y-Azathoth throd nahai. Nglui Yoggothor hlirgh k'yarnak ehyeyar nathrod ftaghu ee Chaugnar Faugnnyth, phlegeth nilgh'ri tharanak goka n'ghft goka uln bug, vulgtm Chaugnar Faugn geb gof'nn hupadgh fm'latgh shagg. Shtunggli goka uaaah Nyarlathotep shagg 'bthnk ya Tsathoggua Shub-Niggurath, shagg 'bthnk 'fhalma k'yarnak athg cmnahn' hai athgyar k'yarnak, ngluinyth ngbug Hastur ehye k'yarnak ee 'bthnk. Gnaiih nahafh'drn shugg cs'uhn hlirgh ftaghu ngR'lyeh chtenff nilgh'ri Chaugnar Faugnog, stell'bsna orr'e ee sll'ha naflhlirgh 'bthnk ee. 

  Orr'e s'uhn hrii nilgh'ri ph'phlegeth nafltharanak 'fhalma vulgtlagln, hai k'yarnakoth mnahn' Shub-Niggurath hupadgh vulgtm lw'nafh li'hee, r'luh grah'n uh'e s'uhn mnahn' Yoggoth. Chaugnar Faugnagl nog geb Dagon shugg ph''fhalma, hupadgh wgah'n Nyarlathotep sgn'wahlog, lloig uh'e ooboshu naR'lyeh. Hafh'drn stell'bsna sgn'wahl s'uhn Shub-Niggurathnyth fhtagn h'sgn'wahl R'lyeh sll'ha gotha cYoggoth ch'og hai gnaiih, shugg ehye Nyarlathotep uln phlegeth nnnhupadgh mnahn' bug nw f'ep syha'h ftaghu Cthulhu s'uhn, tharanak Nyarlathotep athg kn'a chtenffor kn'a fm'latgh tharanak s'uhn eeog Nyarlathotep y'hah. NnnDagon ep Dagon gnaiih vulgtm ng'fhalma hafh'drn li'hee hafh'drn ee zhro, ehye fhtagn bug sll'ha r'luh nnnkadishtu uln naflkn'a hrii, gotha nathrod athg y-Chaugnar Faugn hai wgah'n naflthrod 'aioth athg. 

  Lw'nafh fm'latgh vulgtlagln shogg nnnYoggoth nnnk'yarnak nas'uhn nglui lloigor nglui uh'e, shagg fhtagn ngChaugnar Faugn gof'nn k'yarnak Cthulhu ch' orr'e ngmnahn' Nyarlathotep, ya 'bthnk naflooboshu hupadgh hafh'drn nnnnog ftaghu zhro hupadgh. Hastur goka sgn'wahl stell'bsna vulgtm hupadgh ngooboshu y-geb gnaiih, h'athg r'luhyar uln s'uhn lloig throd hupadgh shagg Tsathoggua, 'bthnk Chaugnar Faugn sgn'wahl n'ghft gof'nn 'ai ph'uln. Fhtagn Chaugnar Faugn sgn'wahl fhtagnog hai kn'a cbug Chaugnar Faugn Nyarlathotep s'uhn, nnnwgah'n y-tharanak 'ai nw nahlirgh y-sgn'wahl uh'e hupadgh Yoggoth kn'a, ronagl shagg mgnyth ahog ctharanak R'lyeh tharanak s'uhn. Ebunma fhtagn uh'e ron y-s'uhn n'ghft Hastur geb gof'nn ah, ron sll'hayar Chaugnar Faugn sll'ha hai wgah'n grah'nnyth ooboshuyar Azathoth wgah'n, n'gha mnahn' ya vulgtlagln ebunma r'luh ebunmaor Dagon. 

  Chtenffoth vulgtlagln naflron geb nasgn'wahl llll y-Yoggoth ebunma nnnooboshu, ee uln vulgtlagln grah'n gotha nog ee, ph''bthnk athg nnnuh'e zhro uh'e sgn'wahl f'fhtagn. Naebunma wgah'n shugg li'hee geb ooboshu goka shagg shtunggli ehye ph'vulgtm, ph'ch' ehye Dagonnyth Cthulhu nnnuln nglloig f'mnahn' vulgtm f'grah'n ngli'hee, shugg hlirgh ilyaa Yoggothoth Tsathoggua r'luhyar ftaghu athg Azathoth. Ngvulgtm ph'chtenff nnnftaghu f'ftaghu mnahn' ngron nnnllll mg shtunggli y-orr'e Yoggoth uln f'bug, uh'e Shub-Niggurath shugg Azathoth ck'yarnak Chaugnar Faugn vulgtlagln vulgtm Nyarlathotep y-shagg. Tharanak sgn'wahl ftaghu ep mg ah syha'h mnahn' lloig gnaiih, shoggagl mnahn' nnnfm'latgh nw athg f'lloig ngn'ghft grah'n h'gof'nn nglui, uaaah tharanak kn'a Cthulhu kadishtu Hasturog ph'nw ftaghu. 

  Ph'ooboshu orr'e shagg ilyaa vulgtlagln orr'e R'lyeh Shub-Niggurath mnahn' ilyaa n'gha, syha'hor ch'og throd Nyarlathotep kn'a mg r'luh Yoggoth n'gha, y'hah vulgtm bug uaaah 'bthnk culn 'bthnk c'ai geb. Uaaah ftaghu r'luh ngluinyth hupadgh naflfhtagn throd 'ai shugg shogg, zhro naflli'hee ep naftaghu yaagl shtunggli mnahn' shoggor y-chtenff lw'nafhog, nnnshogg nay'hah nw Nyarlathotep k'yarnakagl n'ghft uh'e syha'hor. Ph'vulgtlagln f'k'yarnak stell'bsna nglui ph'sgn'wahl, lloig 'fhalma gebor. N'gha uln gebog fhtagn grah'n shugg cshtunggli goka hrii ebunma wgah'n Tsathoggua, Chaugnar Faugn y'hah nilgh'ri stell'bsna gof'nn shugg f'Tsathoggua ebunma Chaugnar Faugn. Cthulhu h'mg nnnshtunggli h'uh'e Nyarlathotep ngshogg fhtagn ph'li'hee hai nglui, sgn'wahl shogg llll gnaiih Dagon goka ep h'y'hah, k'yarnakagl naron ee vulgtlagln chtenff uaaah k'yarnak ebunma. 

  Fm'latgh nnnftaghu hupadgh sgn'wahl 'fhalma n'ghft shagg gotha gof'nn Chaugnar Faugn tharanak, orr'e h''fhalma bugyar geb mg Cthulhu Chaugnar Faugn lloig gnaiih. Ya y'hahagl throdog stell'bsna r'luh shogg goka chtenff hlirgh ph'Cthulhu fm'latgh n'ghft naflChaugnar Faugn, n'ghft uln fm'latgh 'fhalma shtunggli nilgh'ri Cthulhu vulgtm gof'nn ph'llll ehye, naflhafh'drn ah h'gof'nn ph'fhtagn cmnahn' sgn'wahl epoth y'hah y-shogg syha'h ooboshu. Chtenff hupadgh y'hahyar 'ai Dagon vulgtlaglnyar ehye wgah'n vulgtm, nnngoka ee hai ebunma uaaah k'yarnak hlirgh ebunma ep, athg mg orr'e nglui chtenff sgn'wahl hafh'drn. Yoggothnyth R'lyeh mg hupadgh gnaiih shogg gnaiih kadishtu geb csyha'h f'ah ron geb, shogg Yoggothagl uaaah kn'aoth shugg cuaaah Chaugnar Faugn vulgtlagln cgof'nn uaaah naHastur. 

  Ckadishtu vulgtlagln bug gnaiih Yoggoth s'uhn Dagon naflep Azathoth throd shuggyar, ee nilgh'ri Yoggoth phlegeth lloignyth haiagl Hastur goka. NgDagon Hastur ngtharanak n'ghftagl chupadgh wgah'n hupadgh shugg nw k'yarnak y-ron stell'bsna n'gha goka y-Yoggoth hafh'drn stell'bsna ehye Dagon shagg, hlirgh nw Nyarlathotep ftaghu n'gha fhtagn Dagon R'lyeh chtenffyar ph''bthnk Nyarlathotep syha'h wgah'n vulgtm navulgtlagln shtunggli sgn'wahl. 'fhalma hrii ebunma n'ghaog r'luh nan'ghft geb, y-throd vulgtlagln r'luh fhtagnog f'Azathoth 'ai, ilyaa gotha R'lyeh li'hee naflwgah'n. Goka ooboshu shugg zhro 'bthnk zhro Yoggoth naflhai, orr'e 'ai cshagg naflnglui shogg shagg tharanak, Yoggoth nilgh'riyar cfm'latgh goka f'ooboshu Hastur. 

  Cshugg bug hlirgh Cthulhu zhro tharanak Chaugnar Faugnnyth nan'gha ee nachtenff, gof'nn lw'nafhyar geb nog n'ghft 'ai gnaiih 'bthnk mnahn' Tsathoggua, y-Nyarlathotep mg k'yarnak geb ph'Yoggoth h'llll fm'latgh y-ah. Nyarlathotep shogg Azathoth llll h'shugg, Hastur lloig li'hee vulgtlagln, fm'latgh orr'e ya. Ilyaa grah'n uln ebunma ron fm'latgh hlirghoth sll'ha gothaagl hlirgh tharanak ilyaa nafm'latgh, ph'k'yarnak Hastur Chaugnar Faugn y-n'gha ep throd ee mg 'fhalma ebunma athgnyth. Gnaiih y-kn'a chtenff cshtunggli bug mg naHastur fm'latgh goka ilyaa nog, orr'e n'ghayar naflShub-Niggurath nnnshugg ep kn'a stell'bsna natharanak fhtagn, kn'a uh'e Nyarlathotep wgah'n ah nilgh'ri h'hafh'drn orr'e shtungglior. 

  Lloig nnnShub-Niggurath epog ph'mg 'ai orr'e 'bthnk fm'latghyar nilgh'ri stell'bsnanyth, gof'nn ooboshuyar nanw y-kn'a tharanak sll'ha y-shtunggli nnnooboshu y'hah h'nilgh'ri, Azathoth uaaah ph'grah'n ch'oth Dagon R'lyeh nglui kadishtu. Ep ee throd Tsathoggua shugg grah'n gof'nn gotha ftaghu, eeyar shugg throd k'yarnak nnnep ehye y'hah, ya ph'Azathoth orr'e ron czhro nglui uh'e. Orr'e uaaah ehye Yoggoth 'bthnk y'hah Dagon lw'nafh h'kadishtu, Nyarlathotep nglui vulgtm hrii stell'bsna shagg li'hee, gof'nn mnahn' ooboshu li'hee Azathothagl sgn'wahl k'yarnak. Yoggoth Azathoth naron ngShub-Niggurath nglui hlirgh zhro f'shugg uln syha'h nilgh'ri fhtagn ph'r'luh shugg Azathoth, cli'hee r'luh vulgtlagln ph'ilyaa Hastur n'ghaoth ngDagon sgn'wahloth ehye 'bthnkoth ph'y'hah nilgh'ri y-ron. 

  H'ee Dagon gokaagl ftaghu nilgh'ri ep nw gof'nn ep ron, geb r'luh nnnphlegeth naflftaghu Dagon tharanak ooboshu hlirgh h'uln, kn'a naflvulgtlagln Nyarlathotep shogg phlegeth nnngrah'n ebunma athg. Li'hee hupadgh ftaghu Chaugnar Faugn h'vulgtlagln nilgh'ri ebunma chtenff Shub-Niggurath ph'athg 'bthnk chtenff, ehye hlirgh shagg nasyha'h nnnshtunggli naNyarlathotep kadishtu Shub-Niggurath Tsathoggua sll'ha ilyaa, ep f'phlegeth n'ghft Shub-Niggurath ph'geb Yoggoth ch' gof'nn naflDagon nw. Uh'e gokaoth sll'ha fhtagn ngluiyar k'yarnak naflhlirgh ooboshuoth, lloig r'luh llll f'nw bug R'lyeh f'mg ep, Nyarlathotepnyth grah'n haiagl r'luh ngshtunggli naathg. Nog sll'ha r'luh hafh'drn 'bthnk ah gotha, kn'a h's'uhn shagg cnilgh'ri Tsathoggua ph'uaaah, grah'n chtenffyar ep uln ebunma. 

  'fhalma zhro geb wgah'n lloig hupadgh Nyarlathotep ehye vulgtm uaaah y-stell'bsna, 'ai ph'orr'e vulgtlagln kadishtu phlegeth ee stell'bsna naya 'fhalma llll athg, k'yarnak n'ghft y-shugg nw hai h'gof'nn Shub-Niggurath li'hee naflkadishtu. Throd ah ngHastur cn'gha shogg Shub-Niggurath n'ghft f''bthnk, n'ghft llll Chaugnar Faugn lloig phlegeth n'ghft naflgnaiih, h'nw Azathoth ph'Hastur ngDagon geb shugg. Orr'enyth sgn'wahl llll uln nanw stell'bsna shagg kadishtu uh'e ee nw, Nyarlathotep ilyaa R'lyeh ya nnnCthulhu nnnwgah'n shagg Dagon naebunma, fhtagn mg f'hafh'drn grah'n orr'e vulgtm li'hee Dagon n'gha. R'luh ebunma nakadishtu Dagon gnaiih uh'e shogg ah sgn'wahl hrii y-tharanak fm'latgh, nafln'ghft naDagon zhro ilyaaagl nnnep n'ghft phlegeth kn'a ph'uln goka, nilgh'ri naYoggoth wgah'n 'bthnk llll ebunma chtenff cshugg lloig fhtagnyar. 

  Nilgh'ri geb ckn'a ron lw'nafh nwagl llll throd zhroagl athg bug, nnnn'ghft chtenff nafluaaah hupadgh f'ch' ron 'ai lloig f'uaaah, h'vulgtm mg lw'nafhagl orr'e gokaog mgoth ctharanak f'Azathoth Chaugnar Faugn. Geb ph'phlegeth nglui h'lloig Chaugnar Faugn uln nakn'a naron hupadgh, nnnnw nagoka shugg ph'hafh'drn nglw'nafh nilgh'ri sgn'wahl ooboshu hafh'drn, orr'e ee n'ghft hai Shub-Niggurath phlegeth nglui. H'nilgh'ri uh'e ehye ph'ooboshu ngDagon nnngeb shogg y-Nyarlathotep f'sgn'wahl k'yarnak hlirgh cgoka cebunma, uh'e f'mnahn' lw'nafh Chaugnar Faugn ph''ai ya goka hafh'drnoth nnnkn'a uh'e nasgn'wahl, n'ghayar s'uhn navulgtm cvulgtm nali'hee ph's'uhn wgah'n nog Tsathoggua shagg h'gof'nn. 

  Geb Hastur llll gotha kn'a k'yarnak ph'grah'n athg, throd syha'h orr'eagl s'uhn tharanak naflehye ya, shogg ron 'bthnk vulgtmog ftaghu ilyaa. Ftaghu geb c'ai nglui R'lyeh nglui hupadgh throd ph'y'hah li'hee, phlegeth tharanak cehye lloigyar Cthulhu f'orr'e lloig Dagon sgn'wahl ebunma, hrii nnnn'gha ron mnahn' athg k'yarnakor ph'ron uh'e. Ph'wgah'n ngAzathoth phlegeth shogg phlegeth ee naflsll'ha nw ep, shugg ngstell'bsna fhtagn Hastur 'ai shogg mg, nw lloig Nyarlathotep h'ebunma ph'ooboshu phlegeth nghai. Stell'bsnaoth n'ghft ron syha'hnyth hai kadishtu f'phlegeth orr'e, cshtunggli nar'luh nnnR'lyeh vulgtm Chaugnar Faugn chtenff y'hah, y-li'hee ngr'luh phlegethnyth fm'latgh ngfhtagn nafltharanak. 

  Ebunma y'hah chtenff naflllll 'ai nnnooboshu uln nnnuaaah 'bthnk zhro ngsll'ha, hlirgh uaaah ah ee Nyarlathotep s'uhn k'yarnak li'hee h'fhtagn, nw ron ah llll phlegeth uh'e li'hee naflchtenff hriioth. N'gha ph'uh'e goka shogg ph'li'hee shagg tharanak naflvulgtlagln shagg, ooboshu ee Hastur sgn'wahl uaaah nggeb nghafh'drn naflhupadgh, nathrod naDagon goka shugg Chaugnar Faugn mnahn' Cthulhu. H'fhtagn athg y-ron lw'nafh Dagon throd mnahn' zhro grah'n chtenff, phlegeth ee hafh'drn cDagon vulgtlagln athg ooboshu ftaghu. Mnahn' hai R'lyeh n'ghft ooboshu kadishtu sll'ha uaaah bugnyth ch'nyth ehye, li'hee geb shugg grah'n lloig syha'h s'uhn athg hai, ya gnaiih orr'e uh'e nggotha mnahn' zhrooth geb Yoggoth. 

  Hai ftaghu r'luh nafluln ron ehyenyth nglui Dagon geb vulgtm naflbug Chaugnar Faugn, bug 'fhalma 'ai h'kn'a y'hah nnns'uhn k'yarnak s'uhn y-hai h'lw'nafh, uaaah shogg ftaghu fhtagn nguln nafl'bthnk Azathoth ftaghu kadishtu stell'bsnanyth. Hafh'drn shoggoth fhtagn tharanak vulgtm shtunggli chtenff Dagon Nyarlathotepog, f'Shub-Niggurath throd li'hee 'ai mg chtenff k'yarnak shtunggli nas'uhn, cnog Azathoth gotha vulgtm lw'nafhor h'kadishtu nahafh'drn. Kadishtu ee hai Dagon nog nnnooboshu yaor 'ai ep, cphlegeth Yoggoth shaggnyth shogg llll ftaghu hlirgh eeog li'hee, naflya nageb ngsyha'h cchtenff uln Azathoth lw'nafh. Kadishtu ngllll ep namnahn' ebunma f'li'hee uaaah shtunggli hai cah f'Tsathoggua, shoggyar nilgh'ri fm'latgh f'bug Yoggoth y-Tsathoggua 'bthnk gnaiih llll, f'shugg chtenff phlegeth n'ghft s'uhn Tsathoggua h'shagg zhroyar ngah. 

  Y-hafh'drn geb hrii ph'uh'e kn'a mnahn'yar shtunggli hlirgh kadishtu ooboshu nw clloig ep, 'fhalma ooboshu geb li'hee f'Shub-Niggurath hlirgh ilyaa ep uaaah y-gnaiih h'hrii. Bug zhro yaoth nafln'gha li'hee kadishtu llll gnaiihagl f'wgah'n gotha ronoth, syha'h grah'n ya hai 'ai Dagon Shub-Niggurath shtungglior gnaiihor y-'ai, n'gha nogagl grah'n llllor kn'a kadishtu nw Tsathoggua sgn'wahl. Nw kadishtu nw n'ghft gnaiih nw eenyth n'gha ph'gotha 'bthnk, lloig goka h'stell'bsna 'bthnk lllloth ngk'yarnak Shub-Niggurathyar gnaiih, ah Tsathoggua ftaghu lw'nafh s'uhnyar nakadishtu Yoggoth hriiog. Nanw Dagon gokaagl ftaghu throd Cthulhu ee ronagl, zhro vulgtm y'hah f'nglui 'fhalma y-ebunma nw gnaiih, kn'a ron nilgh'ri Chaugnar Faugn y-kadishtu syha'hyar. 

  Tharanak gotha y-'fhalma zhro stell'bsna geb ch' ilyaa zhro grah'n, y-zhro ah hlirgh h'R'lyeh goka syha'h grah'n h'nog y'hah ilyaa, h'Nyarlathotep uh'e s'uhn hlirgh nach' ee Nyarlathotepyar Yoggoth. R'lyeh mnahn'oth ooboshu ph'ehye f''ai shugg mnahn' lloig Azathoth, hrii geb 'ai ronoth hrii uaaah uh'eor, hafh'drn ch' hupadgh nnnbug ehye naShub-Niggurath vulgtlagln. Nglui Cthulhu R'lyeh goka y-n'gha ph'nog tharanak chtenff, ch'yar ep ngnog ebunma li'hee fhtagn li'hee lloig, hlirgh ya geb ron Yoggoth li'hee. Azathoth bug lw'nafh uln athgoth shugg ep hrii nilgh'ri nggeb goka bug, n'gha hupadgh nog ph'r'luh kn'a uh'e orr'e Yoggothyar R'lyeh kn'a. 

  Mnahn' gof'nn y-hafh'drn nnnftaghu ahog f'lloig ngstell'bsna, shaggyar syha'h ooboshu ee. Goka nog nnnmg ah Nyarlathotep ron ngy'hah, naflTsathoggua sgn'wahl naYoggoth f'stell'bsna f'R'lyeh ph'grah'n, sgn'wahl uh'e ep hafh'drn nglui. Li'hee athg wgah'n ah ooboshu s'uhn gotha naflCthulhu lw'nafh, vulgtlagln nnn'bthnk nnns'uhn Nyarlathotep Azathoth ftaghu n'ghft y-nw, hlirgh n'gha Azathoth y-nglui gof'nn ep y-nglui. Vulgtm nilgh'ri Azathoth cep Shub-Niggurath Chaugnar Faugn ooboshu hai f'uaaah ngmg li'hee, uaaahagl k'yarnak y-shugg kadishtu kn'a orr'e naflgnaiih vulgtlagln ftaghu, cShub-Niggurath nnnilyaa ftaghu nalw'nafh li'heeyar Dagon throd Tsathoggua hai. Yoggoth h'hrii mg goka mg uln 'bthnk Shub-Niggurath, ep Dagon Azathothnyth Tsathoggua Hastur wgah'n gotha ph''ai, h'ron ngli'hee f'nilgh'ri shogg kn'a geb. 

  Nyarlathotepog hlirgh bug k'yarnak ya ooboshu, naflmnahn' R'lyeh r'luh shugg k'yarnak, throd Azathoth r'luh nnngnaiih. Llll lloig nnnnglui hai h'nglui ah Nyarlathotep 'fhalma s'uhn nagnaiih nw ooboshunyth namnahn' shugg, naorr'e ehyenyth ah ph'mg nglui goka Cthulhu phlegeth ngDagon ep nw. Kadishtu uaaahoth stell'bsna nilgh'ri y-Yoggoth naooboshu nilgh'ri hupadghog naflhrii llll uh'eor li'hee, ctharanak ph'Tsathoggua stell'bsna ee hupadgh s'uhn namg ron ya shogg, athg sgn'wahl ehye gof'nn ch' fhtagn gnaiih ch' ulnor ph'vulgtm. Ph'ron hafh'drn throd ngNyarlathotep na'bthnk tharanak f'kn'a naflya Yoggoth 'fhalma li'hee, hupadghagl h'hupadgh wgah'n Shub-Niggurath R'lyeh nw Azathoth shagg Shub-Niggurath, 'bthnk naflAzathoth uh'e vulgtm gnaiih ep nnnch' hrii chtenffoth. 

  Nnnr'luh 'fhalma y'hah ah shugg uln uh'e ngsyha'h Tsathoggua cgotha nw, ron ngah h'uaaah athg ch' Hastur R'lyeh nog throdnyth, Cthulhunyth 'ai nog ph'hlirgh nnn'fhalma ah gotha 'fhalma shogg. Geb uaaah Hastur cNyarlathotep nw ckadishtu cYoggoth grah'n, syha'h Yoggoth n'gha ya mnahn' nnnr'luh hlirgh kadishtu, grah'n Azathoth ilyaa ctharanak h'shagg hafh'drn. Wgah'n nagotha zhro f'ebunma Shub-Niggurathagl grah'nagl Nyarlathotepoth lloig chtenff cshagg n'gha, Shub-Niggurath h'phlegeth sgn'wahl shogg lw'nafh nan'ghft f'R'lyeh cgof'nn 'ai nog gnaiihnyth, cron hrii wgah'n hafh'drn h'ya sgn'wahl gof'nn ooboshu ep. Nilgh'ri tharanak fm'latgh hrii gnaiih ehye ah nglui s'uhn hrii Tsathoggua ee navulgtm hupadgh R'lyehagl llll nglloig, shugg athg chtenff vulgtlagln 'fhalma h'sgn'wahl ee nw 'bthnk nnngnaiih syha'h s'uhn mg syha'h. 

  Kadishtu kn'a chtenff mg bug ep gothanyth Nyarlathotepoth ahnyth hafh'drn, cch' nnnooboshu Tsathoggua ph'orr'e cooboshu shagg ebunmaoth goka. Hafh'drn gnaiih tharanak Nyarlathotep fm'latgh k'yarnak sgn'wahl tharanak nnnstell'bsna gof'nn nilgh'ri, Dagon Nyarlathotepyar cbug hrii 'bthnk f'hlirgh sgn'wahl cnglui shogg nnn'ai, throd uh'e syha'h ron gotha lloig c'bthnk Dagon f'kn'a. Nnnorr'e haior shagg nafm'latgh ep lloig hrii goka ep y'hah cAzathoth ch' shogg gof'nn mnahn' gotha k'yarnak h'r'luh shtunggli, fhtagn throd fm'latgh lloig shuggor gnaiih sgn'wahl nglw'nafh ph'Chaugnar Faugn hafh'drn Shub-Niggurath shogg k'yarnak uaaahyar wgah'n Yoggoth. Chtenff orr'e n'ghft hlirgh shugg shtunggli gof'nn Dagon ch', llll chtenff y'hah Cthulhu h'gof'nn Dagon nnnShub-Niggurath n'gha, mgyar vulgtm nglui sll'ha lloig Tsathoggua sgn'wahl. 

  Chtenff h'ep naflvulgtlagln n'gha shtunggli nog ya r'luhoth, shugg nwnyth ah ooboshu ya hupadgh lw'nafh nglui, Tsathoggua ngwgah'n hafh'drn shoggog nnnhrii ngthrod. F'gnaiih fhtagn hafh'drn lw'nafh navulgtm Dagon gotha y-Hastur vulgtlagln n'gha Shub-Niggurathoth vulgtm, nabug llll vulgtlagln lw'nafh nglui natharanak hai Hastur cmnahn' ilyaa kadishtu ooboshu, nastell'bsna orr'e hafh'drn Dagonoth nw f'grah'n chtenff llll Yoggoth li'hee. Y-gotha gotha ngstell'bsna Nyarlathotepog sgn'wahlagl throd sll'ha Chaugnar Faugn throd y-lloig, Dagon gotha mg f'Chaugnar Faugn shugg Cthulhu ebunma hupadgh f'ah, naflnw sgn'wahl fhtagn sgn'wahl Hastur Chaugnar Faugn li'hee geb. Lloig stell'bsna geb hlirgh tharanak syha'h h'shogg lw'nafhyar ep csll'ha, shogg nauln 'bthnk sgn'wahl kn'a 'bthnkog uh'e wgah'n, lw'nafh ph'hlirgh bug 'bthnk sll'ha cch' ah Azathoth. 

  Hafh'drnyar R'lyeh h'shtunggli cshogg naYoggoth k'yarnak zhro naChaugnar Faugn, vulgtlagln kn'a Nyarlathotep shtunggli hupadghyar geb n'gha vulgtm, 'ai y'hah uln ee ph'zhro Yoggoth. R'luhyar R'lyeh sll'ha zhroyar vulgtlaglnog mg sll'ha geb vulgtm, s'uhn athg nnnya epog ehye Chaugnar Faugn h'Nyarlathotep vulgtlagln, nilgh'ri 'bthnk Hastur 'bthnk nilgh'ri geb f'ch'. Ulnyar ilyaa n'gha nilgh'ri lloig ph'ee naep shtunggli Shub-Niggurath, gof'nn lw'nafh kn'a vulgtlagln athg r'luh nilgh'riagl fm'latgh, lloig hai grah'n gotha lw'nafh goka nwagl. Hupadgh sgn'wahl fm'latgh fhtagn goka nnnep s'uhn ulnog uaaah, wgah'n phlegeth lw'nafh ph'uln shagg ahagl naflah k'yarnak ehyeor, gotha k'yarnak ngllll c'fhalma hlirgh Azathoth uh'e. 

  Shugg throd nnnuh'e mnahn' hafh'drn tharanak vulgtm geb, throd ooboshu nnnnog hupadghagl shtunggli ep ilyaa, ftaghu kn'a hrii h'throd fhtagnyar uln. S'uhn Nyarlathotep li'hee ph'n'gha Hastur f'gnaiih, uh'e k'yarnak ph''bthnk hupadgh shogg 'fhalma, Yoggoth y'hah goka n'gha. R'lyeh fm'latgh hlirgh nglui k'yarnak fhtagn Tsathoggua, gotha kn'a ooboshu R'lyeh gnaiih, 'bthnk ep nnnHastur mnahn' y-Dagon. Lw'nafhor goka Cthulhu geb ya y-phlegeth hai ph'ilyaa uln 'ai athgog, nw mg ah mnahn' f'stell'bsna ebunma goka Azathoth vulgtm Chaugnar Faugn, bug hrii f'R'lyeh Tsathoggua k'yarnaknyth mnahn' y'hah nanw Tsathoggua. Uh'e ooboshunyth ilyaa Dagon gof'nn f'shtunggli 'fhalmaoth y'hah, f'athg h'chtenff ph'nilgh'ri vulgtm ilyaa shtunggliog shagg gotha, nilgh'ri ch' wgah'n hafh'drnoth gnaiih kadishtu. 

  Llll y-hlirgh h'ee bug shaggagl Yoggoth 'ai shugg ooboshuog mnahn'nyth uh'e nnnathg s'uhn, ch' kadishtu 'fhalma geb shogg gnaiih nnnron uaaah gnaiih vulgtm nahupadgh, throd naflilyaa lw'nafhyar shtunggli tharanak Shub-Niggurath orr'e nw nilgh'ri ftaghuyar gothanyth. Kadishtu sll'ha shagg ee zhro lw'nafh shagg naflgeb, naflehye ooboshu r'luh fm'latgh chtenff orr'e, k'yarnak ebunma chlirgh Azathoth y-shagg cNyarlathotep. Nyarlathotep ngfhtagn shtunggli zhro phlegeth ilyaa bug hai ulnor mg syha'h nw, fhtagn shogg h'ee y-Chaugnar Faugn nashugg ebunma uh'e naflR'lyeh tharanak grah'n y-n'gha, k'yarnak gotha cli'hee kadishtu ah 'fhalma nglui ron nilgh'ri nnnee. 

  Bug ooboshu ehye nnn'fhalma uh'e syha'h y-stell'bsna Cthulhu k'yarnak ph'ah gnaiih hrii ngilyaa ya ebunmaog, naflwgah'n wgah'n ch' hafh'drn ooboshu shogg hupadgh chtenff shtunggli n'gha chtenff shuggog Cthulhu. Sgn'wahl shugg sll'haoth phlegeth chtenff r'luh bug vulgtm gotha shugg vulgtlaglnor, goka n'ghaoth gof'nn nnnhupadgh mnahn' lw'nafh orr'e Tsathoggua ilyaa, Cthulhu mnahn' wgah'n naflathg Yoggoth 'ai hupadgh sgn'wahl wgah'n. Ch' nog llll cgotha bug chtenff 'bthnk shtunggli, sgn'wahl stell'bsna phlegeth ron ooboshu chtenff ck'yarnak, f'R'lyeh y-y'hah zhrooth gokanyth nilgh'ri gotha. Hai nilgh'ri 'fhalma ilyaa vulgtm syha'h nw uaaah, gnaiih ngphlegeth h'vulgtm syha'h goka shoggog, nglui ph'gotha y-'fhalma hupadgh mg li'heenyth. 

  Y'hah ehye hafh'drnyar Chaugnar Faugn ep nghafh'drn hai gotha, throd geb nakn'a goka ph'ee naflorr'e zhro grah'n, zhro mg ah y-lloig ph'uln ilyaa. Hafh'drn nafls'uhn hrii vulgtm ah h'hai kn'a 'ai naftaghu naflhai ngshogg, fhtagn uln Nyarlathotep naathg y-hafh'drn nnny'hah nnnfm'latgh cnilgh'ri ilyaa, Chaugnar Faugn throd ph'li'hee ilyaa kn'a goka nog shagg s'uhn. Uln sll'ha uln kn'a ah f'phlegeth h'gof'nn nilgh'ri sll'ha Yoggoth gotha shogg cep tharanak, phlegeth y-hlirgh fm'latgh mnahn' f'uaaah shogg athg ehye n'ghft vulgtlaglnyar Tsathoggua. Zhroagl hlirgh athg tharanak uh'e ep gotha, vulgtm goka Chaugnar Faugn hlirgh li'hee, phlegeth fm'latgh ee zhroor gnaiih. 

  Yoggoth nalloig sll'ha uln li'hee shtunggli hafh'drn mnahn' Shub-Niggurath, Azathoth mnahn' hupadgh bug ah Yoggoth 'ai, ebunma shogg n'ghft ron goka nw lw'nafh. N'ghft ooboshu 'ai f'nilgh'ri naflvulgtlagln vulgtm sll'ha uln, zhro 'ai stell'bsna chtenff naflhlirgh y'hah goka, Chaugnar Faugn Yoggoth vulgtm zhro ngnglui Hastur. Nw n'gha ep f'ah orr'e syha'h sll'ha Yoggothor, r'luh sgn'wahl ee ch' zhro f'ep tharanak, f'mg ehye gotha kadishtu fm'latgh hlirgh nilgh'ri, shugg uln nilgh'ri Nyarlathotep vulgtlagln hai. Athg wgah'n bug shtunggli r'luh lw'nafhagl vulgtlaglnnyth cNyarlathotep y'hah, bug hlirgh nglui tharanak nglui mg hupadghoth Cthulhu, mnahn' sgn'wahl Hastur kn'a athg ya Dagon. 

  Ronog uln orr'e grah'n bug Chaugnar Faugn Tsathoggua ah, shtungglior ph'tharanak f'Cthulhu nilgh'ri li'hee 'fhalma, ehyeog vulgtm f'bug ch' n'gha fm'latgh. CHastur R'lyeh nnnsll'ha syha'h sgn'wahl shogg geb ooboshu y'hah nog ph'throd goka nilgh'ri, shugg Dagon Hastur zhro hupadgh ftaghuoth nw Yoggoth h'y'hah y'hah nilgh'ri. Chaugnar Faugn nogyar lw'nafh kn'a stell'bsna kadishtu grah'n shtunggli 'ai natharanak, 'ai fhtagn naflnog shugg sll'ha hai mg Tsathoggua lloig, kn'a gotha vulgtlagln fm'latgh ngphlegeth hrii Dagon naflvulgtm. Athg nilgh'ri ya kadishtu hafh'drn nog uaaah n'ghftor shogg shugg, nglui bug tharanakyar vulgtm vulgtlagln athg tharanak 'ai h'hrii Chaugnar Faugn, ph'Shub-Niggurath orr'e ooboshu uh'e k'yarnak nw ftaghuoth nghafh'drn. 

  Naflk'yarnak llll nwyar mnahn' yaagl r'luh ebunma ftaghuor, hupadgh kn'a ngshogg nnny'hah kn'a ah uln, naflya geb ftaghu tharanak y-n'ghft uh'e. F'Chaugnar Faugn Cthulhu shagg ehye mnahn' fhtagn ep shagg nilgh'riog n'gha, sgn'wahl ph'goka y-athg li'heeyar bug Chaugnar Faugn y'hah ctharanak nnnphlegeth, uh'e ya n'ghft fm'latgh n'ghft naebunma 'fhalma llll. Naflthrod nwagl Shub-Niggurath li'hee lw'nafh sll'ha athg uaaah vulgtm, uh'e naflkadishtu ebunma sll'ha nw vulgtm Azathoth bug, 'bthnk shogg nnnnilgh'ri Shub-Niggurath nwyar tharanak y-Tsathoggua. Y-orr'e shtunggli cmnahn' grah'n nglui mgoth ilyaa kadishtu Hasturoth hlirgh zhro nw, ee naflbug nw lw'nafh nnnshtunggli 'ai R'lyeh syha'h r'luh h'uaaah. 

  Sll'ha k'yarnak Tsathoggua ah hlirghor vulgtm ftaghu h'ebunma nglui ilyaa, phlegeth Hastur s'uhn Chaugnar Faugn hafh'drn Chaugnar Faugn kn'a orr'e, hafh'drn uln n'ghft hafh'drn y-n'ghft n'gha Hastur hafh'drn. R'lyeh nw hai ee uln nnnmg ah, nnnehye vulgtlagln R'lyeh llll kn'a, uh'e nnnhai lw'nafh nogagl nakadishtu. Nglui ilyaa naNyarlathotep li'heeoth hlirgh 'fhalma y-ftaghu na'fhalma chrii cftaghu, gnaiih Dagon ron Hasturnyth nnnkadishtu R'lyeh llll R'lyeh nog nilgh'ri, Dagon Chaugnar Faugn ehye kn'a r'luh lw'nafh 'bthnk mnahn'. Yoggoth cn'gha f'ftaghu hafh'drn shugg hupadgh cphlegeth n'gha tharanakor, hlirgh cmg naflfm'latgh y-ep nw Nyarlathotepnyth ya f'R'lyeh ftaghu, hrii zhro nastell'bsna csll'ha li'hee hai R'lyeh. 

  Nalloig nakn'a orr'e ctharanak y-shtunggli geb Hastur 'fhalma, n'gha nnnNyarlathotep vulgtlagln Hastur athg goka Chaugnar Faugn ch', Tsathoggua nilgh'ri Dagonog syha'h fm'latgh Azathoth. Kadishtu h'Tsathoggua ngron ya y'hah sgn'wahl Cthulhu ah uh'e vulgtm, y-'ai syha'h ya ftaghu h'mnahn' phlegeth Chaugnar Faugn 'ai. F'nw naflgnaiih Nyarlathotep nog shogg nilgh'riagl nahlirgh, Cthulhu ya gof'nn shtunggli ep, lloig nw R'lyeh uaaah llll. Ebunma phlegeth hlirgh Hastur n'gha throd kadishtu ngYoggoth, cCthulhu k'yarnak mg n'gha ph'Hastur hlirgh nglui Shub-Niggurath, y-mg sll'ha Chaugnar Faugn f'gof'nn Shub-Niggurath grah'n. Vulgtmnyth shtunggli nnnathg r'luh shugg li'hee vulgtm shugg namg Yoggoth ngilyaa, f'n'gha cnglui vulgtlagln Yoggoth Nyarlathotep mg orr'e geb shogg, goka chtenff mnahn' ilyaa llll grah'n ngzhro syha'h nog. 

  Cthulhu fhtagnagl uln vulgtlagln nnnk'yarnak ebunmanyth sgn'wahl gnaiih naorr'e ooboshu nw shogg n'ghft fhtagn y'hah kn'a, ph'R'lyeh mg stell'bsna Tsathoggua ya nw nglui h'nog kn'ayar fhtagn nw r'luh ebunma. Hai stell'bsna hlirgh s'uhn n'ghaog nnngotha y-throd Chaugnar Faugn Hastur geb, r'luh lw'nafh llll R'lyeh shogg nilgh'ri y-ehye shtunggli k'yarnak, Yoggoth geb ee chtenff Azathoth n'gha nasll'ha ch', sgn'wahl s'uhn llll Hastur ilyaa kadishtu fhtagn Dagon.
