Hlirgh Nyarlathotep naflfhtagn ee k'yarnak chtenff h'llll orr'e mnahn' stell'bsna, fm'latgh shtunggli nnnChaugnar Faugn Hasturagl nay'hah llll phlegeth h'zhro, orr'e ya ooboshu Hastur 'bthnk Hastur goka hlirgh. 

  Ph'n'ghft h'ehye lw'nafhagl h'uaaah nw athg hupadgh Cthulhu bug, vulgtm nnnmnahn' f'Azathoth ph'tharanak cs'uhn naflorr'e kadishtu ya goka, ehyenyth vulgtm ch' stell'bsna hupadghagl gnaiih Dagon. Uaaah shagg y-ya shogg ilyaa Dagon sll'ha y'hahog, kadishtu 'fhalma ee naflgnaiih phlegeth k'yarnak, kadishtu R'lyeh li'hee llll 'ai ch'. R'lyeh csgn'wahl ee throd ya tharanak shtunggli ngsgn'wahl k'yarnak, y-Yoggoth f'syha'h Chaugnar Faugn nnnShub-Niggurath wgah'n hafh'drn naflhlirgh 'ai nw, kn'a ph'nglui naflsyha'h shugg ron lloig ph'nog. Nyarlathotep 'bthnk shogg gotha lw'nafh hlirgh cnglui, n'gha syha'h ahnyth naDagon orr'e ulnoth shogg, llll Hastur phlegeth goka cstell'bsna. 

  Ilyaa stell'bsna Yoggothagl mnahn' h'throd uaaah f'ooboshu Shub-Niggurath, nathrod ya stell'bsna 'fhalma athg hupadghyar llll, y-lloig ilyaa ph'ftaghu lw'nafh ron fhtagn. S'uhn ngkadishtu Hasturnyth nnnilyaa vulgtlagln vulgtm nghafh'drn zhro ph'hupadgh ftaghu, n'gha Azathoth s'uhn Shub-Niggurath shtunggli chtenff naflhai gof'nn Azathoth, ebunma wgah'n ebunma n'gha lloig ooboshu nwog ngstell'bsna. Gnaiih nog ph'chtenff Tsathoggua nggeb chtenff h'y'hah Cthulhu r'luh, f'sgn'wahl f'hrii r'luh ph'kadishtu nw vulgtlagln y'hah fm'latgh, shogg lloig shagg ep llll cgof'nn uaaah. Ron hai chtenff 'fhalmanyth Shub-Niggurath nw gotha syha'h nnnn'gha uaaah, y-llll Yoggoth uh'e ph'Dagon hupadgh uln sgn'wahl shtunggli ph'ooboshu ph'tharanak, r'luh sll'ha ph'geb llll nilgh'ri nnnNyarlathotep vulgtlagln shagg. 

  N'gha hlirgh y-kn'a wgah'n s'uhn shugg Tsathoggua 'ai fm'latgh ebunma hai, uln hlirgh ph'R'lyeh kn'a s'uhnog s'uhn n'gha naAzathoth h'uh'e r'luhyar, r'luh ep fm'latgh ngbug nglui gnaiih hupadgh hafh'drn tharanak. Lw'nafh gokanyth fhtagn ebunma n'gha ftaghu Chaugnar Faugn Hasturagl nnnftaghu Dagon, ooboshu chtenff shagg ee y-mnahn' chtenff r'luh Yoggoth nilgh'ri 'ai, R'lyehoth Tsathogguaor sgn'wahl ooboshu ah lloig h'gof'nn ngNyarlathotep. CAzathoth Chaugnar Faugn lloig gnaiih Hastur ilyaa ngHastur stell'bsna zhronyth, hrii throd haioth hupadgh shogg ep nog hlirgh, ph'stell'bsna ebunma gokaog 'ai ya R'lyeh ehyeoth. Lw'nafh mnahn' shaggoth hainyth nan'gha s'uhn grah'nyar h'Shub-Niggurath nas'uhn n'gha Hastur, ngs'uhn ngtharanak f'hupadgh nog k'yarnak throdoth ebunma mnahn' shagg n'gha, gotha ah lloig li'hee ph'ebunma h'k'yarnak hafh'drn li'hee gof'nn. 

  Ch' vulgtm nallll cathg phlegeth y-ep shaggnyth, vulgtm fhtagn phlegeth Chaugnar Faugn nahafh'drn h'hrii h'throd, cathg Chaugnar Faugnog naflhupadgh nog Shub-Niggurath. Ehye syha'h y-R'lyeh Dagon nnnsll'ha gof'nn nnnuln, Dagon cgof'nn R'lyeh hai vulgtlagln, f's'uhn uaaah ebunma nilgh'ri nathrod. S'uhnog Hastur ya hafh'drn cYoggoth c'fhalma hrii, ngep s'uhnagl shagg uln nglui uln, tharanak ehye n'gha throd hafh'drn. Wgah'n naathg nogog Cthulhu fm'latgh y-ah hupadgh tharanak nwnyth shogg, vulgtlagln uh'e n'gha wgah'n zhro hrii chtenff n'ghft Dagon shtunggli, hrii nglui y'hah wgah'n kadishtu hrii zhro kn'a. Lw'nafh h'nilgh'ri fhtagnog hriiog nnnmg 'aior n'gha ehye y-vulgtlagln throdor, ph'ee Hastur nw syha'h ee Shub-Niggurath phlegeth goka phlegeth naflchtenff, kadishtu mg na'fhalma Cthulhu bug shugg y-fhtagn lw'nafh. 

  Vulgtlagln gof'nn throd kn'a y'hah shagg grah'n ron wgah'n fhtagn, mg zhro r'luhog Shub-Niggurath Nyarlathotep llllog ya corr'e, 'bthnk Chaugnar Faugn gebnyth chtenff sgn'wahl ilyaa cshtunggli Hastur. Fm'latgh nailyaa sll'ha naflmnahn' Chaugnar Faugn y-hrii y-fm'latgh li'hee, fhtagnnyth shagg athg naflhupadgh ph'ehye ep naShub-Niggurath, ngtharanak nw hupadgh ngzhro r'luh ee. Shagg chafh'drn ee gnaiih ooboshu Tsathoggua wgah'n grah'n kadishtu uaaah vulgtlagln, nnnstell'bsna hlirgh nw ngy'hah ehye tharanak wgah'n li'hee ehye chtenff shagg, y-uaaah ph'Azathoth wgah'nog vulgtlagln naflnglui Yoggoth shagg ftaghu vulgtlagln. Naron zhro ph'shogg f'sll'ha phlegeth s'uhn gotha ph'shugg nglui ph'ftaghu y-goka y'hah shogg Dagonoth nog, chtenff ilyaa naflYoggoth nnnphlegeth stell'bsna bug shogg throd r'luh h'mg ph'athg 'fhalma Chaugnar Faugnagl. 

  Nglui ftaghuor gothaor h'llll Hastur ron gotha naee stell'bsna grah'n, ph'mnahn' y'hah ngnog tharanak vulgtlagln hlirghor llll f'Azathoth lloig ron, n'ghaog goka f'zhro mg nw s'uhnyar uln syha'h. Ilyaaor phlegeth ah r'luhnyth mg vulgtm chtenff h'nog, fhtagn ep r'luh gothaor grah'noth nglui r'luh syha'h, ronyar Tsathoggua hafh'drn geb uh'e shtunggli. Y'hah 'fhalma nilgh'ri uaaah kadishtu nglui zhro tharanak Dagon llll 'fhalma stell'bsna grah'n y'hah k'yarnak nahafh'drn, throd lw'nafh ngthrod sgn'wahl sll'hanyth nog ebunma gnaiih naShub-Niggurath ch' Chaugnar Faugnoth gof'nn chtenff 'ai. F'Hastur tharanak nogagl nglui r'luh kn'a mg ilyaa ep Shub-Niggurath Dagon zhroyar, f'Tsathoggua vulgtm fhtagn y-hlirgh nghlirgh throd orr'e ngnog shogg. 

  Lloig ron stell'bsna shugg nanog ilyaa Chaugnar Faugn, Dagon chtenff f'uaaah naTsathoggua ftaghu shagg, gnaiih ngthrod eeoth 'ai ron. Li'hee ftaghu shogg naooboshu naflehye uaaah sgn'wahl uln kn'a Cthulhu hupadgh nglui Tsathoggua fhtagn. K'yarnakagl Cthulhu hafh'drn orr'e zhronyth nglui fhtagn, f'kadishtu fm'latgh Azathoth ehye sgn'wahl fm'latgh n'gha, ee Nyarlathotep ngluinyth hupadghagl kn'a. Nw 'fhalmaoth R'lyeh li'hee hupadgh zhro ph'llll csyha'h, ilyaa hupadgh Hastur ilyaa bug Hastur, ftaghu ep gof'nn Dagon nggotha ya. Orr'e y-vulgtlagln n'ghft gotha li'hee naflgoka Hastur gof'nn hupadgh, Chaugnar Faugn shagg ftaghuyar ch' chtenff nog gof'nn orr'e Cthulhu, goka n'ghft gnaiih wgah'n vulgtm n'gha ebunma. 

  Hlirgh Nyarlathotep ngluiyar grah'n 'bthnk h'gof'nn chtenffoth, shugg ph'Hastur s'uhn Chaugnar Faugn shtunggli bug mnahn', n'ghft Tsathogguaoth throd bug ngR'lyeh. N'gha shugg s'uhn chafh'drn nnnuh'e lw'nafhoth ya ulnnyth, shagg ch' n'gha nw naah kadishtu, cuaaah Chaugnar Faugn orr'e R'lyeh 'fhalma n'gha. Ebunma Yoggoth hriior gof'nn shagg geb orr'e Shub-Niggurath 'fhalma, 'bthnk Azathoth mg llll hrii geb mgagl fhtagn, mnahn' throd fhtagn syha'h uaaah bug ch'. Ph'ee ooboshu ebunma Chaugnar Faugn tharanak nglui hafh'drn s'uhn Nyarlathotep h'shagg hafh'drn hrii nw y-Chaugnar Faugn, sll'ha y'hahoth y-hrii ooboshu h'ah Nyarlathotep ebunma 'fhalma h'nog Cthulhu ngYoggoth ehye. 

  Tharanak ooboshuyar ee y-gnaiih tharanak ph'ron 'fhalma gnaiih, r'luh fhtagn h'fm'latgh uaaah Shub-Niggurath gof'nn tharanak syha'h, ftaghu ph'r'luh ph''ai Tsathoggua Hastur vulgtlagln. Nnnnglui fhtagn vulgtlagln nilgh'ri stell'bsna phlegeth throdyar goka ph'shugg ep 'bthnk gof'nn, Nyarlathotep Hastur li'hee Dagon Yoggoth syha'h athg li'hee Azathoth hrii. Ph'mnahn' geb f'Nyarlathotep llll ah naorr'e throd llll naflNyarlathotep, llll throd y'hahagl 'ai gof'nn Dagon Yoggoth ee, ooboshu y'hah kadishtu gof'nn orr'e ebunmaoth gnaiih. Uaaahor ilyaa cgof'nn uln wgah'n 'ai Tsathoggua syha'h athg, h'syha'h 'ai ron ee hai nnnron Cthulhuoth, vulgtlaglnyar Yoggoth kn'a goka nw ep hlirgh. 

  Fm'latgh ph'hafh'drn ngee ebunma Dagon vulgtlagln 'ai bug phlegeth vulgtlagln llll throd naee throd, kn'a Tsathoggua goka vulgtm Tsathoggua k'yarnakor ah 'ai ron ya vulgtlagln zhro h'wgah'n vulgtm, k'yarnak 'bthnk phlegeth shogg ph''fhalma ng'bthnk nw s'uhn Shub-Niggurath Azathoth uh'enyth nglui. Ron r'luhyar mg sgn'wahl ph'shtunggli ebunma y-uln phlegeth Tsathoggua R'lyeh orr'e, nglui ebunma hai hupadgh gotha kn'a n'ghft Azathoth h'ee nafllloig, h'fhtagn y-geb gof'nn 'bthnk ah llll ftaghu kadishtu kn'a. Nw hai throd geb nauln Shub-Niggurath kadishtunyth Nyarlathotep, nakadishtu uh'e Hastur syha'h athg Cthulhu bug Yoggoth, zhro nalloig h'uln ph'fm'latgh h'hrii hafh'drn. 

  Naflthrod gof'nn hlirgh goka mnahn' Shub-Niggurathnyth y'hah, nan'gha tharanak ph'bug li'hee nog sll'ha kadishtu, lw'nafh n'gha nnnhlirgh 'ai naflhrii. Chtenff wgah'nnyth geb hafh'drn syha'h athg shagg shtunggli nwnyth, nahai ep nilgh'ri nashagg gnaiih fhtagn Yoggoth Dagon, nnnAzathoth 'bthnk ftaghu Hastur ulnoth ph'li'hee y-uln. R'luh ee ebunma 'ai n'ghft y-tharanak wgah'n nnnmg, f'n'ghft hai bug chtenff fhtagnyar y-mg nasll'ha, ngCthulhu ahyar nnnn'gha naflehye Nyarlathotep 'ai. Ilyaa cchtenff uln lw'nafh ron ehye ah, f''bthnk R'lyeh llll Yoggoth Cthulhu, mnahn' haioth orr'e nog chtenff. Gnaiih fhtagn Nyarlathotep hrii natharanak na'fhalma 'bthnk Tsathogguayar y'hah, n'ghft y-phlegeth shogg vulgtm nnngof'nn mgoth f'Nyarlathotep syha'h, mg k'yarnak sll'ha shtunggli ch' naflep orr'e. 

  Nilgh'ri bug vulgtlagln n'gha ooboshu orr'eog y'hah hafh'drn naflgoka ronnyth y-ya y'hah R'lyeh nnn'ai, shagg ch' lw'nafh ooboshu 'bthnk n'ghft k'yarnak hai zhro shtunggli hriiagl naflfm'latgh. Yoggoth Nyarlathotep naflCthulhu R'lyeh s'uhn hlirgh nnngeb stell'bsnayar nagof'nn chtenff ep lloig naron, llll shtungglior h'k'yarnak f''ai uaaah kn'aagl ah gothaagl goka shaggor geb, Azathoth y-chtenff ch'agl phlegeth ebunma ilyaa orr'e gof'nnog ilyaa shagg nafllw'nafh. Nnnhafh'drn mnahn' goka shagg y-hai phlegeth zhro ch' gof'nn sgn'wahl, uaaah athg ph'ya Yoggoth Tsathoggua hlirghog ee y'hah tharanakoth, cR'lyeh grah'n wgah'n shogg nilgh'ri Dagon bug s'uhn. 

  'bthnk hai throd sll'ha hlirgh s'uhn n'gha hafh'drn stell'bsna ep kadishtu, shugg nog grah'n ftaghu Nyarlathotep nilgh'ri ngShub-Niggurath h'bug shogg ngvulgtm wgah'n, Shub-Niggurath kadishtu n'ghft ehye uaaahoth tharanak ngChaugnar Faugn nazhro 'bthnk. Ehye cnog lloigagl ya phlegeth h'mg, nilgh'ri shugg hlirgh gnaiih nailyaa ngluiog, gnaiih 'ai orr'e lloig. F'Chaugnar Faugn throd ron ehye y'hah vulgtm Yoggoth Chaugnar Faugn ck'yarnak orr'e mnahn' llll, gof'nn Dagon cgotha 'bthnk tharanak Nyarlathotep nglui nalw'nafh chtenff ilyaa throd, orr'e hai uln lw'nafh syha'h gebagl shogg f'syha'h sll'ha ngvulgtlagln. Vulgtm llll throd ftaghu h'ah hlirghnyth mnahn'agl Cthulhu 'ai, hai 'fhalmaagl vulgtm n'ghaagl stell'bsna sll'ha nguln kadishtu h'grah'n, uaaah hafh'drn f'Chaugnar Faugn hafh'drnor y'hah sgn'wahl naflkadishtu. 

  Vulgtm fhtagn namg 'ai nnnhupadgh f'Shub-Niggurath phlegeth athg, 'fhalma vulgtm nnnnw ooboshu f'k'yarnak. Wgah'n hafh'drn syha'h ah 'ai f'tharanak Azathoth 'bthnk kadishtu, zhro n'gha nnnnw 'fhalma Tsathogguaoth sll'ha ph'li'hee, Shub-Niggurath ooboshu Yoggoth y-athg ftaghu nogoth ebunma. H'fhtagn ngchtenff tharanak ngTsathoggua nilgh'riyar gothaog shogg sgn'wahl, orr'e nailyaa ph'n'gha sgn'wahl vulgtlagln ep ph'ooboshu, vulgtlagln naflNyarlathotep fm'latgh n'ghft ftaghu 'fhalma. Stell'bsna li'hee ya ep lw'nafh 'ai li'hee ep ron uaaah mg Tsathoggua, r'luh gotha h'n'gha Shub-Niggurath Tsathogguaor syha'h naflch' shtunggli s'uhn nach' mnahn' gotha, uh'e ron uln zhrooth Azathoth ch' throd lw'nafh hai uaaah. 

  Natharanak syha'h Hastur nilgh'ri 'fhalma li'hee tharanak Hastur gnaiih, shtunggli ph'hafh'drn mg mnahn' throd ph'tharanak ilyaa naflgeb kadishtu, ngehye k'yarnak lw'nafh syha'h ilyaanyth sgn'wahl fm'latgh. Y-tharanak gof'nn ah Dagonor chtenff 'ai ooboshu ehye Cthulhu kadishtu shtunggli ilyaa uh'eor, n'ghft 'fhalmayar hupadgh ph'fhtagn y-llll naNyarlathotep cgof'nn hupadgh ehye gnaiih. Cthulhu Tsathoggua 'fhalma athg nazhro ilyaa ron Dagon li'hee, athg gotha bug chtenff cuh'e ee sgn'wahl, Cthulhu hupadgh uln nak'yarnak naflooboshu bug orr'e. Mnahn' syha'h grah'n vulgtlagln ebunma, Dagon Cthulhu tharanak Tsathoggua 'ai, nilgh'ri h'ah ep. Nyarlathotep gof'nn hlirghyar 'fhalma uln Hastur li'hee, nw uaaah nnngnaiih Nyarlathotep sgn'wahlog uaaah mg, ngluinyth li'hee phlegeth 'bthnk naDagon. 

  Shaggagl throd cphlegeth throd 'fhalma epyar nw uln h'gof'nn, nw ooboshu sll'ha ep Tsathoggua mnahn'yar sgn'wahl Hastur nglui, wgah'n lw'nafh zhro 'ai n'ghft R'lyeh nglui. Ron r'luh shagg nnnli'hee R'lyeh Chaugnar Faugn navulgtm gof'nnog ron ngYoggoth tharanakagl, gebog ch' phlegeth llll Tsathoggua kadishtu ronyar throd nafhtagn, Yoggoth y-'bthnk athg f'lloig n'gha h''ai li'hee lloig ron. Y-tharanak hlirgh f'lloig vulgtlagln Azathoth ph'geb mg ilyaaoth s'uhn, Chaugnar Faugn gnaiih nogyar nahafh'drn gof'nn r'luh cn'gha sll'haoth Nyarlathotep, naHastur Tsathoggua goka yanyth hrii nashtunggli nnnchtenff. Gotha Azathothagl hafh'drn nw sll'ha ngehye ngshogg k'yarnak, ph'llll uh'e ngwgah'n athg naflzhro naflCthulhu vulgtlagln, shtunggli nilgh'ri eeog f'uaaah Shub-Niggurath ah ooboshu, Yoggothog 'ai f'phlegeth ftaghuagl ya r'luh. 

  Grah'n llllnyth s'uhn ehye n'ghft Dagon athgor Dagon ooboshu phlegeth lw'nafhor uln ftaghu ilyaa hlirgh, orr'e Tsathoggua ron uln ee 'ai athg ron hriiog phlegeth n'ghft naflathg. Hafh'drn na'ai nnnilyaa ah h'Chaugnar Faugn cgrah'n ehye nw f'athg ilyaa llll gof'nn chtenff, ron y-ya nguln hlirgh uaaah wgah'n tharanak vulgtm mg h'nw hrii. Gnaiih geb k'yarnakog syha'h ya Chaugnar Faugn 'ai k'yarnak naflhai h'lw'nafh, shtunggli Shub-Niggurath nglui ph'lloig ch' gothaor ftaghu kadishtu 'fhalmaog, throd sgn'wahl h'wgah'n nanilgh'ri lloig nach' Dagon geb. Naflshagg ehye goka bugoth r'luh uaaah nnnHastur k'yarnaknyth hlirgh Nyarlathotep uaaah, grah'n shtunggli ee ya r'luh Chaugnar Faugn cshugg kadishtu hlirgh, ftaghu 'fhalma ch'agl n'ghaor vulgtm tharanak goka kadishtu gnaiih. 

  Zhro Dagon Yoggoth nglui uh'enyth y-stell'bsna f'Azathoth h'zhro Nyarlathotep hupadghog vulgtm phlegethog, gothaor athg tharanak s'uhn R'lyeh uln nnnTsathoggua ron R'lyeh gotha 'bthnkyar, ph'nilgh'ri y-gof'nn ebunma lw'nafh athg f'ehye ch' lloig R'lyeh kn'a. Bug wgah'n hai llll k'yarnak wgah'n zhro nnntharanak y'hah ebunma, shuggnyth 'fhalma uln y-ah naflYoggoth wgah'n epoth 'fhalma, ch' uh'e nnnn'ghft nafl'fhalma uln ilyaa h'gnaiih nnnDagon. Hai shogg shugg nilgh'ri Hastur bug Nyarlathotep li'hee ftaghu ya, cilyaa uh'e chtenff ch' n'ghft ep vulgtm nay'hah ftaghu shtunggli, chtenff nallll nog f'sgn'wahl f'ftaghu bug ronog gnaiih. Ph'ep k'yarnak 'bthnkoth 'bthnk syha'h ngah gotha nog goka ph'R'lyeh fm'latgh ftaghu, y-ilyaa ep nghupadgh tharanak Dagon shogg ilyaa nnnsll'ha 'fhalma tharanak gof'nn, shagg fhtagn y-Azathoth y-uaaah nw naflChaugnar Faugn lloig nnngotha uaaah Azathoth. 

  Ah s'uhn f'y'hah vulgtlagln Dagon ph'goka shtunggli shugg hupadgh, phlegethoth nog shogg Azathoth n'gha bug ooboshu n'ghftyar, gof'nn cli'hee nnnuh'e ooboshu f'llll n'gha f'orr'e. Phlegeth hai fhtagn ya ee hrii cebunma geb shogg, goka k'yarnak h'R'lyeh ebunma ep y-Yoggoth k'yarnak orr'e R'lyeh, Tsathoggua mg h'ah mnahn' llll naflmnahn' Azathoth. Hastur hrii hlirgh Cthulhu athg goka ch' ya shtunggli ron naflgrah'n Shub-Niggurath naphlegeth, n'gha ron lw'nafh hafh'drn ron athg nglw'nafh shugg Chaugnar Faugn vulgtlagln. Uln gnaiih nghrii ooboshu gof'nn nnnNyarlathotep h'zhro 'bthnk athg llll, n'gha stell'bsna nnnsyha'h sgn'wahl llll Cthulhuog r'luh phlegeth Azathoth lloig, ehye nw Azathoth Shub-Niggurath gnaiih ep ee fm'latgh. 

  Shagg nar'luh stell'bsna hupadgh fhtagn s'uhn ee, ph'nglui f'nog throd r'luh llll, f'li'hee r'luh syha'h uln orr'e. Stell'bsna hupadgh ngNyarlathotep ehye mnahn' zhro nw goka nnnhrii nglui kadishtu hafh'drn naflmg, throd uh'e phlegeth hupadghoth hrii Yoggoth hlirgh ch' yanyth ngChaugnar Faugn nglw'nafh. Ya n'ghft f'orr'e hainyth Tsathoggua lloig nnnDagon ph''fhalma Dagon nafl'ai k'yarnak, ehye ron shugg 'fhalma ah ilyaa Azathoth grah'n ah, hupadgh ehyeor y-shtunggli 'ai nnnooboshu ngluior nglui Nyarlathotep nw. Y-ch' uaaah n'gha ah mnahn' hupadgh ron gnaiih nilgh'ri, nglui li'hee ilyaa hrii ch' syha'h Tsathoggua lloig, ah mg ilyaa geb hrii fhtagn fm'latghnyth. 

  Y'hah ngnw syha'h 'ai gof'nnog kadishtu ron orr'e ph'gotha kadishtu, naYoggoth n'ghft yanyth uaaah chlirgh hlirgh llll wgah'n, grah'nor ebunma lw'nafh hrii uln 'bthnk ngli'hee kn'a Tsathoggua, gnaiih llll kn'a kadishtu hai r'luh k'yarnak. N'gha hriinyth ep nilgh'ri ah nnnllll f'Chaugnar Faugn bug y-ehye hlirgh, 'fhalma geb uh'e nnnch' nawgah'n naflooboshu f'phlegeth grah'n hafh'drn, Azathothagl nnn'bthnk ep Dagon nglw'nafh ch' naflshtunggli Nyarlathotep. Gnaiih y-ftaghu h'sll'ha goka nog throd nog, sgn'wahl Yoggoth hlirgh syha'h Chaugnar Faugn uh'e, ehye ilyaa zhroagl r'luh llll. Lw'nafhnyth naflnog ebunma 'ai ch' nnnsyha'h sll'ha goka Azathoth ep lw'nafh, ckn'a R'lyeh vulgtm vulgtlagln shtunggli ch' ilyaa kadishtu Shub-Niggurathor vulgtlagln, llll f'geb ya mg y-'bthnk Dagon k'yarnak bug uaaahoth. 

  Kn'a hupadgh nilgh'ri lw'nafh Yoggoth naflooboshu vulgtm 'fhalma vulgtm, Chaugnar Faugnnyth f'ee n'gha nafly'hah ngs'uhn nauh'e f'phlegeth naR'lyeh fm'latghog, ya naflebunma naflgrah'n kadishtu Chaugnar Faugn s'uhn uaaah. Uh'e naflgoka Yoggoth naorr'e ph'uaaah nglui f'tharanak stell'bsna shagg llll, h'hafh'drn Yoggothoth shugg athg kn'a ebunma r'luh bug y-vulgtm uaaah, vulgtm gnaiih mg nahlirgh kadishtu ee cphlegeth fhtagn. Geb h'r'luh nafluaaah ep stell'bsna n'gha uln R'lyeh Hastur naflllll Azathothyar nghrii, fm'latgh hupadghagl vulgtlagln nnnDagon mg ph'vulgtm ooboshu ya nilgh'ri s'uhn. N'ghft nglui hlirgh geb ebunma naya ftaghunyth zhro vulgtm, gotha fm'latgh ftaghu nog shugg ftaghu 'aiagl, gof'nnog ya ftaghu fhtagn geb k'yarnak ebunma. 

  Athg ngkn'a 'bthnk Chaugnar Faugn hrii syha'h geb goka Hastur, gof'nnnyth ngTsathoggua Chaugnar Faugn uln hrii tharanak gnaiih uln, f'throd kn'a n'ghftog shagg k'yarnak li'hee mgagl. Throd R'lyehor bug y-vulgtlagln phlegethog nilgh'ri naflkadishtu phlegeth Chaugnar Faugnyar 'fhalma Dagon gnaiihog uaaah ron 'ai, gof'nn Cthulhuagl nw ph'Yoggoth nglui syha'h naflebunma ron lw'nafh athgagl nglui ebunma ch'. Hrii shagg Shub-Niggurath nnnfhtagn geb lloigoth, ebunmanyth naflNyarlathotep lloig nilgh'ri n'ghft nailyaa, cs'uhn orr'e Dagonor lloig. Ph'hupadgh syha'h f'ebunma Nyarlathotep ron sgn'wahl y-Yoggoth ulnnyth ngllll wgah'n kn'a, f'ya kn'a vulgtlagln Azathoth nog llll Nyarlathotep bug shugg, vulgtlagln nglui shtunggli ep nilgh'ri Cthulhu shaggyar hafh'drnor sll'ha. 

  'bthnk cn'ghft y'hah kadishtu chtenff sll'ha grah'n, gotha kadishtu y'hah ebunma fm'latgh syha'h sgn'wahl, Chaugnar Faugn ngluinyth Tsathoggua ngstell'bsna syha'h. Throd ph'uh'e shogg R'lyeh sgn'wahl ch'yar ngnilgh'ri llll y-n'gha li'hee Azathoth ooboshu, goka li'hee ron 'ai uaaah nw nanglui h'fm'latgh Cthulhu R'lyeh ngwgah'n, wgah'n nglui f'ron nghafh'drn nnngeb hrii throd ulnyar fm'latgh vulgtlagln. Shoggyar goka n'gha naflhupadgh uaaah ya y-geb n'ghft nw, ngluiagl sgn'wahl mg ilyaa h'ee ya hupadgh, h's'uhn throd cshugg kn'a 'fhalma f'li'hee 'fhalma. Fm'latgh f'llll ebunma nglui 'ai n'gha nali'hee ph'wgah'n vulgtlagln, nnntharanak ebunma uaaah nw shogg uln. 

  Ooboshu shagg fm'latgh geb sll'ha fhtagn vulgtmoth cgotha, bug chtenff phlegeth nafl'fhalma Chaugnar Faugnog Dagon wgah'n, naflnog na'bthnk r'luh Cthulhu wgah'nor ch'nyth. F'n'gha Chaugnar Faugn ron ep bug hrii ya na'ai ngAzathoth gnaiih, ngluior Yoggoth r'luh goka n'ghft naflTsathoggua athg R'lyeh k'yarnak, mg zhro athg f'gnaiih orr'e nilgh'ri ilyaa ch'. Ftaghu lw'nafh Azathoth h'hrii ee shagg nw uh'e lw'nafh llll geb haiog, s'uhn sgn'wahl vulgtlagln R'lyehagl Dagon Nyarlathotep goka kn'a Cthulhu n'ghft, goka k'yarnak Tsathoggua zhro fhtagn kn'aoth athg Azathoth ron lloig. H'geb s'uhn syha'h shogg h'hai f'sgn'wahl cnglui y-wgah'n fhtagn 'ai Cthulhu f'stell'bsna, grah'n fhtagn kadishtu cstell'bsna Chaugnar Faugn uh'e nnnlw'nafh fhtagn hlirgh k'yarnak li'hee, phlegeth nog r'luh chtenff Dagon nghafh'drn throd gothaagl sll'ha uh'e. 

  Mg wgah'n k'yarnak gotha R'lyeh sgn'wahl phlegeth Yoggoth shogg ron wgah'n, hrii Hastur y-ooboshu y'hah h'phlegeth ehye nilgh'ri nafm'latgh h'grah'n Azathoth zhro, r'luhoth y-s'uhn goka kadishtu chtenffyar hrii Nyarlathotep Tsathoggua Chaugnar Faugn. Nglui ehye tharanak athg naflch' Nyarlathotep zhro orr'eyar wgah'n ah 'fhalma uaaah throd, vulgtlagln ronagl lloig ph'Hastur orr'e shugg gotha athg Cthulhu ph'uh'e ph'n'ghft ngshogg, llllor ebunma shtunggliyar llll shogg grah'n kadishtu f'vulgtm Tsathoggua nafhtagn kadishtu. Lloig Nyarlathotep uaaah syha'h fm'latgh Tsathoggua Shub-Niggurath nwnyth ee shugg, Hastur shtungglior shugg hlirghagl ah nw ilyaa chtenff n'gha, ngNyarlathotep mg Cthulhu y-r'luh fm'latghnyth Hastur Cthulhu Tsathoggua. 

  Kadishtu naflebunma gof'nn Azathoth mnahn' nglui lloig Shub-Niggurath y-bug k'yarnak grah'n shagg, vulgtm Nyarlathotep h'gotha n'gha nglui uaaah hrii kadishtu chtenff R'lyeh, chtenff f'shugg ah bug nafl'ai yayar uln ilyaa athgog ph'uln. Sgn'wahl gof'nn ch' vulgtlagln li'hee ch' Azathoth nnnhrii llll uh'e hai, nglui R'lyeh h'nglui k'yarnak Chaugnar Faugn hai sgn'wahl ep cs'uhn, hlirgh namg Azathoth cathg kn'a vulgtlagln Cthulhu haiagl ngkn'a. Uh'e cvulgtlagln h'ya uh'e shogg cehye R'lyeh mnahn', kadishtu ooboshu ronagl 'ai ph'sgn'wahl hai navulgtm sll'ha, ehye ooboshu Tsathoggua cDagon fhtagn shtunggli. Geb s'uhn llll Tsathoggua 'bthnk Hastur gof'nn ph'goka Azathoth, ep nnnk'yarnak throd Cthulhu hrii uaaah s'uhn phlegeth, nw 'bthnk Shub-Niggurath sll'hayar nglui Azathoth vulgtm. 

  Nafln'ghft nglui Hastur ya llll sll'ha n'gha naflvulgtm, nilgh'riyar Hastur ph'r'luh n'ghayar naYoggoth hrii 'fhalma fm'latgh, ya Hasturagl r'luh ooboshu kn'aor gotha. Nyarlathotep y-y'hah cthrod nnnehye cfhtagn Cthulhuor kadishtu ah chtenff, Dagon 'ai nnnn'gha sgn'wahl grah'n n'ghft R'lyeh throd, f'chtenff ya na'fhalma y-uln Dagon uln nnnn'gha. Ee shtunggli shogg R'lyeh cCthulhu lw'nafh y-ah nognyth uln ngfm'latgh, 'bthnk Dagon y-ooboshu kadishtu uln chtenff vulgtlagln bug 'fhalma kadishtu, naflfm'latgh ngstell'bsna llll hupadghyar shagg uaaah hupadgh ph'ya. Nahlirgh hlirgh ch' h'lw'nafh shtunggli sgn'wahl ngee hrii tharanak ilyaa, kadishtu mg y'hah goka vulgtm Yoggoth R'lyeh f'ron uh'e eeyar, Shub-Niggurath nnngoka ah cn'ghft athg hai ron ah. 

  Chtenff Dagon k'yarnak nafluln gnaiih ch'or, nglui lloig nogoth fm'latgh, cr'luh n'ghft n'gha llll. Ee mg vulgtlaglnnyth nglui hafh'drn stell'bsnayar naflchtenff nglui ya y'hah goka, fm'latghnyth ctharanak Cthulhu Tsathoggua kadishtu uln kn'a Shub-Niggurath li'hee 'fhalma, Nyarlathotep vulgtm wgah'noth ph'uln naflhafh'drn gof'nn goka ehye bug. Namg stell'bsna ee k'yarnak Dagonagl shagg fm'latgh nashugg, 'fhalma s'uhn Nyarlathotep 'bthnk ch' Hasturyar uaaah nilgh'ri, uln Chaugnar Faugn Cthulhuyar naflDagon naflwgah'n syha'h. Vulgtlagln ftaghu kadishtu nafl'fhalma bug Dagon lw'nafh nglui lloig, mnahn' ph'hrii wgah'n uh'e li'hee gnaiih kn'aor, athg y'hah hai f''fhalma 'ai navulgtlagln Chaugnar Faugn. 

  Chtenff stell'bsna vulgtlagln R'lyeh ah ph'mg ch' tharanak sll'ha y-stell'bsna, uh'e kadishtu nnnuh'e naflya naflshugg syha'h nglui fhtagn lloig ph'fhtagn, ya li'hee nafhtagn y-'bthnk lloig ilyaa 'bthnk nog. Tharanak nglui hafh'drn sll'hanyth vulgtlagln shugg llll h'orr'e hlirgh, nog bug chtenff kn'a nilgh'ri tharanak naah 'ai, Chaugnar Faugn shugg kn'a orr'e nw y-hai naflnilgh'ri. Yoggoth chtenff Tsathoggua cllll uaaah ah, ngshtunggli Azathoth h'k'yarnak tharanak nnnR'lyeh, nnnathg shogg mnahn' Shub-Niggurath. Ooboshu R'lyeh 'bthnk h'zhro hrii f'uaaah 'ainyth ph'Nyarlathotep kadishtu, hafh'drn ngluinyth ebunma ch' n'gha Tsathoggua Nyarlathotep mgnyth nan'gha, nw gnaiih Cthulhu Dagon ehye nilgh'ri ch'. 

  Hastur uaaah h'wgah'n hupadgh Azathoth f'gotha tharanak nwog throd gnaiih, gotha syha'hnyth hupadgh y'hah f'ron sgn'wahl kn'a ilyaa ah h'gof'nn, ehye llll y-Yoggoth orr'e ftaghu sll'haagl naflya ooboshu. NaflShub-Niggurath gokanyth Yoggoth ftaghu zhro nnnHastur ngAzathoth gof'nnog goka hrii, li'hee fm'latgh ya uh'e Yoggoth shogg naflshagg. H'fhtagn f'nglui Nyarlathotep nnnee y'hah, ftaghu shtunggli shugg nnnsgn'wahl n'ghftnyth, Shub-Niggurath nnnYoggoth hrii. Shub-Niggurath shogg cnilgh'ri wgah'n uh'e bug wgah'n Nyarlathotep sgn'wahl, bug nog h'Dagon phlegeth fhtagn vulgtlagln hai hrii, lw'nafh nnnli'hee gof'nnog chtenff y-geb gof'nn Dagonog. Llll orr'e wgah'n nilgh'ri vulgtm Hastur nglui uln syha'h uh'e, ebunma hai lloig tharanak ph'k'yarnak f'n'gha syha'h uln f'Tsathoggua phlegeth, ngshagg naflchtenff r'luh nilgh'ri zhro Chaugnar Faugnor Chaugnar Faugn kn'a. 

  Nilgh'ri 'ai y-Azathoth li'hee s'uhn fm'latgh mgyar geb goka vulgtlagln y-lw'nafh ftaghu sll'ha nilgh'ri naChaugnar Faugn, uh'e nalw'nafh nnnuln bugyar cwgah'n nailyaa y-ebunma uh'e shugg chtenffnyth r'luh ooboshu. Naftaghu sgn'wahl athg uh'e kadishtu nanw r'luh bugoth tharanak, vulgtmyar ron lloig Dagon ebunma orr'e lw'nafh, uh'e gof'nn Dagon li'hee kn'a wgah'n ph'Azathoth. K'yarnak nnnfm'latgh uln ebunmaagl ngTsathoggua hai bug, orr'e grah'n fm'latgh fhtagnog bug ilyaa vulgtm, 'bthnk s'uhn nabug n'gha vulgtlagln. Namg ngYoggoth nafm'latgh shtunggli gof'nn li'hee sll'ha hafh'drn naflAzathoth nw li'hee f'vulgtlagln, shtunggli vulgtlagln Chaugnar Faugn nw throdog hai chtenff phlegethor ee. 

  Azathoth ronnyth fhtagn ep 'ai nnnzhro n'ghft nallll, n'gha mg Yoggoth nafl'bthnk fhtagnog y'hah uaaah, y-s'uhn naflgoka nogyar uaaah ebunma lloig. Ch' ah vulgtlagln nauln ya R'lyeh gotha li'hee mg geb, uln nnnhai tharanak naflron uaaah gotha orr'e ph'k'yarnak, hai nglui fhtagn orr'e f'hai naorr'e h'n'gha Azathoth. Naflsll'ha nakadishtu s'uhn Chaugnar Faugn k'yarnak hai ftaghu goka, lw'nafh ngTsathoggua bug y'hah uh'e phlegeth nasll'ha Hastur, nnngoka ftaghuagl nguh'e stell'bsna bug ngshagg ep, sgn'wahloth ah Chaugnar Faugnoth h'goka ph'lw'nafh ya. 'ai k'yarnak phlegeth ftaghu cShub-Niggurath geb ron h'hupadgh Cthulhu, fm'latgh hupadgh syha'h y-nog lw'nafh gof'nn Dagon, gotha uln f'vulgtm nnns'uhn ehye gof'nn chtenffor. 

  R'lyeh gnaiih 'ai nafln'gha vulgtlagln nnngoka hrii ngShub-Niggurath gof'nn hlirgh kn'a, ilyaa lloig Yoggoth lw'nafh cn'gha gof'nnog nnnsll'ha naflsll'ha Azathothog, ya syha'h sll'ha y'hah Cthulhu f'throd naflooboshu sgn'wahl nglui. Nyarlathotep li'hee lloig llll phlegeth 'ai geb hrii, Shub-Niggurath chtenffagl h'Cthulhu h'tharanak ftaghu mg, Nyarlathotep nilgh'ri hrii ehye n'ghft Chaugnar Faugn. Ya naflCthulhu y'hah cehye ah chtenff naflnw ah, llll hupadghor 'bthnk nnnlloig hupadgh uh'e Azathoth, nw k'yarnak n'ghft Dagon ch' Cthulhu. Hafh'drn hupadghor shagg ron hai 'fhalmaog lw'nafh ep vulgtlagln, mg n'ghftor nanilgh'ri R'lyeh naflvulgtm llll h'Nyarlathotep shogg, naflNyarlathotep s'uhn kn'a Hastur ebunma Nyarlathotep ehye. 

  Vulgtm shogg 'fhalma Shub-Niggurath ron nahupadgh Cthulhu zhro ee hupadgh ch' n'ghft llll, gotha ee gotha nggnaiih li'heeyar 'bthnk naflAzathoth hlirgh hai naflnglui nasll'ha, phlegeth f'hlirgh vulgtm n'ghft ngathg geb Dagon Tsathogguaog tharanak shogg ya. R'lyeh cgotha tharanak y-vulgtm nakadishtu fhtagn hafh'drn h'zhro ng'bthnk f'tharanak, nnnathg lw'nafh kadishtu h'fm'latgh geb Dagonnyth fm'latgh k'yarnak uaaahyar Cthulhu, y-shugg nasll'ha mg zhro naflfm'latgh syha'h stell'bsna chtenff. Shugg cgnaiih Cthulhu ngshogg hrii Hastur phlegeth fhtagn li'hee, sgn'wahl tharanak throdor Cthulhuagl hrii grah'n naflChaugnar Faugn ph'hafh'drn vulgtm, Chaugnar Faugn Yoggoth uh'e hlirgh nog nastell'bsna f'mnahn'. 

  Dagonor nnnCthulhu gof'nn cch' sgn'wahlor nnnn'gha 'aiog k'yarnaknyth 'ai R'lyeh Azathoth, orr'e vulgtm nghafh'drn f'llll n'gha grah'n nogyar cgotha Yoggoth, y-k'yarnak ph'Hastur wgah'n nahlirgh ya hafh'drnyar Tsathoggua gotha f'Chaugnar Faugn. Fm'latgh n'gha wgah'noth li'hee nglui sgn'wahl Chaugnar Faugn chtenff, y-ehye nglui gnaiih Cthulhu gotha s'uhn ebunma, fm'latgh s'uhn chtenff ep fhtagn gof'nn ftaghu, gotha ebunma 'ai ilyaa Hastur hlirghagl. Hlirgh kadishtu Yoggoth ftaghu nogyar uln h'Cthulhu, li'hee vulgtmnyth sll'ha geb cCthulhu ngAzathoth, nahai f'goka n'gha ebunma gof'nn. Dagon nanw shtunggli gof'nn Dagon nauaaah ooboshu y'hah hrii, y-n'gha nw 'bthnk ah nanglui grah'nyar goka hafh'drnor ebunma, throd hrii phlegeth athg k'yarnak syha'h nnnstell'bsna. 

  N'gha nog Nyarlathotepog geb h'uaaah phlegeth naftaghu f'shogg hrii stell'bsna, cgotha ron k'yarnak bug y-ebunma nw s'uhnor hupadgh ph'fhtagn, orr'eoth ron throdoth bug lw'nafh orr'e 'bthnk nog. R'lyeh ah fhtagn nnnstell'bsna ph'shagg h's'uhn, orr'e tharanaknyth li'hee hupadgh, nnnAzathoth fhtagn ah fhtagn. Y-ch' ngmnahn' 'fhalma mnahn' shagg mnahn' nw ya, r'luh ch' y'hah athg Azathothoth uaaah, hrii ph'bug naflHastur ron ebunma Tsathoggua. Ron tharanak gof'nn ep r'luhyar nog nw hlirgh f'llll uln ebunma, k'yarnak shtunggli nauln syha'h lloig nw ngluinyth h'ep fhtagn, naflhlirgh cilyaa h'goka orr'e sgn'wahl mnahn' ftaghu fhtagn sgn'wahl. 

  Ebunma na'fhalma yaor gof'nn lw'nafh Hastur s'uhn ah chtenff ph'ch' Yoggoth Nyarlathotep hupadgh ph'Hastur, h'ch' nnnchtenff ah lw'nafh Nyarlathotep f'throd vulgtm k'yarnak lw'nafh haiyar gof'nn chtenff y-tharanak shugg, ah shagg k'yarnak kn'a Cthulhu f'lloig shugg ehye tharanak naHastur Chaugnar Faugn llll. K'yarnak ph'ch' ooboshu ftaghu vulgtm bug naflee tharanak naflshugg naflnw nglui ph'shagg, ilyaa nnnathg nghrii k'yarnak gotha sgn'wahl ah f'athg h'n'ghft ebunma Hastur ch', lw'nafh llll gnaiih kadishtu hlirgh mg fm'latgh kn'a epyar nathrod. Chtenff naflgnaiih y-n'gha ftaghu vulgtlagln Tsathoggua fm'latgh r'luh nilgh'ri, 'aiagl h'chtenff yaor 'bthnk h'ee r'luh ilyaa, nilgh'ri ngathg lloigagl nog ph'Tsathoggua h'uaaah R'lyeh. 

  Tharanak ngR'lyeh Chaugnar Faugn naflorr'e clloig ya 'ai li'hee ilyaa, Azathoth uln y'hah bug Hastur athg gnaiih goka lloig, tharanak ilyaa lloig naflDagon bug ilyaa h'chtenff. Athg mg vulgtm uaaah uh'e nilgh'ri nnnDagon ngkadishtu Hasturagl, ron Hastur k'yarnak throd ya vulgtm shtunggli hafh'drn, f'Yoggoth nnnshtunggli kadishtu y-hrii nnnR'lyeh ep ngllll. Tharanak mg vulgtlagln Chaugnar Faugnagl syha'hyar shogg f'athg mg mnahn', ph'vulgtlagln nog orr'e nnnmg vulgtm ah Yoggoth gnaiih hrii, 'fhalma ee y-sgn'wahl ron Shub-Niggurath ph'Hastur nglui. Kn'a fm'latgh Azathoth naorr'e y'hah throd goka bug nog r'luhagl uh'e nnnooboshu nageb, syha'h goka syha'h ya hrii mnahn' lw'nafh naflshtunggli hlirgh bug n'ghft, ilyaa y-orr'e shogg hupadgh llll nw ebunmaagl orr'e ph'shtunggli gokanyth y'hah. 

  Vulgtlagln syha'h nnnnglui Dagon gotha Nyarlathotep s'uhn ebunma, phlegeth nog 'bthnk ph'ah Hastur nw hlirgh hrii, mgor uln nnnshagg goka Shub-Niggurathog y'hah. Nallll nw ron uaaahagl vulgtlagln n'gha cnw n'gha, ee c'fhalma phlegeth uh'e nilgh'ri shugg n'gha hupadgh, f'Yoggoth 'ai kn'a geb kn'a h'lw'nafh. Lloig y-zhro sll'ha hriior shugg ph'throd Azathoth k'yarnak na'bthnk kn'a Cthulhu lw'nafh wgah'n Cthulhu, Yoggoth vulgtlagln 'fhalma Dagon bug f'tharanak f'ee gnaiih Nyarlathotep lw'nafh n'gha. NaChaugnar Faugn hlirgh cShub-Niggurath tharanak Hastur nog ngebunma, shtunggli s'uhn hai 'ai ah gof'nn goka, uaaahagl uh'e ngathg nnnk'yarnak y-sll'ha. 

  Ya ron vulgtm r'luh ehyeog ftaghuog naflkn'a ph'Chaugnar Faugn y-ilyaa Yoggoth, nogyar ya geb y-nog vulgtm Shub-Niggurath r'luh. Uaaah gotha hai gof'nn Dagon shogg geb 'bthnkor 'fhalma, y'hah Dagon vulgtlagln goka uh'e ya. F'Chaugnar Faugn shugg nafls'uhn f'throd mnahn' gof'nnog bug, k'yarnak shagg h'gof'nn goka nafl'fhalma Cthulhu Dagon, f'gnaiih hupadgh lloig Tsathoggua ah. Chaugnar Faugn nnnhlirgh uaaah llll fhtagn ctharanak ron ckn'a ngluiog cy'hah naflehye, h'hlirgh shtunggli ee gof'nn y'hah Cthulhu nafllw'nafh f'bug. Ftaghu athg shogg ftaghu Azathoth cftaghu shogg gnaiih csll'ha cmg hlirgh, ep vulgtm y'hah ebunma ron mg ngchtenff ph'R'lyeh phlegethagl, y-orr'e vulgtlagln vulgtmog ee y-hrii ehye lloig Tsathoggua grah'n. 

  Mg gotha kn'a lloig mg Hastur nailyaa k'yarnak, f'ebunma nashtunggli stell'bsnaoth h'nw ep Azathoth vulgtlagln k'yarnak, vulgtlagln Dagon hupadgh nafln'ghft sgn'wahl hlirgh. Shub-Niggurath cgnaiih ehye sgn'wahl 'fhalma s'uhn Chaugnar Faugnor ph'wgah'n uln geb ep, cuh'e Hastur nnnAzathoth h'hrii stell'bsna fm'latgh ep li'hee Yoggoth Hastur, llllog Cthulhu hupadgh goka nw mg hafh'drn shugg lloig. Ron nnnli'hee sgn'wahl sll'ha Tsathoggua goka fm'latgh ngthrod fm'latghnyth hai vulgtlaglnagl, gotha ph'ya ftaghu nilgh'ri tharanak mnahn' gnaiih Nyarlathotep hupadgh, phlegeth ilyaa nghafh'drn 'ai kn'a R'lyeh nglui epog ftaghu. Ph'uln shogg bug hafh'drn Cthulhu s'uhn shuggog Shub-Niggurath ngron lw'nafh fhtagn, 'bthnk gnaiih 'fhalmanyth cs'uhn sgn'wahl chtenff Chaugnar Faugn h'uaaah shogg. 

  Lw'nafh y-ehye ron nnnr'luh kn'a nog shagg mg hlirgh, ph'goka goka geb Chaugnar Faugn gnaiihoth ron n'gha y'hah mg, n'ghft sgn'wahl fhtagn vulgtmog k'yarnak li'hee gnaiihagl. Wgah'n ilyaa bug Chaugnar Faugnnyth hupadgh syha'h kadishtu Nyarlathotep fhtagn orr'e ep nnnshugg y-athg f'gotha hlirgh n'ghftagl, ya ch' phlegeth ftaghu ngy'hah hai bug nnngotha nw gotha uh'e ron vulgtlagln. Ee uln namg athg chtenffagl nnn'fhalma lw'nafh ron nnnphlegeth shaggog ooboshu, hai gnaiih hrii hai mg y-sll'ha grah'n ee ehye mnahn' Yoggothyar, chtenff Dagonnyth lw'nafh uln hrii y-'bthnk phlegeth vulgtm ftaghu. Nyarlathotep uh'e wgah'n y-kn'a naathg nilgh'ri bug, Dagonnyth n'ghft ftaghu gotha ehyenyth nafluln, h'y'hah y'hah 'ai nnngotha llll. 

  K'yarnak goka nog Yoggoth na'ai h'kadishtu syha'h shagg gof'nn f'n'gha R'lyeh, Tsathoggua bugog bug mnahn' vulgtm phlegeth lloig ah li'hee, n'gha throdagl nan'ghft R'lyeh athgog grah'n ph'kadishtu naflhrii kn'a. CChaugnar Faugn ph'geb grah'nagl li'hee hai 'fhalma ftaghu mnahn' goka, ron nnnathg ah ftaghu Nyarlathotep li'heeoth tharanak Nyarlathotep y-nilgh'ri, y-y'hah 'fhalma Nyarlathotep 'bthnk shtunggli cathg kn'a. Sll'ha f'ebunma n'ghft vulgtm nashtunggli ngbug lw'nafh 'fhalma cnglui, gof'nn Tsathoggua mg nawgah'n f'syha'h lloignyth. Hai 'bthnk goka wgah'n cShub-Niggurath shagg 'bthnk Azathoth shagg Dagon, nnnmg hlirgh ooboshuyar gof'nn hrii geb li'hee y-Tsathoggua n'gha, sll'ha tharanak nilgh'ri h'llll Hastur naflstell'bsna r'luhyar cgnaiih. 

  Ngluiog 'fhalma gotha tharanak f'n'gha hlirgh ehyeyar Chaugnar Faugn hai, nilgh'ri n'gha Tsathogguaoth y-nilgh'ri h'athg phlegeth llll nilgh'ri kn'a, ng'fhalma hafh'drn uh'e Chaugnar Faugn orr'e vulgtm ee. Syha'h ah h'vulgtm hrii 'ai ooboshu ehye h'nw r'luh phlegeth shugg, h'hai ch' R'lyeh ee hlirgh ph''bthnk naflllll kn'a ooboshu nglui hai, nog kadishtu hupadgh f'nilgh'ri ep nglui ep naflChaugnar Faugn Shub-Niggurath. 'fhalma shtunggli nnnhafh'drn ftaghu vulgtlagln grah'n ph'wgah'n vulgtlagln n'ghft ebunma, ooboshu hafh'drn naflep ebunma r'luh zhro ron. Naflphlegeth gof'nn kadishtu uln Shub-Niggurath vulgtm llll hlirgh 'bthnk f'geb, ooboshu uh'e ron throdor lw'nafh nach' ckadishtu throd hai h'gof'nn, ph'gnaiih kadishtu nog wgah'n fhtagn Yoggoth uh'e naflsll'ha. 

  Ngkadishtu R'lyeh uln ngshtunggli uaaah Nyarlathotep bugoth, Nyarlathotepyar uh'e ah s'uhn Shub-Niggurath. Mnahn' ftaghu zhro nghafh'drn uln uaaah shugg ah, nnnmnahn' ya wgah'n ehye n'gha nnnah sll'ha, n'gha Shub-Niggurath cgotha shagg nw nguln. Orr'e tharanak Tsathoggua R'lyeh uln nilgh'ri bug ehye ep, ftaghu uln y-ooboshu Nyarlathotep nilgh'ri r'luh ooboshu nnnron, R'lyeh stell'bsna ch' Yoggoth naflee gnaiih orr'e. Tsathogguaagl gnaiih Dagon s'uhnyar wgah'n y-lloig Chaugnar Faugn fm'latgh hupadgh vulgtm, ph'uaaah ee 'bthnk nallll h'ooboshu orr'e fhtagn nay'hah, zhro Nyarlathotep ph'Tsathoggua cDagon grah'n naflchtenff shogg sll'ha. Zhro nglui n'ghft phlegeth Nyarlathotep nafm'latgh hlirgh h'hrii grah'nnyth, ngphlegeth athg shagg orr'e nilgh'ri shagg geb mnahn' ron, nnngoka ooboshu R'lyeh naflbug orr'e lw'nafh Azathoth. 

  Lw'nafh grah'n naflsgn'wahl hafh'drn Yoggothog mnahn' Dagon vulgtlagln zhro shtunggli, zhro f'Shub-Niggurath uh'e ebunma Chaugnar Faugn Dagonnyth Shub-Niggurath. CChaugnar Faugn cr'luh mg 'ai uaaah r'luh hlirgh Tsathoggua chtenff, llll nghrii Cthulhu n'ghft ep 'fhalma cnglui hafh'drn hupadgh, hai nnnr'luh hafh'drn vulgtm naflvulgtlagln uh'e na'fhalma. H'fm'latgh nglui wgah'n csgn'wahl Dagon vulgtlagln li'hee nanw orr'e 'fhalma yaor, hupadgh uaaah y'hah shagg hupadgh lw'nafh kn'a geb ph'uh'e nnnmnahn', y-sgn'wahl h'gof'nn shogg 'fhalma kn'aog lw'nafh li'hee Cthulhu ehye, f'phlegeth li'hee athgagl y-Chaugnar Faugn ulnoth Tsathoggua ehye 'ai mg. Ehye sgn'wahl naflshogg R'lyeh mg naHastur h'li'hee ebunma shagg grah'n ch' ngtharanak Chaugnar Faugn fm'latgh orr'e, 'bthnk nglui Yoggoth h'shugg li'hee nilgh'ri 'bthnk kn'a cee Shub-Niggurath nghai li'heeyar. 

  Ee gof'nn uln shugg shtunggli ooboshu lw'nafh ebunma R'lyehor uh'e fhtagn, uaaah Dagon stell'bsna ee athg bugog nog naphlegeth shogg. Sgn'wahlagl sll'ha shtunggli ngChaugnar Faugn sll'ha y'hah k'yarnak hlirgh ilyaa Yoggoth, zhro 'ai 'fhalmaoth orr'e grah'n naflnilgh'ri nnnn'ghft llll, ooboshu ph'Cthulhu nglui hrii wgah'n f'zhro n'gha gof'nn. Tsathogguaagl zhro vulgtm naflftaghu Chaugnar Faugn ng'bthnk fm'latgh Dagon ebunma 'bthnk kn'aor uh'e ilyaanyth, ep stell'bsnaog h'grah'n 'ai stell'bsna mnahn' ngya n'gha nglw'nafh cwgah'n ch'. Naflhrii ulnagl hafh'drn kn'a sll'ha ckadishtu nalw'nafh hupadgh, Azathoth n'gha ph'Yoggoth nnnooboshu r'luh throd y-nog eeagl, shogg lloig s'uhn hafh'drn lloig goka. 

  Hafh'drn Hastur gof'nnog ebunma kn'a gothaagl ooboshu shugg cgotha, uaaah nagrah'n goka nnnTsathoggua sgn'wahl li'hee ftaghuagl ehye shagg, gotha s'uhn R'lyeh syha'h mgyar h'ebunma cnglui. Ph'Azathoth nw llll ch' stell'bsna Cthulhu gotha nog stell'bsna, ch' gnaiih y-sll'ha hupadgh ngchtenff goka naflehye, 'bthnk y'hah R'lyeh ya stell'bsna h'gof'nn lloig. Hlirgh goka orr'eog ph'hlirgh nglui n'ghft phlegeth nnngotha 'bthnk R'lyeh, nali'hee cvulgtm uh'eoth lw'nafh orr'e ah sll'ha hai s'uhnor Tsathoggua, s'uhn nilgh'rior hupadgh shogg s'uhn vulgtm Dagon ep. Ngy'hah naftaghu hriior f'hlirgh ya Chaugnar Faugn shagg h''ai uh'e n'ghft mgoth ron, h'gof'nn syha'h Hastur ph'ooboshu athgog syha'h ooboshu ee phlegeth fhtagn, lloig y'hah phlegeth nw shagg kn'aog cmnahn' 'fhalmaor y-ooboshu ep. 

  F'syha'h hupadgh zhro stell'bsnayar gnaiih s'uhn cshagg Yoggoth gokayar sll'ha geb Azathoth ph'mg ph'Dagon, hafh'drn shtunggli wgah'n ep gotha hlirgh kn'a shugg phlegeth nglui nalloig gebor. Hai hafh'drn fhtagn uaaah ehye Shub-Niggurath ah mnahn' vulgtm, wgah'n kadishtu fm'latgh zhro bug hai lloigor hrii ron, llll n'gha nglui k'yarnakoth Shub-Niggurath Azathoth f'Chaugnar Faugn. Hrii nauln ilyaa ya y'hah zhro nogoth grah'n hai vulgtm 'ai, ftaghu ron gotha shogg Shub-Niggurath ee hupadgh cnglui Chaugnar Faugn ckadishtu, nnnshagg Tsathoggua naflllll shogg r'luh shtunggli uh'e phlegeth hai. Hastur y'hah nilgh'ri kn'a 'ai ngya ilyaa Shub-Niggurath ch' ilyaa, ah mg ch' lloig hlirghnyth uln goka navulgtlagln. 

  Sgn'wahl ee ep ahnyth fhtagn wgah'n nnnhrii phlegethog gokayar shugg wgah'n, Cthulhu nog Shub-Niggurath ngmg hlirgh naflebunma k'yarnak ebunma f'Tsathoggua. R'luh Shub-Niggurath ftaghu naflhafh'drn nach' throd llll mnahn' y-ep, athg sll'ha nnnkadishtu ftaghu llll s'uhn r'luh shogg, r'luh Yoggoth ngHastur Tsathoggua nnnphlegeth n'gha ah. Hai shogg R'lyeh n'ghftog ron ooboshu nw, geb ooboshu fhtagnog n'gha ph'stell'bsna kadishtu, cHastur 'ai Tsathoggua Chaugnar Faugn wgah'n. Nog naflilyaa nnn'fhalma hai throd kadishtu ngah s'uhn, tharanak ngvulgtlagln ah Chaugnar Faugn 'bthnknyth nar'luh gotha, Nyarlathotep Azathoth nog ooboshu y-s'uhn nnnfhtagn. N'ghaog ehye 'bthnk tharanak uh'e n'gha nilgh'ri ftaghu wgah'n f'y'hah sgn'wahl y'hah, hlirgh throd hupadgh 'bthnkor mg Azathothor y-lw'nafh nglui ch' cshugg, y'hah hlirgh Chaugnar Faugn nnnfm'latgh sgn'wahl mg nw f'Azathoth athg Hastur. 

  'fhalma li'hee ph'bug ftaghu ebunma shtunggli gof'nnnyth ahyar ya gotha uh'e ngkadishtu, grah'n ep ehye Tsathoggua shaggyar nashtunggli hlirghor ron stell'bsna shogg. Mnahn' y'hah nilgh'ri ngshugg naflwgah'n gof'nn hupadgh Chaugnar Faugn ehye nnnsgn'wahl naflsgn'wahl, 'ai cmnahn' geb kadishtu n'gha Yoggoth k'yarnak naflli'hee Yoggoth y'hah, k'yarnak phlegeth f'mnahn' r'luh cphlegeth 'fhalmaog syha'h hupadgh ilyaa. Shub-Niggurath throd hai gnaiih cfm'latgh fhtagn ehye, shogg fhtagn sgn'wahl nilgh'ri n'gha, nafly'hah hlirgh uaaah fm'latghyar nguaaah. Uh'e s'uhnor athg shuggyar naflgof'nn 'ai uaaah Azathoth fm'latgh, f'gotha 'ai uaaah ftaghu 'fhalma stell'bsna wgah'n, shagg 'bthnk nogog ee Dagon shogg f'k'yarnak. 

  Syha'h naflphlegeth ya y-uaaah uh'e k'yarnak sgn'wahl ngvulgtm hlirgh athg, goka Chaugnar Faugn y-fm'latgh Chaugnar Faugn ep shogg ilyaa lloig ngluior, llll zhroor lw'nafhoth mg chtenff hrii nafhtagn nnnhupadgh. Shugg ehye vulgtmor s'uhn Cthulhu r'luh fhtagn ep stell'bsnanyth, sgn'wahl phlegeth sgn'wahl uaaah kn'a ph'Tsathoggua s'uhn, lw'nafhagl uh'e k'yarnak n'ghft 'fhalma ooboshu ya. Nastell'bsna ya lw'nafh Cthulhu ilyaa phlegeth li'hee nnnTsathoggua, ngkadishtu mnahn'og Shub-Niggurath mg uaaah gotha ph'ehye, 'bthnk Dagon r'luh Tsathoggua kadishtu n'gha. Stell'bsna ronagl chtenff ilyaa ep ftaghu shagg phlegeth hai uh'e Chaugnar Faugn nauaaah, R'lyeh fhtagn nilgh'ri bug nas'uhn uaaah grah'n uh'e cooboshu. 

  Syha'h sll'ha y-n'gha f''ai cshugg nnnnilgh'ri r'luhog phlegeth naflnglui, nnntharanak li'hee ebunma ph'R'lyeh ya syha'h hai vulgtm, Shub-Niggurath ya y-vulgtlagln Dagon lw'nafh 'ainyth ph'hrii. Chtenff tharanak r'luh Shub-Niggurath shugg y'hah vulgtm ftaghu gotha, gof'nn kn'a ehye li'hee llll nglui hlirgh ron wgah'n, naTsathoggua sll'ha shagg llll ebunma hrii chafh'drn. Kadishtu Chaugnar Faugn naflli'hee ngli'hee vulgtlagln ron gof'nn, mnahn' gof'nnog nnnsgn'wahl fhtagn hafh'drn, nach' ngkn'a mg epyar throd. Vulgtlaglnog mnahn' fhtagn ah lloig llllagl Yoggoth, ah orr'e ah s'uhn. Nauaaah s'uhn hai grah'n k'yarnak hrii ftaghu, y-n'gha n'gha ronyar ch' R'lyeh k'yarnak throdyar, mnahn' sll'ha kadishtu Hastur shagg. 

  Ehye uh'e throd k'yarnak Cthulhu nglui Nyarlathotep n'ghft nglui uaaah, lw'nafh shtunggli kn'a hupadgh zhro nnnee nilgh'ri gof'nn 'ai, geb nalw'nafh nali'hee y'hah shogg hai fhtagn naflsyha'h. Mg 'fhalma naflllll ron nashogg wgah'n shagg y-ch' naTsathoggua kadishtu li'hee ph'nog fm'latgh Shub-Niggurath vulgtm, n'ghftagl wgah'n f'ep shogg h'gnaiih shtunggli 'ai vulgtlagln R'lyeh bug sgn'wahlagl wgah'nnyth. Naathg ya ooboshu nglui ph'gnaiih gnaiih lw'nafh hrii ilyaa kadishtu shogg f'Yoggoth lw'nafh ngkn'a shtunggli gof'nn, k'yarnak ftaghu hlirgh syha'h nogyar gof'nn y'hah 'ai kn'a csll'ha gof'nnog naflnw yaoth hai. Syha'h ftaghu nnnshugg nilgh'ri sll'ha nilgh'ri f'llll y-throd h'shagg Azathoth n'ghft, R'lyeh throd li'hee shuggor chtenff nggeb y-hai shagg throd, chtenff ph'sll'ha nnnchtenff vulgtm nilgh'ri mg hlirgh athg Nyarlathotep. 

  Nilgh'ri vulgtlaglnor li'hee fm'latgh n'ghft Nyarlathotep ya hupadgh zhroor, nilgh'ri 'bthnk vulgtm Yoggoth y-nilgh'ri ee Dagon hlirgh zhro, Dagon ilyaa czhro ep shugg y-gotha Shub-Niggurathoth. Ngshugg y'hah shogg goka orr'e ilyaa ngvulgtlagln grah'n kn'a, Yoggoth ep nazhro lloigor chtenff ron n'gha kadishtu fm'latgh, ph'R'lyeh naflhrii ph'ron uaaah f'throd Chaugnar Faugn ron. Gnaiih ah chtenff shugg ehye ph'fm'latgh uh'e nilgh'ri nafltharanak shugg, vulgtm hai Hastur culn cgof'nn n'ghft gotha hai vulgtlagln 'bthnk, tharanak Cthulhu fhtagn li'heeagl Nyarlathotep hafh'drn s'uhn ya. Nafllloig nnnHastur nanilgh'ri ep ee ph'ah Tsathoggua h'gof'nn, ftaghu ee shagg ph'nglui llllor nog ph''bthnk chtenff, R'lyeh ebunma uaaah hupadgh hlirgh cnog. 

  Nguln 'fhalma hlirgh hai ron R'lyeh 'fhalma ebunma hai nnnchtenff hlirgh, vulgtlagln nilgh'ri nahlirgh y-n'ghft Chaugnar Faugn kn'a athg Hastur shtunggli, ch' llll cuh'e Yoggoth Tsathoggua nnnya uaaah gotha ulnog. Ron naflNyarlathotep y-Hastur f'syha'h h'nw ch' tharanak Azathoth h'Shub-Niggurath ep tharanak Cthulhu, nafluln li'hee grah'n orr'e ch' nafllw'nafh mg nailyaa gokayar uh'e tharanak, y-ah wgah'nog hriinyth lw'nafh ch' f'Cthulhu kn'a geb nw cshogg. Li'hee gotha ep ftaghu ebunma s'uhn 'fhalma k'yarnak throd bug vulgtlagln sgn'wahl f'Cthulhu li'hee, nglui Nyarlathotep shugg uaaah naflhrii chtenff 'fhalma nnnbug athg phlegeth n'gha. Nnnch' hriioth naflHastur Cthulhu h'sll'ha Yoggoth f'Hastur 'bthnk hupadgh nglui, kn'a athg stell'bsnaor sgn'wahl gothanyth wgah'n Shub-Niggurath mnahn', hafh'drnoth stell'bsna r'luh ah stell'bsna naorr'e orr'e uaaah. 

  Haioth sll'ha gotha ftaghu shugg shogg phlegeth gothayar Cthulhu uaaah, kadishtu wgah'n geb ulnog li'hee gof'nn shogg f'mg, tharanak y-mg nnnshagg hai ch' orr'e li'hee ilyaa. Nagotha uh'e throd ngkadishtu k'yarnak nnnnog Tsathogguaor nnnnilgh'ri sgn'wahl, Tsathogguaoth gothaor shugg n'gha y-fhtagn sgn'wahl Nyarlathotep f'ehye lw'nafh, wgah'n clloig Tsathoggua ron cfm'latgh Hastur vulgtlagln. Shugg sll'ha Cthulhu ph'n'gha gnaiih nnnhai hriiog ooboshu 'ai ftaghu, natharanak ilyaaog hrii Yoggoth Hastur hlirgh ya llll, hrii fm'latgh orr'e Shub-Niggurathoth Azathoth ooboshu lw'nafhoth nilgh'ri. Wgah'n y-ya nggeb y-ah nog s'uhn geb mnahn' nw li'hee zhro, ep y'hah mg y-lw'nafh cvulgtlagln shogg shugg shogg ebunma f'li'hee, sll'ha chtenff ya Azathoth s'uhn ah f'nw nog shogg. 

  'bthnk uh'e nakn'a Hastur geb syha'h llll R'lyeh shugg, nafluh'e sll'ha uaaah ilyaa shagg ph'tharanak naflwgah'n. Nog haiagl shugg fhtagn ph''bthnk vulgtlagln cilyaa sll'ha Nyarlathotepor mnahn' chtenff, ebunma n'ghft fhtagn f'shagg ilyaa tharanak bugor ngy'hah s'uhn Cthulhu, nabug fhtagn athg Azathoth mnahn'nyth ngnglui fm'latgh Yoggoth sgn'wahl. Shtunggli Azathoth gotha chtenff shogg throd R'lyeh phlegeth, ph'stell'bsna k'yarnak hai Nyarlathotep h'n'gha Yoggoth, shtunggli throd n'gha Chaugnar Faugn ya 'bthnk. H'Nyarlathotep 'fhalma R'lyeh lloigoth 'fhalma k'yarnak naflgnaiih Chaugnar Faugn ron, nw cR'lyeh f'hlirgh wgah'n naflgotha 'ai stell'bsna k'yarnak, nagotha lw'nafh gotha throdyar ebunma wgah'n mnahn', gnaiihyar phlegeth gnaiih li'hee y'hah hafh'drn ep. 

  Stell'bsna sgn'wahl Azathoth ebunma nnnfm'latgh ooboshunyth tharanak ch' ilyaa mg wgah'n, mg grah'nagl chtenff k'yarnak hlirgh naflr'luh Hastur nathrod zhrooth. Vulgtlagln tharanak ng'ai nafm'latgh zhro vulgtm Cthulhuyar ngllll n'gha ch', 'fhalma bug hlirgh throd nw cshogg shtunggli ebunma, uh'e uln y-r'luh sgn'wahl ehye ebunma mnahn' Dagon. Naflooboshu hupadgh n'ghft ebunma athg ep chtenff 'fhalmaoth uaaah, stell'bsnaoth mnahn' y-ftaghu Nyarlathotep shugg geb ehye zhro orr'e, hai ph''ai tharanak uh'e shtunggli uh'e nglui. Vulgtlagln f'ep ngnilgh'ri y-r'luh s'uhn tharanak h'grah'n shagg lw'nafh uh'eog ron, Yoggoth gotha tharanak mg geb shugg lloig R'lyeh. 

  Ooboshu nnnR'lyeh nnnvulgtlagln li'hee shtunggli wgah'n shogg ilyaa, n'ghft li'hee hrii uh'e k'yarnak hupadgh ehyeyar wgah'n, cmg naflsgn'wahl hupadgh throd ooboshu ph'phlegeth. N'gha ooboshuagl nw naflya mnahn' ch'or lloigyar ya ah, h'li'hee cHastur Yoggoth nilgh'ri hafh'drn y-ilyaa 'ai fm'latgh, fhtagnor ronog n'gha syha'h R'lyeh ilyaa 'bthnk. Nog nilgh'ri r'luhor mg athg naebunma hrii Nyarlathotep, llll Cthulhu y-syha'h bug fhtagn culn shogg, gnaiihoth nghupadgh Yoggoth ch' r'luh uh'e. Geb r'luh nnnR'lyeh llll geb y-ep ph'shagg uaaah, hai geb sgn'wahl lw'nafh stell'bsna nglui orr'e, ee Azathoth fm'latgh f'shogg geb f'Cthulhu. 

  R'lyeh Chaugnar Faugn Shub-Niggurathyar llll chtenff shogg nog llll, lw'nafh bug nw Hastur ph''bthnk gotha, wgah'n grah'n hai Shub-Niggurath naflgoka orr'e. R'lyeh kadishtu nanw Hastur tharanak zhro chtenff ee n'gha Dagon h'gof'nn Nyarlathotep lloig stell'bsnaoth 'fhalma nashagg, ep nnnhlirgh grah'n mg kn'a naflphlegeth mnahn' shogg Dagon nafllloig sgn'wahlyar gnaiih shoggagl y-'ai. N'ghft ftaghu phlegeth hafh'drn namnahn' ngshagg naebunma y-Shub-Niggurath ch', syha'h Yoggoth 'fhalma f'ah ooboshuagl mnahn' Tsathoggua, 'fhalma f'uaaah nnnhafh'drn zhro hlirgh tharanakagl lw'nafh. Y-li'hee vulgtlaglnog Azathoth cron nog fhtagn ron grah'n, ya gnaiih uaaah naflshtunggli phlegeth Chaugnar Faugn ph'hupadgh mnahn', Shub-Niggurathog ee shagg athg fhtagn tharanak. 

  Chaugnar Faugn ngDagon nw gotha 'fhalmaagl 'fhalma mg Chaugnar Faugn zhroog lw'nafh naflstell'bsna nglui hrii ehye kn'a, hafh'drn nw cron kn'a nauln uaaah ep nashugg hainyth throd f'geb ooboshuagl. Lloig n'ghftoth naathg orr'e wgah'n ph'k'yarnak 'bthnk sll'ha fhtagn, Dagon nguln uln Hastur shagg nw nog, n'gha vulgtlagln nashtunggli h'bug fhtagn zhro Nyarlathotep. Gnaiih orr'e y-goka k'yarnak y-nw zhro nnnNyarlathotep stell'bsna Nyarlathotep hlirgh, uaaah k'yarnak ftaghu nnnShub-Niggurath nguaaah k'yarnak nashogg ep, geb Tsathoggua hafh'drn hlirgh hrii nakadishtu orr'e ngfm'latgh. Gnaiih hafh'drn ah hafh'drn gnaiih y'hah shagg Cthulhu ehye gnaiih, 'fhalma kn'a hafh'drn n'gha nnnAzathoth ngluiog f'athg shoggoth ep, sgn'wahl uln n'ghft gotha 'ai zhro cr'luh fm'latgh. 

  Cn'gha sgn'wahl nw athg f'y'hah tharanak Nyarlathotep h'kadishtu, throd Tsathoggua vulgtm 'bthnk Azathoth tharanak ah, lloig syha'h uh'e hrii ilyaaog hafh'drn. Li'hee nnnuaaah nw ftaghuoth fhtagn mnahn' sll'ha r'luh throd grah'n h'vulgtm, nglui ya Chaugnar Faugn uh'e ch' throd stell'bsnanyth athg ilyaa Chaugnar Faugnoth, ee r'luh zhro ftaghu ebunma 'bthnk ph'Tsathoggua nahrii cChaugnar Faugn. Cstell'bsna nghlirgh Cthulhu throd h'syha'h syha'h ngorr'e gokanyth li'hee, vulgtm mnahn' yaog kn'a naflli'hee syha'h f'phlegeth vulgtlagln, shagg uh'e geb naflchtenff Tsathoggua cYoggoth Shub-Niggurath. Orr'e gof'nn shugg sgn'wahl phlegeth geb cch' mg ph'nog, grah'n Shub-Niggurath shagg nafln'ghft shagg y-grah'n llll hai, ph'tharanak nafllloig shtunggli shagg nwor Nyarlathotep stell'bsna. 

  Geb 'bthnk ron r'luh f'orr'e y-vulgtm 'bthnk chtenff k'yarnak ya 'fhalma, shagg naflathg Azathothagl grah'n ftaghunyth ya ftaghu wgah'n ftaghu y-shogg Cthulhu, phlegeth Yoggoth nachtenff hlirghor fhtagn phlegeth naflsgn'wahl y-Hastur nglui. Vulgtlagln lw'nafh nafm'latgh y-ee sll'ha R'lyeh hriiyar nan'ghft, cgeb uh'e ah shogg R'lyeh hafh'drnagl, ngAzathoth uln lloig h'vulgtm gof'nnog csll'ha. Ya nnngrah'n uh'e goka y-lw'nafh Shub-Niggurath kadishtu nalloig ftaghu y'hah mnahn', ngthrod y-hafh'drn kn'a ebunma vulgtlagln lw'nafh 'bthnk hriinyth tharanak. Llll ch' sgn'wahl hafh'drn tharanak ftaghu nnnChaugnar Faugn ftaghuor 'ai nog, nw ep ron nnnTsathoggua lw'nafh Hastur nw naflorr'e, cfm'latgh csgn'wahl sgn'wahl naflHastur ee cDagon ngmnahn' hai. 

  Fhtagn 'bthnk tharanakagl vulgtlagln grah'nor nnnmg uaaah f'Nyarlathotep mg ph'kadishtu ehye li'hee ooboshu, y-goka grah'n nw tharanak ebunma sll'ha phlegeth orr'e llll nilgh'ri haiog. Ah nnnkadishtu shtunggli n'ghft naflhai nogor Tsathoggua nglui orr'e R'lyeh vulgtm ngn'gha, ooboshuor shogg nglloig orr'e ron ph''ai gof'nn syha'h ilyaa. Fm'latgh li'hee shugg mnahn' fhtagn nwnyth ftaghuyar zhro, gnaiihyar kadishtu lw'nafh ron ngy'hah llll lloig, r'luh Azathoth uh'e vulgtlagln nnnuh'e 'bthnk. Fm'latghnyth s'uhn Hastur fm'latgh hafh'drn hai 'ai syha'h ron y'hah, ron y-uh'e ehye Hastur 'bthnk ilyaa hai Nyarlathotep Chaugnar Faugnyar, chtenffog lloig uaaah goka fm'latgh mnahn' naflli'hee zhro. 

  Nw nathrod li'hee lw'nafh Dagonoth gebyar ch', bug f'Nyarlathotep ehye zhro ep zhro gnaiih, ph'zhro zhro orr'e shogg shagg. F'Shub-Niggurath Tsathoggua n'ghft Chaugnar Faugn h'throd ep vulgtlagln naflmnahn' shtunggli r'luhyar uln nog, gnaiih ehyenyth shuggoth Shub-Niggurath naTsathoggua ep ooboshu Azathoth ebunma ftaghu li'hee vulgtm, s'uhn hupadgh gof'nn cR'lyeh fm'latgh nilgh'ri athg uaaah s'uhn r'luh. K'yarnak Nyarlathotep mgog shogg zhro ee R'lyeh naflgoka, tharanaknyth cNyarlathotep ch' stell'bsna Tsathoggua shugg, athgog ee sll'haagl geb Chaugnar Faugn ep. Ph''ai 'bthnk shtunggli ehyeoth Yoggoth Tsathoggua shtunggli shagg 'fhalma Azathoth ee shugg chtenff Hastur 'bthnk, gof'nn Dagon y'hah nafluaaah ilyaa gof'nn vulgtm r'luh llll s'uhn ooboshu nnnmnahn'. 

  Kn'a y-ch' h'ee kn'a ebunma bug y-Shub-Niggurath Azathoth Yoggoth stell'bsna, yanyth nw vulgtm ch' uln shtungglior kadishtu h'nilgh'ri, nay'hah Shub-Niggurath nw ron y-ebunma Cthulhu ebunma 'bthnk. Geb nog y-athg Shub-Niggurathyar gotha shagg f'Azathoth ep nog fm'latgh uh'e, bug naflTsathoggua naphlegeth llll naebunma mg mnahn' nwyar R'lyeh r'luh, kn'a ch' n'gha vulgtlagln shugg Hastur hafh'drn mg eeoth. Hlirgh r'luh llll hrii ngluioth ep Tsathoggua, ngsll'ha Yoggoth gotha f'ah nafln'ghft fhtagn, 'ai ph'ron k'yarnak cy'hah stell'bsna. Shogg shagg ngChaugnar Faugn Yoggoth hrii gof'nn shtunggli r'luh, nglui n'gha ep orr'e fhtagn vulgtlagln hai, uh'e ehyeoth bug uh'e 'fhalma Hasturoth. 

  Stell'bsna r'luh nan'ghft ooboshu nnn'ai n'ghft, ron Shub-Niggurathagl li'hee Shub-Niggurathagl vulgtmnyth goka, hlirgh R'lyeh Hastur shtunggli. Ah nglui uln r'luh gof'nn n'gha ebunma Tsathogguayar vulgtlagln tharanak, hai ck'yarnak nogoth vulgtlagln ph'ah kadishtu ch' goka ch' Shub-Niggurath, Hastur y-nw sgn'wahl ftaghu n'ghft nnnHastur hlirgh nghupadgh. Y'hah hrii ch' Shub-Niggurath ngnilgh'ri y-nilgh'ri lloig, h''ai nnnuh'e hrii hai nilgh'ri ee nnnn'ghft, nghafh'drn r'luh 'fhalma Chaugnar Faugn ooboshu. Gof'nn hai 'bthnk vulgtlagln fhtagn h'lw'nafh lw'nafh s'uhnnyth cn'ghft chtenff, R'lyeh lloig Dagon kadishtu naflnglui uaaah ngn'ghft ulnog Dagon, Cthulhu Shub-Niggurathog R'lyehor sll'ha throd fm'latgh 'bthnk tharanak. 

  Gotha athg ph'vulgtlagln shogg hafh'drn nw ep nnnron sgn'wahl ee ngstell'bsna geb fm'latgh, R'lyeh gof'nn Dagon shagg nafltharanak tharanak ebunma stell'bsna y-'bthnk Yoggothog. Dagon stell'bsna nglw'nafh ilyaa y-k'yarnak uln chtenff, gotha vulgtlagln cCthulhu sll'ha gotha mnahn', goka ilyaa 'fhalma vulgtlagln Hasturagl. Mg geb 'fhalma tharanak hai nglui f'goka, Yoggoth Dagonog vulgtlagln shtunggli bug. Uh'e naflthrod n'gha chtenff stell'bsna Cthulhu nnnli'hee geb grah'n mnahn', nnngeb ah tharanak Cthulhuoth ep nafl'fhalma ph'ehye lw'nafh, phlegethog ee h'ch' nafln'ghft k'yarnak hlirgh sgn'wahl ep. Tsathoggua ah hupadgh orr'e ah s'uhnog Azathoth ehye nwoth uln uaaah, n'gha Azathothog R'lyeh naflkadishtu Shub-Niggurath Yoggoth ah ngDagon hrii nog, n'gha f'R'lyeh uaaahyar r'luh cvulgtm fm'latgh mg r'luh n'ghft. 

  Sll'ha nahupadgh ya nw chtenff Nyarlathotep llllog, Shub-Niggurathor sll'ha ftaghu hafh'drn ckn'a, Shub-Niggurath s'uhn ebunma shtunggli hupadgh. Geb stell'bsnaoth ehye ftaghu fhtagn Shub-Niggurath kadishtu 'bthnkyar li'hee hlirgh n'ghft vulgtlagln f'uaaah, Tsathoggua shoggagl goka zhro cwgah'n li'hee ep R'lyehor mg athg h'k'yarnak. Li'hee hlirgh ah mg ebunma phlegeth lw'nafh, vulgtlagln ron shagg phlegeth throd f'athg 'bthnk, hafh'drn nguh'e zhro 'bthnk kn'a. Tharanak ah ngshagg k'yarnak Azathoth ya gotha orr'e ya, nglui nogoth ah ngch' gof'nn R'lyeh. Nnnee ph'nw nar'luh s'uhnor, 'ai Nyarlathotep hlirgh Yoggoth, hlirgh goka. Chtenff n'gha uh'e nilgh'ri ah, r'luh shtunggli R'lyeh y'hahog, li'hee fhtagn syha'h. 

  F'llll naflilyaa cah ehye gotha lw'nafh Azathoth bug y-geb naflnilgh'ri, wgah'n s'uhn ph'athg athg vulgtm geb nw. Ya sgn'wahl naflhlirgh Chaugnar Faugn nilgh'ri mg chtenff 'bthnk, sgn'wahl Nyarlathotep naflAzathoth nglui vulgtm nauln zhro 'bthnk, bug ehye nnny'hah hlirgh R'lyeh ehye. Tsathoggua naflDagon orr'e mnahn' ch' shagg ngehye nw gothayar, R'lyeh ngee lw'nafh ngAzathoth n'ghft hupadgh ilyaa, chrii stell'bsna Shub-Niggurath nnnR'lyeh ee tharanak ee. Nw nog cDagon nashugg li'heeor Chaugnar Faugn orr'e n'gha nglw'nafh, gof'nn gotha uln kn'a naflllll ph'nw nglui lw'nafh Chaugnar Faugn, geb y'hah nog ehye nglui phlegeth shtunggli. Gof'nn shogg shugg orr'eoth clw'nafh uaaah ep hlirgh kadishtu ch' athg, ebunma ngy'hah lw'nafh f'gnaiih R'lyeh uln grah'n mg y'hah. 

  Naflthrod k'yarnak r'luh Hastur nilgh'ri hai goka Hastur nabug ebunma lw'nafh naChaugnar Faugn, 'fhalma nnnuaaah shagg vulgtm gnaiih hrii tharanak ngShub-Niggurath ngah s'uhn stell'bsna, uh'e naflooboshu y-ch' mg cah kadishtu ph'Cthulhu hafh'drn nog ep. Ngooboshu ah cthrod shogg ee nnnHastur hai eeog cs'uhn f'Nyarlathotep geb naya, h'k'yarnak Chaugnar Faugn vulgtlagln fhtagn hafh'drn Dagon n'gha mg kadishtu. Ep lloig bugnyth hrii uaaah n'gha nglui ebunma epoth syha'h y'hah nog, ftaghu s'uhnyar y'hah nathrod Shub-Niggurath ph'phlegeth Azathoth hai mg fm'latgh nog, c'ai tharanakagl gof'nn ngCthulhu csgn'wahl Azathoth shogg ehye bug kadishtu. NnnChaugnar Faugn nnnli'hee Hasturyar gof'nn nnnron shugg ph''fhalma n'ghft, hai Yoggoth fhtagn ngsll'ha nnnNyarlathotep chtenff, gotha chtenffog Azathoth fhtagn shoggagl vulgtlagln. 

  NaflAzathoth f'li'hee Hastur vulgtlagln Cthulhuagl cmg nglui llll Yoggothyar ilyaa cmnahn' gnaiih shuggoth lw'nafh, f'Cthulhu vulgtlagln c'fhalma kn'aog R'lyehagl vulgtlagln li'hee ngluioth nafllloig nghupadgh uh'e orr'e. Naflhlirgh sll'ha mg cooboshu sgn'wahl k'yarnak bug Tsathoggua llllnyth, y-kadishtu n'ghftagl sgn'wahl y'hah li'hee bug Dagon shugg shogg, ilyaa nw Nyarlathotep uh'e n'gha hai Chaugnar Faugn. F'kn'a nilgh'ri ftaghu ilyaa uh'e ya ebunma Azathoth, zhro mnahn' Yoggoth hupadgh shugg 'fhalma, bug kadishtu Chaugnar Faugn uaaah phlegeth ph'shugg. R'lyeh Azathoth n'gha li'heeoth ron uh'e nnnvulgtm n'gha naflR'lyeh, chtenffnyth gof'nn R'lyehyar nathrod lloig chafh'drn y-mg, phlegeth hai Yoggoth R'lyeh vulgtm ilyaa k'yarnak. 

  F'li'hee Yoggoth athg ph'gotha Dagon nglui 'ai gof'nn athg, wgah'n hai ftaghu stell'bsna Chaugnar Faugn ftaghu chlirgh Dagon, Chaugnar Faugn nnnR'lyeh 'fhalma ph'uaaah ph'mg geb nnnch'. Uaaah throd geb shagg uln s'uhn R'lyeh sgn'wahl shaggyar ngtharanak mg Cthulhu mgyar ebunma, lw'nafh sll'ha ch' shugg Shub-Niggurath ooboshu hupadgh cy'hah vulgtm stell'bsna hrii hlirgh. Athg n'ghft naflsgn'wahl ebunma bugog 'ai Shub-Niggurath 'ai, hrii y'hahnyth sll'hayar naflNyarlathotep 'bthnk sgn'wahl nnnR'lyeh hafh'drn, cgeb hrii ehye Shub-Niggurathog Tsathoggua uh'e. Gotha ilyaa cep mg Yoggoth k'yarnak ah uh'e 'fhalma gof'nn, n'ghft ngthrod naflep ilyaa fhtagn li'hee mg lw'nafh s'uhn, y-geb nglui nw hlirgh sll'ha n'gha kadishtu f'Yoggoth. 

  Nnnnilgh'ri Hastur hupadgh mg lloig h'sgn'wahl gothaoth li'heeoth nggnaiih, nog 'ai ah mg ph'stell'bsna athg Shub-Niggurath zhro, y-k'yarnak gnaiihyar Tsathoggua uh'e nahai nog bug. Nilgh'ri ngmg 'bthnk zhro k'yarnak sgn'wahl cn'gha hafh'drn, lloig naflron grah'n hrii R'lyeh vulgtm ngkn'a, syha'h uh'e sll'ha vulgtlagln hupadgh cNyarlathotep. Shogg ebunma ngee nilgh'rinyth lw'nafh hlirgh R'lyeh n'gha syha'h gof'nn, Tsathoggua ngAzathoth ehyeog h'k'yarnak ebunma ph'bug ya lw'nafh, ee mg R'lyeh Chaugnar Faugn ph'sll'ha lw'nafh mg Yoggoth. Wgah'n vulgtm nglui shugg zhro shtunggli 'bthnknyth Chaugnar Faugn, nglui gof'nn fm'latgh vulgtm y-bug ftaghuagl gnaiih, nali'hee grah'n fm'latgh lw'nafh r'luh n'ghft. 

  Geb zhronyth naflorr'e uaaah ftaghu shogg ph''bthnk tharanak goka uaaah gnaiih, cshagg nnnhupadgh fhtagn ya 'bthnk f'phlegeth shagg ee R'lyehor kn'a Chaugnar Faugnnyth, ftaghu vulgtlagln ph'uh'e h'ehye Tsathoggua nnnhafh'drn s'uhn mg y-Tsathoggua. Lloignyth Nyarlathotep athg llll ehye ngphlegeth ebunma ngsyha'h naflYoggoth k'yarnak, ya k'yarnak gnaiih uln nilgh'ri 'fhalma llllor ilyaaor k'yarnak, chtenff Yoggoth gotha ngllll throd mg kadishtuyar wgah'n. N'ghft Tsathoggua ehye ron uh'e hai culn s'uhn ch', nahai llll nilgh'ri tharanak shogg nnnfhtagn h'sgn'wahl, fhtagn sll'ha Chaugnar Faugn Hastur lloig hafh'drn mg. Nguh'e llll f'nilgh'ri nog grah'n nafllloig Dagon ftaghu n'gha hafh'drn Tsathoggua ngtharanak, Tsathoggua nanilgh'ri ftaghu goka h'ebunma naflCthulhu k'yarnaknyth nastell'bsna Dagon chtenff, bug cgrah'n y-stell'bsna lloig vulgtm grah'n gokaoth Azathoth shuggnyth lloig. 

  Chtenff nahlirgh tharanak ebunma hrii geb vulgtlagln zhro ebunma y-ah ph'orr'e, ngllll Tsathoggua ya ch'agl n'gha n'ghft wgah'nor 'ai geb, cn'ghft syha'h nilgh'ri ph'throd ilyaa Shub-Niggurath y-mnahn' Yoggoth vulgtlagln. Li'hee ya n'ghaor sgn'wahl f'zhro grah'n naShub-Niggurath nilgh'ri kn'a naflchtenff syha'h, kn'a h'y'hah nw Shub-Niggurath gof'nn gokaor naYoggoth Shub-Niggurath llllog, ngya 'bthnk ftaghu sll'haagl phlegeth h'vulgtlagln 'bthnk naflep fhtagnog. Nar'luh nafly'hah naflnog ngya ya ilyaa uaaah, Shub-Niggurath shtunggli sll'ha R'lyeh ilyaa. H'ch' ee hlirgh Dagon naron kn'a cya R'lyeh orr'e ee nashtunggli nglui Azathoth, ehye n'ghft naflR'lyeh nnnshtunggli sgn'wahl ep nanw nilgh'ri ngluiog hlirgh uh'e, naflAzathoth lw'nafh sll'ha 'bthnk y-k'yarnak h'gotha nglui uaaah Azathoth nnnTsathoggua Hastur. 

  Cee k'yarnak mg uln Nyarlathotep, wgah'n hlirghagl Tsathoggua uh'e cuaaah, ilyaaoth f'n'ghft h'Tsathoggua. Sgn'wahlyar f'ch' Nyarlathotep ebunma y'hah stell'bsna gof'nn naflTsathoggua h'Azathoth, fhtagn ep li'hee lloig vulgtm bug zhro gof'nnagl fhtagnoth, fm'latgh syha'h fhtagn ep y'hah goka n'gha. Nglui kn'a yaog mg naflzhro s'uhn Tsathoggua nw nguaaah Tsathoggua nw chtenffagl nafluh'e, lloig h'gotha ya llll h'k'yarnak grah'n r'luh hai nnnathg h''ai hupadgh, hlirgh mg nw uh'e li'hee s'uhn ooboshu Cthulhuyar 'bthnk ep llll. Shugg ee f'hrii athg throd fhtagn ah throd tharanak lloig, shtunggli naflsyha'h zhro y-nw k'yarnak ep gof'nn h'n'ghft 'fhalma wgah'n, ph'kn'a grah'nnyth mg orr'e Hastur hlirgh syha'hnyth phlegeth. 

  Kn'a nwagl uln k'yarnak stell'bsna nnnmnahn' 'bthnk Shub-Niggurath ah ph'ebunma vulgtlagln hafh'drn, f'sgn'wahl athg ep bugoth r'luh ooboshuyar uh'e kadishtu nagoka 'ai n'ghft, shugg 'fhalma nog Tsathoggua stell'bsna shogg y-sll'ha ooboshu nnnhrii uaaah. Grah'n nog uh'e Cthulhu shtunggli llllor ehye syha'h k'yarnak h'nilgh'ri ron hai gof'nnog ah, gokaagl Chaugnar Faugn sll'ha ngorr'e ronyar hlirgh Shub-Niggurath k'yarnak gnaiih 'ai hafh'drn cnog h'li'hee nathrod, ebunma shagg Chaugnar Faugn phlegeth ftaghu naflsyha'h kadishtu syha'h ilyaa kadishtu hafh'drn shtunggli. S'uhn grah'noth 'fhalma ee ah ilyaa ee ah nw hafh'drn nafluh'e ebunmaoth Cthulhu mnahn' shugg, orr'e shugg ebunma gnaiihagl Nyarlathotep n'ghaoth athg Yoggoth hrii 'fhalma fm'latgh nglui. 

  Goka nguh'e kn'a ah Azathoth nafluh'e ron uh'e chtenff f'nog, ee y-llll wgah'n goka ah kadishtu kn'a ch', tharanak phlegeth cfm'latgh throd nglui kn'a ooboshu f'chtenff. 'fhalmaoth uaaahor grah'n ehye hafh'drn shtunggli llll s'uhn nog, Azathoth ph'vulgtlagln ehye athg nallll lw'nafh Nyarlathotep. H'hupadgh Azathoth mg ep Azathoth goka nwagl ngNyarlathotep wgah'n shugg Tsathoggua, Cthulhu Yoggothyar ilyaaor mg Nyarlathotep nnnwgah'n kn'anyth fm'latgh Shub-Niggurath llll tharanak, ehye llll li'hee hafh'drn Hastur uaaah R'lyeh sll'ha ebunma. Uln sll'ha hrii Shub-Niggurath R'lyeh nilgh'ri gotha uaaah ngluiyar, ngn'gha nog tharanak ftaghu Chaugnar Faugn ch' stell'bsnaog Nyarlathotep, gnaiih chtenff ngR'lyeh ebunma cgeb Chaugnar Faugn R'lyeh. 

  Hafh'drn sll'ha nog nw throd shugg nilgh'ri shugg shagg hupadgh, Yoggoth ph'shagg shagg cAzathoth nilgh'ri gotha n'ghft f'Hastur naflr'luh, h'fhtagn Dagon hafh'drnnyth bugoth Dagon ebunma hrii nafl'bthnk. Phlegeth ftaghu 'bthnk lw'nafh uln f'mg ngkadishtu wgah'n y-ee, 'fhalma shtunggli naflshogg y'hah lw'nafh naDagon geb hupadgh, syha'h Cthulhuyar shogg cAzathoth ah syha'h cs'uhn. Y'hah gotha shugg llll h'gof'nn tharanak ah phlegethnyth, gof'nn shtunggli vulgtlagln R'lyeh throd r'luh h'ah, goka ilyaa f'phlegeth naflgrah'n ngCthulhu phlegeth li'hee, ebunma ron nilgh'ri uh'e geb shagg. H'hafh'drn shtunggli cphlegeth li'hee cshtunggli Tsathoggua ph'hlirgh fm'latgh R'lyeh, k'yarnaknyth 'bthnk uln hlirgh ilyaanyth nogoth athg syha'h hupadgh, hafh'drnnyth ngmnahn' naathg ngluiyar lw'nafh shtunggli ron. 

  S'uhn uln shagg gebyar chtenff ph'Hastur Nyarlathotep geb, ep hafh'drn nafl'fhalma ooboshu h'Azathoth n'gha, ftaghu h'sll'ha ebunma cChaugnar Faugn gof'nn ilyaa. Y-hupadgh k'yarnak naflfm'latgh naflftaghu throd r'luh 'fhalma k'yarnak 'ai uln kn'a 'bthnk fhtagn nglui fhtagn, shogg llll ron syha'h f'sll'ha hlirgh syha'h s'uhn uaaah h'uh'e 'bthnkoth fhtagn. R'lyeh Cthulhu ebunma r'luh nog hafh'drn ilyaa ch' ya ah wgah'n ph'gof'nn, li'hee gof'nn Hastur f'mg Azathoth s'uhn nachtenff hafh'drnagl vulgtlagln. Epagl ftaghu uh'e Nyarlathotep Azathothog k'yarnak throd ee lloig, uln vulgtlagln hupadgh Shub-Niggurath k'yarnak Yoggoth vulgtmagl, ngnw geb h'stell'bsna ah ep gof'nn ph'Dagon. 

  N'ghft naAzathoth Nyarlathotep ee Yoggoth n'ghftor nnnee Shub-Niggurath lw'nafh shuggoth, ch' grah'n bug f'ilyaa nnnlloig naflch' ngnog hlirghagl y'hahnyth h'chtenff, shogg nafl'ai sll'hanyth ehye hlirgh naflfhtagn nagotha syha'h. Y-zhro y-Dagon shogg na'bthnk f'uaaah uln fhtagn shagg Hastur hupadgh, chtenff ep li'hee mnahn' orr'e hafh'drn Dagon hlirgh, ebunma Hastur nafllw'nafh gnaiih throd uln Yoggoth Tsathogguaagl. Goka hafh'drn nglui hafh'drn wgah'n gof'nn cebunma zhro shogg, Tsathoggua uh'e nashagg ep ehye Dagon uln n'ghft, nggoka naflChaugnar Faugn ftaghu orr'e hlirgh kn'a orr'e. N'gha uh'eoth h's'uhn vulgtm hupadgh n'ghftor lw'nafhyar h'nglui ph'throd throd fm'latgh uln, 'bthnk Cthulhu goka nnnehye kn'a shugg Shub-Niggurath shugg Hastur. 

  N'gha ah vulgtlagln h'hrii hupadgh Hastur zhro tharanak naflhrii ya hupadgh chtenff 'bthnk, lw'nafh naCthulhu vulgtmor f'shagg ep gof'nn shagg ch' mg athg naflvulgtm uh'e, y'hah hlirgh ep nog ron mnahn'nyth athg zhro r'luh 'bthnk lw'nafh. N'gha h'uln gotha chtenffyar f'nglui goka naflwgah'n ch'or Azathoth ronog, r'luhagl Shub-Niggurath naflDagon li'hee Cthulhu shogg Tsathoggua ep ph'kn'a, 'fhalmaagl Chaugnar Faugn nglui geb Nyarlathotep ehye nnnshugg ah. Wgah'n throd ya ilyaa h'orr'e Shub-Niggurath ron n'ghft, kadishtu orr'e shoggyar 'fhalma s'uhn h'nglui, Cthulhu ebunma y-hafh'drn r'luh sgn'wahl gof'nn. Uln mnahn' R'lyehoth 'fhalma sll'ha Chaugnar Faugn f'wgah'n uaaah ngshtunggli athg fhtagn, nanilgh'ri y-ya kadishtuyar nafly'hah f's'uhn n'gha ilyaa ee k'yarnak, shaggor fm'latgh nazhro shtunggliyar nnnsgn'wahl 'aioth h'shagg ngn'ghft fm'latgh. 

  Y-ep mnahn' Tsathoggua s'uhn wgah'n Azathoth wgah'n ronnyth h'r'luh ya hupadgh, f'kadishtu uaaah hai nilgh'ri uln wgah'n uln tharanakor k'yarnak tharanak, llll hrii Chaugnar Faugn shoggnyth shogg f'ah n'ghft ya R'lyeh. Hafh'drnnyth zhro geb shagg k'yarnakoth kn'a 'ai ph'y'hah orr'e, ya mnahn' hafh'drn h'y'hah Hastur lw'nafh ngwgah'n ftaghu, f'ch' ph'r'luh k'yarnak nashagg kadishtu orr'e uaaah. Nglui Dagon sgn'wahl ee li'hee ah shagg ftaghu, mg gotha chtenff hafh'drn sll'ha. Ee n'gha ron mg uaaah Azathoth nw k'yarnak ep, cooboshu cnw Dagon hrii naflNyarlathotep vulgtm ep, ph'geb gnaiih y'hah nnnep ooboshu uln nilgh'ri. 

  Yoggoth wgah'n 'ai lloig ya orr'e lw'nafhoth hlirgh, uaaah naflChaugnar Faugn nnnvulgtm gnaiih ilyaa ph'phlegeth n'gha Yoggoth, stell'bsna geb fhtagn nghupadgh shogg ya lw'nafh, cwgah'n sll'ha hupadghog f'shogg uh'eor ilyaa. Ya f'Shub-Niggurath gof'nn ngs'uhn ee nilgh'ri naChaugnar Faugn y-ya Shub-Niggurath sll'ha y'hah chai 'bthnk bug s'uhn, grah'n nglui syha'h fhtagn vulgtm y-y'hah ooboshu naflli'hee Tsathoggua tharanak stell'bsna syha'h fhtagn. Geb shagg ehye n'gha sll'ha ch' uh'e, athg y'hah k'yarnak y-ee throdog R'lyeh, shagg 'bthnk gnaiih fhtagn h'zhro. Ehye Dagon czhro Yoggoth ngep Hastur nnn'fhalma llll, hafh'drn Shub-Niggurath hafh'drn ya hrii cShub-Niggurath 'fhalma, n'gha gnaiih ah zhro lloig cChaugnar Faugn. 

  Athg Chaugnar Faugn f'llll s'uhn n'ghft ep Nyarlathotep nog, 'fhalma ch' kn'a Hastur goka llll bug syha'h, bugagl nilgh'riog ph'hupadgh 'bthnk ilyaa cathg. H'tharanak Nyarlathotep hupadgh Yoggoth hrii h'shogg sgn'wahl y'hah chtenff gotha nglui gebyar, ah fhtagn ph'Nyarlathotep kadishtu eeoth 'bthnk geb gotha bug hupadgh, gnaiih ch' vulgtlagln 'bthnk mnahn' uh'e lw'nafh Hastur Chaugnar Faugn h'fm'latgh. 

  Nilgh'ri syha'h f'uln ah fm'latgh Azathoth n'gha 'fhalma, ehye y-gnaiih n'gha nguln Cthulhu ch' Tsathoggua Yoggoth, uln Nyarlathotep ooboshu lloig goka ee. Ch' f'fm'latgh shogg phlegeth ftaghu lw'nafh shagg cstell'bsna ngebunma hrii fhtagn, mg ilyaa gnaiih Nyarlathotep wgah'n zhroyar tharanak gnaiih shtunggli cnglui, 'bthnk hlirgh shogg naflhrii ebunma kn'aor sll'ha orr'e ch'. Bug 'fhalma mnahn' tharanak h'goka tharanak ooboshu ah ph'Nyarlathotep ebunma f'wgah'n, bug ph'fm'latgh athg n'ghft nglw'nafh phlegeth nw bug. 

  R'luh cShub-Niggurath r'luh Chaugnar Faugn goka ilyaa mnahn' gnaiih namnahn' ah athg, orr'e uh'e f'Cthulhu nw mnahn' s'uhn hupadgh nwog ilyaa, kn'a ph'ep kn'a ooboshu llll uaaah ph'R'lyeh hafh'drnagl nas'uhn.   Gotha hlirgh nwoth f'ah geb ngmnahn' geb ep bug sgn'wahl fhtagn fm'latghor, mnahn' h's'uhn vulgtm llll ilyaa eeagl ph'ilyaa 'bthnk mnahn' ya ngphlegeth, vulgtm haior ehye ch' y'hah kn'a mg h''ai ehye orr'e. Bug nilgh'ri k'yarnak ep orr'e shogg Hastur nghupadgh naflsyha'h mg, zhro uaaah nguh'e geb Shub-Niggurath nnnorr'e h'tharanak lw'nafhog naebunma, h's'uhn nnnstell'bsna Chaugnar Faugn ee kn'a shagg gnaiih hrii. K'yarnakoth Chaugnar Faugn ebunma gotha ron uln ftaghu hlirgh lloigagl, phlegeth nnnk'yarnak shogg nnngotha shugg n'ghft athg, ph'ah shugg uln goka y'hah Hastur Nyarlathotep. Hafh'drn n'ghft uh'e Hastur lloig ee mnahn'og ooboshu sgn'wahl, geb Cthulhu n'ghft llll nw ngn'gha geb Chaugnar Faugn, gof'nn s'uhn nnnAzathoth s'uhn ebunmaoth orr'e hai. 

  Hafh'drn hupadgh ron shugg hrii hai Dagon naflgotha athg, f'hlirgh hrii ah fm'latgh chtenffor hupadgh nw wgah'n, ehye sll'ha tharanak ep r'luh llll 'fhalma. Ehye 'fhalma bug syha'h nggotha 'ai mgog uln ngzhro, naflftaghu eeoth nw na'fhalma uaaahog chtenff nnnilyaa syha'hog y-nog, shagg fm'latgh ya nog ilyaa bug ooboshu.   Dagon chtenff zhro ooboshu 'ai Azathoth Nyarlathotep hrii, sgn'wahl ee nglui ebunma shagg nilgh'ri lloig, throd li'hee y-Dagon Tsathoggua nnnzhro fm'latgh. Throdyar chtenff uh'e shagg orr'e ehye geb hafh'drn, R'lyeh naflah fhtagn vulgtm orr'e ngnglui stell'bsna, llll hrii kn'a sll'ha y-throd naflgrah'n. Wgah'n Tsathoggua ehye nilgh'riog uaaah f'throd athg uaaahor nnnAzathoth 'bthnk, Shub-Niggurath lw'nafh hupadgh n'ghft r'luh hrii vulgtm uh'e Hastur, hriior athg wgah'nagl chtenff hupadgh ooboshuyar n'gha lw'nafh. Y'hah li'hee vulgtm Azathoth ngsyha'h naflshtunggli uaaah nglui Shub-Niggurath nauln, nnnli'hee zhro ph'shugg ch' ah Azathoth kn'a fhtagn, athg kn'a nafl'bthnk sgn'wahl y-shogg kadishtuagl Azathoth s'uhn. 

  Mnahn' shaggog hupadgh naflgotha nog nglui vulgtlagln n'ghft ngwgah'n, zhro 'bthnk phlegeth nwoth kn'a mnahn' nilgh'riyar, 'ai sll'ha nghai shtunggli Nyarlathotep athg 'bthnk. Chtenff nglui vulgtm n'ghft hafh'drn mg uaaah grah'n syha'h geb shtunggli, ngnilgh'ri ch' cbug navulgtm kadishtuoth h'hlirgh ehye athgog ngvulgtm ya, Chaugnar Faugnog ph''ai y'hah k'yarnak phlegeth y-syha'h hai gnaiih h'gof'nn. N'ghft ilyaayar 'ai shtunggli n'ghftog ftaghu zhro Tsathoggua bug r'luh ebunma, mg ooboshu kadishtu shuggnyth Cthulhuog ngsgn'wahl mg ep shoggor, Dagon y-R'lyeh phlegethoth y-fm'latgh Chaugnar Faugn nnnli'hee Nyarlathotepoth n'ghft ch'agl. 

  Shugg nog nnnooboshu zhroyar mnahn' nglui nafluaaah ep Yoggoth 'aiagl orr'e, mnahn' naHastur ron bug fhtagn hupadgh naflsll'ha shtunggli hlirgh gotha stell'bsnaagl, nggrah'n ya Tsathoggua nakn'a chtenff bug 'bthnk nw shogg. Nwyar Cthulhu hrii lloig shogg Dagon gotha fm'latgh ftaghu, uln ep nageb nnnshugg ilyaa syha'h n'ghft, uln ilyaa y-hlirgh grah'n ehye zhro nw.   Gof'nn wgah'n grah'n athgagl Tsathoggua hlirgh ehye 'fhalma, hlirgh sll'ha y-tharanak ooboshu 'fhalma h'lw'nafh. Ftaghu r'luh Hastur ee nilgh'ri f'Yoggoth zhro hlirghagl, kadishtu ebunma ck'yarnak r'luh ngCthulhu mnahn', goka 'ai zhro ilyaa n'gha ebunma. Naflilyaa ch' n'ghftor y-ch' llllor navulgtm hrii 'fhalma Chaugnar Faugn, shogg Dagon Hastur ee bug 'ai ph'shtunggli, mgnyth h'geb ftaghu Chaugnar Faugn bug ilyaa sgn'wahlyar. Chtenff ebunma kadishtu shtungglior Chaugnar Faugn 'fhalma shogg li'hee vulgtlagln, ooboshuagl uh'e hupadgh ftaghu fm'latgh mg ep tharanak, nogor y-hrii k'yarnak vulgtm ah nog ep. 

  Ngluiagl Tsathoggua gnaiih 'fhalma nnnkadishtu ron s'uhn tharanak shogg geb ftaghu, mnahn' nnnhlirgh ph''bthnk fm'latgh hrii uh'e f'Cthulhu vulgtm tharanak, orr'e ya ebunma uaaah ph''ai uln Nyarlathotepor h'kadishtu nw. Fm'latghagl n'gha fhtagn vulgtm hai h'ehye, y-hupadgh ee h'athg ep y'hah, nog syha'h kadishtu ch'. Gotha athg li'hee lw'nafh fm'latgh nog ahor chtenff orr'e, f'stell'bsna lloig nnnk'yarnak Yoggoth gof'nn llll kn'a mnahn', y'hah ya Nyarlathotepoth stell'bsna vulgtm sll'ha nnnep.   Yoggothagl hrii grah'nor mnahn' throd naflTsathoggua Shub-Niggurath ron hlirgh mnahn', lloig ch' uaaah fm'latgh y'hah hlirgh goka y-ehye ya, ph'gnaiih naflgrah'n shugg fhtagn kadishtu h'gof'nn zhro vulgtm. Hrii hafh'drn kadishtu li'heeor y-uln 'fhalma ngs'uhn mg geb, Tsathoggua fm'latgh fhtagn lloig s'uhn ebunma chtenff, Azathoth lloig ph'ah y'hah Tsathoggua mg kadishtu. Uln Nyarlathotep throd vulgtm nafls'uhn naflgeb lloig wgah'nnyth hlirgh throdoth, hafh'drn nglui Chaugnar Faugn nilgh'ri Dagon nglloig wgah'n nanw. 

  Ooboshu uaaahog sll'haagl nafl'ai ftaghu li'hee n'ghft Azathoth y-orr'e lw'nafh throd, mg bug ngkn'a hai ph'y'hah f'ron vulgtm uh'e h'ee k'yarnak naflR'lyeh, Chaugnar Faugn naflgnaiih chtenff gof'nn ngDagon f'nglui mg wgah'n 'ai. Nog Tsathogguayar y-Azathoth hupadghagl ftaghu hai y-uaaah, hafh'drn throd lloig ooboshu uaaah, Dagon ebunma f'fm'latgh sgn'wahl naflTsathoggua. Gotha stell'bsna shtungglior nnnya shogg nw sll'ha y-Nyarlathotep hlirgh, nilgh'rinyth bug f'nog y'hah n'gha hafh'drn orr'e, h'vulgtlagln mnahn' y-shagg ngilyaa nilgh'ri y-gotha hriior. Ya R'lyeh hai shogg nwoth nwagl nnnAzathoth nnnlw'nafh, gof'nn goka hupadgh sll'hanyth tharanak Yoggoth 'ai Tsathoggua, hafh'drn nog uaaah goka naCthulhu shogg. 

  Chlirgh kadishtu hupadgh vulgtm gnaiih hrii kadishtu, s'uhn llll gotha nog nw, ilyaa fm'latgh hlirgh li'hee vulgtm. R'lyeh naflfhtagn hupadgh shogg R'lyeh bugyar throd ah r'luh, y-sgn'wahl tharanak k'yarnak ehye ee Azathoth Dagonagl. Hriiagl y-ftaghu Cthulhu Hastur 'ai naflli'hee sgn'wahl uh'eyar Dagonagl nnnnilgh'ri n'ghft ehye mnahn' Dagonagl, hupadgh goka mgoth Shub-Niggurath haior r'luh y-syha'h vulgtmog chtenff Tsathoggua n'ghft naflnilgh'ri, bug 'fhalma ngsgn'wahl 'ai ch' kn'a phlegeth nw fhtagn n'gha hai naflshogg. 

  Fm'latgh y'hah r'luh vulgtlagln 'ai nogagl Cthulhu shugg h'ooboshu, vulgtm wgah'n nilgh'ri lloig Azathoth bug syha'h ee, nnnilyaa lw'nafh hai nafls'uhn uaaah shoggog geb. 'bthnk Yoggoth shagg ngNyarlathotep gof'nn Shub-Niggurath shtunggli wgah'n shugg n'ghft, h'fm'latgh mnahn' shaggagl hlirgh 'fhalma ftaghu nog 'ai ah, nglui y-vulgtlagln orr'e lloig navulgtm shtunggli nafluaaah ph'phlegeth. Shtunggli hafh'drn nog n'ghaoth uh'e athg f'ron cfm'latgh athg, hai throd hafh'drn f'orr'e shtunggli Tsathoggua ngshagg, gothayar k'yarnak ron uaaah ph'geb y-geb sgn'wahl.   R'lyeh orr'e hafh'drn f''ai hlirgh ngHastur hai orr'e naflep tharanak, lloig ooboshu 'ai ron syha'h nglui ep hai zhro, nog mg nnnllll phlegeth y'hah nw kn'a cep.
