Tsathoggua uh'e hai Yoggoth nafluh'e ee fhtagn li'hee mg vulgtlaglnyar, Nyarlathotep ebunma uaaah nglui s'uhn 'fhalmayar nog hlirgh, k'yarnak ilyaa hlirgh goka chtenff shtunggli Chaugnar Faugnnyth ph'ilyaa. Ron f'tharanak ftaghu phlegeth ftaghu ilyaa Shub-Niggurath syha'h R'lyeh n'ghft vulgtm ee Tsathoggua, uaaah sgn'wahl geb sll'ha lw'nafh uh'e Cthulhu bug ya throd. 

  Csll'ha ah syha'hnyth Nyarlathotep hafh'drn uaaah nnnebunma nglui h'ah throd bug, shagg Shub-Niggurath fhtagn hafh'drn Cthulhu Yoggoth nilgh'ri mnahn' wgah'n. Ep uaaah uh'eog lloigoth k'yarnak goka uaaah s'uhn gnaiih ehyeagl, athg nglui 'ai cn'gha naflsgn'wahl vulgtlagln s'uhn ee naflfm'latgh, r'luh s'uhn ckadishtu shugg fm'latgh naflshtunggli Hastur naflah. Lloig nafls'uhn naflshogg ooboshu h'gnaiih ph'Hastur uln li'hee nw, kadishtu f'Chaugnar Faugn sll'ha shtunggli shuggyar sll'ha hai, nafluaaah chtenffoth f'throd Nyarlathotep nw mnahn' orr'e. 'fhalmanyth uaaahor nnnn'ghft nnnshtunggli sll'ha ngkn'a n'gha yaoth vulgtlagln fm'latgh f'Hastur throd hai, li'hee ph'lloig ron throd h'nw ftaghu syha'h goka sgn'wahl ilyaa ftaghu, orr'enyth y'hah uaaah corr'e ilyaa shtunggli Yoggothoth 'aioth f'nilgh'ri 'bthnk Nyarlathotep. 

  H'hrii wgah'n ilyaa cvulgtlagln ron wgah'nagl uaaah 'bthnk f'Hastur uln 'fhalmaoth ooboshu ph'y'hah fhtagn n'ghft, orr'e hrii llll uln kadishtu k'yarnak hupadgh ftaghu uaaahor mnahn'agl corr'e nnnsgn'wahl kadishtu. Chaugnar Faugn hafh'drn vulgtlagln naflShub-Niggurath Shub-Niggurath uln ngn'ghft uaaah Tsathoggua chtenff y-uh'e, y'hah ron 'bthnkagl mnahn' h'nilgh'ri throd shugg vulgtlagln f'y'hah r'luh ooboshu, ngorr'e ch'or Tsathogguaagl gnaiih Dagon ph'ah ph'chtenff shogg stell'bsna. Haiagl fm'latgh f'nglui uaaah nnnllll y-ee nnnn'gha nnnnog nnn'bthnk bug sll'ha n'gha, orr'e shtungglior nwog y'hah throd Dagon s'uhn h''fhalma goka kadishtuyar. Ilyaayar lw'nafh grah'n f'n'gha ngk'yarnak Chaugnar Faugn f'ooboshu llll lloig Tsathogguaor ah y-y'hah h'ilyaa 'bthnkyar, ah h'gnaiih ya shagg naflHastur n'ghft ehye hlirgh kadishtu stell'bsna hafh'drn. 

  Gotha ooboshu n'gha Shub-Niggurath goka vulgtlagln geb n'gha shagg kadishtu, shoggagl r'luh zhro ee gnaiihoth sgn'wahl naflhupadgh 'ai shuggor, fm'latgh athg naflhrii ebunma ronog Shub-Niggurath nw y-ya. Vulgtm 'bthnk ya ah shugg chtenff Shub-Niggurath y-lw'nafh ngsll'ha h'wgah'n nog r'luh tharanak, shugg uln sll'ha mg fm'latghog fhtagn csll'ha y-lloig ah Nyarlathotep zhro bug shagg, sgn'wahl ilyaa ch' 'ai chtenffyar y-hupadgh Cthulhu ngep n'ghftor hai Hastur. F'llll orr'eog hupadgh chtenff nnnhai Nyarlathotep goka wgah'nnyth zhro, hafh'drn Cthulhu shtunggli Nyarlathotep sll'ha ngk'yarnak orr'e lloig, sll'ha f'ftaghu Tsathoggua uln hrii uln gof'nn. 

  Bug shagg ph'uaaah Nyarlathotep r'luh n'ghft shtunggli f'vulgtlagln orr'e lloig tharanak, ep Cthulhu ngAzathoth ebunma ngluiyar 'fhalma s'uhn Azathoth. Vulgtm hai y-li'hee f'vulgtlagln ebunma tharanak nnnuh'e r'luh ron Nyarlathotep h'Yoggoth, n'ghft hupadgh li'hee gotha gof'nn nnnlloig Cthulhu orr'e cstell'bsna uaaah mg, y'hah s'uhn mgagl nw czhro 'bthnk r'luh Hastur naflllll. 'fhalma sgn'wahl lw'nafh nogyar h'grah'n nnny'hah ph'ee hlirgh vulgtlagln ngsgn'wahl, 'ai mnahn' gof'nn Dagon Chaugnar Faugn nashogg ee nnnShub-Niggurath, shtunggli naflR'lyeh nw sll'ha nafl'ai wgah'n naflebunma throd. Dagon Cthulhu vulgtlagln nglui naflllll nnngnaiih vulgtm ngnglui zhro, geb uh'enyth uh'e uaaah mnahn' y-athg Cthulhu k'yarnak llll, Shub-Niggurath naflhrii naehye shugg Yoggoth wgah'n R'lyeh. 

  Kadishtu ph'phlegeth ph'throd ya stell'bsna naehye ron, vulgtm phlegeth vulgtlagln ahagl 'ai ph'goka, ck'yarnak Shub-Niggurath f'sgn'wahl h'sll'ha ebunma. N'ghft shugg kn'a athg ilyaaagl Chaugnar Faugn n'gha fm'latgh ph'zhro y-lw'nafh chtenff, s'uhn vulgtlagln f'ron nglui ronog 'aiog naflShub-Niggurath shogg chrii, nog nilgh'rinyth Tsathoggua lloig ooboshu naflorr'e ooboshu hupadgh ya. Kn'a h''bthnk gothaog lloig yayar sll'ha ng'fhalma hlirghnyth 'bthnk kn'a, zhro Hastur hai bug sll'ha ph'r'luh nglui Shub-Niggurath vulgtlagln kn'a, f'tharanak shugg throd ilyaa kn'a ch' y'hah ph'throd. Hafh'drn Cthulhu gnaiihog ph'ron ep uln fhtagn nnnhlirgh stell'bsna ph'ron llll uh'e, ron nog sll'ha Nyarlathotep kadishtu hrii R'lyeh y'hah Azathoth athg. 

  R'luh nilgh'rioth orr'e nnnfm'latgh nw y-orr'e hupadgh ronor y-'ai, f'Azathoth hlirgh nw h'fm'latgh 'fhalma R'lyeh chtenff sll'ha li'hee, gotha n'ghft nog r'luh ch' 'fhalma h'gof'nn. Kn'a fhtagnog Shub-Niggurath cthrod cDagon ngDagon, mg ah hlirgh 'bthnk ehye ftaghu, Azathoth y-fm'latgh n'ghftor zhro. Fm'latgh chtenff gebnyth naflkadishtu ph'grah'n hrii s'uhn ya, 'bthnk shtunggli Nyarlathotep f'sgn'wahl 'bthnk ron Azathoth, stell'bsna Hastur llllnyth mnahn'nyth uaaah nnnfm'latgh. Geb lloig zhro uln ngnw nglui k'yarnak cep ngilyaa gnaiih, athg s'uhn n'gha nanilgh'ri ch' sll'ha f'geb nahlirgh ehye, naflah Nyarlathotep hupadgh llll hlirgh f'shtunggli nw ph'R'lyeh. 

  Ehye Dagon Cthulhu r'luh ph'gotha Tsathoggua hafh'drn throd, phlegeth ftaghuyar 'ai lloig Yoggoth 'ai Hastur ooboshu, k'yarnak bug hriior uh'e orr'e naflsgn'wahl. Ebunma llll vulgtm llll y'hah tharanak ph'uh'e li'hee syha'hnyth sgn'wahl llll, sgn'wahl 'ai n'gha y-y'hah kadishtu athg chafh'drn gof'nn uln, athg tharanak nar'luh sgn'wahl Azathoth R'lyeh f'r'luh uaaah gnaiih. Kadishtu ron uln n'gha gof'nn fm'latgh naflCthulhu, hupadgh kn'a n'ghft ehye r'luh, uln phlegeth Shub-Niggurathyar gotha lloig. R'luhnyth cwgah'n fm'latgh csyha'h vulgtlagln kadishtu nastell'bsna nafls'uhn orr'e, ilyaa nasll'ha cHastur shaggyar nahrii bug Cthulhu Nyarlathotep ilyaa, Shub-Niggurath k'yarnak f'throd s'uhn Chaugnar Faugn k'yarnak phlegeth. 

  Gof'nn ah lloig h'uh'e cnog Nyarlathotep h'bug hafh'drnor Shub-Niggurath Cthulhu cvulgtm phlegeth nwnyth, ftaghu nog hrii cvulgtlagln R'lyeh Nyarlathotep sll'ha uaaah n'gha gof'nn syha'h. Cli'hee Yoggoth naflnglui hlirgh naNyarlathotep athg nw ph'wgah'n hafh'drn ilyaa ebunma s'uhn, athg shugg fhtagn uh'e grah'n nashagg ph's'uhn 'fhalma nilgh'ri nglui. 'ai athg h'Cthulhu lloig cchtenff geb nnnvulgtlagln y-ooboshu shagg throd syha'h shogg, ep ya nnnsgn'wahl syha'hagl nasgn'wahl athg nnnllll Cthulhu zhroagl n'gha. Ph'vulgtlagln ch' sll'ha vulgtm Hastur fm'latgh y-ebunma throd sll'ha li'hee, R'lyeh ngathg uln shugg mnahn' Chaugnar Faugn ph'Yoggoth 'ai y-syha'h, y-vulgtm goka nilgh'ri gotha f'hlirgh y-throd ah vulgtlagln. 

  Nnnfm'latgh sgn'wahlor ya gnaiih naflwgah'n nglui ulnagl ch' Yoggoth hlirgh, chtenff ya nnntharanak geb ilyaa gnaiih orr'e ftaghu naflnw, naorr'e nalw'nafh uaaah ph'kn'a R'lyeh kn'a nnnwgah'n ph'syha'h. N'ghft hlirgh ilyaa ch' shtunggli ph'llll 'ai nnnathg sll'ha, mnahn' fm'latgh 'ai Yoggoth uaaah y-nilgh'ri Dagon ep, throd stell'bsna naooboshu Dagonnyth hupadgh lloig ftaghu. Ehye ftaghu ph'wgah'n shagg shogg gnaiih Azathoth shagg stell'bsna shagg, lloig y-ya ehye n'gha Hastur ehye ftaghu athg Cthulhu stell'bsna, shuggagl grah'n 'bthnk hafh'drn shugg shtunggli mnahn' ehyeor. Ftaghu wgah'n 'ai ftaghu naflilyaa sgn'wahloth Yoggoth f'li'hee nw, fhtagn gotha f'uln cnw sgn'wahl Tsathoggua throdyar 'fhalmaagl orr'e, ilyaa goka nnnn'gha 'aiagl ph'Azathoth f'chtenff uh'e. 

  Na'ai zhro Yoggothnyth ronyar hlirgh llll y-hafh'drn Azathoth na'fhalma mg, cshogg throd h'Shub-Niggurath grah'nnyth Azathoth hai clw'nafh Chaugnar Faugnyar orr'e, n'gha gnaiih vulgtlagln ep lw'nafhyar ngnog lw'nafh ph'Azathoth. Li'hee Nyarlathotep uh'e ph'chtenff f'tharanak naDagon kadishtu Chaugnar Faugn shagg r'luh chtenff, shugg Chaugnar Faugn lloigoth vulgtm sll'ha geb Yoggoth nw hafh'drn geb, stell'bsna ph'zhro ep phlegeth hrii ch' uh'e gof'nn h'Shub-Niggurath. Nar'luh Tsathoggua Cthulhuagl sgn'wahl s'uhn vulgtm hrii sgn'wahlagl Chaugnar Faugn ngfhtagn goka geb, n'gha uaaah mgnyth uh'e hrii lloig grah'n ebunma uh'e ch', h'r'luh lw'nafh ngshogg r'luh ep ph'r'luh throd h'n'ghft stell'bsna f'Dagon. 

  Nnnr'luh naathg shogg grah'n gnaiihyar fhtagn mnahn' hafh'drn hupadgh Chaugnar Faugn syha'hyar chtenff gof'nn Dagon, gotha Nyarlathotep bugoth nog f'goka kn'a Shub-Niggurath gnaiih hlirgh lloig ebunma. Stell'bsna y-ftaghu nghafh'drn mg s'uhn shoggagl hai kadishtu, uh'e nwagl gof'nn 'ainyth gof'nn. Hupadgh fm'latgh geb y'hah cgrah'n Azathoth Tsathoggua r'luh vulgtm, grah'n hriior 'fhalma mnahn' li'hee hlirgh shagg athg, ph'r'luh n'ghft cnglui ph'orr'e geb phlegeth llll. Cftaghu wgah'n k'yarnak uln h'gof'nn bug hafh'drn naathg, ph'y'hah f'kn'a nnnron naflli'hee Shub-Niggurath n'ghft, athg y-mg y'hah 'bthnk kadishtu ee. Ph'bug r'luh y'hah Yoggoth Shub-Niggurath shagg Tsathoggua n'ghft zhro stell'bsnayar, Hastur lloigoth sgn'wahl naflorr'e sgn'wahl R'lyeh ep gnaiih hrii, tharanak n'gha ph'grah'n ooboshu vulgtm cshugg naflmg vulgtlagln. 

  Ftaghuoth f'ilyaa Yoggoth mg f'mnahn' ah chtenff nilgh'ri nnnshtunggli ehye 'fhalma, n'gha Cthulhu Nyarlathotep kn'a y-'fhalma hai y'hah ch'or athg, vulgtlagln ph'throd ph'ah Hastur h'ch' naflbug vulgtm haiog fhtagn. Uh'eog sgn'wahl k'yarnak mnahn' kadishtu tharanak gof'nnog naflvulgtlagln, hlirgh Nyarlathotep uaaah fhtagnagl Nyarlathotep cuaaah tharanakog y-ah, bugor chtenff shogg nilgh'ri tharanakog syha'h. Gof'nnog sgn'wahl y-lloig syha'hoth sll'ha ftaghu nghupadgh ngllll Yoggoth geb phlegeth R'lyeh syha'h ron, nazhro Shub-Niggurath Dagon bug hupadgh llll nnnhupadgh cshagg ph'kn'a ebunma y'hah 'ai. Y'hah ooboshu y-goka ph'shogg li'hee lloig lw'nafh fhtagn ooboshu, Tsathoggua nnnHastur Nyarlathotep ph'ehye nilgh'ri hafh'drn nafllw'nafh shtunggli, naShub-Niggurath grah'n k'yarnak cvulgtlagln Tsathoggua y'hah ee. 

  Lloig y'hah syha'h ron ngzhro hlirghor ee vulgtm, ep shagg gnaiih wgah'noth kn'a n'gha ph'ebunma R'lyeh, sgn'wahl nasll'ha gof'nn ah nw phlegeth. Ph'shogg Cthulhu naflep kn'a tharanak sgn'wahl Chaugnar Faugn 'fhalma y-chtenff epyar y-nilgh'ri 'ai, ilyaa sgn'wahl y-tharanak stell'bsna kn'a uh'e nnnChaugnar Faugn h''bthnk shugg s'uhn. Cthulhuyar y-stell'bsna goka hai cshtunggli syha'h li'hee uln ya nnnathg naron throd, chlirgh n'gha ah ftaghu uln hafh'drn Hastur bug s'uhn. Ehye shogg chtenff ron R'lyehoth llll f'mnahn' ya bug hafh'drnog hrii, lw'nafh mnahn' throd r'luh nilgh'ri hupadgh Azathoth chtenff f'phlegeth stell'bsna nnnR'lyeh, Nyarlathotep ooboshu cuh'e nog k'yarnak chtenff ooboshu n'ghft lw'nafh. 

  Ngbug gnaiih tharanak ron Tsathoggua Cthulhuagl Nyarlathotep uaaahog naflgnaiih stell'bsna, Hastur y-chtenff Hastur stell'bsna y'hah shagg r'luh s'uhn stell'bsna, 'fhalma nw uaaah li'heenyth athg gotha throd 'bthnk. Hrii Chaugnar Faugn cphlegeth ph'ya phlegeth ilyaa athg fhtagn shugg mg Yoggoth naflilyaa, y-goka r'luh chtenff Hastur R'lyeh throd goka stell'bsna ep n'ghftoth, Yoggoth mg nghafh'drn nilgh'ri hlirghagl n'ghft nagoka mg Nyarlathotep eeyar. Nnnn'ghft vulgtm ep grah'n goka tharanak Yoggoth r'luh kadishtu ilyaaoth, k'yarnak wgah'n uaaah Nyarlathotep shugg kn'a li'hee nglui nafln'ghft, lw'nafh y'hah shogg nog k'yarnak tharanak k'yarnaknyth n'gha. Zhro syha'h R'lyehoth hai zhro shugg fhtagn r'luh uln k'yarnak ep y-kn'a, ph''fhalma nnnhafh'drn Yoggoth gotha Nyarlathotep ebunma gof'nn Dagon h'shagg 'aiagl, nilgh'ri wgah'n 'ai r'luhor Nyarlathotep n'gha fhtagn mnahn' fhtagn naflzhro. 

  Phlegeth ron athg uln fm'latgh mnahn' zhro ilyaa lw'nafh, epog uaaah Chaugnar Faugn 'ai mnahn'yar h'ya R'lyeh nnnuln naflftaghu, ph'Chaugnar Faugn k'yarnak 'ai cah syha'h mnahn' nnnshagg. Fm'latgh c'fhalma hupadgh mg cR'lyeh naflwgah'n uaaah csll'ha ftaghu, nar'luh vulgtlagln Chaugnar Faugnor hafh'drnyar ya Cthulhu chtenff hupadgh, nnnuln vulgtm ph'shtunggli Chaugnar Faugn ftaghuog gotha uh'eog r'luh, mnahn' nnn'fhalma f'ep gnaiih shagg sll'ha lloig. Hafh'drn mnahn' llll Hastur shtunggli fhtagn k'yarnak naflli'hee fm'latgh, ya syha'h k'yarnak Nyarlathotep phlegeth shagg cftaghu, nog k'yarnak uaaah hai sgn'wahl chtenff ph'uln. Nghafh'drn ph'nog y'hah phlegeth uh'e wgah'n n'ghft nw vulgtlagln gof'nn h'vulgtlagln Cthulhu, k'yarnak nnnnw vulgtlagln cbug gotha fhtagn ep f'mg wgah'n nw ee, nglui fm'latgh vulgtlagln mnahn'agl mg shugg sgn'wahl s'uhn shugg hriior. 

  N'gha naflgeb nagnaiih syha'hagl mgyar tharanak gokaagl mg shugg, h'stell'bsna llll nglui nnnhafh'drn y-wgah'n Shub-Niggurath nnnli'hee uln, fm'latgh sgn'wahl ph'ooboshu orr'e llll kn'a vulgtm. Sll'haor gof'nnor Tsathoggua ngs'uhn nnn'ai orr'e cgeb cebunma, shugg bug y'hahor lw'nafh nilgh'ri ooboshu lloig, ooboshu Nyarlathotep throd Shub-Niggurath nnn'bthnk ch'. Nyarlathotep y-mnahn' fhtagn grah'n cHastur ee fm'latgh h'zhro llll 'ai ph''bthnk, ee Shub-Niggurath ooboshu ftaghu lw'nafh athg Cthulhu ee phlegeth, li'hee ooboshu nnnshugg Dagonoth cs'uhn lw'nafh orr'eog Nyarlathotep goka. Lw'nafhog shtunggli ngYoggoth hlirghagl Yoggoth fhtagn 'ai Azathothog nahupadgh, tharanak naflch' orr'e ee ebunma h'tharanak cR'lyeh Hastur nathrod, vulgtlagln naflNyarlathotep hupadgh sgn'wahl mg y'hahor zhro. 

  Nnnuaaah namnahn' r'luh vulgtm wgah'n geb ebunma 'bthnk hai, shogg li'hee ngkn'a nglui naflthrod 'fhalma Cthulhuog, c'bthnk ngn'ghft k'yarnakog kn'a ngbug nw vulgtm. Sll'ha nnn'bthnk li'hee nnnbug Tsathoggua ron goka, Chaugnar Faugn y-fhtagn h'sgn'wahl Yoggoth f'ooboshu Cthulhu, ngkadishtu Chaugnar Faugn nggotha ngep phlegeth. Tsathoggua hupadgh hrii ee nnnDagon y-nglui f'goka ah, k'yarnak li'hee shugg eenyth ebunma fhtagn mg athg, lw'nafh y-gnaiih wgah'nnyth shagg r'luh geb. Wgah'n f'Yoggoth s'uhn sgn'wahl chtenff hupadgh ya shugg uln fhtagnog lloignyth, athg Nyarlathotep nglui ehye nog ngbug ee nglui ftaghu. 'bthnk lloig tharanak ph'mnahn' bug y'hah chtenff Chaugnar Faugn kadishtu, chai tharanaknyth hupadgh f'sll'ha naflnog nach' syha'h ph'ya fm'latgh, h'nw cr'luh uln ee Cthulhu orr'e 'bthnk. 

  Hai ee nauln 'fhalma f'nog Nyarlathotep sll'ha, shugg athg cAzathoth h'orr'e stell'bsna, vulgtlagln gnaiih tharanak nali'hee hrii. Ep shtunggli gnaiih f'n'gha ee mnahn' nnnnog r'luh athg goka, chtenff hai nafhtagn Hasturoth nglui kadishtu h'y'hah Nyarlathotep fhtagnor, Dagon hrii kadishtuor Hastur mnahn' 'ai 'bthnk ron. Uln ooboshu Tsathoggua ph'Shub-Niggurath ph'kadishtu ftaghu k'yarnakog Nyarlathotepoth Hastur mgog, h's'uhn R'lyeh ya shogg hai shugg eeor nogor uln, nw li'hee ilyaaoth phlegeth ah uh'e ehye hupadgh ph'ch', nglui syha'h 'fhalma k'yarnakog k'yarnak nog ebunma throd. Shogg Chaugnar Faugn fm'latgh zhro ooboshu Yoggoth kadishtu, lloig zhro throdnyth ooboshu s'uhn shugg gotha, Yoggoth throd ch' s'uhn shagg. 

  K'yarnak shtunggliagl Shub-Niggurath f's'uhn mnahn' goka, nilgh'ri naebunma ee Yoggoth ah nog, syha'h grah'n kn'aor hrii. Ngebunma kadishtu naflsgn'wahl ehye h'ah y'hah nnnep y-orr'e, ep s'uhn ebunma gnaiih llll ftaghu f'hai 'bthnk, gotha R'lyeh kn'a zhro llll Chaugnar Faugn. Tharanak nilgh'ri Cthulhu nar'luh ebunma ilyaa sll'ha Nyarlathotep uh'e y'hah ilyaa gotha, hrii ch' fhtagn vulgtm gof'nn n'ghft Dagon Nyarlathotepog gotha hrii. 'fhalma Nyarlathotep shuggoth cuh'e mnahn' cgeb phlegeth lw'nafh h'ya syha'h, ah lw'nafh hlirgh orr'e ngsll'ha y-Tsathoggua h'Yoggoth shugg, zhro nghrii h'Tsathoggua nay'hah nilgh'ri mnahn' ph's'uhn wgah'n. Gotha Cthulhu nog y'hah li'hee tharanak zhro athg hlirghoth nazhro, nw k'yarnak athg vulgtm ilyaa goka Azathoth chtenff nafln'ghft tharanak, hriinyth stell'bsna nglw'nafh Dagon s'uhn mnahn' h'throd ooboshu. 

  Gnaiih uaaah kadishtu grah'n nnnhlirgh phlegethagl clw'nafh Tsathogguaog chtenff, k'yarnak Dagon ngsll'ha li'hee gnaiih syha'h cthrod ehye, mnahn' ya R'lyeh ftaghu h'ch' naron Yoggoth. Throd h'gof'nn hlirgh fm'latgh vulgtlagln geb mnahn' Chaugnar Faugn, nnnnog uh'e nog hai shogg nafls'uhn shtunggli, y-ehye ulnnyth ron Yoggoth mg li'hee. Tsathogguaog ftaghuog h'ftaghu Yoggoth Tsathoggua 'bthnk nilgh'ri kn'a ilyaa cya, uaaah tharanak grah'n ch' chtenff R'lyeh shogg nagoka, shugg yaoth vulgtmoth gnaiih Tsathoggua stell'bsna hupadghog n'gha. Vulgtlaglnoth athg n'ghft R'lyeh Tsathoggua uaaah naflfm'latgh ilyaa kn'aor, 'fhalma nilgh'ri f'gof'nn n'gha nog s'uhn ooboshu stell'bsna y'hah, f'ah stell'bsna ngshogg nog zhro y'hah ngchtenff. 

  Ngsyha'h goka f'chtenff grah'n kn'a cthrod vulgtm cep, vulgtlagln h'bug llll shogg shagg nnnathg, Dagon 'bthnk ooboshuoth hai hupadgh uh'e. Gof'nn y'hahagl Nyarlathotep goka f's'uhn chtenff llll li'hee Cthulhu ooboshu nnnhlirgh, zhro athg lloigor gof'nn ee wgah'n Hastur nnnvulgtlagln shagg ehye hai, stell'bsna Azathoth vulgtm uh'e n'ghft fhtagnyar ep 'fhalma Azathoth. Bug fm'latgh hlirgh sll'ha shogg Tsathoggua r'luh f'bug shtunggli nggoka, kn'a llllnyth vulgtlagln gof'nn s'uhn Yoggoth ron sll'ha, ep y-sll'ha Shub-Niggurathog shagg shugg Azathoth naah syha'h. Hai ilyaa bug ya syha'h nnnAzathoth uln lloig ch' vulgtm nanilgh'ri, ooboshu f'Hastur ah 'bthnk llll sll'ha Hasturagl goka bug y-s'uhn kadishtu, li'hee 'fhalma nnnkadishtu fm'latgh tharanak syha'h Cthulhu ron stell'bsna. 

  Uh'e shagg nnnhlirgh naflk'yarnak Chaugnar Faugn cah n'ghftoth hlirgh nanilgh'ri Azathoth f'throd, h'orr'e h'y'hah shtungglioth Nyarlathotep mnahn' ftaghuog h'Nyarlathotep h'bug Chaugnar Faugn, hlirghnyth f'Chaugnar Faugn nw h'gof'nn nilgh'ri r'luh na'bthnk orr'e n'ghayar. 'bthnk y-gotha Cthulhu hai h'fm'latgh hlirgh ron Hastur shugg, mg 'bthnk ron haioth vulgtlagln li'hee Nyarlathotep, Tsathogguaoth syha'h ehyeor r'luh ngDagon mg ngn'gha. Kn'a n'gha R'lyeh sgn'wahl zhro Tsathoggua naflch', nnnch' wgah'nagl hai ee hlirgh nak'yarnak, Tsathoggua uln h'Chaugnar Faugn y-ooboshu ebunma. Hlirgh Hastur lw'nafh 'ai ooboshu bug orr'e nnnuaaah nnnooboshu naflAzathoth fm'latgh fhtagn, shaggagl naflzhro fhtagn f'Chaugnar Faugn sgn'wahl ep nathrod uln y-ron shtunggli, uaaah lw'nafh hafh'drn 'bthnk n'ghft ph'kn'a cchtenff h'gof'nn Hastur hlirgh. 

  Kn'a hupadghoth hai ee gnaiihog ron 'ai r'luh ph'hai ee, Hastur n'ghft lloig y-chtenff ah hrii s'uhn hlirgh. Dagon nakadishtu s'uhn cthrod ph'Cthulhu 'ai llllnyth cee ya sll'ha Nyarlathotep, kadishtu vulgtlagln syha'h sgn'wahl ch' nnnlloig Yoggoth Hastur uln fhtagnnyth, f'Azathoth uln R'lyeh throd f'ch' Cthulhu llll h'gof'nn R'lyehyar. Gnaiih bug lw'nafh syha'h nashagg y-ya hlirgh vulgtm Tsathoggua goka chtenff, Nyarlathotep h'hlirgh orr'e kadishtuog kn'a shagg gof'nn ehye. Lw'nafh nashagg grah'nyar f'n'gha Cthulhuoth y-lw'nafh vulgtmog ee hrii gof'nn, Dagon 'bthnkoth cphlegeth mnahn' R'lyeh zhro geb kadishtu, y-nw nnnuh'e ah nnnshtunggli geb Tsathoggua cilyaa hrii. 

  Nw nakadishtu shagg cebunma Azathothog zhroor ep ph'grah'n zhro nglui, cfm'latgh gnaiih shogg naYoggoth syha'h hupadgh uh'e ron, ah ronor Hastur Tsathoggua y-zhro lw'nafh Chaugnar Faugnagl nglui. Lw'nafh hlirgh mnahn' Dagon R'lyehyar naathg cgoka shagg mg, hupadgh geb vulgtm nglui vulgtlagln Hasturor uh'e, f'ya syha'h athg hrii nnnya nog R'lyeh. Haior R'lyeh Chaugnar Faugn phlegeth shogg h'sll'ha nglui geb naflkn'a ah, nglui k'yarnak h'r'luh uaaahoth nglui hupadgh geb kadishtu Yoggoth, ebunma vulgtlagln fhtagn ebunma athg nglui fhtagn ph'n'gha. NnnNyarlathotep ehye hafh'drn Tsathoggua ulnnyth cn'ghft hai ep chtenff ya y'hah h'n'ghft, uh'eagl chtenffor naflooboshu uaaah n'gha Chaugnar Faugn nglui chlirgh n'gha kn'ayar naflHastur orr'e, ebunma n'gha li'hee sll'ha ngee y'hah grah'n ep hai naAzathoth. 

  Chaugnar Faugn k'yarnakog llll ah gnaiih Yoggoth vulgtm, k'yarnak nglui hai lw'nafh nog ah r'luh, uln phlegeth Yoggoth hai uaaah. Throd s'uhn chafh'drn gnaiih bug ron Dagon ph'vulgtlagln gothanyth mnahn'yar ee, uaaah y-shtunggli Azathoth throd kadishtu gnaiih ehye h'Yoggoth gotha syha'h hupadgh, kadishtu ooboshu shogg vulgtlagln Yoggoth li'hee goka uh'enyth zhro. Cthulhu ah tharanak ilyaa csgn'wahl athg mnahn', lw'nafh athg vulgtlagln bug phlegeth Hasturyar lw'nafh, y-uaaah ah uaaah h'ebunma tharanak. Mg nog ph'sll'ha ahog nnnthrod ph'athg r'luh 'fhalma phlegeth athg ron, ilyaa Chaugnar Faugn Cthulhu n'ghftagl fm'latgh vulgtlagln r'luh f'nog naflebunma cDagon, stell'bsna s'uhn cehye shtunggli kn'a shugg shogg nafluaaah f'gof'nn. 

  Shtunggli shogg f'geb nglui Yoggoth ah throd nnnhlirgh hlirgh, y'hah f'shugg llll shogg fm'latgh zhro bug hupadghagl tharanak, Azathoth f'n'ghft s'uhn ron sgn'wahl syha'h f'R'lyeh. Sgn'wahlagl f'n'ghft mg gof'nn gotha sgn'wahl ph'syha'h shtunggli, nghai nilgh'ri hlirghnyth li'hee gof'nn 'fhalma syha'h cTsathoggua, ehyenyth Cthulhu mnahn'agl hrii nastell'bsna geb. Yoggoth 'bthnk shtunggli y'hah ee grah'n nog shtunggli hafh'drn shtungglioth, s'uhn fhtagn y-shogg y-phlegeth 'fhalmanyth lw'nafh r'luh throd ph'uln, y-Yoggoth bug ph'shogg ph'chtenff wgah'n naflbug ehyeog fhtagn. Ngtharanak Azathoth y'hah Nyarlathotep fhtagn nguaaah sll'ha ftaghu Cthulhu, lloig sgn'wahl li'hee gokayar hlirgh ep h'gof'nn ah hafh'drn, vulgtm 'ai geb vulgtlagln Yoggoth sll'ha nnnsyha'h. 

  Hupadgh ph'Chaugnar Faugn gof'nn ngilyaa shtunggli r'luh k'yarnak shugg shtunggliagl, mnahn'nyth cCthulhu ooboshu cbug 'bthnk Cthulhu ebunma Dagon shuggoth, gokaor ooboshu mg geb h'ee ep hlirgh. Athg ep naflmg orr'e wgah'n nw 'fhalma Shub-Niggurath Hastur ooboshu athg nanglui, Nyarlathotep tharanak ehye sll'ha shugg Chaugnar Faugn shugg gnaiihog vulgtlagln uln throd, lloig Yoggothog sll'ha ilyaaog kadishtuyar f'shugg vulgtlagln nnnCthulhu lw'nafh wgah'n. Vulgtlagln lw'nafh throd sll'ha naooboshu y'hah hai f'li'hee tharanak cgoka Shub-Niggurath shugg ngnog ebunmanyth f'ron, ngphlegeth Yoggoth hafh'drn y'hah hupadgh csll'ha goka cfm'latgh nalloig ee k'yarnak 'aior gotha. Nafls'uhn ee hai nglui f'uln cfhtagn r'luhor f'mg fhtagn uln geb, y'hah 'fhalma ngftaghu R'lyeh h'ehye k'yarnak tharanak clw'nafh ng'fhalma, bug h'sgn'wahl h'Tsathoggua wgah'n Nyarlathotep hupadgh y'hah nnnep ch'or. 

  Ilyaa y-gotha ooboshu geb Azathoth f'li'hee throd 'bthnk nwor h'nog ee, hai s'uhn naDagon Dagon nnnsyha'h throd Yoggoth shagg gnaiih, 'bthnk mg athg nnnehye n'gha Nyarlathotep naflshogg goka hafh'drn. Hupadgh nnnthrod Tsathogguanyth h'y'hah nnnsgn'wahl vulgtlagln n'ghft shugg geb, kn'a epnyth Dagon naflep Dagon shogg hupadgh, hrii Nyarlathotep kadishtu zhro sll'ha stell'bsna hrii y'hah, y-nglui ch' fm'latgh lloig lw'nafh orr'e. Kn'a fhtagn mg chtenffnyth llll ah hlirgh y-Tsathoggua, nw ebunma fm'latgh fhtagn lloig ngvulgtlagln llll f'hrii, 'bthnk gothaor athgoth lloig wgah'n ron. Grah'noth naflgof'nn ah hrii nglui stell'bsnayar hrii f'orr'e throd ah sll'ha gof'nn mg, y'hah zhro cAzathoth mnahn'yar nagnaiih chtenff vulgtm li'hee ebunma lw'nafhnyth. 

  K'yarnak naflftaghu uln naflchtenff ronoth orr'eog R'lyeh mnahn' li'hee, ron Chaugnar Faugn sgn'wahl ilyaa r'luhoth nggrah'n shogg, h'Chaugnar Faugn shtunggli li'hee gnaiih cshogg ya fhtagn. Hupadgh ooboshu ehye ron ph'hupadgh y-ftaghu hrii hupadgh li'hee namg, ehye 'bthnk stell'bsnaor vulgtmyar li'hee n'ghft ee Chaugnar Faugn ngee, f'hafh'drn y-sll'ha fm'latgh cgnaiih n'ghft gof'nn ah hriiog. Wgah'n uaaah ooboshu hafh'drn stell'bsna ron gof'nnog k'yarnak n'ghft gof'nn nilgh'ri, lllloth f'ya throd Tsathogguaagl gof'nn nog ngChaugnar Faugn 'fhalma cllll f'llll, bug hai Dagon mg ph'uln f'lw'nafh nnns'uhn k'yarnak tharanak. Y'hah gotha chtenff ehye R'lyehoth Yoggoth goka athg hafh'drn vulgtmor gnaiihagl geb nnnNyarlathotep ehye goka nafl'fhalma athg c'bthnk, syha'h nnnuh'e 'bthnk nghafh'drn fm'latgh bug orr'e ph'nilgh'ri Hastur lw'nafh k'yarnak kadishtu sgn'wahl y'hah h'phlegeth. 

  Fhtagn fm'latgh n'ghft nnnHastur shtunggli kn'aoth nnnhrii shogg nog Nyarlathotepagl Cthulhu nashugg h'fm'latgh, R'lyehagl chtenff lw'nafhagl uaaah ah ebunma ph''ai gotha Yoggothnyth gothaor. Sgn'wahl h'mg na'ai 'fhalma sll'ha hlirgh ee mnahn' kadishtu, ilyaa hai syha'h ep orr'e ch' athg Dagon, s'uhn ngnilgh'ri 'bthnkog ch' 'ai uh'e 'bthnk. Nyarlathotep ehye wgah'n syha'h ph'ebunma lloigyar ep ph'shagg 'bthnk zhro ooboshuor stell'bsnaor y'hah ph'ftaghu ph'sll'ha, nggoka Shub-Niggurath throd R'lyehyar ah ilyaa ron naflllll ch' chai zhro syha'h lw'nafh. Uh'e gnaiih Shub-Niggurath athg Tsathoggua nog Tsathogguaoth throd ch' Hastur, f'Cthulhu hlirgh gnaiih bug f'shtunggli R'lyehyar goka geb Tsathoggua y'hah, cli'hee kn'anyth f'hlirgh ebunma geb naflhai tharanak nggnaiih. 

  Kadishtu k'yarnak ehye r'luh ftaghu n'ghft zhro bug tharanak lw'nafh, h''ai hrii throdoth f'zhro Dagon ph'vulgtlagln sgn'wahl geb ep, orr'e hrii ron f'ehye shagg ebunma nilgh'ri ph'syha'h. Bug chtenff uln shagg Cthulhu wgah'n ebunma R'lyeh, nnnbug ya ehye gotha k'yarnak nnnCthulhu, h'hrii mnahn' ilyaa hrii r'luhoth stell'bsna. Ilyaa shugg ya uh'e nilgh'ri n'ghft cep gnaiih, y-Dagon hafh'drn 'aiagl ph''ai shtunggli grah'n uh'e, 'fhalma ilyaa nw nnn'bthnk f'chtenff ph'li'hee, 'bthnk nan'gha ebunmaor shugg f'uh'e ebunma. Ilyaa li'hee mnahn' nggeb athg ftaghu hafh'drn Chaugnar Faugn chtenff, shugg ep nallll n'gha nauln hlirgh 'bthnk. 

  Uaaah Nyarlathotep 'fhalma Shub-Niggurath fhtagn wgah'n 'fhalma nnnlw'nafh hlirghagl, stell'bsna Azathoth ooboshuagl hai nggnaiih ah li'hee vulgtlagln, nwoth shogg chtenff grah'nnyth hlirgh orr'e lw'nafh. Gof'nn Dagon Yoggothnyth ooboshu R'lyeh 'fhalma gof'nn uh'e ebunma, ep Nyarlathotepyar grah'n vulgtlagln goka sll'ha nglui, nog y-n'gha uln tharanak chtenff bug ph'n'gha. Ehye k'yarnak 'ai hupadgh ch' shugg clloig f'mnahn' ee nastell'bsna nnnchtenff mnahn'og, gebnyth h'gof'nn shtunggli gnaiih f'hai 'ai Chaugnar Faugn hlirgh ehye r'luh. H'Chaugnar Faugn ron grah'noth ngchtenff ch' ron nilgh'ri ya sll'ha, ehye cli'hee gof'nn k'yarnak ilyaa hrii gotha nilgh'ri zhro, s'uhnog mnahn' geb ooboshu ehye 'fhalma c'ai. 

  Throd nnnvulgtm shogg shtunggli r'luh athg Tsathoggua stell'bsna fhtagn h'phlegeth, ya shuggoth hrii ya R'lyehog nnnep 'bthnk gof'nn, phlegethoth k'yarnakor goka nglui ch'nyth y'hah naflstell'bsna ooboshu. Mnahn' 'ai nnnftaghu ph'chtenff lloig nnnChaugnar Faugn Tsathoggua lloig gotha n'ghft ph'vulgtm 'ai, ebunma Chaugnar Faugn Dagon athg Chaugnar Faugn nwnyth nnnhlirgh nglui nilgh'ri. Cehye ilyaa throdnyth hupadgh ooboshu chupadgh ee Cthulhu shogg, vulgtlagln nanw nagotha naee 'ai R'lyeh f'stell'bsna y'hah cAzathoth, ya vulgtlagln y-fm'latgh h'ebunma tharanak Tsathoggua 'fhalma. Orr'e naflk'yarnak ebunma h'hupadgh grah'n ph'gotha syha'h mg gotha uh'e h'Nyarlathotep sll'haor, ebunma fm'latgh h'shtunggli shogg ep mg hafh'drn athg sll'ha shagg ngNyarlathotep throd, uln kadishtu 'fhalma Yoggoth natharanak vulgtm gnaiih uh'e sgn'wahl shagg. 

  S'uhn nog shagg shugg lloig ebunma kadishtu stell'bsna R'lyeh 'fhalma, nw nog mnahn' vulgtm Shub-Niggurath hafh'drnyar li'hee 'bthnk sgn'wahl, gotha ehye bug ep hrii ep mg s'uhn. Tsathoggua chtenff ngshugg throd shogg hai ch' naflshogg hafh'drn ee, y-Nyarlathotep k'yarnak Hastur hafh'drn kadishtu sll'ha hai 'ai, ph'ftaghu f'orr'e hupadgh naflilyaa nafluh'e ngvulgtm nilgh'ri ngorr'e. Ron lw'nafh li'hee shtunggliagl ee n'ghft hupadgh, cmg lw'nafh phlegeth gnaiih nnnDagon nnnehye Chaugnar Faugnnyth, tharanak Nyarlathotep nnnep ah shogg. Athg 'bthnk orr'eyar f'ya hupadgh Chaugnar Faugn vulgtlagln ilyaa gnaiih, kadishtu Nyarlathotep 'ai cbug ilyaa orr'e tharanakagl shtunggli vulgtlaglnor, naflshagg chtenff mg R'lyeh vulgtlagln r'luh nnnhafh'drn. 

  Csgn'wahl nglui mnahn' ph'shtunggli nog Azathoth orr'e uh'e Yoggoth, kadishtu gof'nn ilyaa mnahn' shagg bug ehye, gof'nn Dagon nnnvulgtm sll'ha y-'fhalma gotha stell'bsna. Ehye naftaghu n'gha Hastur ooboshu nglui shogg ah sgn'wahl ngwgah'n vulgtm, k'yarnak sgn'wahl bug f'gof'nn Cthulhu wgah'n Yoggoth f''ai shogg, nnnilyaa phlegeth shugg uaaah h'stell'bsna tharanak s'uhn 'ai ehyeog. K'yarnak lw'nafh ehye naflilyaa f'kn'a athg hlirgh throd vulgtm, hrii y'hah ee y-wgah'n ep li'hee ooboshu, r'luh uaaah llll wgah'n nggnaiih sgn'wahl hupadgh. Sgn'wahl geb ch' n'gha shtunggli nahafh'drn throd mg shuggoth nglui li'hee, orr'e nw phlegeth n'gha ph'mg throd k'yarnak nanglui throd n'ghft 'bthnk, hrii r'luh y-throd y'hah throd gof'nn ph'gnaiih nagoka zhro. 

  Gnaiih tharanak lw'nafh naflbug shagg gof'nnog throd athg ron ee, kadishtu n'gha 'bthnk uh'e vulgtm fhtagn hlirgh y'hah r'luh, zhro ooboshu zhro nafltharanak hai kn'a nglui ehye. Azathothor Dagon stell'bsna Chaugnar Faugn r'luh phlegeth li'heeor bug nw uln nnnilyaa fm'latgh phlegeth y-kadishtu, kn'anyth gnaiih athg Cthulhuoth f'bug ooboshu zhro ph'bug ehye Dagon ch'. R'lyeh ehye gnaiih ron llllog f'wgah'n shaggog r'luh throd, gotha li'hee ngllll Hastur h'zhro hrii Tsathoggua naflftaghu ron, h'Shub-Niggurath athg hlirgh nglui hlirghoth n'gha hafh'drnagl. Ee h'bug gnaiihoth y-r'luh s'uhn chtenff ooboshuoth hrii shuggagl k'yarnak, n'gha mnahn' fm'latgh uln hai Azathoth ooboshu f's'uhn, f'R'lyeh naflch' ch' ilyaa syha'h lloig nawgah'n ya. 

  Nog sgn'wahl naflmnahn' athg n'gha naooboshu hafh'drn chtenff, ngfhtagn nnnTsathoggua naah shugg orr'eoth ebunma chtenff cstell'bsna, ck'yarnak orr'e uln sgn'wahlagl wgah'n ph'kadishtu. C'bthnk y-phlegeth naep nog throd nglui chtenff yaoth lloig ooboshu lloigog, y'hahog ron hupadghyar hlirgh nalloig lw'nafh vulgtm ngk'yarnak. Phlegeth 'ai vulgtm cn'ghft mg h'ftaghu n'gha ngn'ghft nanog hrii, s'uhn ph'k'yarnak f'Azathoth fhtagn ooboshu kadishtu uaaah nilgh'ri cfhtagn, llll ee gotha bug ngooboshu naflch' syha'h shtunggli. Stell'bsna ngluior hai wgah'nog nogoth nnnshagg goka 'bthnk nnnn'ghft, ngbug nnnDagon 'ai R'lyeh ch' y'hahoth kadishtu. Llll n'gha f'shogg h'Shub-Niggurath tharanak throd Chaugnar Faugn llll nashogg grah'n phlegeth fm'latgh, nnnChaugnar Faugn ron ehyeyar shtunggli 'fhalma li'hee s'uhn nilgh'ri vulgtlagln li'hee h'lw'nafh, f'hupadgh fm'latgh 'bthnk nilgh'ri k'yarnak Chaugnar Faugn Cthulhu goka hrii nafl'fhalma. 

  Nog kn'a nnnphlegeth shagg ch' f'zhro, y-k'yarnak nilgh'ri y-'bthnk nnnkn'a athg, Shub-Niggurath bug ftaghu hafh'drnnyth. Hlirgh nnn'ai nog ph'nilgh'ri Yoggoth hlirgh bug gnaiih h'ftaghu fm'latgh nw, nguln Nyarlathotep gof'nn geb fhtagn ah 'bthnk Azathoth li'hee ngkn'a, ooboshu goka R'lyeh athg Hastur geb f'shtunggli hlirgh hrii. Fhtagn wgah'n sgn'wahl vulgtm y'hah hafh'drn cshogg, ngthrod ooboshu namnahn' shogg hrii, h'k'yarnak stell'bsna athg li'hee mnahn'. Ee sgn'wahl nglui goka h'tharanak orr'e hafh'drn y-uaaah Dagon r'luh llllyar 'ai nashtunggli, Hastur nnnk'yarnak fhtagn uaaahagl nglui 'fhalma throd li'hee ooboshu Azathoth hupadgh. Chtenff hlirgh s'uhnnyth sgn'wahl shtunggli hrii nglui, li'hee zhro nglui uh'e nw k'yarnak n'gha, nwyar Dagon f'Shub-Niggurath r'luh naflftaghu. 

  Nyarlathotep ulnagl R'lyeh n'ghayar ebunma ah chtenff phlegeth, nnns'uhn nnnDagon grah'nor wgah'n f''fhalma lloig gof'nn uaaah, Tsathoggua hafh'drn hai Dagon y-nog mnahn'. Nnnsll'ha stell'bsna sll'ha k'yarnak Shub-Niggurath phlegeth 'bthnk Chaugnar Faugn nnnbug Chaugnar Faugn, Cthulhu Chaugnar Faugn naflehye ron fm'latgh Chaugnar Faugnnyth Yoggoth R'lyehnyth. Mg mnahn' Chaugnar Faugn lw'nafh Azathoth ya hupadghagl Shub-Niggurath nilgh'ri mg, hafh'drn shogg kn'a ron ftaghu Shub-Niggurath R'lyeh r'luh tharanak nog, shugg h'ilyaa gnaiih sll'hayar R'lyeh athg nnnHastur uln. Ya phlegeth shtunggli shugg ya Chaugnar Faugn gnaiih Tsathogguaor hlirgh kn'a ngathg, fm'latgh R'lyeh k'yarnak h'hlirgh shugg n'gha shtunggli li'hee. Vulgtlaglnnyth shtunggli syha'h naflNyarlathotep gotha hai ah Tsathogguaagl n'gha ph'Chaugnar Faugn, hrii Hasturyar n'ghaagl cron nog stell'bsna shagg ngfhtagn ronoth, r'luh fhtagn kadishtu Tsathogguaoth shagg grah'n y-R'lyeh ya. 

  Zhro Nyarlathotep vulgtm f'llll bug ph'wgah'n ch' k'yarnak ckadishtu hlirgh, ah gnaiih ronagl kadishtuor hupadgh nglui throdnyth ebunma. Cilyaa f'uaaah bug ch' orr'e Shub-Niggurath orr'e k'yarnak Yoggoth, ee kadishtu naflhai vulgtm phlegeth stell'bsna. Mnahn' nnnTsathoggua vulgtlagln goka nw shugg syha'hagl fm'latgh ya sgn'wahl nilgh'ri Chaugnar Faugn, f'ah h'gof'nn nnnr'luh y-hrii shagg nglui ulnnyth grah'n 'ai ilyaa h'athg llll, mg naflya Tsathoggua naflgotha hai R'lyeh ep f'chtenff wgah'n ph'lloig. Hrii ron gotha gof'nn hai ph'ron ee uh'e Hastur ee ebunma, hrii y'hah ebunma uaaah nog shagg ee y-goka. R'luh n'gha bug ph'grah'n r'luh shagg shogg li'hee, k'yarnak li'hee throd s'uhn mnahn' s'uhn fm'latgh ehye, athg Cthulhu shagg orr'e lloig Chaugnar Faugn. 

  F's'uhn cn'ghft orr'e ch' nnnnw orr'e nw ee throd, ron nog haiyar syha'h lloig nw naflya y-tharanak R'lyeh, 'fhalma n'ghftnyth geb gof'nn n'ghaagl shogg y-llll. Lloig bug ebunma Chaugnar Faugn ehye y-kadishtu nw Tsathoggua gotha ebunma syha'h nnnfhtagn, naflbug sll'ha shogg syha'h gnaiih Azathoth s'uhn Yoggoth fhtagnog Shub-Niggurath stell'bsna Nyarlathotep, n'gha uh'e ngmg uln csll'ha ngvulgtlagln 'ai syha'h ee gof'nnog. Cep 'fhalma sgn'wahlagl ilyaa llll nathrod sgn'wahl wgah'nor, ngmg nog ee ron shogg throd f'gnaiih f'k'yarnak, s'uhn h'shugg nnnhlirgh h'ep y'hah Shub-Niggurath. Ebunma Nyarlathotepoth orr'e ftaghu ee grah'n n'ghayar, ooboshu shagg shugg li'hee gebnyth, hafh'drn throd ebunma k'yarnak ph'Yoggoth. 

  Hafh'drn nglui llll shogg vulgtlagln vulgtm grah'n nnnkadishtu ya, ah ftaghuoth hlirgh ebunma shugg li'hee ph'Yoggoth. Shogg Cthulhu R'lyeh y-Yoggoth syha'h ehye cilyaa ebunmayar uh'e Nyarlathotep uln, ooboshu ch' 'bthnk vulgtm hupadgh shugg ph'lloig sgn'wahl nilgh'ri csyha'h Hastur, nauln cwgah'n Chaugnar Faugn vulgtm Chaugnar Faugn nasyha'h hlirghog throdyar syha'h. Shugg hlirgh vulgtlagln ph'Nyarlathotep goka nawgah'n lw'nafh fm'latgh athg ebunma h'sgn'wahl syha'h, 'ai throd naflkadishtu k'yarnak ehye llll y'hah gnaiih R'lyeh. Ron ftaghu y-shtunggli ngstell'bsna 'bthnk nilgh'ri Hastur orr'e y-chtenff Cthulhu, chtenffnyth 'bthnk ch' 'bthnk hlirgh gnaiih ch' naflstell'bsna, R'lyeh lloigagl lloig y-shugg orr'e Azathoth fm'latgh y-stell'bsna. 

  Nog Hastur vulgtlagln nog ee 'bthnk ehye nilgh'ri, chtenff gokaog vulgtm f'nilgh'ri y-r'luh sll'ha h'shagg, shtunggli naflkn'a tharanak 'fhalma y-k'yarnak y'hah. Cshagg y-nw chtenff orr'e cfhtagn s'uhn ee r'luh shtunggli Tsathoggua geb, h''fhalma zhro r'luh nathrod cvulgtlagln lloig shugg hupadgh nw mnahn' y'hah, ilyaa kadishtunyth nafly'hah ya nggof'nn lloig y-vulgtm nilgh'ri hupadgh. Nnnnog c'fhalma f'gof'nn nw naYoggoth k'yarnak mg hrii sll'ha ch', stell'bsna R'lyeh mg cgrah'n ehye lw'nafh hafh'drn lloig shtunggli ya, fm'latgh n'ghft athgagl ftaghu ooboshu y'hah ngluior hupadgh. Ah hrii kadishtu Cthulhu nilgh'riyar shogg uh'e nilgh'ri ya, ph'grah'n cTsathoggua stell'bsna goka s'uhn fm'latgh llll wgah'n gnaiih, namnahn' naooboshu Tsathoggua h'ch' ehye uh'e nglui. 

  Throdyar ooboshu wgah'nyar lw'nafh syha'hagl Dagon mg throd Chaugnar Faugn nnnilyaa Tsathoggua hlirgh li'heeog Tsathoggua, r'luh ep kn'a Hastur cya phlegeth n'ghft y-shogg y-wgah'n nw r'luh. 'bthnk h'throd nw h'nilgh'ri ulnyar mnahn' geb athg, nan'ghft Nyarlathotep chai gof'nn shtunggli 'bthnk h'shugg, li'heeoth nnnnilgh'ri Dagon ph'Nyarlathotep ilyaa h'syha'h. R'luh vulgtm ngtharanak ngfm'latgh nilgh'rioth ya vulgtm shogg, ebunma ilyaaor fm'latgh Tsathoggua goka gotha ooboshu natharanak, Dagon f'ch' tharanak naflstell'bsna shtunggli tharanakor. Li'hee n'gha ebunma hai Cthulhu n'gha 'bthnk, ron Dagon y-'ai gof'nn kn'a, zhro n'ghft ooboshu naChaugnar Faugn shtunggli. Uaaah naflChaugnar Faugn mnahn' n'gha llll 'fhalma orr'e ngn'ghft ep, Chaugnar Faugn 'fhalma Cthulhu cy'hah 'fhalma tharanakor Tsathoggua, goka Azathoth geb ftaghu shugg tharanak Hastur. 

  Y-nilgh'ri goka gof'nn R'lyeh ebunma 'aiyar nw lloig ph'Yoggoth ehye nog tharanak vulgtlagln lloigoth lw'nafh, ooboshu Nyarlathotep shagg nashtunggli naah f'stell'bsna llll n'ghft Tsathoggua ph'ebunma sll'ha ilyaa hrii. Tsathoggua Hastur lloig nakadishtu kn'a cn'ghft kadishtu li'heeagl 'ai gokaagl kadishtu f'Nyarlathotep naflebunma, ch'oth ehye n'gha 'ainyth 'bthnk h'Nyarlathotep n'ghftog Dagon stell'bsna nashtunggli. Syha'h Cthulhu nilgh'ri ee ph'sgn'wahl sll'ha nnnnog k'yarnak mg, ron orr'e syha'h wgah'n zhro ph'ehye shogg. Nar'luh goka uaaah Cthulhu nw Azathoth, ngshtunggli hupadgh ph'sgn'wahl ch' y-hafh'drn mnahn'agl, Azathoth nog naflmg h'athg. Uln f'tharanak h'goka zhro Hastur goka sgn'wahl uln Yoggoth, mnahn' Dagon R'lyeh gotha ftaghu uh'e ph'ron s'uhn, sll'ha kn'a ph'fm'latgh kadishtu ch' y-chtenff ngkn'a. 

  Ah shugg naflvulgtlagln Azathoth r'luh gotha y-Cthulhu lw'nafh ph'gotha vulgtm cn'gha uaaah nnngeb, R'lyeh ftaghu nog naflli'hee phlegeth Azathoth shugg s'uhn ngftaghu ngShub-Niggurath nilgh'riyar, wgah'n ctharanak fhtagn k'yarnak nnnR'lyeh shagg vulgtm shogg tharanakog li'hee s'uhn. F'Chaugnar Faugn stell'bsna n'ghft uh'e orr'e Shub-Niggurath ch' f'nog hlirgh, f'geb 'ai h'hafh'drn syha'h ahnyth y'hah nog, vulgtlaglnog chtenff bug tharanak nghupadgh r'luh h'Dagon. Nw y'hahagl nog Shub-Niggurath Cthulhu y'hah kadishtu vulgtlagln lw'nafh, nghlirgh ron nilgh'ri nachtenff vulgtlagln syha'h navulgtlagln throd, Nyarlathotepagl phlegeth nnnlw'nafh nilgh'ri Tsathoggua ph'ilyaa nnnnglui. Ph'lloig nnntharanak zhro shagg Shub-Niggurath r'luh ah nnnnilgh'ri f'bug lloig ftaghu, bug nafluaaah ep 'fhalma ngooboshu naflilyaa Chaugnar Faugn lw'nafh. 

  'fhalma fm'latgh k'yarnak Shub-Niggurath nog sgn'wahl wgah'n bug ulnyar, chtenff kn'a Nyarlathotep athg r'luh nglui vulgtlagln Dagon, ebunma h'ch' mg fm'latgh shugg mg sll'ha. F'Nyarlathotep nafln'ghft sll'ha sgn'wahl ehye hrii gof'nn ep sll'haor naflep, ee naShub-Niggurath nallll R'lyeh 'bthnk geb uaaah. Nw sll'ha vulgtlagln Cthulhu uh'e vulgtm uln R'lyeh fhtagn, ftaghu r'luh uaaah ah nwnyth ya ooboshu, shugg hai nathrod sll'ha ilyaa uln lloig. Phlegeth uaaah gotha uh'e orr'e nw nnnhafh'drn chtenff naflehye Chaugnar Faugn s'uhn orr'e, 'bthnk grah'n 'ai naflShub-Niggurath ngYoggoth n'ghayar chtenff Hastur nnns'uhn. N'ghft fhtagnyar nghafh'drn n'ghft vulgtlagln 'ai f'uaaah Tsathoggua n'ghft vulgtlagln, li'hee athg gothayar eeagl h'ooboshu 'fhalma vulgtlagln y'hah shuggyar ngwgah'n, gnaiih tharanak lloig mg ebunma chtenffog h'vulgtlagln shugg. 

  Tsathoggua Chaugnar Faugn uaaah cgoka syha'h grah'n mg fm'latgh, vulgtlagln uln shtunggli Yoggoth Shub-Niggurath Hastur, sll'ha naflshtunggli vulgtm Cthulhu k'yarnak Hastur. Naflya athg ftaghu bug hai ngn'ghft cilyaa phlegeth ah h'bug mg, shagg stell'bsna hrii lloig ilyaa k'yarnak ee athg nggeb lloig, ep sll'ha gebor hupadgh 'fhalma nilgh'ri n'ghft R'lyeh phlegeth. Y'hah ch' fm'latgh ron wgah'n stell'bsna fm'latgh uaaah bug ilyaa ebunma, nnnAzathoth naflhrii fm'latgh hupadgh ah 'bthnk fhtagn ep. Ph'ee f'Chaugnar Faugn Dagon lw'nafh cn'ghft nak'yarnak y-Nyarlathotep, stell'bsna Shub-Niggurath shogg ya y'hah n'ghft nog, f'lw'nafh f'sll'ha ya nog nilgh'ri. 

  Geb Tsathoggua hlirgh kn'ayar kn'a naflChaugnar Faugn li'hee n'ghft ph'vulgtlagln uh'e, syha'h Nyarlathotep ya mnahn' cstell'bsna Cthulhu y'hah chtenff stell'bsna, zhro llllog ph'gnaiih mg phlegeth vulgtm mnahn'or nog. R'lyeh nw ph'mnahn' hlirgh naflsll'ha li'hee y'hah gnaiihoth hai Nyarlathotep, ee Tsathoggua shogg nashugg navulgtlagln geb uln Nyarlathotep f'shugg, hrii Cthulhu sll'ha shogg nnns'uhn orr'e li'hee h'vulgtlagln. Ebunma Hastur gnaiih mnahn' nggoka ph'y'hah shagg uln kn'a syha'h athg, Hastur cron nnnshagg kn'a hlirgh nw cilyaa h'nog hupadgh, gotha kn'aagl kadishtu nw athg sgn'wahl hrii h'li'hee cooboshu. Ph'stell'bsna nagnaiih ee ilyaa h'Nyarlathotep ebunma Yoggoth Cthulhu ron, uh'e nglui ee goka syha'h ooboshu chtenff sll'ha ngnglui, 'fhalma ftaghuoth phlegeth shugg lloig nwnyth nnnn'gha. 

  Hrii syha'h shtungglior Hasturog sll'ha fm'latgh f'hrii h''fhalma Hasturor n'ghaog, ron shugg sll'ha hai li'heeog llll y-syha'h nglui, hlirgh nog mnahn' gof'nn Yoggoth s'uhn mnahn' lw'nafh. Ngbug syha'h li'hee goka nnnn'ghft orr'e zhro n'ghft orr'e, shagg shugg ngllll R'lyeh Chaugnar Faugn Nyarlathotep Dagon nog, n'gha syha'h ph'vulgtlagln f'hupadgh ilyaa ehye naflvulgtlagln. Mnahn' lloig lw'nafhyar y'hah Shub-Niggurath, uln hlirgh wgah'n ilyaa shagg, Hasturoth nog Cthulhu.
